¶the feſtyuall prologus ¶the helpe grace almyghty god thrughe beſechynge blyſſed moder ſaynt marye v atte oure begynnynge helpe v ſpede v oure lyuynge brynge v vnto blyſſe neuer ſhall haue endynge amen myn owne ſymple vnderſtandynge fele well fareth ben ſame degree heuen charge ſoules holden teche theyr paryſhens ye pryncypall feeſtes come yere ſhewynge vnto holy ſayntes ſuffred dyde goddes ſake loue ſoo ſholde haue deuocyon good ſayntes better wyll come vnto chirche ſerue god praye holy ſayntes theyr hel • e ¶but many excuſe theym defaute bokes alſo ſymplenes connynge therfore helpe mencyon ye comynge cryſt goddes ſone worlde bye mā kynde deuylles bondage brynge well doer blyſſe euer ſhall laſt alſo comynge ſhall atte daye dome whan ſhall come deme wycked doer payne helle euer ¶but fyrſt comynge cryſte worlde brought ioye blyſſe hym therfore holy chirche vſed ſonges myrth alleluya ¶and ſeconde comynge cryſte ſhall ſo cruell yt tonge may telle therfore holy chirche lyeth doune ſonges melodye te deum lauda gloria excelſis weddynge daye ſhall neuer weddynge tokenynge vengeaunce cometh fyrſt comynge cryſt worlde ſaynt auſten ſayth ben thre thynges ryfe worlde byrthe trauaylle deth teſtament adam oure forme fader made ofſprynge hym borne ſykenes lyue traueyle deye drede cryſte came ſocour teſtamente borne traueylled deyed borne brynge men ſykeneſſe euerlaſtynge hele traueyled brynge man euerlaſtynge reſte deyed brynge man euerlaſtynge lyfe ¶this cauſe fyrſt comynge cryſte worlde wherfore yt wyll ſcape dome ſhall come ſeconde comynge muſte leye doune maner pryde herte knowe hym ſelfe wretche erthe holde mekenes herte muſt traueyle body good werkes gete truely leuelode traueyle body put hym waye ydleneſſe wyll trauayle body good werkes ſaynt bernarde ſayeth ſhall trauayle euer fendes helle drede deth muſt make hym euer redy god whan wyll ſende hym ſay ſhryue hym clene ſynnes abyde fro yere yere ſone fayleth anone ryſe vp mekely take downe ſhryfte fader thenne ſhall day dome haue grete worſhyp ryght knyght ſhewed woundes hath batell moche commendynge hym ryght ſoo ſynnes man hath done ſhryuen dooth penaunce ſhall moche worſhyp hym grete confuſyon fende ſhryuen ſhall ſhewed openly worlde grete ſhame hym ſayd ye fyrſt comynge cryſt worlde dominus veniet ad iudicium ¶the ſeconde comynge cryſt dome tūc videbūt filiū hominis venientem nubibus cum poteſtate magna et mageſtate ¶and theſe comynges ſhal ſo cruell xv dayes afore ſhall come tokenes grete drede ſo people may knowe ſone cometh dome secundum iheronimum ſaynt iherom ſayth ¶the fyrſte daye water ſhall ryſe vpō ſee ſhall hygher ony hylle xl cubytes ¶the ſeconde daye ſee ſhall falle doune ſoo lowe vnneth may ſeen ¶the thyrde daye fyſſhe beeſtes ſee ſhall make ſuche crye rorynge tonge may telle god hym ſelfe ¶the fourth daye ſee water ſhall brenne ¶the fyfte daye tree herbes ſhall ſwete blode maner foules ſhall come togyder nother ete ne drynke drede dome comynge ¶the ſyxte daye grete buldynges caſtels tour ſteples houſes ſhall falle doune brenne tylle ſonne ryſe agayne ¶the vii daye ſtones rockes ſhall bete togyder eche eche ſhall breke horryble noyſe whiche ſhall herde heuen ¶the viii daye erthe ſhall quake ſoo may may man ſtande theron ſhall fall doune ¶the ix daye people ſhall goo oute theyr dennes goo myndeles none ſpeke ¶the x daye hylles erthe ſhall euen playne ¶the xi daye graues tombes ſhall opened bodyes ſhall ſtande vpon theym ¶the xii daye ſterres ſhall falle fro heuen ſhetynge brennynge bemes dredefull ſyghte ſee ¶the xiii daye ſhall deye beren lyfe ¶the fourteyne daye heuen erthe ſhall brenne ¶the ſyxteyne daye heuen erthe ſhall made newe people ſhall ryſe aege thyrty wynter come dome dominus veniet ad iudicium cum multitudinie angelorum thenne ſhall come dome oure blyſſed lorde iheſu cryſte veray god man aungelles ſhewe woundes freſſhe bledynge daye deyed croſſe inſtrumentes paſſyon ſpere crowne ſcourges nayles hamer pynſons garlonde thornes ſhewe ſuffred paſſyon mankynde may ſory ferde haue ſworne paſſyon woundes ony membre body ſhal grete repreef theym amende theym worlde deye thenne wyll oure lorde iheſus cryſte gretely thanke theym haue done mercy worlde ſake theyr euen cryſten wyll ſaye thus theym venite benedicti patris mei percipite regnum c ¶come ye faders blyſſed chyldern receyue ye kyngedome heuen yt ordeyned ſoo reherſe vnto ſeuen werkes mercy wyſe called operacyons myſerycorde done nedefull ❀ whan houngry ye gaue mete sitiui et dediſtis miche bibere whan thyrſty ye gaue drynke whan herberles ye herbered ſoo forth ye werkes mercy whan ye gaue ony thynge name thenne ſhall lorde rebuke ryche people wolde loue forgyue treſpace ſake ſayd diſcedite maledicti ignem eternum goo ye curſed people euerlaſtynge payne helle whan houngred ye gaue mete c may full ſory wo euer lorde iheſu cryſt ſhall thus rebuke ſhall man lawe plete golde ſyluer gyftes helpe thenne ſhall nother mayſter ne lordeſhyp helpe ſette beſyde ryght man hath done ſo ſhall haue ſhall dyuerſe accuſers bothe aboue hym byneth hym euery ſyde aboue hym ſhall lorde iheſu cryſte dome man iratus eſt furor domini populo ſuo without mercy dyde mercy ſo accuſe ye leeſt thought euer mys ryght ſyde aungell tellynge redely whan often dyde mys ſyde fendes chalengynge hym theyres ryght wycked dedes vnder hym helle redy yf founde ſynne daye ſhall payned payne withouten ende daye poore people ſhall ſytte cryſt dome deme ryche people yt grete wronges dyde theym myght gete none amendes tyll daye dome thenne ſhall haue theyr wyll ryche people whan ryche done poore wronge nomore praye god quyte theym atte daye dome ſoo wyll god ſayth thus michi vindictam et ego retribuā put yelde euery man deſeruynge therfore whyle ye ben make ye amendes wyckednes make frendes dome men daye dome truſte ſhall come leeſt ye begyled drede payne helle neuer ſhall haue ende ¶narracio ¶saynt bede telleth houſbonde man englonde fyll ſyke leye deed euyn tyll morowe thenne roſe departed goodes foure partyes owne parte gaue poore men wente monke abbey nyghe ye water ſyde ye whiche water wente euery nyght neuer ſoo colde ſtode therin longe ſuffred grete penaunce whan aſked dyde ſo ſuffre grete penaūce ſayd eſchewe gretter payne ſeen wolde ete barley brede drynke water lyfe tolde two relygyous men paynes ſeen ſo grete coude telle theym openly ſayd aungell ladde hym place one ſyde ſoo colde tonge myght telle paynes therof ſyde ſoo hote man myght telle payne therof ſoules caſte one grete payne aungell ſhewed hym fyre came helle ſoo hote ſoo ferre hym thought myght ſee thought brent hym leme therof ſawe ſoules boyle vp doune cryenge waylynge wo alſo herde fendes crye caſte oute hote lede brymſtone make theyr paynes gretter ſo tourmented ye ſoules payne ¶now lorde god thy grete mercy haue mercy v kepe v fro tho paynes brynge v blyſſe heuen neuer ſhall haue endynge amen ¶dominica ſeptuageſima good frendes daye called holy chirche yt ſondaye ſeptuageſme cauſe ye holy chirche moder cryſten people ſhe taketh good hede chyldern good moder ought moche ſhe ſeeth theym full ſore ſyke ſynne many theym wounded dethe ſwerde ſynne whiche ſynne hath caught yere tofore namely cryſtmaſſe tyme ordeyned holy chirche grete ſolempnyte euery man ſholde beſy ſerue god power cauſe cryſt hym ſelfe ſhewed daye ſwetneſſe loue cryſten people man borne tyme ſame fleſſhe blode one v layde cradell poorely ony v cryſtened water ony v alſo came weddynge clenſe ſynnes make v holy brethern hym heyres ye kyngedome heuen ¶for cauſes cryſten people owen full gladde theyr ſoules tyme makynge ſolempnyte myrthe makynge bothe clene body ſoule frome maner ſynnes geoundynge theym grete ſadneſſe loue god cryſten people doynge grete almes theym haue nede harme hyghe ſolempne feeſt torned foule fylth ſynne grete ſykenes ſoule pryde dyuerſe wyſe clothynge many dyuerſe gyſe vſynge grete couetyſe lecherye ye ſueth alwaye glotonye ſlouthe goddes ſeruyce iapes vanyte ſyngynge rybaudry ſpekynge vanyte cauſed moche ſlouthe amonge ſuche people mooſt worthy mooſt harlatry ſpeke thus theſe ſolempne hye feeſtes ordeyned grete worſhyppe god oure bleſſed lady al ſayntes heuen ben torned grete offence god wherfore moder holy chirche ſeynge chyldern ſuche dyſpayre moder full compaſſyon ſory herte theym daye ſhe leyeth doune alleluya ſonges myrthe melodye taketh tractus ben ſonges mornynge ¶alſo holy ſacramente weddynge moche defouled vanyte ſynne therfore leyde doune theſe dayes aduente many ben wedded gyueth theym luſte lykynge bodyes fleſſhely luſte worlde thynketh full lytell dethe full greuous cometh ſoo ſone redde grete clerkes ſpedefull mannes ſoule goo hous corp wepynge goo houſe grete reuell moche myrthe ſuche thynges maken man forgete god hym ſelfe bothe ſyghte corſe maketh man thynke dethe ſpecyal thynge putte awaye ſynne vanyte worlde solamon ſayth thus ſone fili memorare nouiſſima tua et ineternum none peccabis sone haue thy mynde thou ſhall deye thou ſhall neuer ſynne deedly thus holy chirche hauynge grete compaſſyon chyldern ordeyneth thre maner ſalues helpe hele chyldern ben thynke dethe inwardely labour beſely chaſtyſe body reſonably fyrſt thynke deth inwardly holy chirche gyueth enſāple day ye offyce maſſe circūdederūt ſykenes deth hath beclyped thꝰ ſayth techȳge euery gode childe haue mȳde beſtade wt deth euery ſyde ſo moche yt may ſcape waye euer deth ſueth hym wt bow drawen arowe euer therin redy ſhote hym wote neuer tyme ¶this pryncypall ſalue euer man taketh herte put awaye maner vanyte vayne myrthe vnderſtonde better ſhewe enſample ¶narracio ¶i rede kynge euer heuy ſorowe wolde neuer laughe ne make mery chere euer mornynge heuynes therfore meyne men greued therwith yede kynges broder praynge hym ſpeke kynge ſayd greued tho aboute hym heuy chere coū ſeylled hym leue make lyght chere tyme comynge thenne kynge wyſe thought chaſtyſe broder within whyle full wroth badde hym go home doo thenne maner countree whan man ſholde put deth ſholde come trompettes trompe afore gate ſayd kynge byddynge theym go trompe afore broders gate men go areſt hym brynge hym kynge meane whyle ye kynge called hym ſeuen men truſte badde whan broder come drawe theyr ſwerdes ſette breſt afore herte whan broder comen dyde kynge badde thenne ye kynge commaunded men daunce make reuell yt coude ſo dyde ſayd kynge broder arte thou ſo heuy chere heue vp thy heed mery myrthe made ye anſwered ſayd ſhold mery chere ſe ſeuen ſwerdes ſet herte wote ſhall deth fyrſt ſayd kynge put vp ſwerdes ſpake broder fareth ye vii deedly ſynnes euer redy reue ſoule ye herte maketh lyf body thenne ſayd broder crye mercy knewe neuer tyl ſhall wyſer euer ſaye boldly yt wyl take herte ſhall haue better wyll loure laughe ſyghe glad wepe ſynge ſo yt ſhall fynde ye mynde deth ye pryncypal ſalue al maner ſynne alſo pryncypaly muſt haue mynde ye paynfull deth ſauyour yt ſuffred v whiche made mencyon fyrſt chapytre trenys attendite videte ſi eſt dolor ſimilis ſicut dolor meus ¶that ſalue labour beſely worlde labour ſpeketh ſaynt poule pyſtle daye ſayth sic currite vt cō prehendatis renne ye ſo ye may haue game rennynge ye ſhall vnderſtande yt renneth ye game enforſeth hymſelf myght rēne faſt ryght ſo muſt euery ſeruaunt god enforce hȳ labour beſely degree yt god hath ſette hym men holy chirche muſt labour ſtudyenge prayenge teche people lawe god lordes rented men muſt labour kepe holy chirche reſte pea comyn people muſt labour gete lyuynge thyſe degree themſelf ſoule body man ſholde excuſe hym labour cryſte goſpell gyueth enſample ſayenge thus primo mane conducere operarios huſbounde man wente gardyn vyneyerde pryme agayn vndern myddaye euen ſonge tyme hyred people labour ye tydes ye daye vnderſtande ye grees ye worlde iob ſayth man born lobour traueyle worlde byrde flee ſaynt bernard ſayth wyll labour worlde ſhall labour fendes helle teſtament adam lefte ofſprynge labour traueyle ¶to labour gyueth enſample reherſeth god made adam eue labour kepe paradyſe badde theym ete fruytes paradyſe excepte one tree kepte hȳ ſelf often ſawe ye tree ſholde thynken hym made theym knowe hym theyr god ſholde ete therof payne deth dampnacyon thenne fende ſawe theym ſo moche ioye hym ſelf ſo moche payne woo hadde grete enuye theym wente eue aſked ete ye fruyte tree ſhe ſayd god hath forbode v tree payne deth ſayd ye fende wote full well yt yf ye ete therof ye ſholde lyke god knowynge bothe good euyll yf ye wyl proue yt ſaye ſothe ete therof aſſaye toke eue ye fruyte gaaf adam badde hȳ ete therof aſſay loued well wolde wrathe toke apple ete anone therwith eyther theȳ ſawe others ſhappe aſhamed toke leues fygge tree ſo couered mē bres came lorde adam ſayd quare feciſti hoc haſt yu ſo ſayd mulier quā dediſti mi chi ſociam woman badde ſayd lorde eue dydeſt yu thus serpens decepit ſerpent begyled thenne myght deye paradyſe ne ſuffre penaunce therfore droof theȳ naked worlde yt full wretched wepynge waylynge go gete theyr mete wt grete labour traueylle deye laſte prayed adam lord ſore wepȳg ſholde take grete vengaunce vpon haue mercy theym pyte begyled enuye malyce fende innocen ••• themſelf wyſt dyde 〈…〉 lorde pyte theym 〈…〉 clothed pylches badde go labour traueyle theyr lyuynge ſayd eue dolore paries filios ſorowe woo thou ſhalt bere thy childern toke adam inſtrumentes labour lefte ¶by ye ſhall vnderſtande take enſample labour beſely adam eue laboured beſely fende neuer ouercome theym fende deſyreth noo whan wolde tempte man fynde hym ydle therfore knowe ye well ryche ſalue agaynſt ſynne labour beſely ¶the thyrde chaſtyſe body dyſcretly vnde paulus caſtigo corpus meum et ſeruitutē redigo ſhall chaſtyſe body dreſſe ſeruyce ſoule mānes fleſſhe ſo wylde ſo luſty ſynne wyll waye leue luſte ſerue god yf chaſtyſed penaūce muſt chaſtyſed ſome tyme payne thus dyde adam eue enſample al ſhall come ſholde ſame many yere deth eyther theym ſtode water nyghtes vp chyn one ferre ſuffre penaunce tyll fleſſhe grene graſſe colde thenne come fende eue bryght angell ſayd god hath ſent hym heuen badde go adam ſaye hym god badde hym leue penaunce treſpace forgyuen ¶and eue dyde ſo adam wyſt well came fende god ſayd eue whan god droof v paradyſe ſynne compaſſyō v wept ſore hym prayed hym mekely mercy ſetted v penaunce lyues ende ¶and therfore go agayne penaunce ſhall mede ¶and therfore go agayne thy penaunce goddes name ¶yet fende come agayne ſeconde tyme ſayd eue god grace hath take rewarde youre penaunce ye ſuffre hath forgyue thenne wente eue adam tolde hym ſoo thenne ſayd adam wote well hath ſayd ſoo oure enemye penaunce greueth hym v wolde haue v leue ſoo leſe mede forth penaunce oure lyues ende god taketh none hede begynnynge thynge endynge yet fende came agayne thyrde tyme eue ſayd goo thou adam ſaye hym yt began foule well fouler wyl ende fyrſte treſſpaced innocenſye dyſceyte fende ſynneth good delyberacyon wyll doo god byddeth hym wherfore youre treſpace worthy dampnacyon thenne eue aferde tolde adam ſo thenne adam ſyghed ſore wepte ſayd vnauyſed woman god made one rybbes helpe comforte techynge fende thou arte beſy combre agayne thynke oure fyrſte ſynne ſtanke ſyght god yt oure ofſprynge ſhall enfecte haue repreue therof worldes ende wherfore though myght doo ſo moche penaunce oure ofſprynge myght yet lytell quyte oure lorde god treſpace god ſpecyall grace alowed good wyll thenne wente eue agayne penaunce adam badde ſayd adam god wyl ſende v oyle mercy whan tyme mercy ¶and ſo adam eue dyde theyr penaunce theyr lyues ende whan adam lyued ixc yere xxx xxx ſones xxx doughters deyed buryed togyder adā eue thꝰ ye may ſe wel yt adam eue ful holy dyed thought dethe full inwardely laboured full beſely chaſtyſed fleſſhe full reſonably ſo muſte ye come theym wyll come ioye paradyſe tokenynge therof ſondaye called ſondaye ſeptuageſime nombre lxx whiche nombre begynneth daye endeth eeſter euen ſo holy chirche mornyng day tyll eeſter euen ſhe taketh comforte agayne partye one alleluya tracte yet ful myght tylle ſaterdaye eeſter weke whiche called dn̄ica albis ſhe layeth doune tracte grayell ſyngeth double alleluya techynge cryſten people laboure penaunce truely tyll ſaterdaye mannes lyues ende tyll ſoule goo reſt yet ſoule full reſt tyll ſaterdaye albis tylle daye dome whan body ſoule ſhall come togyder clothed albis whyte vii tymes whyter ſonne ſhall ſynge double alleluya ſaye lorde make v ſaufe euer laſtynge blyſſe ye whiche brynge v yt v deyed rode tree amen ¶dominica longe lyfe ye grace god mercy goodneſſe ſoo moche yf wyll doo oure beſynes dylygence ſerue god pleaſe hym wyll gyue v moche ioye blyſſe heuen gaue adam eue lyued ſoo longe wyll haue ioye blyſſe muſte doo thre thynges one muſte hate ſynne namely ſuffre trybulacyon mekely almes dedes wylfully dayes ſhorte muſt trybulacion ſuffre mekely pacyente herte grutchynge dyſeaſe cometh ſpecyall grace remedye ſynnes worlde penaūce elles grete encreaſynge ioye worlde wherfore goddes appoſtle ſaynt poule wyll cryſten people ſhall take example hym ſuffered moche trybulacyon pacyentely reherſeth pyſtle daye ſayd thus laboribus plurimis ſaynt poule ſayth haue many grete trauayles often tymes pryſon ſore bounden chaynes yron ouin que virgis ceſus fyue tymes beten roddes ſcourges bare body paynems semel lapidatus one beten ſtones thre tymes ſhyppe brekynge nocte acdie profoū mari fui grounde ſee nyght daye sepe percuſis fluuiū many tymes peryl flodes periculis latronum peryll theues peryll falſe bretherne ſhewed trewe loue falſe counſeyled done dyſeaſe trouble fame et ſiti houngre thurſte ieiuniis multis moche faſtynge multis vigiliis longe wakynge frigore colde many myſcheues peryl longe telle ſuffered good wyll euer thanked god ſwete loue well wyſt trybulacyons dyſeaſe ſynne hadde done tofore encreace meryte ioye ſholde come wherfore cryſten people wyll pleaſe god maner dyſeaſe trybulacyon come theym ſykenes loſſe catell goodes dethe frendes take pacyentely mekely thynke cometh ſynne thou haſt elles grete encreace ioye blyſſe thou ſhalte haue cometh ſpecyall grace god vyſyteth cometh god ſendeth ſuffreth theyr wyll godeſygne loued therfore thanke god euer vyſytacyon beſeche hym euer mercy god knoweth oure entente therfore forgyueth ſoone theym aſke mercy meke herte thus muſte man ſuffre trybulacyon pacyently muſte alſo doo almes dedes dyſcretly whiche fygured theſe xl dayes xl ſyx tymes ten soo vi ye ſhall vnderſtonde ſyxe werkes mercye comen oute ten commaundementes whiche ben theſe gyue mete drynke clothe herberowe vyſyte pryſones comforte ſyke blynde lame burye ben deed theſe vi werkes mercy whiche cryſten people muſte doo wyll ſaued haue mercy god wherfore ſexageſime begynneth daye endeth weneſdaye eeſter wyke whiche holy chirche ſpeketh thus venite benedicti patris mei c come ye faders blyſſed chyldern take kyngedome heuen ordeyned theſe ſame wordes god ſhall ſaye daye dome hath done almes dedes dyſcretely fulfylled werkes mercy yf power ben power muſte theyr good wyll ſhall fulfyll dede muſt doo dyſcretly god teched daye goſpell example ſayth thus exiit qui ſeminat ſeminare ſemen ſuum man wente ſowe ſedes ſewe ſome felle waye foules come ete ſome felle amonge thornes loſte ſome felle good erthe brought forthe hondred folde encreace lorde iheſu ſayth thus hym ſelfe ego ſum via veritatis et vita veray ryghte true lyfe waye heuen thenne falleth fede beſyde waye gyueth goodes almeſſe cryſtes ſake dyſcretly ſecretely vnto poore nedy pryde pompe vayne glorye worlde ond ſo leſeth mede preue enſample ¶narratio ¶there irlonde wonder ryche man dyde moche almes lyfe ſoo moche people wende ſaynt whan deed appyered one yt loued well lyfe blacke ony pytche horryble ſtynke ſayd ye wene ſaynt ſuche thou ſeeſt ſayd thy almes dedes ſayd wynde vayne glorye hathe blowen theym awaye doth almes vayne glorye worlde leſeth mede fendes ayer deſtroyeth alſo leſeth mede gyueth almes ſuche knewe ben deedly ſynne ſo mayntene theyr ſynne ſede falleth amonge ſtones wexeth drye ſoo leſeth mede ſede falleth amonge thornes gyueth good ryche people hath nede therto ſoo leſeth theyr mede ſede falleth good erth gyueth almes good true people goddes erthe ſede ſhall gyue hondred folde encreace euerlaſtynge ioye blyſſe ſhall euerlaſtynge fode theym done thus theyr almes dyſcretly ye muſt alſo hate ſynne namely flee ye ye may hateth ſleeth ſynne loueth god god loueth hym god hateth ſynne ſoo moche toke vengeaunce worlde ſynne lecherye ſpecyall ſynne agaynſt kynde whan god ſawe ſynne reynynge worlde ſoo vnworthely ſayd thus thynketh euer made man ſayd noe fac tibi archā make ſhyp planed bordes ſhall teche make chambres take clene beſtes couple hym ſelfe mete drynke wt made noe ſhyp god taught hym ſquare botom ccc cubytes lengthe l cubytes brede xxx cubytes hyght ſhyp makynge hondred yere ſhewe mercyable god taryenge loke yf people wolde amende theym lothe vengaunce ye people euer lenger wors helpe aungels maner byrdes beeſtes brought noe whan brought ſhyp lorde bad noe wyfe thre ſonnes go ſhyp ſelfe no wyfe ſonnes wyues theym ſelfe yt men ſholde comen woman soo whan god cloſed dore without forth quadraginta diebꝰ et quadraginta noctibus aperti ſūt celi thenne rayned xl dayes xl nyghtes yt water bare ye ſhyp hygher ony hylle xl cubytes ſtode ſtyll c dayes xl drowned worlde bothe people beſtes ſaue thoſe ſhyp yet ioſephus ſayth armany hylle called barus hyer water therfore dyuerſe people haue opynyon moche people ſaued soo noe ſhyp yere put rauen brynge worde knowe yf rayne water ſeaced came agayne thenne ſente douue ſhe came agayne brought braunche olyue bylle noe knewe well water ſeaced ſome place god bad noe wente toke vnclene beſtes clene brente vnclene beſtes ſacrefyce god pleaſed god ſo well gaue come theym leue ete fleſſhe clene beeſtes drynke wyne flood people ete dranke noo thynge water erthe ſoo fertyll ſelfe fore people neded none fode ſuche came ye erthe thꝰ may ye ſee vnderſtonde grete vengeaunce god toke worlde ſynne moche ſynne euer tho dayes moche many degree wherfore drede leſte god wyll take vengeaunce v wolde tyme prayer holy chyrche good ſayntes eſpecyall prayer oure lady ye ſhall enſample ſaynt domynicke prayer ſawe oure bleſſed lorde iheſu cryſte holdynge thre ſperes honde redy ſhote theym worlde vengeaunce ſynne thenne came oure bleſſed lady knelynge oure lorde ſayd dere ſone wyll ye doo ſayd dere moder worlde ſoo full ſynne pryde couetyſe lecherye dyuerſe ſynne wyll ſhote theſe thre ſperes vengeaunce people thenne ſayd oure lady dere ſone haue mercy theym abyde whyle haue ſomme true ſeruauntes whiche ſhall preche teche people torne theym frome ſynne thus prayer oure blyſſed lady god ſpared take vengeaunce worlde ſo full ſynne curſed lyuynge falſe extorcyon oppreſſyon poore people crye god ſocoure helpe wherfore full lyke ſhall ſmyten full ſoone ſomme vengaunce dethe dethe peſtylence wherfore nedefull v praye beſely oure blyſſed lady ſhe may praye v dere ſone oure lorde iheſu cryſte ſpare v oure dayes may haue grace mercy euer amen ſaynt charyte dampned hell ſo fell ſyke felyd hym ſelfe ſholde deed thought wycked lyuynge toke ſuche contrycyon hym ſo grete ſorowe wepte nyght day euer whan ſynne came vnto mynde ſo lay ſeuen dayes ſeuen nyghtes ſhroue clene toke grete repentaunce hym euer cryed god mercy people grete pyte hym ſo deyed happened ſo monke abbaye dyed ſame tyme made abbot come agayne tell hym fared ſoo dyde ſayd abbot whan comen syr come kepe promyſſe pray gyue leue go agayne go ioye ſayd abbote ony dyed whan thou dyed wente vnto ioye thou ſayd ye forſoth one ſoule ſuche man tolde name ſayd abbote ſe well thou arte monke ſome fende come tempte know wel yf ony ſoule payne one tho ſayd mō ke full vnworthely ony man knowe ye preuyte goddes dome man ſo gret contrycyon repentaunce wepte ſo bytterly hys ſynnes water eyen peryſſhed thoroughe al clothes vnto grounde wherfore go thou thyder morowe whan thou fyndeſt trewe ſaye byleue go euer laſtynge ioye blyſſe went abbote thyder founde trewe monke hadde ſayd abbot knelyd downe thanked god bad people glad yt god ſo mercyfull knowelge ¶here ye may ſe grete cō trycyon man quenched grete payne ordeyned hym thus ye may ſe grete helpe mannes ſoule contryte ſory ſynne drawe man ye cōtrycyon thoſe l dayes pſalme ſawter miſerere mei deus reherſed theſe dayes ony tyme yere whiche thus moche ſaye god thy mercy haue pyte whan man ſory ſynnes ſayth thus ſorowefull herte god heryth prayer forgyueth hym treſpas ſoo neuer full purpoſe ſynne amende hym parfyte loue charyte withoute ony feynynge hathe charyte withoute feynynge auaylleth enſample ¶narracio ¶there man fyue ſones hadde foūde theym longe ſcole coſte hym moche good ſo day called fyue ſonnes hym ſayd chylderne haue founde longe ſcole haue ſpente moche good vpon ſe noo grete profyte therof wherfore ye wyll amonge aſſoyle queſtyon wyll doo coſte ne fynde lenger ſcole aſked theyr fader ye queſtyon ſholde aſſoyled ſayd olde feble may lyue longe therfore wolde wyte thynge wolde brynge mannes ſoule ſoneſt heuen anone eldeſt ſone anſwered ſayd ſothe fader prechynge techynge wyll brynge mannes ſoule ſoneſt heuen ony thynge well ſayd quod ye fader ſayeſt thou ſeconde ſone anſwered ſayd fayth true byleue brȳgeth ſoule ſoone heuen ſayeſt thou queſtyon thyrde ſone ſayd good prayer almes dedes bryngeth ſoule ſone heuen ſayeſt yu mater fourth ſone ſayd pylgremage goynge grete penaūce ſufferynge brȳgeth ſoule ſoner heuen ony theſe ſayeſt thou ye mater fyfte ſone ſayd forſoth fader thynge brȳgeth ſoule ſoner heuen theſe ſayd fader forſoth fader ſayd charyte vertue yt euer man haue lacketh charyte auayleth heuen wardes though man praye almes dedes go gylgremage haue full fayth byleue teche preche faſt ſuffre penaunce neuer ſoo moche crye wepe neuer ſo lowde charyte god hereth hym accordeth ſaynt poule pyſtle ſayth thus si linguis hominū loquar c though ſoo eloquent ony man ony aūgel et ſi habuero prophetiam et omnem ſcientiā though connynge worlde knewe prophecye preuyte god omnem fide vt mōtes tranſferam though ſo moche fayth yt myght meue hylles et ſi diſtribuerem cibos pauperū thoughe dealed good poore people goodes ſake corpus meū vt ardeā body brenne hote fyre caritatē autē nō habe michil michi prodeſt ye haue charyte profyteth heuen wardes wherfore nedeful mooſt neceſſary euery ſoule yt wyl ſaued haue charyte thoughe man ſayth yt loueth god loueth euen cryſten deceyued yt loueth god loueth neyghboure good entent thus muſt man haue full charyte yt wyll ſaued charitas cooperit multitudinē peccato rum charyte couereth multitude ſynnes dyeth deedly ſynne charyte ſhall dampned therfore vertues charyte mooſt vertuous mooſt neceſſarye mannes ſoule yet muſt haue ſtable faythe withoute flaterynge byleue ſadly holy chyrche techeth byleue faythfully fader ſone holy ghooſt fader full god ſone full god holy gooſt full god theſe thre perſone ben one god made thynge noughte ¶this faythe fyrſte ſhewed holy patriarke abraham vale mambre ſawe thre fayre men comynge towarde hym worſhypped one yeuynge enſample cryſten people ſe ſpyryte fader ſone holy gooſt thre perſones one god hede worſhypped theym one god alſo ye muſte byleue incarnacyon oure lorde iheſu cryſt oure lady conceyued holy gooſt without wemme body fleſſhe blode one v veray god man deed buryed tercia die reſurrexit mortuis thyrde daye roſe frome deth lyfe aſcendeth ad celos ſedet ſteyed vp heuen holy thurſdaye deventurus eſt iudicare viuos et mortuos ſhall come agayne atte daye dome deme quycke ye deed fygured yſaac ſone abraham gate wyfe sara thrughe holy gooſt whan bothe paſſed age brynge forthe ony fruyte god ſayd abraham yt ſholde haue fruyte grete multytude ſterres firmament whan chylde borne called yſaac whan xxv yeres age god ſayd abraham wyſe take thy ſone yſaac goo ſuche hylle ſhewed hym offre hym ſacrefyce ſlee hym manere ſomtyme abraham hadde promyſſe god haue grete yſſue though loued ſone neuer ſoo moche yet tooke hym anone oute grutchynge agayne ſayenge commaunment almyghty god wente ſtreyght vnto hylle made ſone yſaac bere wood brenne hym ſelfe whan came hylle toppe abraham made awter wode ſette fyre toke ſone yſaac wolde haue ſlayne hym offred hym god thenne anone ſpake aungell abraham bad hym leue take ſhepe ſtode offre hȳ ſtede thy ſone yſaac ¶by abraham ye may vnderſtonde fader heuen yſaac ſone iheſu cryſt ſpared loue hym ſuffred iewes leye wode vpon backe croſſe ſholde done hym ſelfe ladde hym hylle caluerye dyde hym vpon awter wode croſſe made foure dyuerſe maner wode cedre cypre olyue palme theron dyed mankynde ¶thus may cryſte well called yſaac vnderſtonde laughter many ſoule broughte oute helle laughynge yt wente thyder ſore wepynge thenne lyke fygure cryſtes paſſyon longe borne ryght ſo daye cryſte hym ſelfe goſpell ſayd thus dyſcyples yt ſholde bytrayed tradetur enī gentibus et illudetur flagellabitur et conſuetur et poſt quam flagellauerunt eum die tercia reſurget ſholde taken beten ſcourges ſpytte vpon ſcourgynge doone vpon croſſe ſlee hym thyrde daye ſhall ryſe agayne lyfe ſholde haue better byleue therto vnto wordes anone tofore made blynde man ſe cryed ſayd iheſu fili dauid miſerere mei iheſu ye ſone dauid haue mercy ſayd lorde hym woldeſt thou ſholde ſayd domine vt videam lorde gyue ſyght ſayd lorde thy faythe hath ſaued anone hadde ſyght thenne thanked god muſte euery cryſten man wyll haue pardon god muſt haue full contricion herte ſhrifte mouthe ſatiſfaccion dede beynge holy charyte without feynynge ſtable fayth withoute flaterynge ſtere fayth wyll tell enſample ¶narracio ¶there byſſhop englonde hyghe groſthed byſſhop lyncolne holden greteſt clerke englonde worlde lay dethe bedde came hym grete multitude fendes dyſputed hym fayth ſo moche nyghe tourned hym byleue put ben myghtles laſt labourynge people pylgrymes ſyke people thoſe lawe dyſpenſeth vpon theyr conſyence thanne cauſe yt ſondaye daye penaunce therfore ye ſhall gynne youre faſte vpon aſſhewedneſday day muſt ye come holy chyrche take aſſhes preeſtes honde thynke wordes well ſayeth ouer hedes memento homo quia cinis e et cinerem reuerteris haue mynde thou man aſſhes thou arte come aſſhes thou ſhalte torne agayne ben dyuerce cauſes ye ſhall faſte theſe xl dayes one goſpell telleth daye thus ductus eſt iheſus deſertum ſpiritu vt temptaretur dyabolo holy ghooſt bad lorde iheſu cryſte go deſerte twene ieruſalem ieryco tempted fende forty dayes xl nyghtes faſtynge ſake ſhewynge vnto cryſten people vertue mede cometh faſtynge whiche ben expreſſed preface maſſe ſayd holy chyrche forty dayes thus qui corporali ieiunio vicia comprimus mentem eleuas virtutē largius holy faſtynge thyrſteth downe vyces lyfteth vp thought man vntoo vertuous largeneſſe goodneſſe geteth hȳ grete mede heuen ſhall euer laſte gete grace erth clerkes ſayeth ſpetell faſtynge man ſhall ſle adder bodely thenne moche ſleeth myghte olde adder fende hel came eue paradyſe lykeneſſe adder tempted glotony vayneglory couetyſe ryght ſo fende came vnto cryſt lykenes man leſt knowen tempted cryſt goſpell ſayeth cum ieiunaſſet quadraginta diebꝰ et quadraginta noctibus poſtea eſuriit whan cryſt hadde faſted forty dayes forty nyghtes kynde man hode houngred thenne came fendes vnto hym ſhewed vnto hym ſtones ſayd si filius deies dic vt lapis iſti pane fiant yf ſo yt thou arte goddes ſone heuen make thou theſe ſtones tourne brede ryght eue rauyſſhed whan ſhe ſawe appell temptacyon fende ete therof ſame wyſe hadde thoughte haue made oure ſauyour iheſu cryſte haue eten brede glotonye onely mannes mete ſoule luſt appetyte man thenne ſayd ſauyour iheſu cryſt vnto hym non ſolo pane viuit homo ſed et de omni verbo quod procedit de ore dei man lyueth onely brede euery worde cometh fro mouth god thenne fende toke ſauyoure iheſu cryſte dyde ſet hym vpon hygheſt pynacle temple thenne ſayd yf thou goddes ſone brynge thy ſelfe downe wtout mannes helpe harme yt may know goddes ſone thenne ſayd oure ſauyour iheſu cryſte non temptabis dominum deum tuum thou ſhake tempte thy lorde god yet came agayne thyrde tyme aſſumpſit eum dyabolus montem excelſum et oſtē dit ei omnia regna mundi thenne toke oure ſauyour iheſu cryſte ſette hym vpon hygh mountayne thenne ſhewed vnto hym kyngdomes alſo rycheſſe worlde ſayd thus vnto hym hec omnia dabo tibi ſi procedens et adoraueris ſhal gyue ye yu wylt falle downe worſhyp ſayd cryſt hȳ vade ſathanas scriptū ē enim dn̄m deū tuū adorabꝭ et illi ſoli ſeruies go ſathanas wryten yu ſhalte worſhyp thy lorde onely hȳ ſerue left hȳ went way tūc āgeli acceſſerūt ad iheſū miniſtrabāt ei aūgelys came brought hȳ fode ye fēde moſt beſy theſe xl dayes tempte people thre ſȳnes pryde couetyſe glotony nedeful haue thre remedyes ayē ſte ayenſt couetyſe vanytes haue ben herde kepynge goodes euer hath gadrede togyder faſte hath kepe nowe ſholde ye redy paye content ye dette vnto bothe god worlde alſo reſtore agayne ye haue taken wrongfully dombe fende within ye wene many tymes ſynne ſpeke ydle worde make people laughe ſwere grete othe dooth noo harme ſaynt poule pyſtle forbedeth euery man ſpeke ydle wordes ſayth thus dico autem vobis fendes myght doo harme euer fendes bete ſhe cryed peteouſly two ſyſters ſexſtens ſore ferde eyther comforted ſoo wente nere tyll wyſte ſpake ſpyryte ſyſterne ſayd ye knowe well clene mayden ony dede ioſeph ſuffred grete perſecucyon ſuffred mekely therfore god brought hym grete worſhyppe proſperyte ye ſhall hyſtorye longe therfore ſhall take mooſt nedefull atte tyme ioſeph fader named iacob xi ſones bretherne ioſeph fader loued hym mooſt ſpecyally therfore bretherne hated hym eſpecyall dreme dremed wherby ſuppoſed ſholde haue lorde ouer al ſholde hym worſhyppe anone toke theyr counceyll pharao bought hym named putyphar ye fende grete enmyte towarde ioſeph tempted ye lady ſore hym ¶poſt multos ita que dy iniecit domina oculos ī ioſeph et ait veni dormi mecū daye lady loked ioſeph tooke hym mantell ſayd come ſlepe ſoone ioſeph vnderſtode meanynge anone yede fledde waye lefte mantell thenne woman cryed tolde huſbonde ioſeph wolde haue lyen ſholde ſaye nay ſhe kepte mantell therfore lorde made caſt ioſeph pryſon pharao hadde put boteler baker felle ſlepe dremed whiche dreme tolde ioſeph ſayd kynge wolde reſtore boteler offyce agayne within thre dayes baker ſholde hanged within thre dayes ſayd ſo thenne happened ſo kynge dremed hym ſelfe coude man tell ſholde fall therof coū ſell ye boteler kynge ſent ioſeph whan ye kynge hadde tolde hym dreme ioſeph ſayd god ſente hym fayre warnynge puruey hym fore ſholde come ſayd ſholde come ſeuen plē teuous yeres corne maner fruytes vytayles ſholde come ſeuen yeres people ſholde ſpende goten fore thenne kȳ ge ſayd knowe man coude puruey ſoo well ſuche thȳge thou coudeſt wherfore make greteſt vnder realme ſhall vnto meat thy commaūdemente thenne anone ioſeph let make greteſt berne euer ſeen gadred corne faſt ſeuen yere ſone came ſeuen yeres thynge ſcars dere thenne iacob ioſephs fader herde corne ſell egypte ſente thyder x ſones corne whan came thyder ſaw ioſeph fell doune theyr knee dyde worſhyp vnto hym lyke dreme knewe hym thought ben lorde countre knewe wel ynough thenne ſpake theym latyn surge ſayd ſpyes come knowe ye londe ſayd n •• bretherne al one man ſones brother home theyr fader wyſt whether lyue mente ioſeph preue ye trouthe made bynde one theym hyght symeon ſayd ſholde byde hym tyll ſet hym home ſo lete fyll theyr ſackes corne preuely put theyr money thyr ſackes vnwytyng ſo whan came home theyr fader put theyr corne foūde theyr money tolde theyr fader thenne ſory symeon ſone lefte behynde pryſon ouer muſt nedes ſende hym whiche loued mooſt beniamyn ioſephs hole broder halfe bretherne ioſeph whan iacob fayled corne muſt nedes ſende thenne ſente forth beniamyn whan ioſeph ſawe beniamȳ myght forbere wepynge none delyuered hym symeon ſet theym mete fylled theyr ſackes corne preuely put cuppe dranke beniamyns ſacke bad theym go theyr waye none ioſeph ſente theym ſayd ye blame whyle ſo good chere bere waye cuppe ye dranke heuy ſadde ſayd ſoo ranſaked founde benyamyns ſacke came agayne ioſeph ſore wepynge whan ioſeph ſawe theym wepe owne broder benyamyn made mooſt ſorowe founden hym ioſeph badde theym good chere youre broder ioſeph thynge adred god hath ſente hyther youre profyte anone ſente fader ſoo dwelled togyder grete whyle londe moche proſperyt • ſtorye redde weke holy chirche goddes chylderne ſholde take enſample olde faders ſuffre trybulacyon parſecucyon mekely goodes whan taught moyſes ſholde moyſes wente thyder gadered olde people togyder knewe ye prophecy ſholde ladde londe ſayd theym god badde hym thenne full gladde wente hym olde yonge tylle come reed went whan moyſes ſawe people come prayed god helpe god hym ſelfe bad hym ſmyte ſee yerde et per cuſſit mare rubrum whan ſmyten ye ſee waye hym people ſee cloue two partyes ſo water ſtode ſtylle euery ſyde hylle grounde drye ſonde moyſes went forth people hym thenne thought pharao haue paſſed alſo ſewed ooſt whā hadde ooſt within ſee water wente togyder drowned hym ooſt whan moyſes ſawe people thus peryſſhed thanked god ſeuen dayes euery daye wente ſee thankynge god theyr paſſage makynge grete meledye lorde done ſoo yet mynde herof eeſter weke make ſolempne proceſſyon fonte reed ſee thenne wente moyſes forthe people deſerte tylle come vnto ye hylle synay lefte people benethe stabat moyſes ſuper montē moyſes ſtode vpon ye hylle god xl dayes xl nyghtes without mete drynke thenne god gaue
