people myght ſpeke hym clerenes abſcondit moyſes faciē ſuam thenne moyſes hydde face kerchyef thenne one leef wryten thre commaūdementes longen god thoſe ben theſe ¶the fyrſt thou ſhalte worſhyp thy god loue hym aboue thynge thou ſhalte dyrecte maner thynge goddes wyll thyn owne ſue thyn owne wyll ¶the ſeconde cōmaūdement thou ſhalte take vayne ſaye thou ſhalte called goddes chylde cryſten man ſerue fende thenne ſame yt vayne alſo thou ſhalte ſwere god parte body thynge yt made forderynge trouthe yet whan thou arte conſtrayned therto ¶the thyrde cōmaūdemēt thou ſhalt kepe thyn holy daye ſaye thou ſhalte erely vp late doune ſerue god holy daye yu arte werkedaye thyn owne werke beſy ſhalte thou holy daye ſerue god ¶the fourth cōmaūdement thou ſhalt worſhyp thy fader thy moder brought worlde alſo thy godfader thy godmoder made cryſten man thy fader vnder god hath cure charge thy ſoule ¶the v thou ſhalt ſlee man nother tonge thy honde thy euyll enſample ¶the vi thou ſhalte ſtele mannes good ¶the vii thou ſhalte doo lecherye ¶the viii thou ſhalte bere fals wytneſſe ¶the ix thou ſhalt coueyte thy neyghboures goodes ne thynge longeth hym ayenſt wyl ¶the x thou ſhalt deſyre thy neyghboures wyfe counſeyll waye doo euyll ſholde harme vylonye huſbonde· ¶theſe ben x commaundementes whiche euery cryſten man woman boūde kepe thus moyſes fygure token cryſt moyſes came gaue lawe cryſte came gaue grace mercye ſame maner moyſes fette people egypte thrughe reed ſee hylle synay ſame wyſe cryſte whan come prechynge myracles doynge fette people derkenes ſynne euyll lyuynge thrughe water baptyſme hylle vertuous lyuynge therfore wyll ſhryue hym clene leue foule lyuynge kepe commaūdementes god made couenaunt kepe cryſtenynge thenne ſhall encreaced hygher ony hylle erthe yt heuen wyll thus muſt fedde fyue loues two fyſſhes ¶we rede daye holy chirche goſpell cryſte fedde fyue thouſande people fyue loues two fyſſhes fyrſt loofe fyue contrycyon ſynne ſeconde ſhryfte mouth thyrde ſatyſfaccyon theyr treſpas fourth torne agayne ſynne often aferde ſhall well fyfte perſeueraunce good lyuynge two fyſſhes ben good oryſons almeſdedes theſe noryſſhed water yt wepynge teeres deuocyon theſe ii fyſſhes geten wyll ¶narracio ¶it wryten yt ſomtyme man yt called pyers ryche man ſo harde begger myght gete good hym thenne tyme happened ſoo many beggers ſette togyder place ſpake pyers myght gete good hym thenne ſpake one theym mayſter ſayd wyll ye leye wt ſhall gete noo good hȳ ſoo made wager thenne wente man forth came pyers place ſat hȳ doune ye porche ye halle dore bode tyll pyers came anone ſawe pyers ſpake ſo horryble pyers grete angre ſeruauntes came hym baſket brede toke loof myght caſt beggers hede ſmote breſte ſayd ſtoppe thy mouth therwith deuyll ſtoppe none begger caught loof ranne way felowes ſhewed loof ſo gate wager thenne nexte nyght happened ſo pyers ſhryuen brought bedde ſo dyed none fendes came take ſoule lady redy bad theym brynge ſoule ſo dyde nothynge helpe ſoule onely loof caſt begger ſayd fendes gaue agaynſt wyl therfore ryght ſholde helpe hym thenne went lady ſone praynge hym graunt ſoule go body gayne loke wolde amende hym thenne lorde bad bere ſoule gayne body whan ſoule body anone ſatte vp gaue grete ſyghynge called hym ſeruauntes tolde theym harde dome hadde dampned loofe caſte ye begger therfore none made ſelle good dealed poore people goddes ſake whan done ſo made hym ſelfe hermyte holy man ¶here ye may well wyte grete almeſdede prayer made man ſoo preuy god ſo ſyker ayenſt dome haue done almes dedes goddes ſake ſhall ſaued yf oute deedly ſynne ¶we fynde auoutry mā take mannes wyfe woman man thā huſbonde greuous ſynne ye ſhal enſample ¶narracio ¶there ſomtyme man made charke cole wood whan hadde made grete fyre leye nyght therby ſoo aboute mydnyght come woman rennynge fore man blacke horſe faſt myght ryde hunted aboute naked ſwerde aboute fyre ſo laſt man ſlewe moman hewe pyeces caſt fyre rode agayne myght soo whan man ſawe done many nyghtes thenne wente lorde tolde hym mater thenne lorde abolde knyght ſayd wyll wyte mente come thyder nyght founde man tolde knyght aſked ye ſpyryte dyde ſo thenne ſayd ſuche man tolde name ſeruaunt lytell tofore woman knyghtes wyfe leye huſbondes lyfe therfore bothe putte penaunce ſayd hors yt ryde ye fende yt breneth c folde wors ony fyre myght yt erthe payne muſt ſo ſuffre tylle helpe good prayer maſſes almeſdedes tolde hym many thynges knyght dyde thynges ſayd ſholde theyr helpe ſo delyuered payne euerlaſtynge blyſſe whiche god brynge v amen ¶dn̄ica paſſione dere frendes daye called ſondaye paſſyon weke daye lorde iheſu cryſte begane paſſyon daye iewes ſuche enuye hym cauſe tolde theyr defautes vyces meſlyuynge ſoo cauſe repreued hym daye full aſſented hȳ dethe ſo boute often letted ſome thynge mooſt fere comyn people helde hym prophete daye knytte theym togyder fully accorded wolde ſpare thynge ſholde deed wherfore goſpell telleth cryſt preched themple iewes rebuked hȳ ſpytuouſly ſayd nūc cognouimꝰ qa demoniū habes knowe thou haſt fende ye tempte hym haue made hym ſpeke ſome euyll wordes whiche myght haue put hym ſome repreef tolde theym goddes ſone redy haue ſtoned hȳ deth knewe theyr malyce iheſus autē abſcondit ſe et exiuit de tēplo iheſus hyd hym ſelfe went ye temple thus lorde daye began paſſyon wherfore holy chirche redeth weke boke iheremye prophete fyrſt prophecyed cryſtes paſſyon tolde maner iewes ſholde doo hym deth thenne ye ſhall vnderſtonde well ſame wyſe yt iewes purſued cryſt deth ſame wyſe fere gretely leſte ben moche fals people cryſtened purſuen cryſt heuen holy ſaynt auſtyn ſayeth ſynne greuouſly purſue hym heuen iewes dyde purſueden hym erthe ¶then yf ye wyte whiche thoſe ben take hede cryſte marked theym ſayd thus qui ex deo eſt verba dei audit god hereth worde god hereth worde god ſwereth many grete othes full falſely theſe ben tho purſuen hym heuen ben gladde theyr hertes whan haue done foule dede grounden foule curſyd lyuynge ſynne wyll amende theym prechynge techynge euer doo foule dedes anone ben redy fyght chy •• whith theym telle theym theyr defautes ſhewed lorde iheſu cryſte harme •• ndycyons people ſuche dayes ſhall haue many enemyes wyll ſaye trouth may preue enſample ¶narracio ¶there ſomtyme mawmette cyte wolde telle oony thynge ſtolen myſſed hadde soo happed tyme yonge man hadde ſtolen thynge ferde mawmette anone wente mawmette ſayd thus well wote thou mayſte doo grete ſhame vylony god byleue vpon thou dyſcouer wyll breke thy heed ſoo wente forthe waye ſoone come myſſed good praynge mawmette telle theym hadde whan hadde longe prayed atte laſte mawmette ſpake ſayd tymes ben chaunged people ben wors ſayth trouthe heed ſhall broken soo wyll ſaye trouthe ſhall ſhente ſoo true man ſhall hunted ſoo plucked ſhall wyte whome ſhall ſpeke whome may telle counſeyll truſte wyll ſoneſt deceyue hym wyll ſomtyme ſpeke mooſt fayreſt wryten booke kynges two knyghtes hadde grete enemyte one one hyghte ioab amaſa ioab ſayd amaſa met heyle broder kyſſed hym honde behynde ſlewe hym knyfe ſmote hym herte ¶thus fayreth nowe dayes moche people ſpeke full fayre people behynde theym wyll ſlee theym ſhrewde knyfe euyll curſed tongue theſe ben purſued hym heuen ſette noughte goddes worde though yf theyr e • e ſynketh downe theyr hertes wherfore god playnethe hym greuouſly prophete iheremye ſayd thus gylte founde faders yf haue treſpaced ony maner thynge telle ala ſhame obſtynat pryde god ryght ſoo treateth v ben wronge profred mercy aſke maketh hym mercyfull theym dyſpleſeth hym ſheweth loue none worthy thus ben theyr hertes harder ony ſtone thus ben wors thā iewes thus vnkynde hym ſhewed v kyndnes euer cryed v ſayd haue left erthe ye ſholde ſcrypture torne agayne wyll receyue ye lo armes redy ſpred clyppe yt heed redy bowed kyſſe ſydes redy ſhewe myn herte hondes foot bleden ſhewe ſuffred thou torneſt awaye frome yf thou parfyte lyfe wyll gyue treſour without nombre ſhall auaunce comparyſon gyue reſte without ende ſo faute ſhall founde thus oure lorde profereth techeth v ben full fewe wyll hym lette theſe wordes paſſe theyr hertes take none hede theyr mynde rycheſſe proſperyte worlde preſent lyfe take full lytell hede lyfe comynge lorde iheſu cryſt ſuffred dethe brynge v euerlaſtȳge blyſſe therfore cryſtes paſſyon maketh ye prophete grete lamentacyon grete vnkyndnes ſeeth mankynde ſayth thus thou man vanyte thou ſtynkeſt thy ruſty ſynne therfore crye wepe thou haſt thy hede garlonde floures haue one thornes thou haſte thy hondes payr whyte gloues haue many blody woundes thou haſte thyn armes ſpradde lede karolles daunces armes ben nayled tre ſharpe nayles thou haſte thy clothes pynched full ſmale body full grete wheles one thynge greueth mooſt thou ſetteſt paſſyon ſuffred full ſore thy ſake thyn horryble ſwerynge thou vpbroydeſte many grete othes myn heed eyen armes nayles ſydes woundes foot bone myn herte paſſyon thou ſholdeſt doo worſhyppe thou dooſt grete deſpyte repreef ¶narracio ¶we rede geſtes romayns emperoure ſent grete man londe iuſtyce came noo man countree coude ſwere othe ye nay whan iuſtyce came amonge theym made people ſwere bookes ſeſſyons gaue theym charge ſoo people toke enſample iuſtyce ſwere men dyde oure lordes paſſyon ſydes armes nayles face woūdes blode herte ſo forth toke ſoo vſe comyn people ſwore dyde thenne daye iuſtyce ſatte offyce charged people came tofore hym fayre woman clothed grene brought fayre chylde lappe blody martyred heed prycked face dyſfygured eyen oute armes broken hondes ſmyten thorugh nayles cutte foot cutte frome legges ſydes rente bowelles herte drawen oute body thenne ſayd woman iuſtyce worthy haue haue thus doo chylde ſayd worthy haue dethe thenne ſayd ſhe thou thy men youre horryble othes haue thus dyſmembred ſwete ſone iheſu cryſte moder vnto thus ye haue taught youre countree wherfore thou ſhalt haue thyn owne dome ſo inſyght people erthe opened iuſtyce felle doune helle people ſore agaſt lefte ſuche othes dyde amende theyr lyues ſoo lete v leue othes lyue cryſten people ſholde reuerence paſſyon lorde iheſu cryſt cauſe redempcyon whiche ſhall come euerlaſtynge blyſſe neuer ſhall haue ende amen dn̄ica palma rum good frendes ye knowe well ſondaye called palme ſondaye cauſe ſeruyce daye lōge wyl telle ſhortely called palme ſondaye saynt iohan ſayth lorde iheſu cryſt came betanye ſayth venit iheſus betaneam vbi lazarus fuit mortuꝰ quem reſuſcitauit reyſed lazar frome dethe lyue leye foure dayes deed lazar broder vnto marye mawdeleyne martha ſyſter thenne iheſu cryſte wyſte paſſyon nyghe toke lazar hym rydynge aſſe came towarde iheruſalem whan people herde therof people wente agaynſt hȳ non propter iheſū tātum ſed vt lazarum viderent quem reſuſcitauit mortuis onely iheſu ſee lazar ryſen frome dethe lyfe alſo ſee cryſt hym worſhyppe acceperunt ramos palma rum et ſter nebāt via toke braūches palme floures ſtrawed waye agaynſt comynge ſome ſpradde theyr clothes waye ſonge benedictus qui venit nomine domini bleſſed cometh name oure lorde kynge iſraell wherfore holy chirche maketh daye ſolempne proceſſyon mynde proceſſyon made agaynſt cryſt alſo ioye myrthe ryſynge dethe lyfe ley al yere dedly ſynne truſt god ben reyſed vnto good lyuynge ouer aungelles heuen make grete ioye vpreyſynge oute ſynne thus take palme floures proceſſyon dyde go proceſſyon knelynge croſſe worſhyp mynde hym doone croſſe worſhyppynge welcomynge hym wt ſonge chyrche people dyde lorde ye cyte iheruſalem thenne iohan belet aſked queſtyon ſayth yt lorde greteſt worſhyp rydynge aſſe euer worlde worſhyp croſſe aſſe queſtyon anſwereth hymſelfe ſayth worſhyp worlde salomon ſayd al vanyte maketh man forgete god hym ſelfe grete trybulacōn dyſeaſe heuynes cauſeth man thynke vpon god crye hym ſocoure helpe knowe hym ſelfe therfore cryſten people ſholde put awaye worldly vanytees bryngeth moche people grete myſchefe many euerlaſtynge payne worſhyp croſſe cauſe redēpcyon ſaluacyon brynge v euerlaſtynge ioye blyſſe hope come thenne anone whan cryſt come cyte iheruſalem went temple droue byers ſellers founde ther ſayd domus mea domus orationis vocabi hous hous prayer ye make denne theues thus lorde gaue cryſten people enſample leue enge ſellynge holy daye eſpecyall chyrche called palme ſondaye bycauſe palme betokeneth vyctorye wherfore cryſten people ſholde bere palme proceſſyon tokenynge yt hadde foughten fende ennemye hath ye vyctory hym ſhryft mouthe ſatyſfaccyon dede mekely doone penaunce grete contrycyon herte theſe maner wyſe ouercame gooſtly ennemye fende helle❀ ¶we rede geſtes romayns ye maner guyſe ſomtyme yf ony londe rebell agaynſt themperoure anone themperoure wolde ſende ſome worthy knyght grete puyſſaunce londe putte theym doune make theym ſubgettes emperoure rome whan knyght hadde done ſoo ſholde ſette chayre arayed clothes golde beſte wyſe braunche palme honde tokenynge hadde vyctory grete worſhyppe broughte rome whan came ony worthy cyte thenne ſholde ſtande one hym bete hym mouth braunche olyue ſayenge thus knowe thy ſelfe vnderſtonde though thou grete haue vyctory make moche thy ſelfe may fortune tyme thou mayſt haue worſe torne moche vylonye worſhyppe therfore proude thy ſelfe thus ſholde ye bete youre ſelfe mouthe youre ſoule braunche olyue vertue mekenes ſoo holde loue meke herte euermore dredynge ferynge leſte ye falle agayne ſynne ſoo leue worſhyppe ye haue truſt thus truly mekenes vertue mooſt ſooneſt ouercometh youre ghooſtly enemye fende ſooneſt gadreth man vertuous lyuynge may haue vertue mekeneſſe pacyence charyte ouercome oure ghoſtly enemye fende euer amen ¶feria iiii poſt feſtum palma rum dere frendes ye ſhall vnderſtonde holy chirche vſed theſe thre dayes ſaythe ſeruyce euen tyde mekeneſſe wherfore calle tenebre holy chyrche calleth tenebris thenne ſeruyce thus done mekeneſſe holy faders tellen thre cauſes ¶one nyght lorde taken went vnto ye mounte olyuete prayed thus pater mi ſi poſſible eſt tranſeat calix iſte fader yf poſſyble bytter paſſyon may paſſe fro yf faders wyl ellys drede fere bytter paſſyō felte ſpyryte ſwette bothe blood watyr ¶and cauſe anone mydnyghte came iudas fyfty knyghtes moche people take cryſt derke coude well knowe ſaynt iames ſo lyke cryſt therfore iudas ſayd quem oſculatus fuero tenete eum ſothe quod hym ſhal kyſſe take ye hym ſaynte iames ſoo lyke ſauyoure iheſu cryſt mooſt parte people called hym cryſtys owne broder thus ye haue herde iudas betrayed owne mayſter thus ſauyour iheſu cryſt take mekeneſſe wich ſpyte enmyte iewes coude doo vntoo hym alſoo betynge oure ſauyour iheſu cryſte alſoo ſpyttynge blyſſed face ¶and alſoo thyrde cauſe whan oure ſauyoure iheſu cryſte ſpredde naked vpon holy croſſe alſo whan holy hondes foot hanged nyne clocke vntoo none thenne ye ſholde haue ſeen ſonne drawe lyghte ſoo obſcure derke throughe worlde ſhewynge vnderſtondynge maker lyght ſame tyme payned vnto dethe thre certayne cauſes ſeruyce nyght done derkenes whiche ſeruyce maketh mencyon iudas betrayed oure ſauyoure lorde iheſu cryſte iewes thenne iewes came preuely coude fere drede comyn people wherfore daye belle ronge vnto ſeruyce ſowne made woode tree wherby cryſten people may haue knowlege vnderſtondynge come vnto holy ſeruyce preuely ſecretely without makynge ony maner noyſe ouer people ſholde ſpeke comynge goynge ſholde ſowne tree ſaye holy croſſe oure ſauyoure iheſu cryſte ſpredde vpon bytter paſſyō alſo wordes ſauyoure iheſu cryſte ſpake hangynge croſſe alſo ſayd vnto blyſſed moder mulier ecce filius tuus woman ſe thy ſone thenne oure lorde commaunded blyſſed moder vnto ſaynte iohan euangelyſte kepynge ſayd theef henge hym ſayd thus domyne quādo veneris regnū tuum memento mei lorde whan thou comeſt thy kyngedome haue mynde thenne oure ſauyour iheſu cryſt ſayd vnto hym hodie mecum eris paradiſo daye thou ſhalte paradyſe toke ſpyryte faders hondes ſayd manus tuas domine c ſoo yelded vp ghooſte thus comynge goynge chirche cryſten people ſholde come leue vanyte ydle talkynge ſpeke oonely vnto croſſe oure redempcyon cauſe whan yt iudas betrayed cryſt ſaw treaſon ſholde deed anone felle dyſpayre henge hȳ ſelfe tre dyſpleaſed cryſt dede treſpace done fore cryſt ſo mercyfull aſked mercy ſholde haue mercy alſo ſeruyce ſette certayne candels quere ye vſe ſome place ſome vſe whiche ben quenched one tokenynge cryſtys dyſcyples wente waye eche whan al theſe candels ben taken way lyght gone yet one bydeth ſtyll whyle tyll ye clerkes haue ſonge kyryes theſe verſes whiche betoken wymmen made lamentacyon cryſtys ſepulcre thenne candell brought agayne another lyght betokeneth bleſſyd lady fayth loſt ſaue oonely lady al enformed taught alſo betokeneth cryſt hym ſelfe manhode deed layde ye ſepulcre thyrde daye roſe frome dethe lyfe gayne gaue lyght loue al deed quenched dyſpayre ſtrokes preeſt gyueth boke betokeneth clappes thonder whan cryſte brake hell yates dyſpoyled theym fet oute adam eue yt bought bytter paſſyon haue ye herde ſomwhat ſeruyce betokeneth thynke vpon vnkynde lorde god ſuffred ¶for vnkyndneſſe ſynne ſtynketh ſyght god ſaynt ambroſe ſayth may noo man fynde payne grete ynoughe punyſſhe vnkyndneſſe ye ſhall enſample ¶narracio ¶i fynde alyſaunder neham telleth ſomtyme knyght whiche went owne countre ferre ſtraunge londe ſeke aduentures happened came grete foreſt herde grete noyſe beſt ſemed dyſpayre wolde wete mente wente nere ſawe grete horyble adder grete length beclypped lyon bounde hym tree laye ſlepte whā lyon woke founde hymſelfe boūde myght helpe hȳ ſelfe made horryble noyſe deſyrynge helpe knyght wolde fayne haue holpen hym drade whan louſe leſt wolde haue fallen hym bycauſe knyght lyon kynge beeſtes dyſtreſſe toke ſwerde dyde ſmyte adder aſonder ye lyon fel ye knyghtes fete alway folowed knyght euery nyght lyon laye beddes foot euery batayle lyon redy helpe mayſter ſo moche people ſpake vntoo knyght lyon yet counſell people lyon inſuſpecte wherfore whan wente intoo owne countre gayne pryuely whyles lyon ſlepte toke ye water went ſhyppe ſayled forth whan lyon awoke myſſed mayſter anone gaue grete rorynge wente hym ſee ſwā hym longe myght whan myght fayled hym thenne drowned knyghte ye may vnderſtonde goddes ſone heuen come oute ferre countree oute heuen worlde boūde mankynde olde adder fende tree inobedyence wherfore ſharpe ſwerde paſſyon loſed mankynde oute boū de made hym free goo wolde therfore cryſten people ben bounde worſhyppe hym thanke hym loſynge buxom hym tyme haue lyfe folowe ſewe lore holy chyrche ſhall paſſe thrughe ye water ſaye thrugh payne dethe ſo ſhall come ioye euer ſhall laſt withoute ende whiche god brynge v amen ¶dyuerſe queſtyons many wyll aſke dyuerſe queſtyons ſeruyce theſe dayes ſuche preeſtes ſuppoſe make redy anſwere putte hȳ ſhame hym vylonye repreef wherfore haue tyteled whiche nedeful euery preeſt knowe yf wyl loke kepe thē redely herte may make redy ſo ſhall hȳ profyte worſhyp fyrſt yf man aſke ſherethurſday called ſo ye may ſaye holy chyrche called cena domini lordes ſouper day day ſouped diſcyples openly ſouper gaue fleſſhe blood ete drynke ſayd thus accipite et manducate hoc eſt corpus meū take ye ete myne owne body anone wyſſhe owne dyſcyples foot ſhewynge mekenes hym ye grete loue theym alſo englyſſhe called ſherthourſday olde faders dayes people wolde daye ſhere theyr hedes clyppe theyr berdes polle theyr hedes ſo make theym honeſt yenſt eſter day good fryday doo theyr bodyes none eaſe ſuffre penaunce mynde hym day ſuffred paſſyon man kynde eſter euen tyme theyr ſeruyce ſeruyce make holy daye wryten lyfe ſaynte ſo beſy ſaterday none made man ſhaue hym none fende redy gadred vp here holy mā ſaw commaunded hym tell dyde ſoo ſayd thou dooſt reuerence vnto thy holy daye therfore wyll kepe theſe here tyll day dome grete repreef anone lefte ſhauynge toke theſe here frome fende made theym brenne owne honde ſuffre penaunce ſo bode vnſhauen tyll monday ſayde al thoo repreef worſhyp ſaterday none thenne iohan bellet ſayth ſherthurſday man ſholde polle clyppe berde preeſt ſholde ſhaue crowne ſoo ſholde nothynge twene god hym here come veynes humour ſtomake ſholde pare theyr nayles hondes foot cometh ſuperfluyte fylthe oute forth thenne ſhryue theym make clene within ſoule thus make theym clene bothe veyle lente hath drawen twene v quere betokeneth paſſyon hydde vnknowen tyll day came whiche thyſe dayes done waye awter openly ſhewed people theſe dayes cryſte ſuffred paſſyon openly hangynge croſſe ſayenge conſūmatum eſt ended ſaye propheſye paſſyon hath ende wherfore clothes myne awter ben taken waye cryſtys clothes take waye hym ſoo done naked croſſe ſaue oure lady moder wounde karchyf aboute hym couer membres auter ſtone betokeneth cryſtys body drawen croſſe ſkȳ ne parchement harowe ſo al bone myght tolde beſoms awter weſſhen betokeneth ſcorges bete lordes body thornes crowned water wyne waſſhen betokeneth blode water yt ranne downe woundes ſyde peryſhed ſpere wyne pored vpon awter fyue croſſes betokeneth blode rā ne downe frome precypall woundes body alſo day paxe gyuen ye maſſe iudas betrayed cryſt nyght kyſſe thus propheſye paſſyon daye ended wherfore nyghte whan ſouped made ſacramente owne body gaue dyſcyples ete drynke began ſacramente maſſe newe lawe ſouper wyſſhe diſcyples foot maner newe lawe full ſayd peter waſſhen clene dedly ſynne hath nede waſſhen betokeneth afflyccyon dedly ſynne thenne yf people aſke preeſtes maſſe ſouper cryſt dyde tourned honeſt ſaluacyon mannes ſoule haymo telleth vpon ye pyſtle ſaynt poule many begynnynge fayth come chirche ſherethurdaye thoſe ryche brought mete drynke theym eten dranke theyr bellyes full thenne atte nyght tooke theyr houſell ſayd cryſte gaue enſample whan ryche ete dranke moche poore people abydeth withoute tylle ryche hath done ſore hū gred thenne ete releef lefte ſoo people toke theyr houſell pyſtle daye telleth ſaynt poule rebuked theym therof tourned foule vſe honeſt clenneſſe holyneſſe ſaye atte maſſe faſtynge people take theyr houſell faſtynge eeſter euen paſcall made chyef tapre chirche ſoo cryſte chyef aboue ye ſayntes heuen paſcall alſo betokeneth pyler lyght fyre wente moyſes chyldern iſraell whan moyſes ladde theym egypte londe byheſt iheruſalem ſoo paſſed ſaue ſounde ſoo ſeuen dayes come vnto ſee thanked god theyr paſſage mynde holy chirche vſeth eeſter weke goo proceſſyon fonte reed ſee cryſten people ben cryſtened fonte water fonte betokeneth reed ſee bloode water wounde cryſtes ſyde whiche power pharao fende helle drowned myght loſte cryſten people ſaued fonte halowed eeſter euen wytſon euen begynnynge chyldern abode cryſtened vnto theſe two dayes cryſtened atte fonte halowynge cauſe many ſo longe abydȳge deed withouten cryſtendome therfore holy chyrche ordeyned cryſten tymes yere ſaue eyght dayes fore theſe euyns chylde ſhall byde fonte halowynge yf may peryl deth ellys thus paſcall halowed lyght newe fyre tapres candelles ben lyght al holynes good techynge good lyuynge cometh cryſt techynge holy chyrche lyghteth cryſtes paſſyon brennyng loue charyte pyeces conſcyence ben ſtycked paſcall maner croſſe thoſe token fyue woundes lorde bede ſayeth ſuffred body ſhall freſſhe ſwete ony enſcence tyl day dome grete repreef ſhall dampned byleue cryſtes paſſyō wyl aſke mercy yeuenes theyr ſynnes fonte halowynge preeſte caſteth water foure partyes fonte cryſte dyſcyples goynge prechynge techynge foure partyes cryſtendome name fader ſone holy ghooſt preeſt bretheth water holy ghoſt makyng worlde borne water whan god adam ſynne curſyd erthe londe curſed water wherfore lawfull man ete lenten ye cometh water droppeth wexe water candell brennyng whiche betokeneth mā hode cryſt fulled water putteth oyle creme water ye vertue ſacramente thoſe ben heuen erthe ioyned gyder preued cryſtes baptyſme fader heuen ſpake ſayd hic eſt filius meus dilectꝰ quo mi • hi bene cōplacui welbeloued ſone wyll pleaſe holy ghooſt sicut columba whyte douue ¶thus • onte halowed two tymes ye yere whytſontyde eſter whan people broughte thraldum cryſtes paſſyon fro ye daunger fende atte wytſontyde holy ghooſt gyuen remyſſyon ſynnes thenne frome fonte people gone quere ſyngynge letanye prayenge ſayntes heuen praye god gyue yt ben cryſten kepe worthy ſacrament goddes pleaſaunce couenaūt haue made theyr cryſtenynge thenne preeſt gooth maſſe cryſte heed holy chirche ryſen kyryeleyſon ſayd euery prayer eſpecyall maſſe grete nede aſke helpe ſocour god kepe v frome maner temptacyon fende putteth v namely goddes ſeruyce gloria excelſis ſayd fader heuen hath grete ioye beholde people ſone hath bought paſſyon ſee pea reſte charyte eche one greyle ſayd thoſe ben newe cryſtened ben yet parfyte walke grace vertues alleuya ſayd grete ioye aungels ſee cryſtenynge nombre reſtored ayen alleluya tract ſayd hyghe ſongen thoughe cryſtenynge waſſhed frome ſynne yet muſt traueyll beſely kepe frome comberaunce fende falle deedly ſynne offertory ſayd woman comen oynementes offre cryſtes body founde hȳ tombe agnꝰ dei ſayd paxe gyuen cryſt heed pea ryſen poſtcomyn ſaid thoſe ben newe cryſtened ſholde houſeled day morowe olde tyme came cryſtenynge people grete age thenne ſhorte euenſonge done chyldern cryſtened wherof gretely noyed ſykenes colde longe ſeruyce thenne endeth vnder ſhorte colet ye ſacramente cryſtenynge ended paſſyon cryſte whiche cryſten people reſtored euerlaſtynge blyſſe ye whiche god brynge v amen ¶in die paraſceues good frendes daye called good frydaye al lorde iheſu cryſt ſuffred daye tourned v grete ioye daye ſuffred paſſyon vnder ponce pylate ſake olde ſawe foule begynnynge hathe foule endynge ſe pylate began curſedly endeth full wretchedly ſaynt auſtyn ſayeth curſed lyuynge fyrſt aſketh curſed ende forgeteth hym ſelfe lyuynge full lyke forgete hymſelf laſt ende pylate knyghtes ſone called tyrus gate hym womā hyght pyle woman fader hyght ate whan chylde borne ſette moders name grande fader ſo bothe name called hym pylate thenne whan thre yere aege moder broughte hym kynges courte knyght ſone nye lyke pylates aege knyghtes ſone rule gentyller manfully goodly beloued pylate ſo hate enuye therof pylate daye ſlewe knyghtes ſone knight wonder ſory yet wolde ſle pylate ſent hym rome hoſtage trybute yt knyght ſholde paye themperour happed yt kynge fraunce ſent ſone thyder ye ſame cauſe thē cauſe whan pylate ſawe beloued cheryſſhed therfore pilate ſlewe hȳ ſo curſed emperour counceyle ye romaynes ſent pylate countre called pō ce people coūtre ſo curſed yt ſlewe ony yt came theyr mayſter ouer whan pylate came thyder applyed hym theyr maners ſo yt wyles ſubtylte ouercame mayſtry gate name called pylate ponce grete domynacyon power kynge iheruſalem ſent made hym lyuetenaunt vnder hȳ londe iury pylate lyked well thoffyce pryuely ſent themperour offyce confermed hym vnwetynge kynge herode tyme beynge kȳ ge wherfore whan kynge herode herde done ſo wrothe enmyes vnto tyme yt lorde iheſu cryſt take became frendes agayne fell bothe one aſſent cryſtes dethe thenne happened afterwarde ye themperour fel ſeke ſent cryſte hele hym tolde hym cryſt heled euer wolde come hym al maner ſekenes ſo euer pylate done hym dethe meſſenger came whan emperour vnderſtode ſente pylate made hym come hym pylate herde ſore aferde toke cryſtes cote ſo whan came rome emperour preſence made pylate good chere whyle cryſtes cote emperoure ſwore ſholde deed thenne toke cote anone cote emperoure ſore wrothe pylate put hym pryſon tyll hadde taken counceyl dethe ſholde deye thenne ſoone pylate wyſt vnderſtode ſholde deed toke owne knyfe ſlewe hym ſelfe therwith whan emperour herde therof dyde vnderſtande hadde ſlayne hym ſelf knyfe thenne anone commaunded bynde grete ſtone forſayd pylates necke caſte hym ryuer rome named tyber without euer ſene people· thenne whan caſten therin fendes made ſuche noyſe aboute cyte rome ſore afreyed thenne whan emperoure ſawe made take hym vp ayen thenne caſte water bytwix two hye hylles ſo longe tyme water many horryble ſyghtes ſeen aboute curſed man ¶thus oure lorde iheſu cryſte ſuffred paſſyon dethe mankynde fyrſte whan taken dyde buffet hym ſtryped hym naked bete hym ſcourges vertice capitis vſ que ad plantas pedum non fuit eo ſanitas frome hyeſt place heed ſoole foot thynge lefte hole hym rawe made crowne thornes ſette heed bete doune ſtaues reed peryſſhed brayne whan payned hym ſo ladde hym forth blody admontē caluarie mount caluarye thende dethe yet woman cyte whā ſee hym ſo foule faren lugged drawen veray pyte wepte vpon hym thenne ſayd lorde nolite flere ſuper ſed ſuper vos filios veſtros ye woman iheruſalem wepe ye vpon youre chyldern ſhall dayes come whiche ye ſhall blyſſe wombes barayne pappes neuer gaue ſouke thus oure lorde preched vengeaunce fylle vpon iheruſalem whiche prophecye iheremye prophete ſpake redde holy chirche theſe thre dayes atte tenebras whiche ſo horryble many dyuerſe myſchyues eſpecyall hungre chyldern laye deed hungre ſtretes thenne waman come grete byrthe hungre tooke owne chylde deed pappes ſlewe parted two partyes ſhe roſted halfe halfe ſhe kepte tylle morowe thenne people came ſtrete hadde ſauoure roſt anone came haue hadde parte therof whan ſawe moder roſte owne chylde ſoone heuy foule dyſmayed wolde ete therof wente theyr waye forth ayen thenne tooke moder chylde ete therof ſayd maner wyſe myn owne ſone myn owne chylde bare body fedde pappes wyll rather ete deye hungre therfore telle ſhewe ſomwhat vengeaunce fylle iheruſalem dethe oure lorde iheſu cryſt thenne ladde hym ye moūt caluarye ſtreyned hym ſoo croſſe euery bone body myght knowen one nayled hym honde foote croſſe lyfte vp croſſe boody togyder grete peyce lete croſſe body falle doune togyder morteſſe body daſſhed bone craked ioyntes vaynes braſte oute blode ſydes armes legges foot hondes ſo blode lefte hym yet toke clothe whyle blode hote wonde aboute body tylle blode colde thenne drewe awaye clothe pulled awaye fleſſhe fro bone grete pyte ſoo whan ſholde deye began iohan belet ſayth deus meus reſpice ſoo ſayd verſes ſuynge tylle come vnto verſe te dn̄e ſperaui ſoo atte verſe manus tuas dn̄e commendo ſpiritum meum redemiſti domine deus veritatis gaue vp ſpyryte grete enſample oure lorde iheſu cryſte gaue cryſten people euery man ſholde haue mynde theſe verſes theym ſaye ſaye theym euery daye ſhall deye maner myſchyuous vengeable deth paſſyon ſaye oryſones knelynge euery oryſon ſaue oryſon ſayd iewes ye oryſon holy chyrche kneled cauſe iewes ſcorne knelynge thre tymes cryſt whan ſcrourged hym thenne thyſe oryſons holy chirche prayed maner people iewes saraſyns cyſmatyks heretyks cryſten people whyle ony man woman ſtandeth acurſyd dampned god dampned ſhall deth repente hȳ made hȳ whyle lyueth preſente worlde take hede ſaynt auſtyn ſayth siſcirem ꝓ certo ꝙ pater meus eſſet inferno non orarem pro illo niſi vt ꝓ dyabolo yf wyſt trouth fader dampned helle wolde neuer praye hym deuyll helle ther prayer holy chirche helped dampned man thenne thyſe oryſons croſſe brought forth whiche cryſten people ſholde worſhyp hym daye deyed croſſe praye lorde forgiue v treſpace cryſt prayed fader heuen forgyue theȳ dyde hym croſſe ¶narracio ¶there knyght ſomtyme grete lorde hadde worthy man vnto ſone ſo happed knyght man felle debate ſo knyghte ſlewe hym wherfore fader man deed gadred grete multytude people dyſtroye vtterly vndo hym purſued knyghte place ſome euerhe wente haue ſlayne hym nyght daye ſo myght haue reſt euer dyde flee fere lyf thenne happed good frydaye knyght ſawe cryſten people go chirche bethought hym cryſte deyed daye croſſe mankynde put hym onely mercy almyghty god wente chirche people ſerue god chirche anone knyght worde come moche people chirche ſwerde drawen honde ſlee hym whan knyght ſawe wyſt well treſpaced hym fylle downe flatte grounde armes ſpradde abrode lorde iheſu cryſte ſpradde armes croſſe ſayd loue daye ſpradde hi armes ye croſſe ſuffredde paſſyon deyed al mankynde haue thou mercy forgyue thy ſones deth thenne knyght thought horryble thynge ſmyte hym whyle laye ſo cryed hym mercy ſo mekely anone put vp ſwerde ſayd hym maner wyſe loue day deyed croſſe mankynde fyrgyue toke forſayd man vp kyſſed hym anone went doo worſhyp croſſe knelynge whan knyght wolde haue kyſſed ye foot croſſe ymage louſed armes fro croſſe beclypped knyght necke kyſſed hym ſpake thus people herde forgyue thou haſt forgyuen loue thus cryſtē people ſholde thenne ſholde haue mercy grace god euerlaſtynge blyſſe amen ¶in die paſce good frendes ye ſhall knowe wel daye called many place goddes ſōday ye knowe wel ye maner euery place worſhyp daye fyre halle ye blacke wynter brondes thynge foule fume ſmoke ſhall done awaye fyre ſhall gayly arayed fayre floures ſtrewed grene ryſſhes aboute ſhewynge grete enſample cryſten people lyke made clene theyr houſes vnto rhe ſyght people ſame wyſe ye ſholde clenſe ſoulys doyng way foule brennȳ ge ſynne lecherye put theſe waye caſt thy foule duſt ſtrewe ſoulys floures fayth thus make ſoulys able receyue lorde god feeſt eſter deponentes omnen maliciam put waye malyce ſorowe ryght ye wyll ſuffre nothynge houſe ſtynketh ſauoureth euyll wher ye may deceyued ryght ſo cryſt whan cometh hous ſoules finde ony ſtynke wrath enuy ony dedly ſynne wyll abyde none goth waye thenne cometh fende abydeth thenne may ſoule ſo forſaken god betaken vnto fende thus thoſe wrath enuy ony dedely ſynne wyll forgyue hathe treſpaced vnto prayer ſhall forgyuenes haue oure lorde ſayeth thus dimittite et dimitte mini forgyue ye ſhal haue forgyuenes therfore euery cryſten man woman ſholde ſerche well theyr cō ſcyence make able receyue theyr ſauiour iheſu cryſt god man ¶narracio ¶there ſome tyme holy byſſhop prayed often tymes beſely vnto god myghte haue grace ſee knowe whiche worthy receyue holy ſacrament come goddes borde thenne tyme houſeled ye people ſaw ſome come theyr face reed blood dropped theyr mouthes ſome theyr face blacke ony pytche ſome fayre reed luſty holde ſome whyte ony ſnowe thenne amonge ſawe two comyn woman come theyr face ſhone bryght ſonne byſſhop grete meruayle ſyght prayed god gyue hym reuelacyon betokeneth thenne came hym aungell ſayd thoſe haue blody face blode droppeth theyr mouthes ben enuyous people wrathfull wyll amende theym ſelfe therof euer backebytynge ſclaundrynge theyr neyghbours ben euer redy ſwere othes therfore theyr mouthes ſhall droppe blacke blode tyll come amendement thoſe haue blacke face pytch lecherous wyll leue theyr ſynne ben grete ſynners many degree wyl amende haue theyr face whyte ony ſnowe thoſe yt haue done grete ſynne ben ſhryuen therof ſory theyr ſynnes wepynge theyr eyen hath waſſhed theyr ſoules made clene ſo ben clene lyfe truely laboure theyr lyuynge thoſe two comyn woman ſhyne ſo bryght paſſynge grete ſynners ſore aferde whan came chyrche toke grete repentaunce theyr hertes yt made vowe god praynge hym hartely take noo vengeaunce wolde forſake theyr ſynne neuer amyſſe wherfore god grete grace mercy hath forgyuen theyr treſpace theyr ſynnes ſorowe theyr hertes hath ſo waſſhen theyr ſoules yt ſhyne bryghter aungell went waye byſſhop kneled doune thā ked god reuelacyon therfore take example theſe two comyn woman ſory ſynnes repent hertes purpoſe neuer torne ayen ſynne truſt verely ye ſhall haue grace ſocoure endles blyſſe wherfore thȳke certayne though ye make gloſȳge wordes dyſceyue gooſtly fader ſaye ye charyte ye begyle ſelfe truſte truly ye ſhall begyle god ſeeth euery corner herte therfore deceyue owne ſoules ye loue god alſo beſy redy meke ſoules clene ſyght god ye ben make houſes ſyght men ye wolde aray beſt clothes ye haue agaynſt comȳge beſt frendes ſo ſholde ye araye receyue beſt frende maker lorde iheſu cryſte tyme ſuffred paſſyon dethe brynge v euerlaſtynge lyfe daye called paſſynge daye eſpecyall two cauſes one daye cryſten people reuerence god ſholde forgyue theym haue treſpaced perfyte loue charyte cryſten people haue myſſe done yere daye ſholde amended ſalue heleth ſores yt charyte caritas cooperit multitudinem peccato rum charyte couereth multitude ſynnes alſo paſſynge daye daye ſholde goddes chyldren paſſe euyll lyuynge good lyuynge vyces vertues pryde mekenes couetyſe largenes ſlouthe holynes enuye loue charyte wrathe mercy glotony abſtynence oute lechery chaſtyte fendes clawes oure mortall ennemye goddes armes grete ennemy make dere frende paſſeth thus worthy come good feeſt whiche lorde iheſu cryſt maketh daye people called alſo goddes ſonday daye goddes ſone roſe frome dethe lyfe ſoo gladded ſeruauntes vpryſynge wherfore holy chyrche maketh myrth melody daye ſyngeth thus ¶hec eſt dy quam fecit dominus exultemus le temur ea daye lorde made ioy glad wt hertes fader heuē aungelles maketh ſo grete melodye vpryſynge ſone maketh daye paſſynge grete feeſt byddeth cryſten people therto well yt ben heuen ben erthe ſhall full welcome cometh feeſt clothed goddes lyuery good clothyng loue charyte alſo euyll ſhall welcome yt ſhal come fendes leuery clothed wrathe enuy goſpell telleth ſhall caſte pryſon hell whyle laugheth make mery ſhall wepe ſory whyle ſome ete drynke goddes borde ſhal gnaſſhe wt theyr tethe ſaye quante ſunt tenebre wo wo wo many derkenes ben ſhall thynke may fele derkenes ſo derke paynes hell ſhall ſo harde wormes ſhall gnawe theym ete theyr euen cryſten erthe falſe backebytynge ſclaundrynge wherfore charge goddes name yt none come thus goddes borde yf ye perfyte loue charyte clene ſhryuen full purpoſe leue ſynne wyſte certayne whiche charyte deedly ſynne muſte lawe holy chyrche loude voyce ſay thus hym audyence people gyue thy houſell thy ſaluacyon thy dampnacyon tyll yu come amendement therfore euery cryſten man woman ſholde ſerche well conſcyence make hym able receyue ſauyour iheſu cryſt helth ſoule maye come fynall lyfe euerlaſtynge ioye amen ¶rogationum ¶feria iiiiiiiii ante aſcencionem dn̄i frēdes thyſe thre dayes ſaye mōdaye tuyſdaye weneſdaye ye ſhall faſt go proceſſyon man woman ſeruaunte ſȳners haue nede praye god helpe grace mercy may excuſe fro proceſſyon may lawfully thenne yt wtdrawe hȳ ſelf fro ye cōmaundemēt holy chirche wylfully ſynneth full greuouſly fyrſt ſynned pryde vnbuxon alſo ſynned ſlouthe knoweth hym ſelf ſynne wyll dylygence come therof ryght withdraweth hym people ben gadred ſerue god ryght ſo wyll god put hym company heuen prayer yt ben done holy chirche tyll come amendemēt therfore cryſten people come oonly gyder praye thyſe thre dayes ſayntes heuen praye god v haue ſȳned many tymes yere ayenſt commaundement god therfore thyſe thre dayes ſhall faſt praye god mercy remyſſyon ſynnes put awaye power fende kepe v myſchyef perylles drede fallen tyme yere ony tyme tyme fall many grete thondres lyght wynges lyncolnyence ſayth fendes fleteren thayer fere ye blaſt thondrynge whan cryſt come helle yates whan dyſpoylled helle ſo yet whan thonder thayer ben ſoo agaſt therof fallen downe thenne go vp ayen tyll haue done rered ſome curſyd dedes make tempeſtes ſee drawe downe ſhyppes make debate amonge people make one ſlee tende fyre brenne houſes drawe downe ſteeples tree cauſe wȳmē ouerlaye theyr chyldern make peple hāge themſelf drowne ſelfe wanhope dyſpayre doo many curſed dedes put awaye ſuche myſcheues power fende holy chyrche hath ordeyned al cryſten people ſhall faſte go proceſſyon theſe thre dayes pray god lady ſayntes heuen helpe ſocoure wherfore theſe proceſſyons belle rongen baners dyſplayed croſſe cometh people ſueth ryght kȳge whan gooth batayle trompettes gooth tofore baners cometh kynge hooſt folowynge proceſſyon belle goddes trompettes baners cometh cometh croſſe cryſtes lykenes kynge cryſten people ſue hym theyr good prayer chaſe awaye fendes haue power lyke curſed tyraunt wyll ſore aferde adred whan hereth trompettes kynge ennemye ſeeth baners ſpleyed felde hooſt comȳ ge towarde hym ſame wyſe ye fende tyraunte hell aferde dredeth hym ſore whan belle rynge baners ben borne croſſe people come prayenge fleeth dare abyde putteth awaye power proceſſyon ¶narracio ¶we rede ye cyte conſtantyne people went proceſſyon dyſeaſe yt people ſonge latyny ſodaynly lytell chylde plucked vp ayre borne heuen angelles taught hȳ ſynge ſō ge setē deꝰ ſctē fortis ſctē et īmortalis miſerere nobis anone laten doune agayn ye erthe ſonge ye ſame ſonge anone delyuerd theyr dyſeaſes ſay englyſſhe holy god holy ſtronge god holy wtout dethe haue mercy v god yt holy neuer ſhall dye haue mercy v god wylleth wyl ſtronge fyght fende ye worlde ye fleſſhe thenne wyll haue mercy v brynge v place thenne angelles ſynge sancte deꝰ ſancte fortis holy god holy ſtrōge god haue mercy v bryng v blyſſe amen ¶in die aſcenſionis dn̄i good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhal haue hye ſolempne feſt holy chirche called aſcenſyon lorde iheſu cryſt daye fayth byleue techeth god god man ſtyed vp heuen wherfore tokenyng paſcall chyef lyght holy chirche hath ſtande openly quere eſter vnto daye remeued awaye tokenynge cryſte chyef lyght holy chirche ſo lorde dyuerſe tymes openly appyered dyſcyples taught theym fayth byleue daye ſtyed vp heuen wyll abyde vntyll daye dome ye ſhall maner ye aſcenſyon eſter daye tyll daye dyſcyples alwaye dyuerſe tymes appyered vnto appyred ſaten theyr mete ete wt ſhewe yt god man fleſſhe blood ſome doubte leſt ſpyryte yt nother fleſſhe ne blood therfore preue trouth ete wt theyr ſyght badde go ye hylle olyuete ſyght dyſcyples bleſſyd ſtyed vp heuen left ye ſteppes foot threſt downe ye harde marbyll ſtone token aſcenſyon thenne ye ſhall vnderſtande ye hylle olyuete betokeneth mercy wherfor cryſte ſtyed vp hylle olyuete ſhewynge wel heed mercy euer redy gyue mercy aſke mercy meke herte thenne vpſtyeng calle aſcēſyon angelles made ſo moche melody yt tonge may telle ſo glade comynge aſcendit velociter ſtyed vp ſwyftly momēt ſo erthe heuen grete clerke phyloſopher yt called rabby moyſes ſayth ferre heuen erthe holy man myght lyue thouſande yere euery daye go thouſande myle yt met waye knoweth beſt waye ſhall met ryghtfull good man ¶thenne aſcenſyon hadde hym grete multytude ſoules whiche fette helle fendes boundes ſtyed vp alſo wt woundes reed freſſhe blody bede ſayth fyue cauſes fyrſt verifye ye fayth reſurrecōn roſe fleſſhe blood deyed croſſe mankynde ſeconde ſhewe woundes fader grete helpe ſocour al mankynde thyrde ſhewe ryghtful dampned yt wyll byleue paſſyon reſurreccyon iiii ſhewe mercyfull vnto wyll byleue aſke mercy fyfth bare hym ſygne vyctorye ſykerneſſe mankynde lyke lorde ſyker hath true aduocate iuge anſwere hȳ ſo lyke wyſe mankynde fynde hym aduocat euermore redy anſwere v nede ye fende ghoſtly enemye maketh ayenſt v wherfore ſayth holy ſcrypture aſykerer attorneye may noo man god vbi mater oſtendit filio pectus et vbera wherfore moder ſheweth ſone breſtes pappes filius patri latus et vulnera ſone ſheweth fader ſydes beten woūdes bledynge ſholde ony thȳ ge put away ordeyned ther ſuche token loue ſhewed may fare yll yt hath ſuche ii frēdes heuē alſo ſtyenge vp heuen lorde iheſu cryſt man hath goten grete dygnyte man ſe owne fleſhe blood ſyttynge ryght ſyde fader heuen trone wherfore aungels conſyderynge ye dygnyte man wolde ſuffre man worſhyp dyde thyncarnacyon cryſt worſhyp man god hymſelfe hath take mankynde hȳ heuen bodely man may ſee moche beholde god boūde thral fende helle nowe made frere lorde iheſu cryſt hath gyuen man fredom aboue ony angel therfore bounde vnto hym hym ſeruyce reuerence worſhyp angelles kept ſomtyme ye yates paradyſe brennynge ſwerdes ſoule myght come inne fayth lorde iheſu cryſt mankynde hath caſt vp ye yates warneth man entre therin ſtedfaſt byleue ſaynt auſtyn ſayth aperuiſti credentibus regna celo rum thou haſt opened yates heuen byleue alſo ye ſhall byleue ryght kyng worlde hath countree offycers dyuerſe degree ſome hyer ſome lower ſome preuyer ſome lorde ſtyenge vp tyme lower angel grete wonder cryſtys aſcenſyon whan ſawe hym fleſſhe blood ſtyenge vp heuen ſo grete multytude ſoules hym alſo grete wondre whan ſawe fendes ayer flee awaye drede fere ſtronge comȳge wonte ſparynge nothȳge aſſayle ye ſoules yt come theȳ thēne flewe awaye grete fere comȳge alſo good angel came ye haſt yt myght doo lorde iheſu cryſte ſeruyce reuerence worſhyp thus grete wonder yt lower angel vp ſtyenge aſketh hyer angel ſayd quis eſt iſte qui venit de eodem cometh worlde blody clothes kyng ioye deth ſuffrȳ ge reed ſcourgynge ſyke deed croſſe ſtronge helle bodely doynge ferfull ryſynge thus hath ouercome ennemys kyng glorye heuen ¶thenne whan lorde iheſu cryſt ſtyed vp heuen thēne dyſcyples ſtandynge moder grete wonder ſyght alſo melodye herde thayer loked vp heuen ſodaynely two angel clothed whyte ſtode theym ſayd thus viri galilei quid ſtatis aſpicientes celū hic iheſus qui aſſumptus eſt vobis men galyle ſtande ye beholdynge heuē iheſus ſtyed vp ſo ſhall come daye dome ayen deme quycke deed therfore cryſten people lyfte vp hertes lorde iheſu cryſte ſtyed vp heuen ſytteth faders ryght honde redy gyue mercy theȳ wyll aſke mercy wt meke herte therfore maner man yt may excuſe hymſelf haue maner excuſacyon yf wyll hymſelf aſke mercy lorde god meke herte ſhall haue mercy ſhall ſaued though man neuer ſo ſynfull wyll aſke mercy meke herte wyl gyue hym mercy cor contritū et humiliatū deus non deſpicies meke contryte herte god ſhal neuer deſpyſe wyll aſke mercy ſory ſynnes lorde wyll take hym mercy thenne ſhewe grete goodneſſe cōpaſſyon yt lorde hath mankȳde ſhall telle enſāple ¶we rede lyfe ſaynt carpe ā man myſſe beleue torned cryſten man faythe narracio forſoke beleue cryſtendome wherfore holy man carpe ſore angred ſo fell grete ſykenes whan ſholde haue prayed god amendement dyde pray god nyght daye myght ſe haue bodely vengeaunce then̄e happed mydnyght prayed thus ſodaynly houſe lay cleued foure partes loked vp ſawe one hanged ſo pyteouſly pyte ſe loked vp heuen ſawe lorde iheſu cryſte grete multytude aungelles ſyttynge trone loked vp agayne ſawe theſe two men ſtandynge hote ouen quakynge tremblynge drede fendes lyke adder wormes comynge oute ouen drawe theſe men ouen ſoo many fendes came dyuers lykenes helpe ouen holy man carpe glad ſe theſe two men haue vengeaunce wonder fayne therof loſte ſyght lorde iheſu cryſt holy aungelles herte theſe two mennes vengeaunce ſorye ſoo longe put vnto theyr payne roſe went hym ſelfe helped euer myght whan ouen carpe gladde therof thenne loked vp heuen ſawe lorde iheſu cryſte ſawe hym ryſe frome trone grete pyte compaſſyon two men came downe toke theym theyr payne ſayd thus carpe extēde manus tuas contra stretche thyn handes ayenſt lorde ſayd thus redy nede ſuffre dethe paſſyon agayne redeme mankynde rather leſe thē ¶by enſample ye may ſe redy lorde iheſu cryſt wyll aſke forgyuenes deſerue mercy euery man amende leue ſynnes full wyll purpoſe ſynne thus ſhall come grace mercy lorde iheſu cryſte ſuffred v mankynde good frydaye paſſyon day ſtyed vp heuen whiche wyl graū te v brynge v therto amen ¶in vigilia penthecoſtes dere frendes ye knowe well ſaterday next comynge whytſon euen ye ſhal faſt come chyrche ſeruyce make clene receyue holy gooſt fader heuen ſendeth amonge mankynde wherfore counceyle charge yf ony fall ony ſynne come amende hym therof wyll redy belongeth take rertayne ſame wyſe man wyll go place ſtynkynge caryon yf ſtoppe noſe hye hym then ryght ſo holy gooſt fleeth frome ſoule combred deedly ſynne aungels wyll ſtoppe theyr noſes moche fouler ſtynketh deedly ſynne ſyght god dooth ony caryon people ye holy gooſt fleeth hym yt abydeth good lyfe clene perfyte loue charyte hath pyte compaſſyon thoſe ben dyſeaſe trybulacyon ſuche holy gooſt vyſyteth cometh ſuche hym lyſteth come abyde comforteth techeth theyr nede ſeruyce feeſt prayſed ony tyme feeſt holy chirche calleth ſayth veni ſancte ſpūs come holy gooſt ſpecyally haue ſocour grace haue parte ye dole yt maketh 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page ſoules vnto bere awaye many leuer tale robyn hode tale rybaudrye wherfore goddes worde ſhal preched ſuche ſome gyueth grace ſoo vnderſtandynge dyuers language englyſſhe frenſſhe walſhe iryſſhe without ony grete trauayle lernynge grete gyft myracle ſpecyall grace almyghty god ony man vnderſtande ony ſuche ſpekynge ¶there ben fyue lettres maketh ye wordes yt may prenounced language ben vnder heuen without one theſe lettres may maner man make ony worde theſe ben aeiou ¶and alſo ſome gyueth grace counceyle good counceyle ſome enſpyreth within ſheweth theym maketh knowe tofore wyll come falle gyueth grace deme better worſer wherfore ſo wyſely dyſcretely people ben gladde ſpeke doo counceyle ſome gyueth grace alſo counceyle lorde iheſu cryſte gaue hym ſelfe counceylynge man wyll lyue perfyte lyfe leue al hath goo relygyon gouerned wardeyns counceyle owne counceyle cometh myghty god ſome gyueth grace ſuffrynge moche bodely ſykeneſſe grete wronges moche dyſeaſe body ſoule loſſe catell lordſhyp mayſterſhyp frendſhyp yt ſuffreth meke herte thankynge almyghty god ſonde yt cometh ye grace ye holy ghoſt alſo gyueth ſome grace lernynge dyuerſe ſcyence ſome lerne one crafte ſome whiche may gete lyuynge trouth ſoo man wyll put dylygence truely labour ſlombre ſlepe ſlewfully vnthryftely due tyme labour beſely holy ghoſt hath gyuen euery man ſome knowynge gete lyuȳge wt trouthe gyueth grace pyte fylleth theyr hertes ſo full pyte cōpaſſyon euen cryſten ben dyſeaſe aduerſyte yt gyue hē goodes helpe ſocoure theȳ nede cōforte theȳ yt may cryſtis ſake alſo mercyable forgyue yt treſpaced ony wyſe ſome gyueth alſo drede god ſo moche yt ben euer aferde dyſpleaſe almyghty god euer thȳke grete vengeaūce god wyll take ſȳne ye daye dome timor dn̄i expellit peccatū drede god horryble paynes helle putteth awaye ſȳne thus nyght daye ſome euer aferde offende god euer beſy well preuyte ye opē ſyght people yt hath gyft hath ſpecyall grace ye holy ghoſt hec ſūt ſeptē dona ſpirituſſctī thyſe ſeuen gyftes ye holy ghooſt departed amonge man kynde gyueth ſome ſome may man excuſe hȳ ye holy ghooſt aſſygneth ſome thyſe tyme cryſtenȳge ye byſſhop ye confyrmacyō reherſeth thyſe wordes ye ſacrament wyll telle ye ye ſacrament cryſtenȳge founden lyf ſaynt iames ¶narracio ¶ther holy byſſhop yt torned lowys kyng fraunce cryſten fayth ſo whan ye kyng came ye cryſtenynge atte halowynge fonte grete preſſe people clerke bare ye byſſhop cryſmatory myght brynge byſſhop ſoo whan fonte halowed came anoyntynge myght come cryſmatory thenne byſſhop lyft vp eyen god prayenge god deuoutly helpe anone therwith ther came doue whyte ony mylke waſ holy ghoſt berynge herbylle vyole oyle creme byſſhop whan opened vyole come therof ſo ſwete ſauour people wondre therof gretly comforted therby contynued tyll ſeruyce done loo ye may well ſee though preeſt ſaye wordes holy ghoſt worcheth ſacrament doth vertue wordis holy ghoſt may deſcende lyghten v may come receyue hym ſaluacyon amen ¶in die pentecoſtes good men wymmen day called whyt ſondaye bycauſe holy ghoſt brought wytte wyſedome cryſtis dyſcyples ſo prechynge cryſtendome may ye vnderſtande many hath wyt wyſdome ben many haue wytte preche well ther ben fewe yt haue wyſedō well many wyſe prechers techers lyuȳg maner thynge prechȳge many ye labour haue wytte cōnȳge ben fewe trauaylleth come good lyuȳge ſo hath wytte connyng gete good fayr ſubtyll wordes neuer ſo fals wyſe wytte holyneſſe ſette gette good falſely knackes mowes wyſe man forſaketh wytte worlde foule loke holy ſcrypture ſayth dn̄s recitauit men pauperis quia ipſū approbauit et nomen eius libro vite ſcriptū fuit lorde hath receyued name poore man hath proued hym pouerte wryten name boke lyf sed nomen diuitis tacuit quia nō approbauit lefte ryche mā hath preued hym though man neuer ſo ryche atte laſt ſhall poore nought bryngeth hym good dedes badde lyueth wel techeth well good enſample lyuynge good doctryne ¶this grace daye gyuen cryſtys diſcyples taught well lyued wel gaue good informacyon techynge good enſample lyuynge techynge lyuynge ſprade thrugh worlde come vnto grace ye ſhall poſt aſcenſionem domini whan lorde iheſu cryſt ſtyed vp heuen dyſcyples grete heuyneſſe mornynge loſt mayſter yt loued full well hym loſt goodes loue forſoke frenſhyp ſerued hym full poore hope ſholde gretely holpen hym thus heuy gretly aſtonyed ſore aferde taken iewes caſte pryſon put deth made ſore durſt go amonge people gete mete drynke yet cryſte badde theȳ aſcēſyon wente cyte iheruſalem halle ſtage ſate togyder prayenge vnto god hole herte one ſpyryte helpe ſocoure ſo comforte theyr dyſeaſe thenne thus praycnge togyder ſodenly grete clowde made ayre lyke blaſt thonder euen therwith holy gooſt came amonge theym et apparuerunt illis diſpertite lingue tan quam ignis lyght came doune amonge lykenes tongue brennynge ſmertȳ ge warmynge harmȳge lyghtnynge flytterynge et repleti ſūt omnes ſpiritu ſancto fylled theym full gooſtly wytte tofore lewde men ſyght vnlettred ydeottes connynge nothȳge coude clergye ſodaynly wyſeſt men worlde anone ſpake maner language vnder ſonne theyr hertes colde grete drede fere deth ſo gretely comforted holy gooſt brennȳ ge loue went preched taught worde god ſparynge noo drede redy ſuffre dethe cryſtes ſake tyme iheruſalem people nacyons drewe temple grete fere blaſte thonder ayre ſtudyed might came appoſtles temple preched maner nacyons vnderſtode thē vnderſtode maner nacyons ſo preched worde god people aſtonyed whā herde appoſtles ſpeke maner language ſayd ſome haue dronken ſo moche wote ſay neyther meane dronken anſwered peter ſayd ben dronken prophecye iohel prophete holy gooſt ſholde giuen plenteuouſly people ſo ſholde ſpeke tongue preche worlde lawes iheſu cryſt people torned faſte ſo within fewe yeres fayth worlde ¶now wyte holy ghooſt appered lykenes tongue ony partye mannes body came ſyttynge rather ſtandynge fyrſt cauſe tongue beſt membre mannes body whā good rule well dyſpoſed whan oute rule worſt venenū aſpidum ſub labiis eorum bytter venȳ vnder tongue ſpeketh euyll ſayeth dauyd pſalter ſaynt iames ſayth curſed tongue fyred fyre hell may chaſtyſed whyle ye fyre brenneth alſo tongue muſte ſpeke wordes fyre ſharpe ſperkelynge ſaye trouthe ſpare prechynge repreue myſdedes holy men olde tyme ouercame droue away ye fyre lyghtnynge holy wordes good prayer brennynge loue god ryght fyre holy ghooſt ſholde dryue away ouercome fyre helle enuy hath euyl lyuynge reygneth moche people hertes appoſtles prechers yt cometh hym ſholde ſpeke brennynge wordes neyther ſharpe neyther drede ne loue ſaye trouthe tell people theyr defautes repreue ſynnes reygneth many dyuers wyſe ſo ſay worde god repreue ſynne wyll leue ſynne ſhall without remedye dampned fyre hell though thou ſholdeſt deye ſpare relate worde god tell trouthe itē deus eſt miſericors penitentibꝰ peccata ſua alſo god mercyfull theym ſory theyr ſynnes wyll leue cū vero confeſſus fuerit et reliquerit ea miſericor diam conſequatur though man done neuer ſoo moche ſynne wyll ſhryue hym forſake ſȳne mercy ſhall folowe hym ſhall haue forgyuenes ſoo come bryght fyre euerlaſtynge blyſſe precyous loue god brenneth amonge aungelles ſayntes kyngdome heuen alſo cometh lykeneſſe tonges fyre kynde fyre make lowe hyghe warme colde make ſofte harde make harde yt ſofte alſo holy ghooſt maketh hertes ben hyghe pryde enuye maketh theym lowe warme loue charyte alſo harde hertes yt haue gaderynge holdynge worldly goodes holy ghooſt maketh theym ſofte lyberall gyue deale almeſdedes loue almyghty god oure lorde iheſu cryſt maketh theym harde alſo ſufferynge harde ſtrate lyuynge doynge grete penaunce theyr ſynnes thus holy ghooſt euer redy make ſalue hele maner ſȳnes othet ſkyll holy ghoſt come apoſtles rather ſyttynge ſtandynge ſyttynge betokeneth mekenes herte reſt pea vnyte whiche ony maner man muſte nedes haue wyll receyue holy ghoſt ryght drye wood wyll brēne clerely without ſterynge soo ſholde euery cryſten man loue brennynge loue charyte clerely without feynynge wrath enuye ony maner malyce eche ſo euery man ſholde fayne welfare maketh haue good tonge ſoone brondes ben caſte twynne dyſcenſyon malyce enuye anone fyre holy ghooſt quencheth ſo thenne ryſeth vp ſmoke grete wrath enuye bytwene partye partye alſo grete greuaunce heuyneſſe ſoule cauſeth fayle grace may haue conſyderacyon reaſon thenne anone wycked ſpyrytes ben redy reyſe vp ſmoke ſame mannes herte ſaye grete wrath enuye euyll wyll may haue maner reſte euer ſtudyenge thynkynge alſo may auenge hym doo vengeaunce vnto enuyes ſoo man euer troubled beſy euer curſyd dedes lykely dampned bothe body ſoule helle euerlaſtynge payne yf haue ſome ſocoure helpe holy ghooſt ſuche thȳ ge may come curſyd wyckede tonges therfore holy ghoſt cometh lykeneſſe tonges brennynge fyre brenne malyce enuye anoynte ſwetneſſe grace loue charyte therfore ſhall praye holy ghoſt gyue v grace ſo tempre tōges may euermore ſpeke good hertes may fedde mekeneſſe▪ may able fedde holy ghoſt ſaynt gregory whan expowned prophecye toke hym deken ſaynt peter wryte expowned made drawe bytwene hym ſaynt peter ſholde ſee dyde ſtandynge thenne gregory ſat chayr holdynge vp hondes eyen heuen warde holy ghoſt come lyke whyte douue foot bylle brennȳ ge golde ſat gregory ryght ſholder put bylle gregoryes mouth whan withdrewe thenne bad peter wryte ſo contynued tyll hadde made ende expowned goſpell ſoo boldely peter hadde grete wonder merueyled therof thē pryuely made hole clothe bytwene gregory hym ſawe ye holy ghoſt fedde hym anone holy ghooſt ſhewed gregory peter done gregory blamed peter charged hym yt ſholde neuer ſaye nothynge whyle lyued whan gregory deed heretyke wolde haue brenned bokes holy man made thenne peter withſtode hym ſayd nay tolde al holy ghooſt done hym whyle expowned prophecye ſo ſaued bokes vnbrenned made grace god gyfte holy ghooſt whiche gyue v grace fedde hȳ lyuynge may haue blyſſe neuer ſhall haue ende amen ¶indie ſancte trinitatis good men wȳmen daye hye ſolempne feſt holy chirche holy trynyte holy chirche wytſontyde maketh mencyon holy ghoſt came cryſtys dyſcyples tyme made mencyon thre perſones ſaye pater filius et ſpirituſſanctus fader ſone holy ghoſt thre perſones one god wherfore boūde al reuerē ce worſhyp may holy trynyte alſo ye ſhall vnderſtande cauſe feſt ordeyned holy feſt worſhypped trynyte fyrſt fyndynge heretykes confoū dynge trynyte worſhypynge fyrſt ordeyned fourme trynyte fyndynge grete clerke iohan bellet telleth fourme ye trynyte fyrſt man adam forne fader came erthe one perſone eue adam ſeconde perſone hem bothe cometh thyrde perſone childe thus trynyte founde man wherfore man ſholde haue mynde worſhyp holy trynyte holy chirche ordeyned weddynge man woman togyder ſo maſſe trynyte ſongen deth one belle ſhall rongen worſhyp trynyte wherfor al cryſten peple ben bounde gretly worſhyp holy trynyte ſeconde cauſe feſt ordeyned confoundynge heretykes lollers deſtroye theym fals opynyons hadde ayenſt holy trynyte ryght heretykes ye begȳnynge fayth wt ſwete wordes fals opynyōs deſtroy fayth ye holy trynyte ye ſame wyſe lolers dayes wt fals ſpyce gyle alſo withdrawe ye peple frō ye true byleue fayth holy trynyte ye byleue fayth holy chirche pope martyr confeſſours deth ryght ſo thyſe lollers purſuen men holy chirche ben maner wayes may fynde deſtroye vndo ſo myght haue theyr purpoſe thus ſhewe openly yt ben goddes ſeruauntes charyte yt charyte ferre god ſuffreth trybulacyon perſecucyon dyſeaſe ye loue almyghty god prayeth enemyes myſdoers wyll vengeaūce put god almyghty wyll quyte thē full well euerlaſtynge blyſſe lorde ſayth thꝰ michi vindictam et ego retribuā put thynge ſhall quyte euery man deſeruynge though god ſuffred holy chirche purſued ſuche myſſe proude heretykes laſt ordeyned ſuche remedye yt holy chirche holpen enemyes confoūded ſhamed thus happed tyme wt themperour rome yt hyght attilia made heretykes iohan bellet telleth whiche emperour purſued cryſten peple ſore hated holy chyrche gretly wherfore made brenne bokes yt myght foūde cryſten fayth almyghty god wolde good holy man yt grete clerke clerke called alpynyons mayntenynge fayth holy chirche made ſtory trynyte ſtory alſo saynt steuen brought vnto pope haue ſongen rede holy chirche coūſeyl ye grete clerke toke ſtory ſaynt steuen lefte ſtory holy trynyte tyll ye tyme yt ſaynt gregory pope thēne preue thē doo thē ſhame yt ben ſuche myſleuynge people wolde beleue trynyte made reaſon many heretykes conſyderacyon ſaynt gregory 〈◊〉 ordeyned feeſt halowed ſtory ſonge redde holy chyrche worſhyp ye trynyte cryſten people· thyrde cauſe hygh trynyte worſhyppynge al cryſten men ſholde knowe maner ſholde beleue trenyte holy chyrche techeth beleueth trynyte ſhall ſaued doo ſhall dampned thenne full expedyent nedefull cryſten people knowe ſholde lyue ye ſhall vnderſtande ye perfyte loue vnto god beleue beleueth perfytely maketh queſtyons fides non habet meritum vbi humana ratio prebet experimentū fayth hath mede ne meryte mannes wytte gyueth experyence good cryſten people make loue medyatour holy gooſt praynge hym lyghten v within ſoules may haue grace come perfyte beleue therfore daye ſette nexte whytſonday hopynge ye holy gooſt wyll redy cryſten people wyl call hym ſpecyally lernynge fayth yet mannes wytte dull lerne thenne may ſe brought grete enſāple thoſe people mooſt commendable yf may enſample come ſooner beleue fader ſone holy gooſt thre perſones one god take hede enſample yſe ſnowe water theſe thre ben dyuers eche ſubſtaunce yet water ye may vnderſtande water fader yſe ſone ſnowe holy gooſt water element hath grete myght ſtrength mayſter alyſaūder ſayth aboue heuen maner yſe lyke cryſtall dooth worſhyp heuen anone vnder erth erthe grounded vpon water dauyd ſayth ye pſalter aboue worlde thynge harde ſtones yren ſomtyme ſwete water▪ water ſo full myght vnderſtande fader power ſo moche gouerneth worlde knoweth thynge cōmaundement ſone iheſu cryſte ye ſhall vnderſtande yſe water congyled harde bryttle iheſu cryſt god man toke ſubſtaunce fraylte mankynde whan conceyued holy gooſt vyrgyn mary borne body god ſuffred paſſyon vnder ponce pylate done vpon croſſe deyed buryed thyrde day aroſe dethe lyfe holy thurſdaye ſtyed vp heuen ſhall come agayne day dome deme quicke deed ſnowe ye ſhall vnderſtande holy gooſt ryght ſnowe water yſe lyght ayre man tell soo cometh holy ghooſt frome fader ſone spirituſſanctus patre et filio nō factus nec creatꝰ nec genitus ſed procedens man ſtudy excedeth mannes wytte ſtudye therupon ſadly beleue fader full god almyghty hym came ſone full god bothe came holy gooſt ful god trenyte knowen clerke gretely lerned dyuynyte whiche ſtudyed beſyly haue broughte boke god wolde beleued one god thre perſones ſo walked day ſtudyenge mater ſe ſonde ware fayre chylde ſyttynge ſee ſonde lytell ſhell thenne thou ſhalte crouned wt croune euerlaſtynge ioye blyſſe whiche brynge v holy trynyte amen ¶de corpore chriſti good frendes ye ſhall vnderſtande day hyghe ſolampne feeſt holy chyrche feeſt corpus raciones prodeſt homini audire miſſam ſecundum auguſtinum ¶saynt auguſtyn ſayeth prouffyteth gretely cryſten people maſſe ſpecyally nyne cauſes ſayth maner wyſe quia illo die qua audierat miſſam remyſſyon ſynne hauynge full truſt byleue cryſte euer redy forgyue al wyll aſke mercy meke herte dauyd ſayth cor contritū et humiliatū deus non deſpicies contryte herte meke lorde ſhall neuer deſpyſe may ſeues whiche men curſed lyuynge therfore ordeyned deed one aſked mercy meke herte ſayd domine dum venet regnum tuum memento mei lorde quod whan thou comeſt thy kyngedome haue mynde anone ge ſorowe moche cauſe mākȳde yt brought fro euerlaſtȳge dāpnacyon euerlaſtȳge ſaluacyon paſſyon thyrde cauſe ye ſacramēt vſed awter man ſholde ye ſyght therof thȳke god iheſu cryſt fader heuen yt hath one ſone yt loued paſſȳ ge thȳge ſpared ſende hȳ downe world ſuffre paſſyō deth ſhedde p̄cyous blood mankȳde bye hȳ ye fendes bondes wryte charter wt owne p̄cyous blood fredom euermore mankynde ſo yt man forfeyt charter dedely ſȳne yt loued god wyll kepe charter god aſketh man loue ſayth thꝰ da mihi cor tuū ſufficit mihi sone gyue thyn herte ynough thenne take hede enſample ¶narracio ¶there erle venys yt called ſyre ambryzt yt loued ye ſacrament ye awter paſſynge well dyde ye worſhyp reuerence yt coude myght ſo whā leye ſyke ſholde deed myght receyue ye ſacramēt caſtynge then̄e ſory made dole then̄e lete make clene ryght ſyde couer fayre clothe ſendell leyde goddes body therin ſayd thus thoſt lorde yu knoweſt yt loue ye herte wolde feyne receyue ye wt mouth durſt therfore may leye yt place yt next herte ſo ſhewe loue herte yt may wherfor beſeche ye good lorde haue mercy euen therwith ſyght people hym ſyde opened thoſt went ſyde thenne cloſed ayen ſo anone deyed departed worlde lete v loue ſacrament lyf reuerence worſhyp thenne laſte ende whan ſhall deye paſſe worlde wyll ſocour v brynge v euerlaſtynge blyſſe thus ſacrament vſed grete mede getynge byleue therin thoughe haue lykenes breed taaſt fleſſhe ſemeth breed quycke ſemeth deed ye muſt byleue verely goddes bleſſyd body toke fleſhe blood ye virgyn mary deyed ye croſſe roos fro deth lyf ſtyed vp heuen ſytteth faders ryght honde ſhal come ayen daye dome deme quycke deed receyue byleueth verely therupon ſhall haue euerlaſtynge lyf ye kyngdom heuen goſpel ſayth qui manducat hūc panē viuet ineternū ſo ereth breed ſhal lyue euer neuer deed receyued byleued thus reus erit iudicio daye dome ſhall dampned euerlaſtynge payne auguſtinꝰ ꝑſona xp̄i manduca non mutabis te ſed tu mutaberis saynt auſtyn ſayth perſone cryſte ete ſhall torne chaūge yu ſhalt torne chaūge ¶narracio ¶we rede iewe went cryſtē man felowe chirche cryſten people herde maſſe et poſt miſſā dixit iudeus whan maſſe done iewe ſayd ye cryſten man siego tantum ediſſē quātū tu comediſti nō eſuriā vt puto tribꝰ diebꝰ yf eeten moche yu haſteten wolde hū gred trowe thre dayes then̄e ſayd ye cryſtē mā ye iewe vere nihil comedi forſoth ſayth ye cryſten mā ye iewe ete maner mete daye ſayd iewe ego vidite comedere puerum pulcerrimū qualē ſacerdos eleuauit ad altare ſawe ye ete childe ye whiche ye preeſt helde vp awter et tūc venit pulcerrimꝰ hō habens mltos pueros ī gremio ſuo then̄e came ſayr man many child lappe et dedit vnicui que veſtrū vnū puerū talē qualē ſacerdos ꝯmedit gaf eche cryſten man childe ſuche ye preeſt ete ¶yet ſharpe byleue ye holy ſacrament wyll telle enſample ¶narracio ¶we rede ſaynt gregoryes tyme woman yt hyght lacyua ſhe made breed ye pope preſtes ſynge houſel wt people whan pope came woman gyue houſel ſayd goddes body woman ſmyled laughed thā pope wtdrewe honde layd oſt vpon ye awter torned woman lacyua ſayd ſmyleſt yu whan yu ſholdeſt receyue cryſtis body ſhe ſayd calleſt yu cryſtis body yt made wt myn owne honde thē gregory ye pope ſory myſbyleue bad ye peple praye god ſhewe ſome myracle womās helpe whan hadde prayed longe gregory wente ye awter ayen foūde ye oſt torned reed fleſſhe blood bledyng ſhewed womā then̄e ſhe cryed ſayd lorde crye ye mercy byleue yt yu art god man goddes ſone heuen fourme breed then̄e badde gregory ye peple praye ayen yt ſholde torne ayen bredes lykneſſe ſo dyde wt ye ſame oſt houſeled womā lacyua therfore lete v ye worſhyp may ſacrament may myſbyleue ¶narracio ¶alſo fynde deuenſhyre beſyde exbrydge woman yt laye ſeke nye deed ſente holy parſone mydnyght haue ryghtes man haſte myght aroſe went chyrche toke goddes body boxe yuory put boſom went forthe warde woman wēt foreſt fayre mede nexte way happed boxe fell boſome grounde went forth wyſt came woman herde confeſſyon aſked yf ſhe wolde houſeled ſhe ſayd ye ſyr then̄e put hande boſom ſought boxe whan founde full ſory ſad ſayd dame wyll go goddes body come agayne anone ſo went forth ſore wepynge ſymplenes ſo came wylowe tree made therof rodde ſtryped hym ſelf naked bete hym ſelfe blode ranne doune ſydes ſayd thus hym ſelfe thou ſymple man haſte thou loſte thy lorde god thy maker thy fourmer creatour whan thus bete hym ſelfe dyde clothes went forthe ware pyller fyre laſted frome erthe heuen aſtonyed therof yet blyſſed hym went laye ſacrament fallen boxe graſſe pyler ſhone bryght ſonne laſted frome goddes body heuen beeſtes foreſt comen goddes body ſtode compaſſe rounde kneled iiii knee ſaue one blacke horſe yt kneled one knee thenne ſayd yf yu ony beeſt may ſpeke charge yt goddes name preſent fourme breed tell thou kneleſt one knee ſayd fende hell wyll knele myght made agaynſt wyll wryten euery knelynge heuen erthe ſhall worſhyp lorde god arte thou lyke horſe ſayd make people ſtele ſuche towne one hanged ſuche toune ſayd holy perſone commaunde goddes fleſſhe bloode thou go wylderneſſe yu ſhalte neuer dyſeaſe cryſten people anone went waye might lenger abyde man wēt forth woman dide ryghtes whiche ſhe ſaued wente euerlaſtynge ſaluacyon whiche brynge v yt v ſhed blode rode tre amē ¶de feſto ſancti andree appoſtoli good mē woman ſuche daiye ſhall haue ſaynt andrewes day ye ſhall faſte euen come god holy chyrche worſhyp holy ſaynt daye thre ſpecyall vertues one grete holynes doynge ſeconde good lyuȳ ge thyrde grete paſſyon ſuffrȳge mā holy lyuynge whan vnderſtode herde ſaynt iohan baptyſt yt preched deſert left al wordly occupacyon went hȳ dyſcyple ſo day cryſt walked ye way ſaynt iohan ſawe hym ſayd dyſcyples ecce agnꝰ dei q• tollit p • tā mundi se lambe god ſhall awaye ſynne ye worlde ſaynt andrewe herde anone left ſaynt iohan baptyſt ſued cryſte whan herde cryſt preche pleaſed hym ſoo well anone went fetched peter broder cryſt preche keſt grete loue god ſoone ſee galyle fyſſhynge cryſte came called anone left fyſſhynge ſhyppe nette yt hadde ſued cryſte euer hȳ vntyll ſtyed vp vnto realme heuen ¶narracio ¶thenne ſaynt andrewe preched amonge people thenne daye preched happed ſoo man amonge people called nycoll lyued many wynters lechery yet grace god thought amende lyfe whan herde worde god ſo grete vertue ſholde put away temptacyonns ſynne lete wryte goſpell bare hym ſoeuer went wc vertue therof abſtayned hymſelfe fro ſynne yet day temptacyon fende forgate hymſelfe went agayne brodelles hous vſed came woman loked vpon hym cryed hym ſayd thou olde ſely man dooſt thou go home agayne ſe ſo many meruayles yt may haue nycoll thoughte yt ye goſpell vpon hym anone went ſaynt andrewe tolde hym caſe prayed ſaynt andrewe pray hȳ yt ſoule myght ſaued thē ſaynt andrewe wolde ete ne drȳke tyl wyſt yf nycol ſholde ſaued saynt andrew faſted v dayes breed water prayenge nyght day came voyce ſayd yu haſt faſted prayed make nycoll ſame thenne ſhall ſaued thenne ſaynt andrewe badde nycoll faſte fyue dayes breed water praye beſely vnto god ſo dyde thenne come voyce vnto ſaynt andrewe agayne ſayd thy prayer thy faſtynge hath made nycoll loſt founde agayne ſhall ſaued ¶narracio ¶alſo myracle yonge man come ſaynt andrewe tyme ſayd pryuely hym syre moder hath longe ſholde lye wolde wyll ſhe hath accuſed byſſhop ſayd yt wolde haue done ſynfull dede wt wherfore wote well yt ſhall deed yet leuer deye ſcaūder moder ſo foule therfore beſeche praye may take mydeth pacyently ſaluacyon ſoule ſayd ſaynt andrewe go forth thy dome ſhall go ſother people come fette hym byſſhop whā moder accuſed hȳ ſayd thȳge helde pea thenne ſayd ſaynt andrewe innocens ſanguis eius dāp nabitur curſyd woman luſt body wrongfully dampne owne childe deth vengeaunce wyl come thenne ſhe ſayd loo ſyr iuſtyce euer ſyth myght haue wyll hath drawen man counſeyll ſocour thenne iuſtyce cōmaūded caſte yonge man water drowne hym put ſaynt andrewe pryſon tyll auyſed deth ſholde deye thenne ſaynt andrewe prayed beſely vnto god helpe ſocour thenne anone come grete thondre made people ſo aferde yt fayne fette ſaynt andrewe pryſon euen therwith come lyghtnȳge fyre brenned ye moder ye yonge man ſyght people thus 〈2 page missing〉 daye waxed wood deyed amonge al people whan maximilia wyfe herde therof anone ſhe toke andrewes body buryed tombe tombe welleth manna oyle togyder people countre knowe whan ſholde dere whan grete plē te whan ſhal plente welleth plentefully whā ſhall derthe ſcarcely ¶narracio ¶it fell ſoo byſſhop loued well ſaynt andrew fende myght wyfe brynge hym purpoſe came byſſhop lykenes fayre woman prayenge hym ſhe myght ſpeke hym counceyle confeſſyon graunted ther syrſhe ſayd knyghtes doughter haue moche cheryſſhed nouryſſhed grete tendernes ſe worlde vanyte truſt vpon haue auowed chaſtyte ſo fader wolde mary worthy prynce wolde breke vowe come pryuely away poore araye thus herde grete holynes come haue counceyle ſocoure helpe you▪ wherfore praye ordeyne ye fende haue power let purpoſe thenne byſſhop conforted badde ſhe ſholde thanke god ſet ſuche purpoſe wolde ſende grace therwith contynue ſayd eſto ſecura filia thou ſeker doughter day thou ſhalt dyne thenne ſhal good aduyſe whan haue dyned deyne ſo ye ſhal ryght well nay ſyr ſayd ſhe leeſt people wolde haue ony ſuſpeccyon bad rule ye ſayd byſſhop therof charge plurimi erunus et non ſoli • ſhall ſo many company ſhall ſuſpeccion thenne ſhe thanked hym fayre ſhe ſet fore byſſhop chayre mete euer whan ye byſſhop loked ſemed ſo fayre gretely tempted ſo almooſt forgete hym ſelf thenne anone came pylgryme gate bete faſte gate within hall ſore aſtonyed noyſe ſo cryed lete lete thenne ſayd byſſhop ſhall man come thenne ſayd ſhe lete hym anſwere ſome queſtyon fyrſt yf worthy come ſo nygh preſence thenne ſayd byſſhop pray make queſtyon auyſed tyme thenne ſayd ſhe vnto meſſenger interroga quod eſt magus miraculū qd deus vn quam paruare fecit aſke hym ye greteſt myracle euer god made fote erth thenne whan pylgryme aſked anſwered ſayd mannes face whiche fote mannes owne face though men woman euer borne ſtode afore yet ſholde knowe one ſome degre whan gaue anſwere gretely commended therfore ſayd ſhe ſe yt wyſe bydde hym gyue anſwere queſtyon aſke hym whyder erth hygher heuen thenne anſwered ſayd thus cryſtes body erthe cryſtes body kynde kynde erthe ſo therfore cryſtes body erthe hygher heuen gyuen ye anſwere well alowed boden come nay ſayd ſhe let hym aſſoyle ye thyrde queſtyon aſke hym ferre frome heuen hell thenne whan oppoſed anſwered meſſenger go agayne ſytteth chayre byſſhop byd gyue anſwere ſhe better tell quando de celo abiſſum cecidit ſhe fende helle ſhe hathe metten ſo dyde neuer ſhe fell heuen pryde preſumpcyon lucyfer whan meſſēger herde heuy gaf anſwer al men myght then̄e fēde vanyſſhed awaye horryble ſtynke▪ thenne ye byſſhop bethought hym temptacyon ſory herte anone made ſende pylgrym yt meſſenger came ayen yate gone byſſhop made men praye god ſende wetynge pylgrym ſo goodly halpe hym nede thenne came voyce hȳ ſayd ſaynt andrewe yt came ſocoure hym loue ſeruyce dyde hym badde hȳ preche myracle peple ſee knowe gracyouſly helpeth wyll praye hym therfore lete v worſhyp praye hym ſocour helpe ayenſt fende euer amen ¶de ſancto nicholao good men wymmen ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſaynt nycolas daye whiche moche prayſed holy chirche ſpecyaly thre cauſes fyrſte meke lyuynge ii heuenly techynge iii grete compaſſyon hauynge ¶fyrſt made lowely pater eius epiphanus mater eius iohāna dictum eſt ſayd fader hyght epyphanus moder iohanne yt whiche yougth gate ſaynt nycolas whan borne made vowes kepe lyue chaſtyte nomore came togyder holde pleſed one childe god hath ſente whiche made hym cryſten called hym nycolas yt mannes name kepeth name ye childe choſe kepe vertues mekeneſſe ſymplenes malyce alſo rede whyle laye cradell faſted weneſdaye frydaye thyſe dayes wolde ſouke one ye daye ther wt helde hym pleſed thus lyued lyf vertues wt childes name therfore childern done hym worſhyp ſaȳtes euer meke without ony malyce ſo yt peple prayſed hym meke lyuynge alſo made byſſhop cyte myrre voyce whiche came heuen whā byſſhop deed byſſhops countre came togyder cheſe thenne came voyce one bad hym ryſe erly morow go chirche dore make hym byſſhop yt ye fynde called nycolas ſo morowe came chirche dore founde nycolas thenne ſayd thus hym quale nomen habes tu thy name lowtynge heed anſwered mekely ſayd nycolas then̄e theym yt dyſeaſe peryll whan fader moder deyed left hȳ wordly good ynough whiche yt ſpende yt poore nedy ¶narracio ¶it felle ſo yt ryche man yt iii fayr doughters yonge wȳmen myſchyef fylle pouerte people ete drynke ſowe ynough thre yere ¶narracio ¶an myracle ther two knyghtes yt accuſed treaſō thēperour fals mater cōmaūded pryſō haue put deth ſoone then̄e cryed god ſaȳt nycolas helpe ſocour ſo ye nyght ſholde deed saynt nycolas came themperour laye bedde ſayd thus hȳ haſt ye wrongfully dāpned thyſe knyghtes deth aryſe vp anone delyuer thē pryſon el wyl praye god reyſe batayll vp ye ye whiche thou ſhalt deye wylde beſtes ſhall ete ye then̄e ſayd themperour hȳ art thou ye ſoo boldely ſpekeſt ſo threteſt then̄e ſayd nycolas ye byſſhop myrre then̄e thēperour anone ſent ye knightes ſayd wytchecraft ye yt thus hath trauayled nyght knowe ye ony man yt hyght nycolas byſſhop myrre then̄e ſoone herde name felle downe ye groūde helde vp theyr hondes thankȳge god saȳt nycolas whan tolde themperour lyf holy ye emperour bade go hym thāke hȳ lyues ſo dyde prayed ye knyghtes praye nycolas threten hȳ nomore praye god hȳ reame ſo dyde thus ye may ſee yt hath grete cōpaſſyon thē yt dyſeaſe then̄e whan ſaȳt nycolas ſholde deye prayed god ſende hym aungell fetche ſoule whan ſawe aungell come ſaynt nycholas louted ſayd manus tuas dn̄e cōmendo ſpiritū meū redemiſti domine deus veritatis ſoo yelded vp gooſt whan buryed heed tombe ſprange welle oyle dyde medycyns al ſores thenne happened many yeres turkes dyſtroyed ye cyte myrre ſaynt nycolas laye whan people cyte barus herde yt ye cyte myrre deſtroyed xlvii knyghtes ordeyned go thyder thenne arayed ſhyppes wente thyder tellynge foure monkes lefte knewe ſaynt nycholas tombe vndyde anone founde ſaynt lawe cryſten man made hym holow ſtaffe put golde therin ſo came lawe ſholde ſwere went ye boke toke iew ſtaffe golde holde meane ſwore payed iewe whan ſworne toke ſtaffe iewe agayne wente homewardes
