baptiſatus aūt iudeꝰ viſo miraculo thenne iewe yt beleue ſyght myracle cryſtened narracio ¶alſo iewe ſawe grete myght ſaynt nycholas myracles werkynge lete make ymage ſaynt nycholas ſet ſhyp kepe good charged ymage kepe well good whyle yt abſent whan man gone came theues ſee robbed man bare away good ſo whan iewe came home agayne ſawe good gone wrothe wt ſaynt nycholas toke ſtaffe bete ymage ſayd ecce oīa bona mea poſui ī vr̄am cuſtodiā lo quod toke good kepynge grete truſte ſtolen awaye ye haue deceyued therfore thou ſhalte abye euery daye tyll haue good agayne thenne theſe theues departed good ſaynt nycholas came ſayd cur tam indirecte feciſtis flagellare haue ye made beten thus ſore thenne ſayd quis e tu arte thou ſpeketh thus v thenne ſayd ego ſum nicholaus ſeruus dei nycholas ſeruaunt god yt ye haue made thus ſore beten ſhewed ſore beten good borne awaye yt taken hym kepe bad goo bere good agayne anone elles goddes vengeaunce ſhall fall ye ſhal hanged hell euerychone ſore aferde bare agayne ye good ſame nyght morowe whan iewe came ſawe good brought agayne anone cryſtened holy man euery yere ſaynt nycholas day grete loue ſaynt nycholas alſo ſone clerke made grete feeſt ſaynt nycholas day thenne happened tyme vpon ſaynt nycholas day badde many clerkes feeſt thenne came fende gate lykenes pylgryme aſked ſome good goddes ſake then̄e good man made feeſt toke ſone almeſſe bere pylgryme ſo chylde went gate thenne pylgryme gone chylde folowed fende whan good way frome faders place fende caught chylde ſlewe whan fader herde therof full ſory toke chylde layde chambre cryed ſorowe ſayd ſaynte nycholas rewarde mede ſhall haue grete worſhyppe anone ye chylde roſe dethe lyfe man ful glad thanked god ſaynt nycholas ¶narracio ¶an myracle man yt prayed god ſaynt nycholas yt myghte haue chylde yf chylde wolde lede chyrche ſaynt nycolas wolde offre cuppe golde ſoone chylde whan chylde reaſonable aege fader lete make cuppe golde whan made lyked hym ſo well lete make thenne wente towarde ſaynt nycholas muſt paſſe ouer ſee whan ſee fader badde ſone take vp ſome water wt cuppe chylde wolde haue taken water cuppe fell oute hande ſee thenne chylde wolde haue caught cuppe agayne fell ſee ye chylde drowned ſee thenne fader made moche ſorowe yet went forthe ye cuppe pylgrymage whan came ſaynt nycholas chyrche offred vp cuppe ſet auter anone caſte frome awter ſet agayne caſt ferder yet thyrde tyme ſet agayne thenne caſt moche ferder thenne came chylde cuppe hande ſayd people yt ſaynt nycholas toke hym vp honde whan felle ſee ledde hȳ ſafe thenne fader gladde offred vp bothe cuppes went home agayne ioye myrthe ¶narracio ¶there ryche man ye prayer ſaynt nycholas hadde chylde made fayre chapell ye worſhyppe god ſaynt nycholas soo happened daye chylde taken enmyes ledde ſtraunge countree ſeruyce kȳnges courte happened ſaynt nycolas daye bethought hym grete myrthe ſolempnyte made daye faders chapell home heuy ſyghed wonder ſore thenne ye kynge herde therof ſayd hym nycholas meneſt thou ſyghe ſo ſore mery thou muſt nedes abyde wt v anone came grete wynde ſmote ye hous braſte chylde caught vp cuppe bare hande ſet gate chapell fader made feeſt thenne made grete ioye myrthe myracle lo thus ye may ſe grete compaſſyon ſaynt nycholas myſchefe dyſeaſe bokes ſaye chylde normandy taken soudan beyonde ſee often beten one whan beten ſaynt nycholas daye put pryſon thenne wept ſore fell ſlepe whā awoke ye chirche fader ¶de concepcione beate marie virginis good men womē ſuche day ye ſhall haue ye concepcyon lady yt whiche daye feeſt moder holy chyrche maketh mynde mencyon ye concepcyon blyſſed lady forthre ſpecyall cauſes fyrſte faders holyneſſe ſeconde moders goodnes thyrd mekenes fader called ioachym ſoo holy man whan fyftene yere aege departed goodes thre partyes one party deled wydowes faderles chyldren ſeconde partye gaue poore nedy thyrde parte kepte hym ſelfe houſholde whan xxxii yere aege grete goodnes anne wedded whan wedded togyder xxii yere whiche tyme anne neuer dyſpleaſed hym wt maner thynge neyther nyght daye ſhe ſoo gentyll hym bothe good holy yet god ſent noo fruyte theyr bodyes baraynes wherfore made vowe god yf wolde ſende chylde wolde offre vp hym temple ſerue god bothe daye nyght thenne day ioachym went neyghboures temple offringes byſſhop hyght yſachar rebuked hym openly people ſayd ioachym falleth barayne haſt fruyte doo frynges people god hath ſent fruyte iheruſalem thenne ioachym ſore dyſmayed aſtonyed rebuke thenne went home wepinge toke ſhepeherde pryuely ſhepe went forth ferre countre amonge mountaynes hylles purpoſed haue lyfe neuermore come home anne wyfe thenne whan ioachym gone anne ryght ſorye prayed vnto god ſayd lorde woo dolefull barayne may haue noo fruyte ouer huſbande gone awaye frome knowe whyder gone lorde haue mercy poore deſolate creature ſhe prayed thus angell came downe comforted ſayd anne good comforte thou ſhalt haue childe thy olde age ther neuer none lyke ne neuer ſhall thenne anne aferde angel wordes ſyght hȳ laye alwaye prayer ſhe deed went ye ſame angell ioachym ſayd thyſe wordes badde ioachym take lambe offre ſacrefyce god ſo dyde whan hadde done ſo myddaye tyll euenſonge tyme lay grounde prayer thankynge god herte morow thangel badde wente homewarde anne wyf ſheep whan came nye home angel came anne badde go gate yt called ye golden gate abyde huſbonde tyl came then̄e ſhe gladde toke maydens wente gate ſhe mette ioachym ſayd lorde thanke wydowe wyf barayne ſhall bere childe woo wepynge ſhall ioye lykynge ſoone anne cōceyued lady whan ſhe born ſhe called maria ye angell badde yt ſhe wened ſhe brought temple lefte amonge virgynes ſerue god nyght daye then̄e ſhe ſo meke amonge virgines lyuynge yt virgynes called quene virgynes soo ſhe mekeſt ſayntes heuen mooſt redyeſt helpe calle ony nede ¶narracio ¶we rede holy wrytte myracle lady ther lordes man gadred moche good lordes rente gaderer went bere lord theues ſette hym robbe hym waye wood muſt nedes go soo whan came woode bethought hym hadde ſayd ladyes ſawter wonte doo kneled downe began ſaye thenne came lady lyke fayre mayden ſet garlonde heed eche aue ſhe ſet roſe garlande ſo bryȝt wood ſhone therof whan done kyſſed erthe went way thenne came theues toke hym ledde hym theyr mayſter whiche ſeen al theſe doynges thenne ſayd womā ſette garlande thy heed ſayd ſyr forſothe ſawe woman garlonde thenne ſayd mayſter thefe wote well thou arte lordes man haſte moche good wolde fayne wyte woman came thou kneled doune ſayd whan ſawe aferde alſo bethought ſayd ladyes pſalter kneled downe ſay prayenge oure lady helpe nede thenne ſayd loue goo thy waye praye v ſo went way ſauf ſounde helpe ſocoure lady ¶but ye ſhall feeſt fyrſte founden kynge englonde hight wyllyam conqueroure ſent abbot ramſey kynge denmarke meſſage whan came ſee came tempeſt derkenes hym wende haue drowned euery man prayed beſyly vnto god lady ſocoure helpe dyuers ſayntes abbot prayed vnto lorde iheſu cryſte holy vyrgyn ſaynt mary full deuoutꝰly thenne came vnto hym fayre woman ſayd vnto theym yf ye wyll haue concepcyon lady worſhyp honoure two dayes ſaynt nycholas daye ſhe wyll redy thelpe ſocoure tyme thenne abbot ſayd ye good wyll wyſte ſholde ſeruyce feeſt thenne ſayd ſhe ſame natyuyte ſaufe torne natyuyte concepcyon abbot ſayd ſholde done wt full good wyll thenne anone tempeſt ceaſed wel ſayled forthe thabbot dyde meſſage came agayne ſauf ſounde ſped well euery degree whan came home tolde ye kynge vyſyon kȳ ge made hym preche realme thus halowed holy chyrche ¶narracio ¶alſo fynde ſeculer chanon tyme went ouer water auoutry woman begynne ſaye oure ladyes matyns inuytatorye aue maria ther wt fende keſte hym downe drowned hym wolde haue hym helle thenne came lady ſayd haſte thou taken man fende ſayd fynde hȳ ſeruyce goynge auoutrye thenne ſayd lady ſeruyce anone reſtored hym lyfe agayne badde hym ſynne badde hym halowe concepcyon ſo dyde good man euer lyfe ¶narracio ¶alſo clerke euery daye vſed ſaye ſeruyce blyſſed lady thenne happed counceyle frendes ſholde take wyfe whan ſholde wedded bethought hym hadde ſayde ladyes ſeruyce thenne made al people go chyrche whyles ſayd ſeruyce thenne kneled downe ſayd ſeruyce tyll came antem lady quam pulchra e amica mea then̄e lady appered vnto hym ſayd ſayeſt thou fayre honeſt wyll thou leue take thenne ſayd lady wyll thou ſhall thenne ſayd lady yf thou wylt leue thy fleſſhely wyfe ſerue ſone ſhall thy ſpouſe thou ſhalte haue crowne euerlaſtynge lyfe kyngedome perdurable blyſſe whiche god blyſſed moder ſaynt mary holy ſayntes heuen brynge v thyder amen ¶de ſancto thoma dere frendes ſuch day ye ſhal haue ſaynt thomas daye cryſtes appoſtle ye ſhall faſt euen hym worſhypp ſpecyally thre cauſes fyrſt preuynge beleue grete wonder way grete myracles dayes holy appoſtle preued ſo fayth left trouble whan dyſciples ſayd lorde ryſen frome dethe lyfe ſeen hym ſpoke hym thomas ſayd wolde beleue tyll put hande ſyde wounde ſpere made thenne viii dayes whan dyſcyples togyder thomas then̄e lorde iheſu cryſte came bodely ſayd pax vobis pea wt ſorde ſayd thomas ynde mitte manū tuam latus meū put thy hande ſyde wounde made ſpere yt ſmote herte et noli eſſe incredulus lenger beleue ſtedfaſt faythe whan thomas done ſo anone ſayd grete wōder dn̄s meꝰ deꝰ meꝰ lorde god beleue yt yu art god man thenne lorde ſayd hym beati qui crediderunt et nō viderunt bleſſyd byleue ſee thou haſt ſeen thou byleueſt yet taryē ge thomas brought v ſadder byleue bleſſynge lorde iheſu cryſte ſpeketh ſaynt gregory ſayth thomas ynde thou haſt holpen fayth woldeſt byleue tyll thou hade feled woundes thenne dyde mary mawdeleyne dyde byleue ye fyrſte ſyght minus eſt enim maria magdalena que ciciꝰ credidit quam thomas qui diu dubitauit thus thomas preued fayth byleue ſo nede neuer varye doubte alſo thomas dyde many marueylles grete woundres yt dayes ¶narracio ¶it happed kyng ynde ſende meſſenger albanus indie requirens artificem ſeke ſome crafty men countree cezar ſeke carpenter ye coude make hym palays pleſaūce thenne lorde iheſu cryſte mette albanus ſent wiht hym holy ſaynt thomas grete ynde whan thomas albanus paſſed ſee come cyte kynges doughter wedded ſame daye wherfore maner people cōmaūded mete amonge peple thomas albanus came ſette mete thomas ete thought euer god luſt ete thenne came botteler thomas ſmote thomas cheke badde hym ete thenne ſayd thomas hym non hinc ſurgam donec manus que percuſſit cambꝰ aufertur ſhall ryſe place tyll honde ſmote brought dogge thenne anone boteler went water lyon mete hym ſlewe hym dranke blood ete body thenne came blacke dogge caught honde yt ſmote thomas brought halle ſyght people layde downe thomas womā vnderſtode thomas wordes anone kneled downe thomas cryed ſayd thou art god el one dyſcyples ryght yu wylt ſo then̄e kyng prayed thomas bleſſe doughter huſbonde thomas glade ther cepit erge predicare beatus thomas therfore bleſſyd thomas began preche tolde theȳ lorde iheſu cryſt yt torned man wedded ye ſame daye frō wyf made hym byſſhop ſame cyte wyf nonne martyr cryſtys ſake thenne went thomas forth ynde kyng make hȳ palays pleſaunce whan thomas come kyng glade delyuered thomas grete ſōme golde make palays thenne rode ye kyng forth meane tyme whā thomas ſholde haue made palays hym thought better make palays heuen erthe deled golde amonge poore people conuerted theȳ fayth then̄e came kyng home wende palays hade redy whan herde thomas albanus hade done wolde haue put theym deth happed owne broder deed ſame tyme therfor put theȳ pryſon vnto tyme yt hade buryed broder god wolde whan broder laye longe deed roſe deth lyf tolde kyng ſeen palays paradyſe thomas made hym prayed kyng myght haue wolde gyue hȳ moche golde toke thomas thenne kyng toke counſeyll ſayd nay wyll haue myſelf lete hym make brother ſeen palays paradyſe made golde arrayed precyous ſtones clothe golde thenne kyng toke cryſtendome many thouſande hym whan byſſhops ſawe kyng ſo moche peple forſoke herlawes torned cryſtendome werefore wrothe thomas thenne one ſayd wolde venge god ſpere ſmote thomas thrugh body ſlewe hym thenne cryſten peple buryed hym tombe cryſtall god wrought many myracles hym honde cryſtys ſyde wolde neuer come tombe euer laye alſo prechynge techynge taught duodecum gradꝰ virtutum aſſignare ¶primus eſt vt deum crederent qui eſt vnus eſſencia et trinus perſonis dedit eis triplex exemplum ſenſibile quomodo tres perſone ſint vna eſſentia ¶primum quia vna eſt homine ſapiencia et de vna procedit intellectus memoria et ingenium memoria eſt vt nō obliuiſcaris intellectum vt intelligas que oſtendi poſſunt vel doceri ingenium eſt vt quod didiceris inuenias ¶secundum exemplum eſt quia vna vinea tria ſunt lignum folium et fructus et hec omma tria ſunt vna vinea ¶tercium exemplum eſt quia caput noſtrum ex quatuor ſenſibus conſtat vno autem capite ſunt viſus auditus guſtus et odoratus et hee plura ſunt et tamen vnum caput ¶secundus gradus eſt vt baptiſmum ſuſcipiat ¶tercius gradus eſt vt fornicatione abſtineat ¶quartus vt ſē ab auaricia temperet ¶quintus vt gulam diſtingeret ¶sextus vt penitenciam teneret ¶septimus vt perſeueraret octauꝰ vt hoſpitalitatē amaret ¶nonus vt voluntatem dei requirat ¶decimus eſt vt facienda quereret ¶vndecimus vt caritatem amicis et inimicis impen deret duodecimꝰ eſt vt cuſtodiat hec vigilē curā exhiberet ¶item appoſtolus omnes qui oderant deum de tribus breuiter inſtruxit faciendis ſcilicet de eccleſiam diligerent sacerdotes honorarent et aſſidue ad verbum dei conuenirent ¶alſo ben many meruaylous wonderfull thynges done daye· daye countre cometh thyde take pardon honde lyeth tombe theyr vſe byſſhop cyte gooth maſſe whan hath ſayd confiteor thenne taketh braunche vyne putteth thomas honde tombe thēne gooth forth maſſe braunche burgeneth grape tyme goſpell ſayd grape ben rype thenne byſſhop taketh grape wryngeth wyne ye chalyce ſo ſyngeth ſame wyne houſeled ye people whan ony man woman cometh worthy receyue houſell anone honde cloſeth togyder wyll open tyll ſhryuen thenne wyl opē alſo yf ony peple debate ſhal brought thomas tombe cauſe ſhall reherſed thenne wyll honde torne hym ryght ſo made one thus thomas preued byleue dyde many wōdres dayes alſo iohan gryſoſtomus ſayth thomas came countree thre kynges coleyne thomas cryſtened worſhypped god byrthe therfore thomas came theȳ taught fayth byleue cryſte byleue may ſaued god brynge v amen ¶de natiuitate domini noſtri iheſu chriſti frendes ye ſe holy chyrche maketh mynde mencyon ye grete myrth melody blyſſed byrth lorde iheſu cryſte veray god man yt day borne moder mary ſocoure mankynde eſpecyall thre cauſes fyrſt gyue pea man good wyll lyght thē derke ſyn̄e drawe v loue hym thenne ye fyrſt cauſe borne gyue men pea good wyll may well preue whan borne angel ſonge thus gloria excelſis deo ioye god heuen peaſe erth mankynde good wyll mydnyght lorde borne kynde thynge pea reſt ſhewynge princeps pacis prynce pea come make pea bytwene god man bytwene aungell man bytwene man man true medyatour betwene god man toke nature kynde bothe bothe veray god man medyacyon knytte loue god man ſoo ſadly yt fader heuē ſpared hym owne ſone ſent hym doune worlde bye mankynde wt precyous blode grete mekenes ioye paradyſe man hadde loſte couetyſe vnbuxſomneſſe thus made peaſe bytwene god man man man whan aungelles ſawe theyr mayſter wrothe man vnbuxſomnes ſynne aungelles dooth hate gretely therfore kept gate paradyſe wolde lette ſoule come paradyſe tyl ſawe theyr lorde ſouerayne borne mankynde take fleſſhe blyſſed vyrgyn mary mooſte beloued moder thenne anone loue lorde angel dyde mankȳ de worſhyp ſpake goodly mankynde ſhepeherdes kept ſheep countree badde theym go cyte bethleem ſholde fynde childe borne layde cratche badde hym worſhyp ſo dyden euer ſyn angel haue ben frendly man lowly haue done reuerence mankȳde thyncarnacyon lorde iheſu cryſt thꝰ made pea bytwene angel man alſo made pea bytwene man man ayenſt tyme yt lorde wolde born made ſo grete pea yt worlde kyngdomes countrees debate warred eche vnto ye tyme lordes byrth ther ſo grete pea man yt called octauyan emperour rome ye gouernaūce worlde worlde ſubget rome dured xxx yere ſo moche yt ther maundement ſente rome ye worlde cōmaundynge maner people ſholde go cyte drewe lygnage laye peny vpon heed offre vp know lechynge ſubget themperour rome muſt ioſeph ladyes huſbonde nedes go ye cyte bethleem offre peple moneye offre toke oxe wt hym ſelle cyte make moneye dute durſt leue lady bēhȳde hym ſhe nye tyme therfor ſet vpon aſſe tooke hym ſo whan came cyte bethleem ſo full peple ſo ioſeph lady myght haue lodgynge torned cabon made betwix two houſes people ye coū tree ſette theyr horſes theyr aſſes beſtes whā come towne market foū de cratche heye ſette oxe aſſe therto ſo taryed nyght whan lytell mydnyght lady badde ioſeph goo towne loke mydwyf tyme come ſhe ſholde delyuered ſoo whyle ioſeph towne mydwyf lady delyuered ſhe lapped ſone clothes layde cratche oxe thaſſe anone knewe lorde fyll downe knee worſhypped hym ete heye thenne anone came ioſeph two mydwyues zebell salome zebell founde lady clene mayden cryed ſayd virgo peperit filium mayde hath born childe thenne salome wolde byleue anone went lady bouſtouſly handled lady probare vellet ſhe wolde preue euen ther hondes dryed vp thenne came angell badde ſhe ſholde go touche ye childe ſo ſhe dyde anone ſhe hole thenne wente ioſeph dyde offrynge people kept lady ſame cabon whyle ſhe childe bedde thus ye may vnderſtāde cryſt gyueth pea people good wyll called hem childern verefyenge fyrſte maſſe ſō ge yt daye holy chyrche ſonge ſoone mydnyghte begynneth thus dominus dixit ad filius meus e tu ego hodie genui te lorde ſayth yu art ſone lorde called hym ſone childe loued hȳ reſt pea whan departeth worlde wyll brynge hym euer laſtynge reſt pea wyll haue reſt pea ſhall go euerlaſtynge payne neuer reſt pea neuer ſhal euerlaſtynge woo thus gyueth pea men good wyl lyghtneth lyketh hym good men ye ſhall vnderſtande cryſte heled oonly theym blynde ſoule combred derkeneſſe ſynful lyuynge ſaynt auſtyn ſayth whan lorde ſholde borne worlde full derkeneſſe ſpecyally ſynne lechery ſynne ayenſt kynde ſo moche almooſt left haue borne mankynde wherfore al thoſe dyden ſynne ayenſt kȳde tyme deyed ſodenly thrugh worlde ſhewynge horryble abhomynable ſynne ſyght almyghty god thenne loked full derke ſynne theyr thoughtes alwaye ſynne euyll lyuynge hadde full grete nede lyghtned wherfor cryſt borne mydnyght tourned derkeneſſe nyght daye lyght lyghtened theym euer couered combred derkeneſſe ſynne ¶alſo ſame tyme lorde borne many doctours ſayen cryſt appered bryght ſterre kynges theſt badde go bethleem worſhyp lytell childe ſholde kyng iewes borne ſo dyde euer ſterre ſhewynge theym tyll came thyder thus lyghtened theym full derke ſynne theſe kynges paynems bileued mawmetry fals goddes byleued cryſte holy lyuers coleyne ¶thus byrth lorde iheſu cryſt made many man loke full bryght tofore ful derke ſynne full derke ſoule euer ſetteth herte mynde thought proſperyte worſhyp welfare worlde maketh ſo inwardly blynde ſoo ignoraunt haue felynge grete ineſtimable grace ghoſtly ſyght ben made blynde abuſed tranſytory rycheſſe wycked worlde couetyſe therof commytte vſury ſo gete theyr good haue deſyre rycheſſe heuen ne ſe lyght ſuche thynges mannes herte mooſt maketh god dyſtroye ſuche mawmetry ſynne lorde borne thenne kynge herode purſued lorde wolde haue ſlayne hym thenne moder bare hym egypte aungell badde ioſeph ſayd accipe puerum et matrē eius fuge egiptum take chylde moder flee egypte ſoone came thyder mawmettes londe fell doune grounde doynge vnderſtande come worlde ſholde caſt downe mawmetry maner ſyn̄e euyll lyuynge pryde couetyſe maner falſhede vſed dayes therfore take hede lorde made maner thynge nought lorde lordes borne poore place poore araye poore mayden gyuynge enſample cryſten people ſet nought ye worſhyp rycheſſe vanyte worlde haue man neuer ſo grete worſhyp neuer ſo moche rycheſſe yet leueth ſhall bere hym good dedes thus lorde ſhewed many thynges byrthe lyghtned many one full blynde tokenynge herof ſeconde maſſe daye ſayd dawnynge whan nyght daye departeth whiche begynneth thus lux fulgebit hodie thus moche ſaye lyghte ſhall ſhyne daye vpon v fader heuen ſēdeth grace gooſtly lyght cryſten people beleue truly lorde borne god man moder mary moder mayden thus beleue truely lorde iheſu cryſte moder mary ſet full lytell vanytees worlde put al theyr hope truſte iheſu cryſte thus byrthe lorde iheſu cryſt lyghtned many one loked full yll alſo drew v hym loue chyldren drawe maketh moche playe thus lorde iheſu cryſte borne chylde fayreſt euer borne drawe mannes loue hym whyle chylde yonge without ſynne amyable louynge thenne mannes aege paſte innocencye doynge sythen loue onely beaute clennes ſoule alſo goodnes eche man bounde drawe hym hym worſhyppe octauyan dyde themperour rome pleaſed ſo moche people empyre rome yt wolde haue worſhypped hym theyr god ye emperoure wyſe wyſt wel man durſt take vpon hym none ſent sybyll ſage aſked whether ſholde ony borne hym ſholde greter thenne myddaye sybyll loked ſonne ſhe ſawe cercle golde ſonne et medio circuli virgo pulcherrima cum puero myddes cercle mayden chylde arme crowne golde whan sybyll ſhewed themperoure ſhe ſayd hym chylde ſhall greter yu arte euer euer ſhall therfore hym worſhyp reuerence thenne anone emperour toke encē ſe dyde worſhyp hym charged people ſame call chylde theyr god hym man thus cryſten people may lerne worſhyppe ſeruyce chylde day therfore thyrde maſſe daye ſayd myddaye tokenynge cryſten people ſholde come offre worſhyppe chylde moder ſhewe ſeruaū te ſubgecte vnto hym knowelege gloryous chylde lorde god eche man ſholde come hym drede therfore offyce ye maſſe daye begynneth thus puer natus eſt nobis chylde borne v ſayth man al cryſten people ſholde bolde aferde come vnto hym haue grace full grace redy gyue mercy aſke mekely due reuerence euer redy gyue mercy grace tokenȳge ſame day cryſte borne bedleem well water torned ranne oyle daye ſhewynge welle grace mercy borne daye yt ſholde gyue mercy grace wolde come hym aſke mercy grace ye ſhall enſample ¶narracio ¶we rede woman defouled lechery almooſt fell dyſpayre drede ſhe bethought ſtreytneſſe cryſtes dome grete horryble paynes hell ordeyned ſuche ſynners ſhe ſore aferde bethought herof cryſtes paſſyon loue ſhewed cryſten people ſhe thought ſhe vnkynde hym ſuffred ſo ſore then̄e ſhe bethought chyldren neuer ſo wrothe ſhewe neuer ſo grete vengeaūce lyghtly wyll ceaſe forgyue wherfore woman cryed cryſt prayē ge hym chyldehode haue mercy anone ſhe herde voyce hye ayre ſayd thy treſpace forgyuen ¶sermo breuis de ſancto ſtephano good men woman ſuche daye ye ſhall haue hye daye holy feeſt moder holy chyrch prothomartyr ſaynt steuen whiche ſuffred deth goddes ſake cryſtes aſcencyon thenne ſtere deuocyon holy martyr wyll tell ſomwhat ſuffred cryſtes ſake boke appoſtles telleth poſt aſcencionem domini aſcencyon lorde ſtyed vp heuen appoſtles laboure preche teche worde god cryſten people fewe ſerue people came came ſo many torne faythe therfore choſe vi holy men good lyuers helpe goddes ſeruyce whiche ſaynt ſteuen one theym fyrſt wyſeſt ſo full grace myght holy gooſt dyde many myracles meruaylous amonge people though man neuer ſo holy yet ſhall haue ennemyes wherfore dyuers countrees enmyte ſaynt steuen came agaynſt hym dyſputed hym haue ouercome hȳ dyſputacyon myght brought falſe wytnes agaynſt hym put hym dethe whan ſaynt stephen ſawe knewe theyr malyce anone thought ceaſe theym one theſe iii wayes ſhamynge dyſputacyon drede reuelacyon prayer holy orayſons fyrſte ſayd ſhamynge dyſputacyon whan began dyſpute hym ſoo full holy gooſt power ne myght gaynſaye hym ſo ouer came theyr mater preued al theyr mater falſe ſayd agaynſte therfore ſayd redy ſuffre dethe verefyenge ſuſteynynge ſayd ſo put grete clerkes knewe lawe prophecye vnto grete ſhame velonye yet wolde beleue alway agaynſtode hym ſo full holy ghooſt preued ſayd grete reaſon trouthe yet wolde byleue holy ghoſt ſpake hym yet yt wolde byleue theyr cōſcyence yt dyde amyſſe ſawe comynte tourne fayth wordes myracles god ſhewed ſyght yet ayenſtode hȳ ſette goddes myracles noughthy malyce enmyte curſyd hertes none reaſō ſcrypture ſo freted hertes hymſelf grutched teeth angre thought myght ouercome hȳ dyſputacyon thenne ſought yf myght haue taken hym ſome worde cryſtys deth myght haue made theym cauſe haue put hym deth▪ thenne saynt stephen knewe malyce lyft vp eyen vnto heuen et vidit celos apertos ſawe heuen open lorde iheſu cryſt ſyttynge faders ryght honde redy helpe hym face ſhone bryght angell heuen whan herde hȳ ſpeke thenne fayne ſtoppe theyr eres though herde hym ſpeke fals ſclaunderynge god ſo anone drewe hym cyte ſtone hym deth dyſſclaunderer thenne toke two yonge men coude beſt caſt ſtones toke clothes layde foot yonge man hyght saule saynt poule thenne whan ſaynt stephen ſawe myght ceſſe theyr malyce reuelacyon ſhewynge tourned deuoute oryſons prayenge yet wolde thenne caſted ſtones hym ſmote brayne thenne cryed god ſayd domine iheſu accipe ſpiritum meum thou lorde take ſpyryte wolde praye deuoutely enemyes hymſelfe kneled downe grounde ſayd pater ignoſce illis quia neſciunt quid faciunt fader forgyue theym wote anone ſlepte god take hede brennynge loue herte god prayed deuoutely enemyes hymſelfe gaf enſample cryſten people charyte eche one praye enmyes yt purſued hym dyde hym dyſeaſe vniuerſa delicta cooperit caritas charyte hydeth euery treſpas prayed enemyes martyred hym ony dyſeaſe ſuffred pacyently martyr god ben thre maner martyrdomes fyrſt paſſyon wyll therto wyll without paſſyon paſſyon without wyll fyrſte ſhewed ſaynt stephen yt ſette next byrthe cryſte ſuffred paſſyō wyll ther saynt iohan euangelyſt wyll paſſyon innocentes ſuffred paſſyō wyll ther ayenſt wyll thꝰ may man martyr though ſhede blood whan ſuffred grete wronge curſyd people thanked god therof toke good wyll prayed enemyes deuoutly clene charyte take hede ye ſhal ſee thyſe thre parfyght loue charyte saynt stephen whan ſholde deye kneled downe prayed enmyes saȳt iohan whan wente towarde ende ſayd often ladde hȳ child loue togyder charyte ynough ſaluacyon innocentes yonge yt coude ſpeke yet ſhewed loue ſygne dyde laughe playe theyr hōdes whā ſawe knyghtes come wt bryght ſwerdes ſlee thenne ſaynt stephen ſo gloryous martyr god ſhewed many fayr myracles hym ¶narracio ¶there honeſt man vii ſones iii doughters myſſehap vpon daye al wrathed moder one grete angre ſhe curſyd al one anone fylle grete vengeaunce vpon hem came ſuche ſykenes theyr preuy mēbres ſo ſore gnawen myght abyde woo walked vp downe coūtree lyke maſed beſtes people ſawe grete pyte theym thenne happed ſo one brethern hyght poule aſyſter hyght palyda came ye chirche ſaynt stephen herde people tell deuoutly ſaynt stephen prayed enmyes martred hym anone kneled downe prayed ſaynt stephen praye god hem wolde true ſeruauntes kneled downe ye chirche prayenge ſaynt stephen hertly helpe anone felle ſlepe ſyght people ſo hole anone wente brethern ſyſtern holpen ſame wyſe ¶narracio ¶an myracle telleth ſaynt auſtyn ther senatour rome wente ihrlm made fayr chapell ſaȳt stephen deyed buryed ſame chapell thenne longe wyf wolde home coūtree wolde fayne haue huſbōdes bone owne countree prayed byſſhop yt ſhe myght haue thē ye byſſhop brought ſaynt stephen bone huſbondes bone ſayd knowe thy huſbondes fro ſaȳt stephen ſhe ſayd knowe huſbondes bone well ynough toke ſaȳt stephen bone huſbōdes whā ſhe came ferre ye ſee angel ſōge wt grete melody thayer ther paſſȳge ſwete ſauour yt came fro ye bone yt paſſed ony ſpycery ye worlde anone herde fendes crye ye ayer ſayd wo wo v stephen beteth v brenneth v bytterly therwith reyſed grete tēpeſt yt ſhyp men went haue drowned grete fere cryed ſaynt stephen anone ye tempeſt ceſſed ye peple herde ye fendes crye thus thou curſyd prynce mayſter yu may nothynge ſhyp stephen aduerſary therin thenne ye prynce fendes ſent fyue fē de brenne ſhyp thenne goddes angell redy droue fendes ye grounde ſee whā came ye londe ye ſhyp fendes cryed ſayd goddes ſeruaūt cometh ſtoned deth ye iewes thenne worſhyp ſaynt stephen people made chirche layde bone therin god wrought many fayre myracle hym ¶de ſancto iohanne euangeliſta good frēdes ſuche daye ye ſhal haue hye feeſt holy chirche ye feſt ſaȳt iohan euangelyſt whiche goddes owne derlynge wherfore holy chirche maketh mynde mencyon ſpecyalte yt lorde gaf hym afore ony dyſcyples lorde gaf hym grace kepe virgynyte kepynge moder lord ſhewed hȳ preuyte gaf hym grace kepe virgynyte yt may denhode ſtori telleth ye peple haue opynyon whā iohan ſholde wedde mary mawdeleyn cryſt called hȳ came ſewed hym iohan lefte ye worldes vanyte ſewed lorde ſo kepte hȳſelf clene mayden tyll paſſed worlde preuynge whan domycyan themperour rome herde ye peple telle ye iohan preched countree yt called aſia▪ iohan made bylde many chirches whan themperour herde ſēte iohan made hȳ put braſō tōne ful ſethȳge oyle whan iohan longe ſoden therin people wende ben ſoden deed thenne ye emperoure bad open tonne whan tonne open iohan came tonne clene ſynne ſo clene brennynge harme partyes body ¶an harde tourment daye iohan ſawe temple iewes full maw metrye thenne prayed god dyſtroy anone therwith fell downe grounde powder wherfore ariſtodimus byſſhop temple ſo wrothe put iohan pryſon thenne ſayd iohan yet wylt thou ſhall make beleue iheſu cryſte thē ſayd ariſtodimus wyll make venym make two mē drynke afore whan thou ſeeſt deed afore drynke thou therof without harme wyl beleue thy god thenne ſayd iohan go thou haſte ſayd thenne ordeyned byſſhop poyſon fetched ii men pryſon yt dampned drynke poyſon anone deed thenne ſayd iohan yf ye gyue venym drynke ſhall call god thenne iohan toke poyſon blyſſed dranke therof neuer worſe rather ſemed better ye fayrer clene frome ſynne ſo clene fro greuaunce poyſon yet ſayd byſſhop wolde beleue vnto tyme ſe theſe two men areyſed deth lyfe deed thenne iohan keſt owne cote ſayd vade et mitte hanc tunicam ſuꝑ corpus defunctorum go lay cote vpon deed bodyes ſay thus appoſtle iheſu cryſte ſente badde ye ſholde aryſe vp goddes name anone aroſe lyfe agayne thenne byſſhop many conuerted beleued iheſu cryſte iohan cryſtned theym byſſhop ful holy man thus iohan grace kepe hym clene bothe body ſoule thus martyr tofore god withſtandynge ſynne alſo keper moder god lorde iheſu ſawe grete clennes iohan whan lorde ſholde deye dyde ſay iohan ecce mater tua se thy moder toke iohan kepynge moder lorde ſayd moder ecce filius tuus se thy ſone ſo betoke eyther whan lorde deed layde tombe iohan toke lady home hym houſe kepte tyll lorde iheſu cryſte ryſen dethe lyfe agayne whā lorde ſtyed heuen kepte lady ſame chamber longe ſhe lyued thus grace kepynge goddes moder grace knowynge goddes pryuete fyrſte whan lorde ſate ſouper ſherethurſday grete loue iohan vnto lorde iheſu cryſte layde heed cryſtes breſt ſame wyſe man layeth body downe welle drynketh body full water ryght ſoo iohan dranke ſoule full gooſtly wyſdome cryſtes breſte ye ſame tyme lorde ſhewed hym preuyte olde wolde leue preche worde god emperoure exyled iohan hym ſelfe alone yle pathmoſe god ſhewed hym ye appocalypſis worlde daye dome ſawe wrote grete informacyon holy chyrch whan emperour deed iohan called agayne cyte epheſye biſſhop came thyder wydowe hyght druſyana yt deed layde bere thenne iohan ſawe moche people wepe make ſorowe thenne ſayd druſyana aryſe vp make ſome mete anone ſhe roſe went forthe though ſhe hadde ryſen oute ſlepe ¶narracio ¶it happened tyme two yonge men prechynge iohan ſolde al good wente forthe iohan ryche men thenne daye came cyte pargame theyr ſeruauntes lytell well arayed ryche men poore men then̄e temptacyon fende forthought al theyr purpoſe ſory loſte theyr goodes anone reuelacyon god iohan knewe theyr purpoſe theyr hertes ſayd ſe fende tempteth maketh forthynke purpoſe ye ſerue god go ye wood eyther brynge burden ſmall yerdes ſoo dyde thenne thorowe prayer iohan god torned yerdes gold iohan ſayd thus take ye gold ye ryche ye tofore knowe well ye haue loſte kyngdome heuen thenne happed deed man ſame tyme moder hym ſawe iohan ſhe anone fell downe knee prayed hym wolde reyſe ſone lyfe dyde wydowe druſiana thenne prayed iohan god deed man anone aroſe agayne lyfe thenne ſayd hym bydde yt tell theſe two men yu haſt ſeen ioye ordeyned haue loſt man tolde ioye paradyſe paynes purgatory hell ſtronge horryble gloryous ye place ordeyned theym ſorye theyr good aungelles loſte ye gloryous blyſſe heuen moche ioye fendes made tornynge ſame men ſory cryed iohan prayed hym praye god wept ſore iohan ſawe theym wepe prayed god theym gaue penaunce whā done ſo anone golde torned yerdes agayne holy men narracio ¶an holy reuelacyon iohan ſhewed preuyte god happed daye ſawe chylde yt lyke haue ben man wherfore iohan brought hym byſſhop badde hym kepe chylde teche hym tyme comynge ſhall man ſo byſſhop kept hȳ whan came mannes ſtate gaue hym folye felin cōpany theues whyle mayſter thefe leder thenne reuelacyon god iohan knewe well ynough came byſſhop aſked hym chylde byſſhop tolde hym thenne iohan blamed hym ſayd yt myſgouerned chylde thenne iohan olde myght well go toke horſe rode ye theues whan thefe ſawe iohan anone fled awaye iohan rode hym cryed ſayd quid fugis fili mi thou ſone fleeſt thou fro thy fader abide dere ſone ſpeke thy fader olde may well go thenne laſt man abode iohan preched ſo yt left foly ſo holy yt byſſhop thus iohan reuelacyon goddes preuyte ¶narracio ¶it wryten lyfe ſaynt edwarde ye confeſſour ye lyeth weſtmynſter yt ſaynt iohan theuāgelyſt appered hȳ went ꝓceſſyon halowȳge ye chyrche ſaȳt iohan came lyke palmer axed good ſaynt iohās ſake ye kynge loued ſaynt iohan well nothȳg toke rynge fynger gaf hȳ ſo iohan rynge vii yere thenne ſaynt iohan appyred two knyghtes beyōde ſee towardes ihrlem aſked kyng fared bad gyue hȳ ye token toke ye rynge aſke kyng who loue gaf awaye bydde hȳ make hym redy ſhal deye ſoone ſo dyde ¶narracio ¶an fayr reuelacyon whan c wynter olde xvii thenne lorde came hym wt dyſcyples ſayd thus veni dilecte mi quia tēpus eſt vt mea menſa cū fratribus tuis epularis come welbeloued derlynge tyme yu come ete wt thy brethern borde feſt then̄e iohan roſe vp anone wolde haue go forth wt hym then̄e ſayd lorde hym vpon ſondaye thou ſhalt ſondaye paſſynge feble die dominica conuenit ad iohannem vniuerſa multitudo populi ſōdaye came iohan grete multytude people thenne iohan made theym lede hym chirche myght ſpeke ſayd ladde hym thus fide ſitis ſtabiles et mandatis dei feruentes yeſtable ſadde fayth feruent cōmaundementes god thenne ſayd one hem ſay ye thus oft v thenne ſayd yf ye loue togyder parfyght charyte ſtedfaſt fayth ynough ſaluacyon therfore ye ſtable fayth feruent commaundementes god thenne commaunded make hȳ graue awter whā made went thenne came ſuche lyght hym grete whyle yt man myght ſee hym whan lyght gone ye graue full māna welled vp ſonde doth water thus departed worlde ye blyſſe heuen yt neuer ſhall haue ende ¶sanctorum innocencium frendes ſuche day called innocentes day ſome call chylder maſſe daye chyldren ſlayne ye daye cryſtes ſake called innocentes yt ſaye without ſynne dyde ſynne god euer gretely greued ſynne eſpecyall proude people agaynſt theyr neyghbour doynge wronge theſe innocentes dyde neuer ſynne ne cōſented wherfore may well ſay lyued without ſhame deyed without blame cryſtened theyr owne blode home ſome theyr moders armes holy chyrche daye ſyngeth redeth worſhyp theſe innocentes within two yere aege therfore aſhamed theyr owne ſhap defouled maner ſpotte ſynne ſynne yt draught kynde fader adam eue adam eue ſame wyſe paradyſe ſtate innocency naked aſhamed theyr ſhape whyle ſynne whan ſynned ſawe theyr owne ſhape aſhamed therof couerd theyr ſhape leues fygge tree ryght ſo whan ſynne begynneth take rode chyld innocency gooth away fro hym knoweth good frome euyll euylll good leueth good doth euyl ſynneth longer innocent greueth god theſe chyldren lyued ſo longe knowe good euyll ſlayne wtin aege innocēcy wherfore lyued theyr lyfe wtout ſhame blame kynge herode ye kynge iewes made ſle without gylte whan thre kynges came kynge herode ſayd hym vbi eſt q natus eſt rex iudeorum borne kynge iewes badde hym tell thē come worſhyp hym ferre eeſt thenne kynge herode foule aſtonyed theyr wordes axed clerkes chylde ſholde borne ſayd bedleem iude thenne kynge herode tolde ſo badde theym goo thyder worſhyp hym come agayne may go worſhyp hym alſo ſo kynges went thyder worſhypped cryſt whan done theyr offrynge cryſt per aliam viā reuerſi ſunt regionem ſuam way tourned home aūgell badde ſo theyr ſlepe thenne kynge herode wonder wrothe anone ordeyned ſle cryſte whan hadde made redy therto happened ſo ye emperour rome ſent hym come hym al haſt myght two owne ſones accuſed hym emperoure treaſon thenne herode lefte purpoſe cryſte tyme rode rome better ſones came home agayne wt worſhyp thā tofore yet alway thought ſle cryſte leeſt cryſt come mannes eſtate wolde haue put hym kyngdome thenne ſent anone badde theym ſlee chyldren bedleem countree yt within two yere aege borne ſame day ſo dyde kynge herode goynge comynge ſo taryenge ii yeres ſo made ſlee euer within two yere aege ſo vengeable partye fell hymſelfe chylde owne ſlayne amonge ſame tyme came aungell ioſeph ſayd hym accipe puerū et matrē eius fuge ī egiptū take chylde moder fle egypte ſo dyde thus innocentes ſlayne without blame aſhamed theyr owne ſhape cryſtned home theyr owne blode fonte therfore ye ſhall vnderſtande thre maner cryſtenynges one water cryſtned fonte theſe chyldren cryſtned theyr owne blode thouſande martyr moo yt ſhedde theyr blode cryſtes ſake thyrde cryſtnynge ye faythe whiche patryarkes prophetes holy faders incarnacyon lorde iheſu cryſt beleued verely comynge cryſte cryſtned fayth thus may ye ſe enmyte ye kynge herode ſhed ſoo many chyldrens blode cryſtes ſake treſpaced hym none wept many moder theyr chylde yt tyme god wrought full fayre tyraunte ſhewed enmyte fell hym ſelfe pared apple wt ſame knyfe ſlewe hymſelfe thus glad ſhedde blode gyltles therfore laſte ſhed owne blode without mercy euer vengeable oft tymes vengeaunce falleth hymſelfe loueth mercy ſhall haue mercye may preue enſample ¶narracio ¶we fyndein ye lyfe ſaynt sylueſter cōſtantyne ye emperour meſell councell lech gadred iiim chyldrē ſlayne theyr blode put veſſel ſhold bathe hȳ themperour came rydynge chare ye chyldren theyr moders cryed dolefully vnto emperoure made grete lamentacion hym thenne emperoure dyde demaunde folowers woman ye made yt lamentacyon peple 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page worthy ſtande themperour good ſtede nay ſayd thē perour wyll ſo lete euery womā take childe yen home wt ſhall deed thēne wȳmē gladde mery toke childern grete ioye wēte home nyght emperour laye saule purſue cryſte dyſcyples brynge dethe therfore whyle cryſt went erth saule wolde neuer come techȳge ſoone cryſt ſtyed heuen anone saule lerned coude iewes lawe began withſtande gayneſayd cryſtes dyſcyples dyſputynge agaynſt purſued myght full entent haue dyſtroyed cryſten faythe daye dyſputed ſaynt steuen myght ouercome hym bethought hym myght brynge hym dethe ſo lefte hym neuer tyll deed ye maner fendes chyldren whan haue done curſed dede glad therof proude herte encreaſe theyr malyce ſo saule gladde dethe ſaynt steuen wolde haue goten hym name wyckedneſſe paſſynge felowes went yt iewes lawes kepynge gate hym lettre warraunt take yt beleued cryſt brynge iheruſalem put dethe whan theſe letter toke ſuche enuy ther wtin hert ayenſt cryſtē people yt whā herde ony man ſpeke anone grete angre wolde ſneſe noſe frooth mouthe angre grynte tethe thretenynge menacynge towarde cryſten people aferde hym daye herde cyte damaſke moche criſten people hyd drede ſo rode thederwarde anone lorde iheſu criſt ſhewed ſwetenes grace whan saule hye pryde wyll haue done mooſt harme aboute myddaye lorde keſte grete lyght grace aboute hym whiche moche bryghter ſonne lyght ſayd vnto saule maner wyſe saule ſaule quid per ſequeris saule ſaule foloweſt thou anone aferde fell downe hors cryed ſayd grete fere quis e tu dn̄e lorde arte thou ſaid lorde hym ego ſū ieſus nazarenꝰ iheſus nazareth yt ye name manhode ſaule anone byleued hym ſayd lorde wylt thou yt ſhall thenne ſawe people hym lyght herde voys ſawe noo thynge anone wente saule toke hym vp hondes blȳ de myght ſee ſo ladde hȳ cyte good mannes hous thre dayes thre nyghtes faſtynge nother ete dranke ne myght ſee euer prayed god drede vyſyon whiche tyme holy ghooſt taught hym cryſtis lawe thenne thyrde daye one cryſtys dyſcyples hyght ananyas god badde hym came hym full ſore aferde ſayd saule frater dn̄s ieſus miſit ad te qui apparuit tibi via saule lorde hath ſēte iheſus appyered waye thou ſholdeſt ſee cryſtned whan ananyas layde honde vpon heed anone ſaw clerely ther felle eyen lyke ſcales fyſſhes whan hadde cryſtened hym called hym poule thenne ete comforted ſtrenghte fewe dayes ye dyſcyples thenne wente temple preched opēly lorde iheſu cryſte preuynge clerkely yt god man none stupebant enim omnes qui audiebant et dicebant forſothe herde hym aſtonyed ſayd grete myracle grace god ſoden conuerſyon ſo curſyd lyuȳge ſo lytell ſo ſoone torned god man thus may ye grete myracle god ſhewed conuerſyon grete ioye holy chirche maketh defendynge grete ioye cryſten people lytell beſy deſtroye cryſten peple anone redy encreaſe cryſten peple yt ſo beſy gladde ſhed cryſten mēnes blood thenne redy ſhede owne blood beſy went put dethe thenne good wyll redy take dethe theym man durſt preche worde god hym cō forte hym ſpared lorde knyght openly preched worde god taught faythe euery place fore ſo proude ſo fyers ſoone made ſo meke ſo lowly fell grounde euery cryſten mannes fote yt treſpaced mekely beſought theym mercy wt full pacyent herte wherfore ſaynt auſtyn lykeneth hym vnto vnycorne kynde bereth horne browe horne ſleeth beeſtes fyghteth wt alſo ſo fyers hymſelfe may hunter take hym thus wyll begyle hym wyll eſpye vnycorne haunteth vſeth walke wyl ſette mayde ſoone vnycorne ſeeth mayde anone kynde wyll fall downe laye hede lappe thenne myght ſtrength gone thenne come take hym thus ſayth ſaynt poule fyrſt ſo fyers hym ſelfe durſt preche ne ſpeke hym drede whan lorde iheſu cryſt ſhewed ſwetenes grace fayre mayde lawe holy chyrch anone poule fell downe grounde ſubget cryſten people herfore holy chyrche gladde defendynge ſet alſo hye enſample hye amendynge lorde ſoo gracyous cryſten people may ſaued wyll forſake myſſe beleue conuerted multo magi gaudium erit celo ſuper vno peccatore penitenciam agente quam ſuper nonaginta nouem qui non digent penitentia ioye heuen vpon one ſynner repentaunt doynge penaunce vpon xcix dyde neuer committe ſynne therfore mooſt blyſſed lorde wolde al conuerted wherfore hye enſample conforte ſynfull people ſet ſaynt poule loke vpon though man done neuer ſo moche ſyn̄e wolde forſake ſynne ſynne thenne company heuen maketh ioye melody conuercyon erthe conuercyon ſaynt poule moche people loue ſynne wt luſt lykynge worlde loue god many neuer wyll leue ſynne neyther loue god ne deſyre blyſſe heuen fere fende drede paynes hell ſome ſaye ye god wyll neuer leſe hath bought ſo dere paſſyon ſay ſo ben wyſe god wyll none loſte beware thou leſe thy ſelfe whyle thou loueſt ſynne god haddeſt leuer ſerue fende god thou arte cauſe thyn owne dampnacyon whyle thou haſt wyll ſerue fende chylde goddes chylde thou leſeſt thy ſelfe god hath ordeyned fendes tourmente theym euerlaſtynge payne ſaynt gregory ſayeth ſhall dampned begynne theyr penaunce worlde party theyr dethe cōtynueth euermore wherfore tell enſample narracio ¶there man offycer lorde ſtode acurſed tyme rode towarde manoyr lordes fell mynde vnbrydled hors ledde hym manoyr lordes thenne anone ye baylyf pereeyued man dyſtraught mynde anone made people bynde hym poſt berne soo whan baylyf ſouped ſeruauntes badde one ſeruauntes go loke man dyde went man whan came ſawe thre offrynge dayes riche mā lambe poore mā payer turtell douues elles douues ſo offred lady wt ſone woman delyuered mayden chylde ſhe ſholde double al thoſe ſame dayes afore ſayd yt ſay comȳge huſbōde childe doubleth tho dayes bothe tournynge blood alſo ſhappe body ye cauſe eue ye fyrſte fourmed womā yt euer wrathed lorde dyd man adam therfore ſhe ye lenger fourmyng thus freſſhely cōplexyon man womā ſhe vnclene herſelfe therfore puryfycacyon ordeyned vnderſtande well lady none nede clenſynge ſhe conceyued cōplexyon man onely holy gooſt ſo yt ſhe clene maner fylth touchynge cōſente man yet ſhe wente temple woman dyde ſpecyally foure cauſes fyrſt fulfyll ſcrypture yt ſayth thus quāto maior e tāto humilia te hygher yt thou arte degree meker thou ſholdeſt make ye thus dyde lady ſhe wyſt well yt ſhe moder goddes ſone heuen ſoo grete worſhyp paſſynge woman yet ſhe made pooreſt companye ſeconde cauſe ſhe fulfylled ye lawe circūciſyō ſone ye ſame wyſe ſhe fulfylled purificacyō
