cryſt therfore ye fende brake wombe ſhedde guttes thā toke ſoule bare helle lorde ſo ryghtfull gracyous yt wyll euery good dede rewarde euery ſynne punyſſhe yt ye ſhall enſample ¶narracio ¶we fynde ſaynt brendan fayled ſee ſawe iudas ſytte vpon ſtone cloth hangȳge hȳ yt laye ye water oftēbete hȳ ye face thā brendan wēde ſome holy mā yt ſuffred yt grete penaū ce aſked name god anſwered ſayd iudas goddes traytoure haue place goddes grete grace curteyſye refreſſheth grete hete ſuffre within meryte euer dyde deſerue thynketh yt paradyſe whyle ſayd ſaynt brandon haſt thou ſtone vnder wherfore dothe bete face ſayd layde ſtone hye waye comyn people ſholde goo eaſed therby cauſe eaſed therby clothe myne owne refreſſhynge nowe hadde ben myne owne ſholde haue refreſſhed moche gaue vnto poore man ſayd brandon longe haſt thou eaſe refreſſhynge ſayd euery ſaterdaye euenſonge tyll euenſonge morowe done fro criſtinaſſe daye xii daye eeſter daye tyll wytſondaye lady aſſumpcyō candelmaſſe daye brandon thāked god ſo mercy full gracyous thinge anone badde ſayle faſte yt gone ſholde tydynges ſoon euen ther came hylle many fendes caſted many brennyng glemes fyre ſee theym ſee brenned euery ſyde theym god kepte theym ſoo noo harme iudas one xii apoſtles nombre muſt fulfylled cryſt ſtyed vp heuen enleuen apoſtles togyder many people place ſayd peter thus good men brederne well knowen iudas one twelue cauſe nombre maye parfyte nedefull choſe one 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 theſe xii men hath lorde iheſu cryſt fro tyme baptyſed tyme aſcencion bere wytnes v vpryſynge doynge thenne ſette theſe two men ioſeph barſabas mathy keſt lotte ſayd thus lorde thou knoweſt hertes al men ſhewe v whiche thou choyſeſt theſe two men lotte fell mathy ſo nombre xi thenne mathy went myrre preche worde god grace holy gooſt dyde myracles torned moche people fayth cryſt thenne fende ſory appered byſſhop iewes lawe lykenes yonge chylde longe here hore badde hȳ take mathy hym dethe elles wyll torne people cryſten fayth thenne byſſhop nye wode wrathe ſent forthe people ſeke mathye whan hym bounde handes behynde hym keſt rope necke ledde hym pryſon bounde hym faſt chaynes iren thenne nyght lorde iheſu cryſte came hȳ grete lyght loſed handes whan well conforted hȳ opened pryſon dore badde hym preche faythe ſpare man thenne preched ſome withſtode hym letted wolde haue torned faythe thenne ſayd mathy theym tell ſhall fall downe pytte helle ſoo anone ſyght men erthe opened fell downe pytte hell body ſoule neuer ſeen noo theym thenne people ſore agaſt ſyght torned fayth grete nombre thenne whan byſſhop herde therof toke hym bounde hym ſent men throwe ſtones hym whan nye deed badde cryſten people take ſtones ſtooned graue hym wytnes martyrdome kneled downe helde vp handes god ſayd lorde beſeche take ſpyryte gaue vp gooſt ¶reynolde cheſter cronycles telleth myracle lyke ſayth whan ſaynt wolſtone vyſyted byſſhopryche people brought man hym dyde neyghbours moche dyſeaſe wolde neuer pea prayenge byſſhop chaſtyſe hym whā byſſhop preched euer ye lenger worſe byſſhop people prayed ſaynt mathy ſhewe ſome myracle man worthy haue anone ſyght people came erthe two fendes brennynge hokes pulled man quycke downe hell whan gone people releued reſt pea euer ¶de annunciatione marie virginis worſhypfull frendes ſuche daye ye ſhal haue hye ſolempne feeſt holy chyrch annuncyacyon lady hath auowed ioyned penaūce muſt faſt euyn ye ſhall vnderſtonde called ye annū cyacyon cauſe fader heuen ſent aungell gabryell miſſus eſt angelus gabriell deo ciuitate cui nomen nazareth cyte called nazareth lady newe wedded ye byddynge god reuelacyon holy gooſt man called ioſeph ſhe chambre prayer ye aungell gabryell came ſayd oure lorde ye ſhe gretely aſtonyed gretynge countre man coude moche wytchecraft ſo helpe fendes made hymſelf lyke aungell came dyuers maydens ſayd ſent frome god meſſage ſo oft tymes laye dyde grete velony whan lady herde tell man ſhe adradde leſt ſhe ſpoke none aungell noo ſuche wordes ne ſuche gretynge made neuer none thenne gabryell aungell conforted ſayd ne time maria īueniſti graciā apud dn̄m drede mary forſothe thou haſt founde grace lorde amonge woman lorde hath choſen moder ſone hym thou ſhalte conceyue fayth loue holy gooſt without ony deed man ſhall ſhadowe quenche fleſſhely luſt lyght lyght gooſtly loue yu ſhall conceyue ſone hygh god thenne anone lady herde theſe wordes anone came ſpyrytuell ſwetnes ioye hert anone ony erthely man coude tell ſo reuerence mekenes ſhe coude ſhe anſwered thus agayne ſayd ecce ancilla dn̄i fiat michi ſcdm verbū tuū lo goddes owne mayde redy goddes wyll prayenge may ryght thou ſayſt thus blyſſed body cōceyued lorde iheſu cryſt euerlaſtynge ioye al ye worlde thus may lyken lady precyous ſtone called onyx clere ony cryſtall ſhal kynde whan ye ſonne ſhyneth hote openeth receyueth droppe dewe heuen cloſeth agayne tyll ix monethes openeth falleth ſtone ye ſame kynde ſo cloſeth agayne cloſe euer neuer openeth thus lady clene oni criſtall hote loue holy ghooſt ix monethes ende ſhe delyuered ſone lorde iheſu cryſte clene mayden ſhe tofore thenne whan angell hadde doone meſſage went way heuen lady went coſyn elyzabeth whiche grete chylde ſaynt iohan baptyſt whan ſhe came elyzabeth ſhe grette mekely ſoone lady ſpake elyzabeth childe elyzabeths wombe played made grete ioye ſawe lorde hadde taken mankynde come ſaue loſte thenne lady dwelled elyzabeth coſyn tyll tyme ſaynt iohan borne mydwyfe elyzabeth toke ſaynt iohan erthe ſhe lerned ſhe neded knowe agaynſt tyme lorde ſholde borne perfyte ynough therof thenne mekely ſhe toke leue went home agayne nazareth thenne thought ioſeph wolde goo loke wyfe dyde went warde whan lady herde comynge ſhe went mete hym grette hym full mekely whan ioſeph ſawe grete chylde meruayled gretely myght well wyſte hadde neuer parte body degree knewe well ſhe hadde made vowe ſhe wolde neuer haue parte mannes bodye thought made wedde ye commaundement holy gooſt grete myracle ſhewynge thought ryght herte worthy dwell company thought herte haue goone home agayne leue thenne came aungell vnto hym ſayd aferde take marye thy wyfe thy kepynge holy gooſt quycke wombe thou ſhalte keper nouryſſher vnto chylde whan borne call iheſus ſhall ſauyoure worlde thenne ye ſhall vnderſtande four cauſes ſaynt ambroſe ſayth lady wedded olde man ioſeph fyrſt yf ſhe cōceyued without wedlocke ye iewes wolde haue ſayd ſhe euyll woman body ſo haue ſtoned deth ſeconde cauſe ſhe ſo ſhamefaſt ſhe herde ony haue put ony defame ſhe wolde haue deyed ſorowe thyrde cauſe ye ioſeph ſholde bere wytneſſe maydenhode fourth cauſe ioſeph ſholde helpe byrthe brynge bethleem egypt ſo ayen owne countree thyſe iiii cauſes ſhe wedded olde man ioſeph alſo begyle fende ſholde knowe hȳ fro childe haue ye herde annuncyacyon ſome people aſke queſtyon ſtandeth wyne potte lylyes bytwene lady gabryell angell ſalutacyon cauſe lady ſalutacyon conceyued fayth ¶narracio ¶it befelle thus vpon cryſtmaſſe daye yt cryſten man iewe ſat togyder ſpake concepcyon lady ſtode wyne potte tofore theym lylye therin thenne ſayd cryſten man byleue lady conceyued lyke lylye conceyued colour grene bryngeth forthe whyte floure without crafte man ony peyrynge ſtalke ryght ſo lady conceyued holy ghoſt brought ſone lorde iheſu cryſt without ony wēme body floure chyef wymmen thenne ſayd iewe whan ſee lylye ſprynge deed ſtalke ſtandeth potte thenne wyll byleue yu ſayſt true anone therwith ſprange whyte lylye deed ſtocke ſtode ſame wyne potte whan ye iewe ſawe ye anone felle downe ye groūde vpon knee ſayd thus lady ſee well thou conceyued holy ghooſt lorde iheſu cryſt goddes ſone heuen thou clene mayden byrthe alſo byrthe ſo anone cryſtened ſo full holy man cauſe wherfor potte lylye ſette bytwene lady angell ryghte iewe dyſputed cryſten man maner concepcyon oure bleſſyd lady lady dyſputed wyth angell maner ſhe ſholde conceyue moder mayde ſhe conſented therto ¶then̄e ye yt wyll faſte fyue euens lady worſhyppe v ioyes yt ſhe ſone fyrſt whan ſhe conceyued holy goſte knew yt ſhe moder goddis ſone heuen ſecōde cryſtmaſſe daye whā ſhe delyuered ſone withoute ony payne body ſhe conceyued withoute luſte body alſo delyuerd withoute payne bodye iii ioye eſter daye whan ſone roſe deth lyfe came kyſſed made ioyefull vpryſyng ſhe ſory deth iiii ioye whan ſtyed vp heuen holy thurſday ſame fleſſhe blode toke body v ioye aſſumpcion whan ſhe ſawe ſone come wyth greate multytude angellys ſaȳtes fetche heuen crowne quene heuen empreſſe helle lady worlde ſo yt ben heuen ſhall doo reuerence worſhyp yt ben erthe ſhall ſeruyce ¶thyſe ben fyue ioyes yt oure lady ſone ye ſhall vnderſtonde yt yt wyll greete oure lady fyue auees ſhall neuer come paynes helle ¶narracio ¶we fynde wryten holy maydē deuoute ladyes ſeruyce euery daye greted wt fyue ioyes thenne happed ſo daye ye ſhe fell ſeke felte ſelfe well yt ſhe ſholde dede fere ſhe ſyghed wonder ſore made greate mone bycauſe ſhe wyſte wheder ſhe ſholde goo deth came oure lady ſayd arte yu ſo ſory yt haſte made ſo glad gretȳg wyth ioyes ſone therfore ſory knowe wel thou ſhalte goo euerlaſtyng blyſſe ioye withoute ende ¶narracio ¶we fynde ſaynt gylberte tyme nye dede quynty whan throte ſo grete well nye dede yt myghte take breth lady came hym ſayde gylberte ſeruaunt euyll yt thy throte ſholde ſuffre penaūce ſo oft tymes gladed ioyes anone ſhe toke fayre pappe mylked throte wente waye anone therwith hole thanked oure lady euer de ſancto georgio martyre gode frendis ſuche day ye ſhal haue ſaȳte georgis daye ye holy martyr wryten lyfe yt horryble dragō beſyde cyte called cyrme ye whiche dragon men ye cyte ſore aferde ſo moche yt coūſeyle ye kynge euery daye gaaf hȳ chyld ſheep ete fere leeſt wolde haue come ye cyte whā ye chyldren ye ſhepe nye ete cauſe yt kȳge himſelf gaaf thē ye ſame coūſeyle cōſtreyned hȳ one doughter gyue ye dragō ye kȳge fere ye peple wt wepȳge grete ſorowe makȳg delyuered thē chyld ſent forth place wont ſet theyre owne chyldren ſhepe wt abyde tyl ye dragō come ye ordenaūce god ſaȳ te george came rydynge yt way whā ſawe damoyſel ī araye hȳ thoughte ſhe womā greate byrth aſked ſhe ſtode wyth ye ſhepe ſuche aray ſo mornȳge anſwered ſhe ſayd gētyll knyghte well maye morne make ſorowe kȳges doughter cyte ſet deuoured dragō yt hath ete ye childeren cyte dyſtroyed muſt haue fader gaaf thē coūſel ther therfore gentyll knyghte ryde hen ſaue thy ſelfe leeſt ye dragō ſlee bothe ye ſayd george damoyſell yt greate ſhame vylony yt knyght well arayed ſholde flee yu woman ſholdeſte abyde wyth yt dragō put oute hede hole ſpytted fyre profered batayle george anone george made ſygne ye croſſe hȳ ſet ſpere ye reſte greate myght bare downe dragon grounde thēne bad damoyſell bynde dragon gyrdell aboute necke lede cyte ſoo dragon folowed hadde hoūde made bow pacyently whan peple cyte ſawe dragon come fledde fere waye thenne george called people agayne ſayd aferd ye wyll byleue cryſt take cryſtendome wyll ſaue ſlee dragon delyuer youre enmye thenne ſo glad anone xxm men without wymen chyldren cryſtned kynge quene fyrſte theyr houſholde thenne george ſlewe dragon bad people tey ox hym drawe cyte ſauoure dyde ye peple harme george bad ye kȳge edyfy chyrches euery corner lōde luſty goddis ſeruyce honoure worſhyp people holy chyrche euer haue compaſſyon ſory poore ony dyſeaſe whan george done thus torned londe cryſten faythe herde emperour hyght dyocleſyan dyde many cryſten men dethe thenne went hym rebuked hym curſed dedes thenne themperoure anone cōmaunded put george anone pryſon lay hym vpryght laye myll ſtone vpon breſt preſſe hym dethe thenne george prayed god helpe lady kepte hym harme ne parte body whan themperoure herde therof dyde take two wheles put full hokes george ſet myddes bytwene two wheles torned ſo raſe fleſſhe fro bone whan george tourment anone prayed god ſocoure helpe anone holpen thenne put hym hote lyme kyl cloſed hym therin ſholde haue brent anone lorde torned colde thre dayes thenne wende haue founde hym brent ſaufe frome maner harme mery thenne brought forthe ſette emperoure george repreued hym falſe goddes ſayd hym fendes without myght power themperour made bete mouth ſtones tyll powned made bete bare body drye brome tyll fleſſhe fell bone people myght ſe guttes yet made hym drynke venymme made ſtrong none haue pyned hym dethe whan george made ſygne croſſe dranke poyſon without grefe ſo moche man yt made poyſon torned cryſten faythe anone doone dethe thenne ye nyght george pryſon god came hym ſayd george good comforte morowe thou ſhalt make ende come euerlaſtynge ioye blyſſe ſet croune heed gaue hym blyſſynge thenne morowe wolde worſhyp falſe goddes themperour made ſmyte heed themperour wolde haue gone palays came fyre lyghtnynge brent hym people ¶we fynde ſtorye anthyoche wryten beſyde iheruſalem fayre yonge knyght appered preeſt ſayd ſaynt george leder cryſten people commaunded ye preeſt ſholde bere hym relyckes come hȳ iheruſalem whan came walles yt people therin ſo ſtronge cryſten durſt come walles· came ſaynt george clothed whyte made croſſe breſte went vpon ladder badde cryſten people come hym ſo helpe ſaynt george gate cyte iheruſalem ſlewe hethen people foūde therfore lete v praye ſaynte george helpe v agaynſt gooſtly ennemye amen ¶de ſanto marco euangeliſta reuerent frendes ſuche daye ye ſhal haue ſaynt markes daye one foure euangelyſtes wrote cryſtes goſpelles preched people thenne marke fyrſt hethen man cryſtened ſaynt peter made hym go preche people goddes worde thenne ſo holy man people wolde haue hym preeſt ſo meke hymſelfe made one thombes cut thouȝt worthy preeſt fot god wolde haue ſo ſaynt peter grete inſtaunce made hym take thorder preeſthode vpon hym thenne beſy bothe daye nyght preche worde god yt ſayd wt worde confermed good enſample doynge grete myracles thus thynſpyracyon ye holy gooſt went cyte alyſauner toure people faythe whan came cyte vneth entred cyte ſho brake thereby wyſt well yt ſholde deed ſawe man ſyt cloute ſhone poore people marke prayed hym amende ſho thenne man poore thought almeſſe helpe hym ye tyme toke ſho began ſewe anone wt nall hurte hande payne ache ſayd god helpe whan marke herde called god anone marke prayed god hym thenne marke ſpytted erthe blyſſed anoynted hande therwith ſayd noīe patris ieſu xp̄i filii dei viui ſanet manꝰ tua name fader iheſu cryſt ye ſone quycke god thy honde hole vocabit aūt hō ille ananias forſothe ye man called anania whan anania ſawe ſuche vertue marke prayed hym dwell ſtyll wt hym cōmoratiſ que ibidē duobus annis dwelled two yeres cryſtened hym houſholde grete holynes marke ſawe hym made hym archebyſſhop ¶thenne people ſawe marke preched cyte toke tyed rope necke drewe hym amonge ſtones tyll fleſſhe fell erthe ſayd drawe bugle bugle place whan drawen nye dethe thenne put hym pryſon tyll morowe thenne ſame nyght cryſte came hym pryſon ſayd pea marke myn euangelyſt aferde wt thenne morowe came fet hȳ pryſon drewe hym tyll deed whan ſholde deye ſayd manꝰ tuas dn̄e ſo gaue vp gooſt afterwarde wolde brenne body thenne came ſuche erthe quaue wt thondrȳ ge durſt man abyde thenne nyght cryſten people came toke markes body buryed thenne fell ſoo euery cryſten londe halowed ſaynt markes daye ſaufe one countre called appolonia whiche countre ſo greued wt hete drought yt coūtree fayled fruyte ſo well nye famyſſhed came voyce frome heuen badde halowe ſaynt markes daye ſholde comforted dyde ſoo anone god ſent plente maner fruytes wyte ſholde faſt daye go proceſſyon ¶we rede cyte rome fell ſuche qualme ſodayne dethe whā man yaned gaped ſneſed anone deyed deyed many ſodaynly thenne pope called pellagius yt commaunded cryſten people yt whan yaned euery man ſholde make croſſe ouer mouthe whan ony man herde man ſneſe ſholde ſay cryſt helpe ſo many ſaued made people go proceſſyon ſo prayenge ſayntes heuen pray god ſo dyde thenne came ſaynt gregory made ſame ſaynt markes daye halow faſt go proceſſyon canonyſed doone euermore thenne came pope whiche called liberius tyme maner fruytes tyme yere grete tenderneſſe ſelfe toke grete harme ſoo tempeſt thonder lyghtnynge vnkynde hetes ſtormes myldewes wormes longe tayled flyes grete vengeaunce punyſſhement ye anone eeſter daye people torned agayne theyr olde ſynner hauynge rewarde ſacramente whyche haue receyued therfore god ſente vengaunce tyme ony tyme yere wherfore holy pope put awaye alle thyſe thynges eſpecyall goddis wreche fro ye peple cōmaunded al cryſten people halowe faſt go proceſſyon ſayd made conſtytucy •• acurſed tylle come amendemente ¶and therfore charge counſeyll thynke ſaued kepe daye ye rule holy chyrche ¶in die philipi et iacobi apoſtolo rum good frendis ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ye feſte phylip iacob ye whiche holy apoſtles feſte cometh wyth feſte eſter ye ſhall faſt euen ye ſhall come chyrche worſhyp god holy apoſtles ¶then ye ſhall knowe well ye phylyp ordeyned apoſtles goo ye countrey called sytha preche ye vnbyleued peple whan came thyder preched ayenſte ye mawmentis yt fendis goddis ſoo toke hym ladde hȳ temple wolde haue conſtreyned hym doo ſacrefyce ¶then beſy doo hym dyſeaſe ſodenly greate dragon came oute ye erth ſlewe thre thyſe myſbyleued peple venemed ye peple ſoo wyth brethynge yt fell thē ſuche ſekeneſſe yt woo ye ſorow yt cryed helpe ſayde phylyp thē yf ye wold holpen heled ſekenes alſo thyſe men rered deth lyfe fyrſte caſte downe ye mawmentis ſette theyr ſtede croſſes oure lorde deyed vpon worſhyppe dyd ſoo glad holpē theyr ſekenes ſoone ſoo holpen thenne phylyp prayed god theſe thre men reyſe dethe lyfe tunc precepit philip pu draconi vt locū ſuum redeſcenderet thenne phylyp commaunded dragon go downe place ayen neuer dyſeaſe man thenne curſed people cyte ſawe phylyp wolde haue torned people toke hym dyde hym croſſe ſo croſſe deyed went euerlaſtynge blyſſe amen ¶of ſaynt iames ye ſhall iacob called amonge ye appoſtles iacobus minor leſſe iames knowe hȳ iacobus maior iames ſaynt iohan euangelyſtes broder whan iacobus iames yt one name called cryſtes owne broder ſo moche lyke cryſt whan iewes wolde haue taken cryſt coude knowe one fro iudas betrayed cryſt kyſſynge whiche knowen taken iames ſo holy fro tyme borne yt longe lyued neuer dranke wyne ale ſyder ne bere maner drynke yt myght make man dronke ne neuer ete fleſſhe ne heed neuer ſhauen ne neuer vſed bawmed oyle maner countre hete ſonne ware neuer lynnen clothe lay knee prayenge ye people yt knee ſo thycke bollen lyke camell ye fyrſt man yt euer ſonge maſſe veſtymentes preeſtes thenne fell ſo ye tyme iheruſalem ye dede cryſtes dethe yt muſt nedes dyſtroyed wherfore holy man iames made byſſhop ielrm left preche torne ye people better lyuynge cōbred ſo wt ſynne yt grace amendement nedes prophecye cryſt muſt fulfylled cyte dyſtroyed wherfore theſe men toke ſaynt iames ſette hym hye place prayenge hym preche fayth cryſte moch people torned cryſt ſtode vp preched good reaſon beleued cryſte ſholde dāpned ye day dome hell mayſter iewes bad caſt hym downe fro ye hye place yt ſtode ſtones bet hym downe tyll deed thenne kneled downe prayenge god forgyue dethe therwith curſed man ſmote hym heed yt brayne fell ſo wyſe gaue vp gooſt thenne vengeaunce cryſtes deth holy mannes dethe cyte ierlm yt tyme ye greteſt cyte worlde neuer lyke haue wonne ſoone dyſtroyed vttermooſt ſo moche yt ye ſtones walles cyte torned vp ſo downe lyke lorde ſayd xl wynter ſholde ſo iewes dryuen dyuers countrees ſo moche al kyngdomes dyſtroyed yet ben vnder kynges euer ſhall ſubgettes poſſeſſyoners yet ſhall ye dyſtruccyon iheruſalem ſhewe vengeable god theym yt glad ſhede cryſten mennes blode whan god wolde haue taken vengeaunce cyte ¶it happed ſo man pylates whiche dyde cryſt dethe came iheruſalem towarde rome tempeſt yt ſee toke hym droue hym vpon londe temple wt grete tempeſt dwelled grete lorde called vaſpaſyan cauſe called ſo maladye noſethrylles dropped oute noſe wormes lyke waſpes thenne ſayd vaſpaſyan mā fro countre comeſt thou anſwered hym ſayd frome iheruſalem wolde go towarde rome then̄e ſayd vaſpaſyan gladde therof haue herde ſay many good lech countre wherfore wolde well yu coude heel yf thou heel yu ſhalte deed thenne anſwered ſayd noo leche ſelfe yt heleth ſeke reyſeth deed lyfe may helpe yt yf wyll ſayd vaſpaſyan syr ſayd iheſus nazareth iewes haue ſlayne yf thou wylte beleue hym thou ſhalte haue yt thou wylte deſyre behole thenne ſayd vaſpaſyan beleue verely thou ſayſt may hele reyſeth men dethe lyfe anone hole thenne anone ſent man themperoure rome gate lycence leue dyſtroye cyte iheruſalem gadred grete multytude people tytus owne ſone hym went iheruſalem thenne meane whyle beſyeged cyte themperour deyed thenne choſen emperoure torned agayne rome left tytus ſone dyſtroye cyte tytus laye ſo ſore cyte enfamyſſhed ſo moche ete theyr ſhone theyr botes fader toke mete ſone ſone fader eyther toke others mouthe huſbande frome wyfe wyfe frome huſbande thenne amonge woman grete byrthe comen gentyll blode ſhe hadde yonge chylde hunger ſhe ſayd dere chylde haue ſuffred payne euer thou dydeſt wherfore good reaſon eaſe aledge honger y• ſholde famyſſhed honger thou alſo wt ſhe toke chylde ſlewe roſted one halfe halfe ſhe kepte tyll morowe ſoo fleſſhe roſted ſauoure wente cyte whan people felt ye ſmell wende plente mete came haue parte thys womā wolde haue hydde ſayde wolde ſee mete ſhe ſhe broughte forth ſhewed ſayde loo haue roſted myne owne chylde ye halfe ayenſt morowe people ſore greued ſyghte went forth leuynge ye woman etynge chylde ¶thenne hunger encreaſed ſo gretely yt dyed ye cyte ſoo thycke yt caſte ye bodyes ouer walles ye cyte ye dyches ſoo fylled ye dyches full dede bodyes ſtenche ſmote forth ye coūtrey enfected peple greatly ſo ye laſt grete nede made thē yelde vp ye cyte ¶then tytus wente wyth hooſt ryght iewes ſolde cryſte xxx pen ſoo ſolde xxx iewes peny thā tourned ye cyte vp ſoo downe ſo moche yt lefte ſtone ſtondȳge vpon nother deſtroyed ye vttermoſt parte lo thus maye ye ſee thoughe god almyghty abyde ſuffre longe ſmyteth ſore laſte taketh greate vēgaū ce theym luſty ſhedde cryſten mennys blood wherfore euery cryſten man woman amende hymſelf praȳg holy apoſtell medyatoure bytwene god maye haue repentaunce theyr hertes ſhryfte mouthe ſatyſfaccyon dede doynge maye come blyſſe neuer ſhall haue endynge ¶amen ¶de inuencione ſancte crucis gode frendis ſuche daye ye ſhall haue inuēcyon ye holy croſſe ye ſhal faſte ye euȳ come god holy chyrche cryſten peple ſholde doo worſhyppe hȳ deyed croſſe thenne ye ſhall vnderſtonde called inuencio ſancte crucis fyndynge croſſe whyche foūde wyſe ſhall tell whā adam fyrſt fader ſeke age wolde fayne haue oute worlde adam ſent seth ſone ye angell kepar paradyſe prayenge āgell ſende hȳ oyle mercy anoynte body therwith whan dede went seth paradyſe ſayd meſſage angell thenne anſwered āgell ſayde yt myght haue tyll yeres fulfylled haue braū che tree thy fader ſȳned ſet graue whā bereth frute ſhall haue mercy erſte ¶thenne toke ſeth braūche come home fonde fader dede ſet braunche faders graue thāgell badde hȳ whyche braūche growed tyl salomon kynge made fell downe fayre werke tēple wolde corde werke tēple salomō made caſte downe therth hyd tyme ſhat byſſhop temple lete make wayre ſame place tree laye weſſhe ſhepe offred tēple whan wayre made called theyr lā gage probatica piſcina yt whyche water came aū gel certeyne tymes fro heuen dyde worſhyp tree yt laye groūde wayre meued water man womā yt came water nexte āgell made hole ſeknes yt euer vertue tree ſoo endurede many wynters tyme cryſt taken ſhold done croſſe ¶thenne tree ordenaunce god ſwam̄e vpon water whan iewes none tree redy make croſſe grete haſte toke ſame tree made therof croſſe ſo dyde oure lorde theron thē ne tree bare bleſſyd frute cryſtes body whiche welleth oyle mercy adam eue theyr ofſprynge whan cryſt dede take downe ye croſſe enuye yt iewes hadde hym toke croſſe two croſſes yt theues hanged eyther ſyde cryſt beryed depe erthe cryſtē peple ſhold wyte done doo worſhyp laye yere ye tyme elyn thēperours moder conſtātyne gadred grete people fyghte maxencius grete water ouer whyche water laye grete brygge dyſceyte conſtantyne maxencius lete make trappe hopynge haue dyſceyued conſtantyne yt ſholde haue fallen water ¶and coſtātyne lay bed ſore aferde maxencius moche bygger peple came hȳ angell wyth ſygne ye croſſe ſhynȳg golde ſayd hym morow whan yu goſte batayle take ſygne thy honde vertue therof yu ſhalt haue victory thenne cōſtantyne wonder glad anone lete make croſſe tree bere tofore hym batayle whan maxencius ſawe nye yt brygge ſo fyers hymſelfe forgete trappe whiche made himſelf ſo came brygge fell downe ye water trappe drowned thenne ooſt wonder feyne yelde thē conſtantyne good wyll thenne cōſtantyne yet criſtened alſo heled leperhode anon coūſeyle pope ſente moder quene eleyne quene iheruſalē prayed go ſeke ye croſſe criſt deyed thys eleyne kynges doughter englonde emperoure rome wedded beaute ſo ſhe made empreſſe rome hubondes deth ſhe kyngdome iheruſalem wry ſhe made gader ye iewes myght founde ſayd yf wold ſhewe croſſe ſholde brente thenne one hyght iudas ſayde knewe beſt ye croſſe thenne ſayde eleyne hym si vi viuere oſtende michi lignū crucis yf thou wylt lyue ſhew ye croſſe god deyed vpon elles thou ſhalt brēt ſo put greate diſtreſſe thenne ſawe muſt nedes telle deye ſayd beſeche lede mounte caluary ſhal byd ſhall ſhewe croſſe cryſte blynde myghte ſee ſo whan brought mon̄t caluary kneled downe prayed lōge whā prayed place croſſe meued erthe quoke came ſwete ſauoure fro place croſſe lay yt ſwete ony ſpycery worlde thēne dygged longe laſt fonde thre croſſes wyſt whiche cryſtes croſſe thother two thenne toke dede body layd one croſſe thenne ye whan came criſtes croſſe anone body roſe lyf thanked god thenne ſayd iudas thou arte cryſte truly ſauyoure world yt iudas cryſtened holy man thenne toke eleyne parte croſſe ſent rome ſone remenaūt therof ſhe made ſhryne ſyluer golde left iheruſalem worſhyp ſhe coude thus holy chirche maketh mynde daye holy croſſe founde ¶thēne rede fynde cyte called byrectus cryſten man hyred hous iewe dwell ¶then man rode whiche nychodemus made mynde cryſte thenne toke rode ſette priuy place hous ſyghte iewes dyde worſhyppe honour connynge thenne fell ſo man went another hous happed leue rode behynde hym vnwetynge thenne came iewe dwelled hous cryſten man hadde dwelled thenne make hym good chere neyghboures came nyght ſouped wt hym ſate ſouper ſpake cryſten man dwelled iewe loked beſyde hȳ corner ſawe rode whan ſawe anone began grynde wt tethe chyde iewe neyghboure ſayd yu arte torned cryſten fayth haſt rode dooſt worſhyp pryuely iewe ſware nay depe coude ſo ne neuer ſawe ye tyme yet notwithſtandynge iewe went tolde neyghboures ſayd man preuy cryſten man rode pryuely hous thenne anone came neyghboures woode wrathe bet man drewe hym tugged hym worſte maner coude ſo laſt ſayd theymage yu beleueſt vpon toke ymage bete ſcourged crowned thornes laſt made ſtrengeſt theym take ſpere wt myght ſmyte herte anone therwith blode water ranne ſydes then̄e ſore aferde therof ſayd take pottes fyl blode bere temple ſeke people dyuers maladyes anoynt theym therwith yf yt hole blode thenne crye god mercy anone lete v cryſtened man woman thenne anoynted ſeke people ye ſayd blode anone hole thenne wente theſe iewes vnto byſſhop cyte tolde hym caſe anone kneled doune knee thanked god fayre myracle whan cryſtned iewes vyoles glaſſe cryſtall aumber put blood ſent diuerſe chyrches blood many men vnderſtōde came blood hayles mylytes tellyth hys cronycles yt many yeres yt iheruſalē dyſtroyed iewes wolde haue buylded ayene wente thyderwardes erly mornȳge fonde many croſſes waye aferde therof tourned homewarde ayene yet ye morowe came ayene ye croſſes full blood fled homwardes agayne eche one yette wolde leue therby ayene yt iii daye thē fyre roſe therth brēt thē euerychone aſſhes ¶deſctō iohanne ante portā latinā frendis ſuch day ye ſhal haue ſaynt iohans daye porte latyn daye called ſoo happed day holy ſaȳte preched worde god cyte yt called epheſye ye iuſtyce ye cyte ſawe yt tourned moche people ye byleue cryſt wold haue hȳ ſacrefyce falſe goddis wolde rather leſe lyfe then̄e ye iuſtyce lete take hȳ cōmaunded hȳ ſette pryſon whyle ſente ye emperour rome knowe ſholde doo hȳ ſoo letter came ye emperour ye whiche letter called iohā ye worſt yt coude ſayde falſe deceyuer ye peple ¶then wrote thēperour ayene ye iuſtyce bad ſholde ſende iohan ayene hȳ rome ſo dyde themperour appoſed hȳ dedes whan iohan ſtoode ſtedfaſte fayth grete ſcorne ye ēperoure made clyppe ſome iohannys hys hede fayre hede whā ſo clypped ye peple lough hȳ ſcorne ſo dyde hȳ greate dyſeaſe lad hȳ gate ye towne rome whyche called porte latine put hȳ tonne hote feruēte oyle cloſed hȳ therin put vnder fyre haue brente hym therin goddis owne derlȳge kepte hȳ ſoo yt noo harme noo parte body whan yt peple wente yt hadde dede vncloſed ye tonne founde hym hole ſoūde ꝑtyes body clothis thȳg touched hym therfore cryſten peple lete make chirche ye worſhyppe god martyrdome yt ſuffred thēperoure myghte ouercome hym noo way martyrdome penaūce exyled yle yt called pathmos herde ſaȳte iohānys moder ſone ſent rome dede grete ſorowe cōpaſſyon ſhe wente rome whā ſhe herde yt exyled ſhe tourned agayne wēte homwarde ſo whan ſhe came cyte yt called vetulā ſhe fell ſeke deyed ſhe buryed beſyde cyte roche whā ſhe layne many yeres ſaynte iames ſone came thyder toke vp moders body ſmellyd ſwete ony ſpicery broughte ye cyte beryed greate worſhyp honoure amen ¶de feſto ſancti iohannis baptiſte good frendis ſuche daye ye ſhall haue hye feeſt holy yt called ſaȳte iohānys day ye baptyſt called ſo baptyſed cryſte ye water flome iordā wherfore ye ſhall faſte ye euyn ye ſhall vnderſtōde knowe howe ye euyns fyrſt foūde olde tyme ye begȳnyng holy chirche ſo ye peple came chirche wt cā dellys brennynge wold wake come lyghte towarde nyghte chyrche theyr deuocyons fell lecherye ſonges daūſes harpynge pypynge alſo glotonye ſynne ſo torned holyneſſe curſedneſſe wherfore holy faders ordeyned people leue wakȳ ge faſte ye euen thꝰ torned ye wakynge faſtynge called vigilia wakynge englyſſhe called euen ye euen wōte come chirche worſhyppe ſaynte iohan people waked home made iii maner fyres one clene bone noo woode called bone fyre nother clene wode bone called wode fyre peple ſyt wake therby iii made wode bone called ſaynt iohannis fyre fyrſt fyre greate clerke iohan belleth telleth certayne coūtrey ſo coūtrey ſoo greate hete whiche cauſed dragon go togyder tokenynge yt iohan deyed brennynge loue charyte god mā deye charyte ſhall haue parte gode prayer ſhal neuer ſaued dragon flewe thayre ſhed water froth kynde ſoo enuenymed water cauſed moche people take theyr deth therby many dyuerſe ſekeneſſe tyme many greate clerkes rad kyng alyſaunder tyme ſholde haue batayle ye kynge iude kynge inde broughte hym many olyphauntis berynge caſtellis tree theyr backes kynde thē haue armed knyghtes ye caſtell batayle ne knewe alyſaundre kynge olyphauntes drad thynge iarrynge ſwyne wherfore made gader gyder ye ſwyne myghte begoten cauſed dryuen ny olyphauntes myghte well iarrynge ſwyne thenne made pygge crye whan ſwyne herde pygges none made grete iarrynge ſoone olyphauntes herde began fle eche one keſte downe caſtelles ſlewe knyghtes meane alexander ye vyctory alſo theſe wyſe clerkes knoweth well dragō hate nothynge ſtenche brennynge bone therfore gadered many myghte fynde brent thē ſo ſtenche therof droue away dragon ſo brought grete dyſeaſe ¶the ſeconde fyre made wood yt wyll bren̄e lyght wyl ſeen ferre chefe fyre ſeen ferre tokenynge yt ſaynt iohan lanterne lyght people alſo people made blaſes fyre ſholde ſeen ferre ſpecyally nyght iheremye prophete many yere iohan borne prophecyed ſpake thus goddes mouthe ſayd prius quam te formaui ī vtero noui te yu formed thy moders wombe knewe et ante quam exires de vulua ſcti ficauite thou yedeſt thy moders wombe halowed et prophetā gentibus dedite gaue prophete people thenne ſaynt iohan ſholde holy borne god ſent angell gabryell zachary ſaynt iohans fader dyde ſacrefyce ſtede abya byſſhop temple prayed god haue chylde bothe wyfe barayne olde thenne ſayd thaungell zachary ne time zacharia drede zachary god hath herde thy prayer elyzabeth vxor tua pariet filium vocabitur nomē eius iohānes elyzabeth thy wyfe ſhall haue chylde name ſhall iohan ſhall fulfylled holy gooſt et multi natiuitate eius gaudebunt many ſhall ioye byrthe hym· thenne zacharye olde prayed haue token beheſte thenne ſayd aungell hym ſholde dombe tyll chylde borne ſoo thenne conceyued elyzabeth whan ſhe quycke wt chylde lady came chylde alſo ſpeke wt elyzabeth anone ſhe ſpake elyzabeth ſaynt iohan plyed moders wombe ioye cryſtes preſē ce ſaw lady ſo lady elyzabeth vnto tyme iohan borne mydwyfe elyzabeth toke ſaynt iohan ye erth whan neyghboures herde elyzabeth ſone full gladde came thyder maner tyme gyue chylde name called zachary fader elyzabeth bad call hym iohan none kynde name aſked zarchary ſygnes chylde ſholde hyght thenne wrote bad call hym iohan god loſed zacharyes tongue ſpake redyly thanked god hyghly thus iohan halowed borne wolde gyue euery man ſyght grace good lyuynge gaue enſample ſoone couenable aege went deſerte tyll lorde came cryſtned hym lyued full ſtraytely iohannis habuit veſtimenta de pilis camillorum iohan clothynge made camell gyrdell hym ſame ſkynne eſca autem eius erat locuſta et mel ſilueſtre forſothe mete leues honyſocles hath whyte floure ye groweth tree eete maner wormes nouryſſhed deſert amonge herbes wormes grete mannes fȳger ſucked hony floures called honyſocles poore people gadereth frye theym oyle theyr mete alſo iohan dyde ete brode rounde leues whiche groweth deſerte vpon tree ſo whan broken rubbed bytwene mannes hondes ſwete ony hony dranke water welle deſerte iohannes lyfe deſerte tyll lorde xxx wynter aege thenne lorde iohan met water flome iordan thenne iohan tolde people cryſt ſayd ecce agnus dei se lambe god haue tolde ſhall fulfyll holy ghooſt ¶thenne went iohan water baptyſed cryſt whan baptyſed ecce aperti ſunt celi heuen opened et vidit ſpiritum dei diſcendentem ſicut columbā ſawe holy gooſt come downe douue et vox de celo dicens voyce frome heuen ſpake thus ecce filius meus dilectus quo michi bene complacui well beloued ſone pleaſeth lerned iohan fyrſt know ye thre perſones trynyte betokeneth two fyres thyrde fyre bone betokeneth iohans martyrdome bone brente ye ſhall ¶we rede kynge herode broder yt hyght phylyp fayre woman wyfe herode loued well helde vnder wyfe wherfore iohan repreued hȳ ſayd non licet tibi habere vxorem fratris tui lawfull haue thy broders wyfe therfore put hym pryſon ordeyned betwene hym wyfe iohan myght deed without troublynge ye people comyn people loued iohan well thenne herode ordeyned make grete feeſt ſtates ye countree ſholde holde hym yf people ryſen ſo whan day wos comen feſt ſholde holden al people ſerued mete herodes wyfe couenaunt twene tho ſhe ſent doughter hal daunce tomble fore geſtes ple • ſed fader ſo well yt ſwore grete othe ſayd pete quid vi dabo tibi aſke thou wylte ſhall gyue thenne moder badde ſhe ſayd caput iohannis baptiſte iohan baptyſts heed thenne herode fayned hym wrothe ſorye yt made ſuche othe gladde herte thenne ſent pryſon ſmyte iohans heed wt ony dome brought damoyſel moder lete bury preuy place ferre frome body thenne nexte nyghte iohans dyſcyples came toke body buryed lay tyll iulyan appoſtata emperoure came way thenne made take vp iohans bone brenne caſt aſſhes wynde hopynge ſholde neuer ryſe agayne lyfe thus ye may vnderſtande holy yt man thenne anone aungell came heuen tolde zacharye conceyuynge halowed moders wombe lady toke hym fro erthe byrthe angell brought name frome heuen cryſtned lorde iheſu cryſte holy man ye ſhall vnderſtande ſaynt iohan theuangelyſt deyed ſame daye holy chyrche maketh mencyō therof day holden cryſtmas weke thenne theſe two iohans holden worthyeſt ſayntes heuē thenne two ſcolers dyuynyte one loued iohan baptyſt iohan euangelyſt daye purpoſed dyſpute mater daye aſſygned thenne nyght eyther iohans appered theyr amantes badde theym leue theyr dyſputacyon well accorded heuen made ſtryfe ne debate thenne morowe ye people eyther theym tolde vyſyon whiche come haue herde theyr dyſputacyon thenne ail ye people thanked god iohans fayt myracle alſo two meſels whiche loued theſe two iohannys ſoo comunȳge ſpake thyſe two ſaȳtes whiche gretter heuē ſoo one ſayde ye one gretter ye ſoo began fyghte then̄e came voyce fro heuen ſayde fyghte heuen therfore fyght ye erth v ben pea ſoo ye therwith booth hole theyr ſykeneſſe thanked god ſaȳt iohannes afterwarde holy men therfore lete v worſhyppe thiſe holy saȳntes yt maye praye v yt may come heuens blyſſe amē sanctorū petri et pauli apoſtolo rum good frendis ſuche day ye ſhall haue ye feſte peter poule ye ſhall faſte ye euē morowe come vnto chirche worſhyp god pray thyſe two ſayntes yt holy apoſtles praye v lorde hath peter one ſyde poule ye ſyde hath woundes open freſſhe bledynge ſhewȳge maner cryſten peple yt ſuffred theſe woundes v fyue welles mercy yt ſuffred v ye ſhal vnderſtōde yt thyſe two appoſtles fyrſte grete ſynners lefte theyr ſynne ſory contryte ſynned nomore lord toke enſāple wyll leue ſȳnne ſhall ſaued yt ſhryuen forſaketh ſȳne mercy folowethe yt penaūce ſhal haue mercy grace gladde fader ſee ſone ryſe frome dethe lyfe alſo gladde oure lorde moche gladder ſee mā ryſe dedely ſynne neuer doo therfore ſhewyng enſample poule bereth ſwerde alle cryſten peole cut away ye cheynes ſynne wyth ſharpe ſwerde confeſſyon dedely ſynne byndeth mā ſore fēde therfore cut away yt cheyne peter alſo redy open gate heuē al cryſtē peple lette ye ſhall vnderſtonde poule fyrſt ſo hye ſoo feerſe ayenſt goddis ſeruaūtis durſt precher deale wt hȳ left grete malyce feerſe gracyous hye proude herte meke lowly al goddis ſeruaūtis ¶peter alſo helde hȳ ſelfe mooſte perfyte ſtedfaſt cryſtis dyſcyples wherfore made boſte vayn glory redy goo dethe wt criſt ſayd thus behoueth dey whā criſt ſayd al dyſcyples ſholde forſake hȳ peter greate booſt ſayd though alle men forſake hȳ wolde yet ouer whan cryſt take peter drewe oute ſwerde ſmote ſeruaūtis ere hyghte malcus ¶but ſoone whan ſawe yt cryſt take ſholde put deth thenne ſwore ſtared neuer knewe forſoke cryſte whā herde cocke crowe remēbred oure lorde ſayde hȳ cocke crew iii thou ſhalt forſake thenne peter wente forth et fleuit amare wepte bytterly hyd caue durſt come amonge bredren ſhame tyl oure lorde ſente hȳ name peter euer aſhamed ſory treſpas booſter vnſtable wordis afterwarde true ſtable groūded ſtableneſſe perfyght lyuynge ſo moche cryſt called hym peter yt ſtone englyſſhe thou layeſte ſtone thou ſhalte fȳde soo peter ſo ſtedfaſt neyther wele wo neuer fleytered euer ſtoode ſted faſt cryſtes lawe euer ſȳne mȳde amēde yt done amyſſe afterwarde grete abſtynence ete brede oyle wortes full ſelden fleſſhe wered ſyngell kertyll mantell euer often herde ony man mynde iheſus anone began wepe full ſore whan herde ony cocke crowe anone roſe vp wolde goo praye ſuffre penaunce wepte many tymes ſo bytterly teres eyen brente face ſo moche cloth boſome alwaye wype away teres thenne ſo folowynge ſoo holy yt euer wente myghte ſhadow ony ſyke body anone hole tyme ſente two dyſciples ferre coūtreye preche whan gone two dayes iourney one deyed ye tourned ayene tolde peter thenne peter toke hym ſtafe bad go laye ſtaffe felawe bad hȳ aryſe ye name god roſe anone wente forth gyder preched thenne many wrothe peter tourned ſo moche peple fayth put hȳ pryſon bonde hym faſte grete cheynes yren tylle nye dede leſte ſholde ſtolen awaye wherfore knyghtes woke ſholde eſcape thus comen people toke enſample made fyres worſhyppe ſaynte peter watche thenne cryſte came peter pryſon came angell peter grete lyghte oure lorde bad anone cheynes brake fylle fro hondes fete wente rome pope xxv yeres tourned moche people cryſtes feyth ſoone came fendis lymme yt called symon magus coude moche fendis crafte made moche people ſyke dyuerſe ſykeneſſe blȳ de ſome lame ſome deef ſo yt peple fere wonder byleued hym thenne peter heled thoſe magus hurte bad ſholde byleue hym thenne ſymon magus wroth wyth peter myghte haue wyll eſpecyall myghte reyſe dede body lyfe peter reyſed thenne ſymon teyed fende lykeneſſe grete dogge peter ſholde come ſlee peter peter bleſſyd hym lete dogge loſe thenne lepte ſymon pulled hȳ downe vnder hys fete thenne peter bad leue hym harme body al rente clothes ſoo ſymon wente almoſte naked away ſymon ordeyned al wayes yt coude haue peter dede lord appered peter ſayd symon et nero cōtra te cogitāt symō nero haue ordeyned thy dethe morowe wyll ſende poule ſeruaunt comforte ye ſhal ſuffre martyrdome togyder ſake ſo come euerlaſtynge blyſſe thenne peter tolde hys bretheren viſyon yt nyghte ſo toke clemente honde ſette chayre made hym pope ſucceſſoure hym thenne morowe came poule preched people ſymon ſo charmed ye emperour ſuche folyſhnes wende hadde goddis ſone symon magus came themperour ſayde two men galylee come cyte one hyghte peter poule ſoo moche dyſeaſe maye lenger abyde erth wherfore commaunde ſuche daye maner peple come capytoll ſyghte people wyll ſtye vp fader heuen whan people come gyder ¶symon wente vp toure capitoll thenne came two fendes lyke two angellis ſette hede garlonde laurell bare hym vp ayre lyke hadde flowen ¶thenne ſayd peter poule broder loke vp ſee ¶thenne ſayd poule falleth praye commaunde anone peter ſayd commaunde angellys sathanas ye lete man go downe men may ſe whome haue worſhypped thenne symon fell downe al braſte thenne themperoure wrothe made lede peter poule forthe dyde peter croſſe heed downewarde ſoo put hym dethe poule gentylman borne worſhyppe ſmote heed thenne people ſawe aungelles crownes ſtandynge croſſe peter hanged whan poules heed ſmyte came fayre plente mylke blode thenne ye nyght came cryſten people layde theyr bodyes togyder graue lay tyll cryſten faythe open rome thenne wolde haue borne eyther body chyrche coude knowe eyther bone then̄e came voyce heuen yt ſayd bone precher leſſe fyſſher whan cryſten fayth came englonde kynge ethelberte lete make grete chyrche weſtmynſter worſhyppe ſaynt peter london ſaynt poule ſo day whā chyrche ſaynt peter ſholde halowed nyght man fyſſhynge temſe vnder weſtmȳ ſter lytell mydnyght came ſaynt peter lyke pylgryme prayed fyſſher ſet hym ouer water dyde ſo peter went chyrche ye fyſſher ſawe grete lyght therwith ſweteſt ſauour euer felte alſo herde meryeſt ſonge euer herde wyſt ioye thenne came peter hym agayne ſayd haſt thou take ony fyſſhe nyght ſayd nay ſo ſtonyed lyght melody myght maner thynge then̄e ſayd peter mitte rethe mari caſt nette theſe wyll helpe ſoo toke grete multytude fyſſhes thenne ſayd ſaynt peter fyſſher peter hath halowed chyrche nyghte toke grete fyſſhe ſayd bere byſſhop ſay yt ſende hym token bydde hym halowynge chyrche ſynge maſſe make ſermon people may beleue preue ye trouthe byd go chyrche ſe candelles ſtycke walles chyrche wete holy water ſoo fyſſher dydde meſſage byſſhop founde true kneled downe knee moche people wt hym ſonge deum laudamꝰ thanked god ſaynt peter ¶secūda die iulii celebrat feſtū viſitacionis marie amonge deuoute cryſten people daye ſyngulerly worſhypped blyſſed lady mary grete mekenes lowly viſytacyon coſyn elyzabeth wyfe zacharye prophete moder ſaynt iohan baptyſt saynt iherome ſayth quid qd humanis poteſt dici verbis minus eſt laude virginis glioſe que diuinis c whiche may englyſſhed thus ſo euer laude pray ſȳge yt ony man woman may make lady laude lytell ferre inſuffycyent frome ye laude yt ſhe worthy haue yt ſo excellently accept god wonderly prayſed patryarkes prophetes appoſtles euangelyſtes yet thy though vnable lete v euer eſpecyall feeſt doo deuoyre power fre ſubſtaunce worſhyppe blyſſed lady vertuous lyuynge deuout prayer folowȳge enſample moche may ye ſhall vnderſtande ye ſayd elyzabeth conceyued myracle iohan baptyſte borne hym wombe vi monethes came thaungel god heuen vnto mary ſaynge vnto yt ſhe ſholde conceyue ye ſone god almyghty token ſhall true thynge poſſyble god doo aungell ſayd coſyn elyzabeth whiche barayne nature aege redy conceyued borne vi monethes chylde wombe whan mary herde beleued therwith conſented forthwith ſhe conceyued ſone god thenne goſpell day ſayth thus et exurgens maria abiit montana c luce lady roſe vp went haſtely nazareth yt galyle mountaynes iury ſoo entred hous zacharye prophete lo goſpell ſayd ſhe went haſtely ſhewynge woman ſpecyally al maydens ſholde tary ye wayne tell tale haue talkynge men thre cauſes lady vyſyted elyzabeth fyrſte yt myght gladde eyther iheronimus vt miraculum miraculo gaudiū gaudio cumularetur ſaye yt myracle myracle ioye ioye ſholde encreaced grete ioye myracle lady ſhe beynge ſtyll vyrgyn conceyued cryſt ſone god alſo grete ioye myracle elyzabeth yt ſhe beynge barayne aege hadde conceyued ſo grete prophete iohan baptyſt ſoo gracyouſly eſcaped reprefe theym barayne amonge people iſrahell lykewyſe ſholde cryſten people folowȳge lady enſample glad neyghbours proſperyte welfare ſory theyr trybulacyon contrary dooth enuyous people chyldren deuyll wyl glad theyr neyghbours hurt dyſeaſe wyll ſory whan fare well ben proſperyte suche condycyons haue ye deuyls howle ſorowe whan doo ony good dedes ioye whan doo euyll wherfore ſuche people muſt punyſſhed helle byde euer theyr fader deuyll prouerbio rum xvii qui ruina alterius letatur nō erit impunitus ſay yt gladde mannes fall ſhall eſcape vnpunyſſhed ſeconde cauſe lady vyſyted elyzabeth ſeruyce helpe nede lykewyſe ſhe ſhewed mekenes god tymes aungell whan vpon ſay frome nazareth mountaynes iury whiche ſcdm albertum forty myle combrous way therto ſalute ſerue olde wyfe ſeruaunt abyde ſo longe grete watche laboure ye tyme iohan borne yes doubtles ¶beholde thou cryſten man woman good lernȳge bothe lorde iheſu cryſt yt wombe membres alſo lady enſample v ſpecyally woman ben taught attendaunt ſeruyable tyme chyldes byrthe euery woman chylde bereth precyous treaſoure wombe ſaye ye ſoule chylde lyfe bernardus votus mundus iſte vnius anime precium eſtimare non poteſt ſaye worlde may tell pryce one ſoule ¶thenne woo ſhall theym whiche ſine fine viuet et regnat ſecula ſeculorum amen ¶de tranſlatione ſancti thome frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue tranſlacion ſaynt thomas ye martyr yt day take oute graue bone layde ſhryne ye ſhall man ordeyned byrth holy man worthy ſaynt yt ſhewed fyrſt moder fader olde age knowē ouer fyrſt knowē moder nyght ſhe lay bed ſlepynge ſhe thoughte thomas laye cradell wepte whan ſhe herde hym wepe ſhe doo chylde ſhal worthy man tofore god cryſten people ſhal hym worſhyppe thenne wexed thomas wyſe actyfe wyſdome yt archebyſſhop caūterbery ſēte hȳ made hȳ chaunceler englonde gouerned offyce ſee yet chaūged one xl dayes alſo man greate almeſdedes caſte greate loue god drad deye ¶thenne rebuked kynge myſdedys yenſt holy chirche oppreſſed reame thenne kynge grete indignacyon exyled hym vpon boke ſholde neuer tary tyll come tofore thomas encreaſe paynes whan thomas ſawe wepte ſorowe grete cōpaſſyō theym yet ordeyned yt better atte eaſe fraū ce englonde thenne whan god wolde yt thomas ſholde paſſe oute world byddyng pope counſeyle kynge fraunce thomas came caunterbery owne chyrche whan kynges knyghtes herde therof four curſed lyuers wente v day feſte cryſtmaſſe ſlewe hȳ owne chirche aulter ſaȳ te benet lefte hym dede thenne monkis place wepynge makynge grete ſorowe beryed hym newe tombe redy made ¶but thenne god ſhewed ſo grete myracles hym pope alyſaunder ſente morowe came ſtatis londe bare ye ſhryne place wyth reuerence worſhyppe cowde wyth worſhyppe ¶amen de ſancta maria magdalena god frendis ſuche day ye ſhal haue feſte mari magdaleyne ſoo holy yt lord iheſu cryſt loued beſt al wymmen next owne moder wherfore ye ſhalle come god holy chyrche praye holy woman yt ſhe wyll praye oure lorde v maye haue grace ſhe ye fyrſte tyme grace dyde penaunce ſhe loſte grace fleſſhly luſte ſo ſhe made myrroure ſynners yt wyl forſake ſynne doo penaūce ſhall haue grace yt whiche loſte ſyn̄e fader grete lorde nye kynges blood greate lordſhyp iheruſalem whiche gaaf lazarus ſone gaaf mary caſtell magdeleyne ye lordſhyp longȳge ther ye whiche caſtell ſhe name called mari magdeleyne ſhe lady therof thenne many bokes ſayen ſaynt iohan euangelyſte wedded oure lordo bad hym goo wt hym kepe vyrgynyte ſo dyde clene vyrgyn magdeleyne went forth gaaf ſynne ſo moche ſhe loſt ye name magdeleyne callen ſynfull woman often ſeen oure lorde made greteſte ſynner yt holyeſte afterwardes ſoo whan oure lorde ſawe tyme gaaf woman grace knowe ſelfe haue repentaūce ſynnes thenne whan mary herde cryſte mannys houſe called symon pharyſe ſhe toke boxe oynemente ſuche ye peple vſed tyme hete ye ſonne went thyder ſhe durſt ſhame goo tofore fete behynde hȳ herde hym ſpeke ſhe toke grete ſorow herte wepte tenderly ye teres eyen ſhe waſſhed cryſtes fete wyth here hede ſhe wyped wt loue herte ſhe kyſſed anoynted noo worde ſhe ſpake ony man myghte ſoftly herte ſhe cryed mercy made vow ſhe wolde neuer treſpace ¶thenne lord hadde pyte vpon caſte oute ſeuen fendis forgaaf ſynnes herynge al thenne ſhe toke ſuche loue cryſte ſhe lefte lordſhyps mawdeleyne goodes ſuch hym forth grete loue hys paſſyon hys dyſcyples fledde frome hym ſhe lefte hym neuer tyll ſhe helpe layde hym tombe whan man durſt go thyder fere knyghtes kepte hym ſhe ſpared cū tenebre eſſent c whā derke dawnynge ſhe toke ſwete bawmes anoynte cryſtes body ſhe ſhewed loue bothe wyll dede wherfore cryſte lyfe heled martha ſyſter reed flyxe ſhe vii yere tofore payned ſore et reſuſcitauit lazarū mortuis reyſed lazar brother frome deth lyfe layne iiii dayes ſtynkynge graue whan lorde roſe frome dethe lyfe appered ſuffred touche hym kyſſed fete thenne whan knowen iewes cryſt ſhewed ſo many token loue whan cryſt ſtyed vp heuen toke mary martha ſyſter lazarus maxencius many put olde ſhyppe ſee haue drowned god ordeyned ſo thynge wyll brought ſaufe londe called myracle reſted vnder banke nygh ye temple thenne mary ſawe moche people comynge towarde ye temple ſacryfyce theyr mawmettes lorde countree came wt magdaleyne gracyous gracyous wordes torned agayne lorde grete luſt ſpeke ſayd thus yf god thou ſpekeſt ſo gracyous ſoo grete power thou ſayeſt praye hym may haue chylde wyfe barayne wyl beleue hym thenne mary ſayd ſhe wolde within ſhorte tyme lady conceyued chylde then̄e lorde anone made ordeyne euery thȳge longed hym go iheruſalem peter wyte hȳ der magdaleynes prechynge true vytayled well ſhyppe made hym redy thenne came lady prayenge hym ſhe myghte go ſo grete prayer ye lorde graunted thenne aſſente thē made mary maudeleyne kepe lordſhyppes goodes yt mary ſette croſſe eyther theyr ſholders bad goo name god whā ſeyled day nyghte grete tēpeſt aroſe ſo moche wende al haue drowned ¶thenne lady ſore aferde therewith ſhe began trauayle ſo delyuered manchylde maudeleyne ſayd ſhe byrth fyll downe dede lorde made greate ſorowe lamentacyon ſayde ala ala wretche ſhal chylde nowe moder dede nedeſt muſt ye chylde deye alſo noo womannys helpe kepe ¶thenne cried maudeleyne ſayde ala mary doſte thou thus thou behote chylde moder dede ye chyde muſt nedys deye fawte woman helpe ſelf loke euer whan ſhal drowned helpe mary haue compaſſyon chylde thenne ſayd ſhyp man caſt body ſee ſhall neuer haue reſte whyle ye ſhyp ſayd lorde ſhe dede lyeth ſwoune fere praye lete v haue ye ſhyp yon de roche leuer graue caſt water none erthe make graue left hangynge roche ſtone chylde moder couered wt mantell toke thē god mary mawdeleyne kepe wente way whan came iheruſalē ſpake peter bad hȳ good cōforte though wyfe dede god myghte reſtore lyfe ayene thenne peter ſhewed hym place lorde quycke dede tolde hym byrthe paſſion reſurreccyon aſcencyō enformed ſayth made hȳ ſtedfaſt cryſte whan ii yere peter ſente hȳ home ayene badde hȳ grete wel mawdeleyne felyſſhyp thenne whā ye lorde came ferre ye ſee ſawe place wyfe laye longed ſore herte goo thyder prayed ſhypman ſet hȳ ſawe lytell chylde ſyttȳge ſee ſonde pleyng ſmale ſtones ſoone ye chylde ſawe hym ranne forth rocke folowed tyll came lefte wyfe toke vp mantell foū de ye chylde ſoukyng moders pappes thenne thanked god mary maudeleyne ſayde mary yu art greate god yt haſte keped yonge chylde ſoukynge vpon dede body greate comforte ioye yu wylte pray thy lorde wyf myghte reſtored lyf euer boūde thy ſeruaūt wyll whyle lyue thenne worde ſhe ſpake ſayde bleſſyd mote yu mary mydwyfe nouryſe chylde whyle haue pylgremage thenne ſayd man wyfe arte yu lyue ſhe ſayd ye ſyr nowe come fro pylgremage ye tolde euery place kneled downe thā ked god mary magdeleyne whan came home foūde mary prechynge techynge peple anone kneled downe thanked tolde peter ſayde prayed telle ſholde wolde doo good wyll thenne mary bad ſholde diſtroye ye temple mawmentry byld chirches make fontes cryſten peple ſo within ſhorte tyme londe cryſtened thenne mary gaaf contemplacyon ſhe went ferre wilderneſſe therty wynters vnknowen ony man deſcendebant angeli et eam ethera leuabant angellis came ſeuen tymes daye bare vp ayre ſhe fedde heuenly fode whā god wolde ſhe ſholde paſſe worlde made holy preeſte ſee angellys bare vp thayre thenne wente nere ye place aſked name god yf cryſten man ſhold ſpeke tell thenne anſwered mary magdeleyne ſayd ſynfull woman yt goſpell ſpeketh wyſſhe cryſtes fete ſhe bad preeſt goo maxencius byſſhoppe byd hym eſter day mournynge chyrche wyl mete whan come ye chirche ſawe howe mary borne vp two cubites fro erthe aūgellys ſore agaſt thē ne mary called hȳ come nere goo ſaye maſſe ſhe myghte houſeled thenne ſyghte ye peple whā maſſe done ſhe houſeled receyued goddis body fourme brede anone therwyth ſhe gaaf vp gooſt thenne toke byſſhop holy body layed tombe ſtone wrote lyfe worſhyppe god dyde ſoo gracyouſly ſynfull peple wyl leue theyr ſynne thus ye maye come euerlaſtynge blyſſe whiche god brynge v amen ¶de feſto ſancti iacobi apoſtoli frendis ſuche day ye ſhal haue ſaȳt iames daye appoſtle ye ſhall faſte euen worſhyppe god holy appoſtle iames holy mā came holy kynde ladyes ſyſters ſone broder ſaynt iohan euangelyſt thaſſent ye appoſtles ſent spayne preche worde god ye people ſo combred ſynne mawmetry myght torne ix perſones yt whiche left two preche ſeuen toke wt hym iurye herde one called hermogines dyſcyple hyght philetus two begyled ſoo people iames torned cryſtes fayth anone torned agayne mawmetry thenne iames blamed thē torne frome euerlaſtynge blyſſe euerlaſtynge dampnacyon thenne hermogynes herde therof came dyſputed wt iames fayth hopynge fendes craft haue ouercome hym thenne iames dyde ſo many myracles yt phyletus forſoke hermogenes mayſter hermogenes wrothe ſent company fendes ſayd go ye brynge iames phyletus bounde vnto whan fendes came iames aungell god redy bounde fendes yt cryed iames appoſtle haue mercy v bounde ſo ſore wt yren chaynes wo v euery ſyde ſayd iames wherfore ye come hyder ſayd hermogynes ſent v hyder brynge phyletus boūde hym goddes aungelles haue bounde v wo v ſuffre payne thenne ſayd iames wyl loſe ſo ye go hermogynes brynge hym hyther bounde hym harme thenne ſayd hermogynes thou haſte ſent v haue boūde yren chaynes wyll bynde brynge iames thenne ſayd iames falſe hermogynes hath doone v moche trybulacyons dyſeaſe gyue v leue auenge bothe v vpon hȳ thenne ſayd iames nay ſoo mayſter iheſus bad good agaynſt euyll thenne iames bad phyletus vnbynde hermogynes thenne ſayd hermogynes knowe malyce fendes praye iames gyue ſome thy power elles theſe fendes wyll ſle iames gaue hym owne ſtaffe wente boldely owne hous toke bokes keſt theym ſee came iames fell downe knee cryed hym mercy thenne iames gladde cryſtned hym taught hym fayth holy man god wrought many myracles hym thenne herde iewes therof toke iames bounde rope aboute necke ledde hym vnto kynge herode prayed hym iames dethe elles wolde torne theyr nacyon cryſtes faythe deſtroye theyr lawe thenne herode commaunded ſmyte heed whā deede hermogynes phyletus wt many dyſcyples toke iames body durſt iewes bury toke theym ſhyppe went ſee prayenge god brynge wolde body buryed thenne god gouerned ye ſhyppe ſo landed spayne quene called lupa yt ſhe wolfe ſhe called ſo curſed lyuynge thenne toke body layde vpon ſtone ſtone waxed ſo ſoft body ſanke downe ſtoone lyke ben tombe made therfore thenne ſome kept corp whyle went quene lupa ſayd ſhe wolde receyue iames lyfe god ſent body thyder buryed wherfore pray place burye body worſhyp ſuche holy man quene dyde wolues kynde wyſt well yt kynge ſpayne yll man maners wolde harme ſent hym praynge ordeyn place body myght buryed dyde curſed man ſhold toke put pryſon bounde faſt hande fote grete yren chaynes ſate mete aungell came lete pryſon badde go theyr way ſo dyde whan kynge herde ſente two knightes wc moche people brynge agayne whan ye knyghtes came brydge yt gone ouer wolde haue gone brydge brake ye knyghtes al people drowned thenne kynge aferde vengeaunce ſent theym peaſybly prayed come agayne ſholde haue theyr deſyre whan came agayne kynge cōmaunded cyte cryſtned whan ye quene herde yt ſhe wrothe thought ye harme dyſpyte ſhe coude ſent prayenge come ſhe wolde ordeyne hym beſt wyſe whan come ſhe ſayd go ſuche hyl haue ox bulles take yoke wayne laye corp therin lete theym choyſe theyr waye thyder lede wayne graunt place bury corp thus ſhe dyde grete malyce hopynge wylde beſtes wolde haue dyſtroyed whan made croſſe tofore beeſtes ſtode ſtyll whyle yoked wayne ſo lete go ſyght ye people ledde wayne quenes palays ſhe repēted cryed mercy god ſaynt iames anone cryſtned gaue palays wt good wyl ſaynt iames yt longeth therto made therof worthy chyrch layde ſaynt iames therin dyde hym reuerence yt myght god ſheweth many fayre myracles ¶narracio ¶there man called bernarde yt hapned take wt enmyes put pryſon dongeon bounde wt grete chaynes yren myght cryed hertely god ſaynt iames helpe ſocoure came ſaynt iames hym conforted hym anone chaynes brake iames hanged necke ſayd veni ſequere come folowe ledde hym top tour yt forty cubytes heyght bad hym lepe downe bere chaynes spayne offre ſaynt iames ſo dyde ¶narracio ¶alſo man yt yede ſaynt iames company pylgrymes helped poore woman yt ſeke bere ſcryppe anone met wt ſyke man myght go ſet hym horſe ryde wēt hymſelfe fote berynge poore woman ſcryppe ſeke mannes ſtaffe grete hete trauayle whā came ſaynt iames fell ſeke laye thre dayes myght ſpeke gaue vp grete ſyghȳge ſpake ſayd thanke god ſaynt iames prayer delyuered grete multytude fendes ryght came ſaynt iames ye poore woman ſcryppe ſeke mannes ſtaffe hath dryuen away ye fendes fro gete preeſt anone ſhall lyue whyle ſayd one felowes good frende go fro thy lorde yt yu ſerueſt ſothely dampned ſhall deye wtin ſhorte tyme foule dethe whan came home tolde theyr lorde ſet nought therby wtin ſhorte tym deed man ſayd ¶narracio ¶there xxx men cōpany yt plyght theyr trouthe eche true go ſaynt iames togyder ſaufe one yt wolde plight trouth ſhorte time one thē fell ſeke laye iii dayes ſpake lay ſo longe ye left hȳ ſauf yt wolde plyght trouth abode whyle ſpake mended felawe caryed hym forth myghte trauayle ſofte happed abode nyghte vnder hyll full ſore aferde curſed peple wylde beſtis man deyed aboute mydnyght came ſaynte iames rydynge ſayde gyue dede body thy felawe come thenne vp behynde morowe rydden xv dayes iourney came mounte ioye halfe myle frome ſaynt iames lete hȳ downe badde man go fet chanons ſaynt iames bery thy felawe ſay thy felawes pylgremage ſtonde ſtede falſe felawe therfore lete euery man woman true ſhall laſte come blyſſe heuē amē de ſancta anna gode frendis ſuche day ye ſhal haue ſaȳt annys daye yt oure ladyes moder daye ye ſhall come god holy chirche praye holy womā praye v rede v holy woman hyghte anna wyll tell thyſe v wymen fyrſte anna moder ye prophete ſamuell yt gouerned ye people iſrahell anna huſbōde yt hyghte eclana chyldren anna lōge tyme grete prayer god ye laſte ſone yt called ſamuel another āna yt wyfe man called raguell doughter hyghte ſare ye whiche ſare vii huſbōdes euer ye fyrſte nyghte yt fynde ſtrangeled theȳ whā wolde haue comuned wt luſte fleſſhe brȳ ge forth frute goddis pleſaūce chylderen ſoone came yonge tobye techynge thangel toby wedded ſare threnyghtes iii dayes forbare wyf prayer ſo chyldrē iii anna thelder tobyes wyf elder tobye olde man dyde ye werkes mercy full ſyly preue mekenes ſuffraūce god made hym blynde day beryed many deed bodyes ſlaȳ wery lay downe hous welles loked vp ye dong ſwalowes fel eyen ſo blȳde toke pacyently thāked god hys vyſytacyō god reſtored hȳ ſyght ayene iiii anna temple iheruſalē whan ioſeph lady bare cryſte yt temple candelmaſſe daye ſhe prophecyed criſt ſholde fall anna ſoo holy yt whan ſhe wedded ſeuen yere huſbonde deyed thenne went ſhe ye temple nyghte daye tyll ſhe iiii ſcore yere olde thenne ſhe grace god ſee hȳ bodely ſhe deyed armes v anna ladyes moder whā lady age brought temple left ye vyrgynes age lerne moyſes lawe ſerue god nyghte daye anna huſbonde called ioachym oure ladyes fader come ye kynred dauyd prophetes told longe tofore kynred dauyd ſholde deſcende downe cryſt wryten bokes yt kepte ye treſorye ye temple kynge herode iheruſalem thoughte torne ye lyfe god hȳ eyre toke bokes oute treſory made brenne mynde cryſt ſholde haue forgotē meane haue torned lygnage dauyd hym wherfore bokes telleth howe ioachym deſcended fro dauyd ¶but whan herode hadde done foule dede yet ther ſome good wyſe men yt copyes bokes thē home ye tolde ioachym came ye kyngdom dauyd dauyd many chylderē one theym called natan ye whyche come leuy nother called panther hȳ came barban yt ioachyms fader yt maryed ladyes moder pater eius ioachym mater vero āna vocati ioachym ladyes fader moder anna whan chylde ſhe gyuen maryage ioſeph ſo ioachȳ anna ended theyr lyfe full vertuouſly therfore god ſayth good tree comyth good frute soo good woman came holy ofſprynge soo lete v ſerue holy woman yt ſhe maye pray v euer amen ¶feſtum tranſfiguracionis domini celebratur vi die auguſti ſatyrdaye euer ye fyrſte hole weke lente redde goſpell mathewe ye xvii chapytre aſſūpſit iheſus petrū iohānē ye whiche ſhewed yt ſauyoure toke iii dyſcyples peter iames iohan brother ledde thē vnto hye moūte yt called thabor trāſfygured byfore thē face ſhone ye ſōne hys clothȳge whyte ye ſnow appered moyſes hely ſpekynge hym c done lernynge grete cō forte ioye yt come ye lorde thus tranſfygured ſoo greate bryghtneſſe betokeneth glory ye ſoule body euery cryſten man woman ſhall haue yf lyue well worlde kepe cōmaūdemētis daye greatly pryuyleged holy chyrche ſo moche yt order ben gyue day thoruth cryſtēdome grete pardon graūted day dyuerſe place ſyon plener remyſſyon alle wele comforte man purueance ſanctyfye ſoule laſte reſurreccyon ſayde ſoule ioyned body maye togyder gloryfyed trāſfygured clerneſſe bryghter ſonne ſo euer endure thenne haue knowlege tranſfyguracyon ye ſhall vnderſtonde oure lorde toke thyſe thre dyſcyples appoſtles cauſe famylyer theym ony alſo peter made afore promyſſe hede ye chyrche prynce appoſtles iohan toke ſynguler loue yt hym vyrgynyte iames cauſe ſholde fyrſte dye loue take martyrdome alſo lorde moyſes dede tranſfyguracyon thouſande yere fyue hondred alſo hely greate prophete thouſā de yeres afore tranſlate paradyſe lyue yet lyue ye ſayde hely preſerued preche agaynſt antecryſt thende worlde ſayde antecryſt ſhall putte deth martyre hym ¶thyſe two toke ſygnefyenge yt ſhall iuge alle dede moyſes thenne body alſo thoſe ben lyue yet ſayde prophete hely paradyſe alſo cauſe bothe faſted fourty daye penaunce ſhewed moyſes exodi xxx hely iii regū xix ſoo rede abrahā ne noe ſuche lymbo moyſes alſo enoch yet alyue ſayd hely paradyſe thenne may lerne pleaſeth moche lorde cryſten people faſt xl dayes ſaye lente may able tranſfyguracyon whiche ſhall paſche day clerely whan ſe lorde maker face face glory ſelfe ſhall tranſfygured ſoule body vnſpekable bryghetnes durynge withoute ende ioye gladnes peraduēture wyll ſay wolde faſt may ye whiche vnderſtande ben nyne cauſes whiche perſone bounde faſt fyrſt womā chylde ſhe muſt prouyde two ſoo congruence ſhe ought haue two meles refeccyons without yt ſhe ſtronge good compleccyon thenne ſhe may faſt ſome daye weke ſeconde ben nouryces gyueth chyldren ſouke thyrde ben ſeke folke may ete whan comyn tyme requyreth haue ye goute excuſed good medycyne breed water fourthe ben poore people haue wherof take good mele theyr refeccyon ſuffyently dewe houre go dore dore fyft poore people lyeth bedred may noo ferder haue mete ynough yf ſuche faſte theyr mede ſhall grete yf ryche people faſt fall dampnacyon ſyxt fote men horſmen haue grete iourneys eete neceſſyte elles excuſed ſeuenth ben thoſe ledeth theyr lyues grete laboure handcrafty men ben excuſed therby eyght ben yonge people ſaynt thomas ii ſecunde ſayth yonge man may excuſed tyll attayne come xxi yere aege ſo longe groweth partyes moche faſtynge may demenyſſhe twelue yere aege lete hym faſt fryday lente ye leeſt xiiii yeres two dayes ye weke xviii thre dayes weke xx foure dayes ye weke xxi dayes lente ¶the ix ben aeged people may ete aege haue good ſtomackes ben hole ben excuſed hec vincencius ¶what forme ordre ſhall kepe oure faſtynge oure lorde ſayd moyſes helye theyr enſample techeth v lorde faſtynge prayed moyſes whan dyde faſt toke good hede lorde ſayd vnto hym whā gaue hym lawes commaundementes hely prophete euer goynge lyke maner wyſe ſhold moche may tyme faſt lente entende prayer dyuyne ſeruyce take good hede ſayd ſermons prechynge preeſte whan pulpytte bere awaye therafter moche ye may rehercynge techȳ ge ſame chyldren ſeruauntes yt ye haue charge power ¶alſo goynge holy place pardon may ſooner releaſed haue forgyuenes ſynnes come mount heuen yt laboure whiche herytaūce ſhall ſe tranfyguracyon lorde god maker redemer moche larger bryghter gloryous euer peter felawſhyp ſawe hym ſayd mount thabor mounte ſhall ſe ſenſybly without fere fallynge downe grounde ſayd appoſtles dyde fader ſone holy gooſt excellent glory reſydent reygnynge lorde god worldes without ende myddes amonge cytezyns ſayntes may tongue ſuffyſe tell ¶of mounte gloryous cyte heuen fynde wrytynge ſorowe heueneſſe waylynge wepynge none nother pouerte ſekeneſſe man hurte man greued hated enuyeth nother couetyſe none deſyre mete drynke ony worſhyp power fere theyr malyce haue man woman brynge theym theyr dongeon helle deth body ſoule ſhall neuer glorye ioy neuer ſhall ceaſe wt euerlaſtynge grace ſhall dyſcorde thynges order accorde contynuell gladneſſe ben thynges quyete reſtfull grete clerte bryghtneſſe ſone ſhyneth whiche ſhall nede lorde hym ſelfe gyueth ſhall gyue yt cyte lyghte iheſus lambe god ſhall lanterne ben none aged people none wretchydneſſe age people ſhall full age lorde xxxii none nyghte nother derkeneſſe gaderynge cloudes none exceſſe hete colde thynges ſo temporate eye neuer ſe ſuche ere neuer herde nother may perceyued mannys herte mynde onely thoſe whiche worthy haue name whome ben wryten boke lyfe whiche haue taken hete worlde theyr penaunce grete paſſion ſtreyte lyfe nowe ben blyſſe heuen ſeruynge day nyght aboue theſe ioye glorye ſhall theym ſhall accompanyed ordres aungelles angel archangelles throne domynacyons pryncypates poteſtates cherubyn ſeraphyn heuenly ſpyrytes ſo hygh vertue beholde ſo innumerable cō pany ſayntes lorde iheſu cryſte dyſtyncte kepynge theyr ordre felawſhyp moche bryghter ſhynȳ ge ſterres heuen lady ye moder god patryarkes fro hȳ eche ſyde ſpace cm myles ſpace compaſſe full whete euery • ere whete ſhynynge alſo bryght ſonne yet lyght comparyſon lyke leeſt bryghtnes clerenes iuſt people gloryfyed hath ſhall haue heuen thenne chi conſydered haue oft mynde remembraunce gloryous hyll heuen ſolempne tranſfyguracyon lorde god ſayntes wel vnderſtande fayth loue herte laboure therfore contynuelly thought worde dede kyngedome heuen aſketh none pryce thy ſelfe ſo moche worthe thy ſelfe therfore gyue thy ſelfe therfore thou ſhalte haue neuer fere pryce pur lorde iheſu cryſt gaue hym ſelfe deye entent make v mancyon kyngdome vnto fader wherfore beware lete ſynne reygne thereby exclude lorde habytacyon within ſoules haue euer ſpyryte lyfe goodneſſe vertue ye may optayne come ſayd tranſfyguracyon heuen amen ¶of ſwete holy name iheſus whiche ſhall ſeuen daye auguſte fyrſt book ſcrypture wryten yt god fynyte goodneſſe hath made man ordeyned hym lorde haue domynacyon lyuynge creature broughte cauſede broughte pleyſed man adam entente ſholde knowe made man gyue euery lyuynge creature name accordynge nature ye propryete therof therfore congruē ce nobleneſſe dygnyte vertue euery good thynge oughte prayſed magnyfyed loued name ſygnyfyeth ſame thynge specyally yf impoſytoure gyuer name hath perfyte ſyence knowlege bothe thynge name euer hath ſhall vſe knowelege man name iheſus ſygnefyeth ye mooſt noble mooſt honorable mooſte precyouſe thynge euer ſhall quia filius dei iheſus name ſone god ſeconde perſone trynyte ante ſeculo worldis creacyon predeſtynate ordeyned hye wyſdome godhede thus nature kynde named called iheſus though terra ex tempore v erthe ſhewede newe impoſycyon ſent releued frome heuen thaungell gabryell whiche hadde heuenly meſſage ſhewed bleſſyd vyrgyne marye ſhe ſholde conceyue vyrgyne aferde ſayd aungell god vnto ioſeph drede take mary thy ſpouſe abyde ſhe hath conceyued ſaye chylde holy ghoſt de ſpiritu ſā cto eſt ¶and ſhal brynge forth ſone et vocabis nomē eius iheſum mathei primo atte cyrcumcyſyon ſhed fyrſt blode vocatum eſt nomen eius iheſus bleſſyd babe theym named called iheſus ¶by whiche name iheſus called clypped cōceyued ſo moders wombe ſayth euangelyſt quod vocatum ē priuſquam vtero conciperetur luce ſecundo ¶o thou bleſſyd iheſu thou ſouerayne iheſu holy heuenly name iheſus beſeche al worſhyp honoure loue thy holy name iheſus v iheſꝰ iheſu ſaye wyll ye aſke cauſe haue deſyred hym v iheſus forſothe iheſꝰ interpretacyon eſt idem quod ſaluator ſeu ſalutare vel ſalus ¶iheſus moch ſay ſauyour helth gyuer helthe ſelf ſynners borne childerne yre haue nede grace ſayth ſaynt poule whome ſhall haue grace delyuered frome ſynne certaynly none iheſu plenus gracie et veritatis et per quem gracia et veritas iohannis primo iheſus full grace alſo grace ſaluacion cometh alſo iheſu grace may hadde alſo good dede ne operacyon may wrought iohannis decimo quin sine nichil poteſtis facere blyſſed iheſus holy faders patryarkys abraham iacob mourned longed propheſyes fygures ſygnes oracle token innumerable wrytē holy ſcrypture though ſcrypture founde perſones name iheſus filius naue wyſe called ioſue iheſus filius ſyrac iheſus ſone ioſodech though eche creature heuen erthe made create foloweth ſame chapytre iheſus onely thus fader makynge creacyon worlde alſo cum eo que cuncta componens iheſus god fader fourmer maker ſhaper theſe thynges ſayd wytneſſeth confermeth euangelyſt iohan ſaynge thus oīa per ipſū facta ſunt et ſine ipſo factū eſt nichil iheſu ſayth holy goſpell thynges made created without iheſu neuer ony creature made iheſu two twenty name ſtyre people haue reuerence oure honourable iheſus graunted euery perſone dyſpoſed ofte blyſſed name iheſu reherced dyuyne ſeruyce dooth bowe knee maketh inclynacyon ſmyteth hymſelf vpon breſte deuocyon reuerence ſoo ofte ſhalle haue xx dayes pardon remyſſyon ſynnes alſo ſayde myghte power iheſu ſhewed ī ſubduȳge wycked ſpyrytes whiche nedeth longe treate manyfeſted innumerable foure euangeliſtes drede ieſu fledde hym caſte oute yt vexed iheſu ſomtyme legyon deuylles one man howe haue noo power ye ſuffraū ce iheſu playnly ſheweth ſtory wryten mathei viii marcy v many place goſpel thus iheſu hys owne perſon alſo diſcyples deuylles curſed ſpyrytes ſubgette obeyed wryten luce x domine ecia demonia ſub • cuintur nobis nomine tuo lorde ſayde diſcyples iheſu grete ioye theym ioyne theyre hōdes togyder maner prayenge goo forth wheder ſoo euer ledde broughte ſoo euer herde ſee ſholde withoute ſeaſynge call bleſſyd name ieſu iheſu ſholde euer theyr mouthes thyſe foure chyldren brought place ſoules tormē ted peyned fendes deuylles wold haue take thyſe ſayd chyldern caſte payne taught cryed called ieſu ieſu ieſu wycked ſpyrites anone tymes fled dredfull wyſyons broughte delectable pleſaūte place ſawe angellys holy ſoules dyuyne ſecretes ye vnſpekable ioyes god iheſu mannys wytte knowynge lyf comprehende leeſt prouynce therof ſene done chylderen broughte ayene ſayde hall clothed ayene ye ſayd relygyous man thenne reſtored theyre proper countreys viii daye ſayd rapte fyrſte ſpoken chylde fyrſte ſene foūden ſuberbes bery table honde thyſe vyſyons ſoo enprynted chyldys mynde alle tyme hys lyf myghte worldely myrthe come herte ony thynge cauſe hym laughe ¶a ſtorye lyke wryten nycholas purgatory reueled saynte patryk paſſed peryllys auoyted deuylles oonly ſayenge iheſu adiuua iheſu miſerere mei alſo deuyll ſayd ſaynt bernarde whan bad hym name iheſu go oute woman vexed ¶o nomen terrybyle iheſu iam cogis exire dredfull name iheſu thou conſtreyneſte departe ſayde fende merueylous thou hy name ieſu ſeen thy hye name iheſu ſoo dredde ſpyrytes theyr owne nature haue comparable knowlege connynge myghte vnto ony erthly creature dare ſpecyally ony cryſten creature ſoo bolde dyſpleaſe doo myghte contrary thy name iheſu ſaye contrarye ſaluacyon hym ware man beware remembre dredefulle worde iheſu ſhall ſay diſpleaſen hym lyuen wyth oute drede hym ite maledicti ignem eternum go ye curſed people frome euerlaſtyne fyre contrary greate ioye ſhall ſayd theym haue lyued drede loued hym timentes autem dominem glorificat sayth prophete iheſu gloryfyeth takethe hys blyſſe men dredynge hym wyth loue ſhall ſaye theym venite benedicti patris mei poſſidete paratum vobis regnum mathei xxv come ye bleſſyd fader take poſſeſſyon kyngedome heuen partenars blyſſe ioye ¶to name alle prophetes bere wytneſſe▪ ſo haue therby remyſſyon ſynnes ¶the myght vertue name iheſu ſayde ſhewed miraculorum operacione merueylous plente full myracles iheſu ſhewed wroughte hymſelfe haue done wrought name whyche ben innumerable manyfeſte bothe hym hys name thouſandes haue myraculouſly heled ſaued blynde neuer ſee haue theyre ſyghte dome theyr
