water ferd full herte iheſu dranke water anone hole ¶narracio ¶of deuoute yonge man alſo redde prayed god haue meanes howe myghte beſt loue hym contynue ſame loue angell appered toke hym byll wherein wryten iheſu fili dei propicius eſto michi peccatori iheſu ſone god mercy full ſynner open thy mouth ete ſayde thangell vertue iheſu name ye trynyte enclyned fauour thangellis ſerue helpe ye deuylles flee frome vexacyons ſwaged heuē opened ¶of alle thyſe yt ſayde yonge man vertuous lyuȳ ge experience ſayd ſtorye cōfyrmacyon ye premyſſes playne ye mouth lorde ieſus laſt chapytre marke nomine meo dicit ielꝰ demonia encient linguis loquuntur nouis ſeconde pryncypall ſayde iheſus name pyte ſocour mayſte thou ſhewe preche pyte mankynde ¶and ſocoure releue hym myſery iheſus wolde meke hymſelfe come man ſo procede yf thou wylte actes myſery pouerte ſapyence ſpecyally cyrcumſtaunce paſſyon fyrſt ought meke v hym dyſtroy pryde ſuffred heed crowned ſharpe thornes yt ſholde forgete hym proſperyte ryght hande peryſſhed wt grete boyſtous nayle haue pacyence aduerſyte beholde payne left hande dyſpyſe erthely vayne ioyes fete nayled towarde erthe myrour ſpectacle ſygne loueth ſpredde armes clyppe boweth heed kyſſe blyſſed body lyke haubergyon mayled droppes blode token pure hole loue mercyful iheſus pytefull iheſus ſuffred ſyde opened herte ſpere perced euery droppe precious blode ſhedde al mankynde thus iheſus hath verefyed prophecye wryten yſaye v quid vltra debui facere et non feci ¶what ought myght woldeſt thou man dyde haue done haue gyuen myn owne lyfe quia maiorem caritatem nemo habet c loue ſhewed gyue lyfe frende holy man ſaynt bernarde ſayth iheſus name paſſyon ſuffycient redempcyon man wolde loue haue man yet ſuffre agayne haue ſuffred ¶o vnkynde wretch worſe vnreaſonable creature yf mourne yt ſorow pyte iheſu thy paſſyon pyte v thou woldeſt tourmented deye v ¶and alſo yf thy holy blyſſed name iheſu pacyent aduerſytees redy ſuffre vexacyons trybulacyons iniuryes wronges repreues ſykeneſſes maner extremytees dyſeaſes yt wyth deſyre ioye wyth thyne apoſtles dyſcyples whome wrytē actuum quinto ibant gaudentes cō ſpectu conſilii quoniam digni habiti ſunt pro nomine iheſu contumeliam pati c ſaynt poule ſayth ſame book xx chapytre redy dey hys mayſters name ieſu paratus ſum mori haue thenne coū ſeylle bernarde ieſus euer thy honde thy mouth thy herte whome yu ſhalte dyrecte ye power bothe ſoule body iheſus iniquit ſemper ſit manu ſemper que ſet ore ſit ſinu quo tui omnes ſenſus dirigantur et actus ſayde laſte prȳcypall ſholde moue euery perſone premyſſes iheſus ſayde wyll ſhall thy rewarde ferre boue thy cytes iheſus ſaythe hys ſeruauntes venite ad omnes qui laboratis et onerati eſtis et ego reficiam vos come ye ſayth iheſus laboure take burden ſhall refreſſhe ſhalle rewarde ſhall recō penſe good iheſu ſurly wyth ioye blyſſe eternall fruycyon vyſyon knowelege bleſſyd trynyte ioye comprehendeth pleyſeth ſuffreth thynge dyſpleyſeth ioye ſhall neuer taken frome v quod nemo tollit vobis ſayth iheſus name none ſaued non eſt aliud nomen ſub celo datum hominibus quo oportet no ſaluos fieri actuū iiii iheſus thenne beſeche graunte v loue ſo folow mekeneſſe pacyence charyte maye come ye euer ſhall ſee preche prayſe abyde ye ioye neuer departe frome amen narracio ¶it redde man lyued many yeres dayes peaſyble wyſe hys wyfe accordynge theyre degree thenne enmye vertuous lyfe intyced theym temted broughte theym bothe vnto ſoule nable temptacion haue deſtroyed themſelf huſbōde knowynge wyues temptacyon ne wyfe huſbonde thys temptacyon troubled theym bothe ſoo moche yt neyther theym coude well ete drynke ne ſlepe euer ſyghynge heuy chere proceſſe tyme vnwoned conforte betwene demaunded aſked eche cauſe theyr heuines ſorow ſhewed man huſbonde many queſtions made woman ſatiſfyenge laſt anſwered ſayde certaȳly trouble daye nyghte erly late etynge drynkynge ſo euer doo occupye tempted hange myſelfe telle wyfe ſayde cauſe heuyneſſe ye neyther ete drynke ſlepe ye haue accuſtomed wyfe anſwered ſayde forſothe syre ſame temptacyon wyll anone thorugh inſtygacyon deuyll bothe conſented agreed perfourme falſe temptacōn anone made redy theyr halter theymſelfe ſholde execute curſed dede haue hanged theymſelfe ſholde begynne fowle horryble dede wyf ſayde huſbonde syre ſayde ſhewe neuer yette taſted ne haue drōke oure beſtewyne lete v ſayd ſhe drynke one therof deye cō ſente graunte ſayde huſbonde ſhe fette deſyred wyne whan theym bothe bleſſyd cuſtome whan ſholde take ony ſuſtenaū ce ſayde one drynke lete v drynke lyke termes thus drynke wyſe name iheſus comyn bleſſynge nomine patris et full et ſpiritus ſancti amen bibamus nomine ieſu ſhe receyuynge drynkynge wyne name iheſu anone theyr temptacyon boyded gone et fugit dyabolus deuyl fledde frome thenne cōtryte ſhewede confeſſyd theyr ſynne openly magnefyenge gloryous heuenly name iheſus ¶bernardus habes anima mea reconditum electuarium cum vaſculo vocabuli quod eſt ieſus quod nulli vn quam ̄ peſti inefficax inuenitur narracio ¶it wreten paynym beynge conuerted criſten fayth wherfore deuylles ſoo moche enuye vexed hym bodely hurte ſenſyble bete hym many tymes ſpecyally bedde thenne man taughte holy manſowed name iheſus foure corner ſhetes hys bedde deuylles accuſtomed come ſenſyble wyſe chābre haue bete vexed hym ¶but whā nere towarde bedde ſterted abacke ſtood ferde ſayde mowynge croked countenaunce ha iheſu ha iheſu thus man ſaued frome betynge ¶he thenne vnderſtondȳ ge ye vertue name iheſꝰ made ordeyned lōge • pere faſtened name iheſus thende whā ſomeuer curſed ſpyrytes apperede vnto hym trouble vexe hym helde putte ſpere wyth name iheſus agaynſte ye deuylles fledde ranne awaye alle cōfuſed thus thys man noo theym troubled ne aſſayled euer delyuered fro alle temptacyons trouble theym vertue holy ſwete name iheſu ¶narracio wolde ieſu yt mē coude folowe loue ieſu knyght yt rede whiche wente iheruſalem whan come thyder vyſyted ordre thoſe place ony acte dede done lorde iheſus byrthe vnto place aſcencyon thenne conſyderynge mo place vyſyte folowe iheſu onely heuen iheſus aſcended conſyderacyon ſo grete deſyre affeccyon iheſu ſoule hym departed body wyſe lerned men vnderſtande man ioye yt pylgrymage iheſu dyſceaſed made herte opened wryten therin ieſus amor meus iheſus loue ſayth ſaynt auguſtyn de ciuitate dei libro decimo octauo capitulo quadrageſimo nono quid amicius quid dulcis nominare nomē ieſu frendlyer louelyer ſweter name iheſu example narracio ¶there woman thynſtygacion ennemy euyll aungell herte fell ſuche obſtynate opynyon ſhe noo wyſe ony perſuacyon wolde forgyue certayne treſpaces doone good holy man truſtynge holy name iheſu extreme ſekenes wrote holy name iheſus forheed anone vertue hygh name iheſus wrought ſo molefyed melted herte wt power herte ſhe forgaue treſpaces aſkynge iheſu forgyuenes induracyon obſtynacion thankynge hym remedy wherfore euery man ought honoure ſanctyfye halowe daye reuerence holy ſwete name iheſu amen ¶sequitur de ſancto laurencio good frendes ſuche day ye ſhal haue ſaynt laurence day goddes owne holy martyr martrydome maximus ſayth ſhyneth holy chyrche lyghtneth worlde wherfore ye ſhal come god holy chirche ſhal faſt euen ¶this ſaynt holy lyuynge grete cō paſſyon ferynge saynt auſtyne ſayth enſaumple doynge commendable prechinge techynge therfore ſaynt laurence gaue cryſten people ſhewe agaynſte malyce mekeneſſe agaynſte coueytyſe largeſſe agaynſt perſecucion tribulacyō loue ſwetnes ¶whan sixtus ••• e ſpayne brought laurence hym rome made hym archedekyn ſerue holy chyrche poure people thenne emperoure enuye hym purpoſed hym dethe thenne laurence ſhewe mekeneſſe agaynſt malyce enquyred faſt poure people wente vnto gaue mete drynke clothes ſo came wydowes housthere many pore people lodged ye whiche wydowe longe ſeke hede ache thenne laurence compaſſyon made hole mekely waſſhed poore people fete ſerued mete drynke herde poore man beſyde place blynde went thyder heled hym euer emperoure ſhewed malyce hym gaue hym mekeneſſe holy deuocyon ſhewed alſo agaynſt couycyſe largeneſſe whan pope sixtus hadde taken laurence treſoure holy chirche kepe gyue hadde moſt nede ¶then̄e bleſſed laurence folowed mayſter ſayd sancte pater noli derelinquere holy fader forſake notte haue deled treſoure thou tokeſt vnto wherfore goo notte thou vnto thy paſſyon alone lete go haue ſerued god gyder ſo lete v ſuffre dethe gyder ſayd pope wyll go fore thou ſhalte come ſuffre penaunce may olde thou arte yonge mayſt ſuffre therfore make redy▪ grete tormente ordeyned thenne ſome herde laurence ſpeke treſoure thenne emperoure ſente laurence ſayd oſtende michi theſauros eccleſie shewe treſoure chirche ellys thou ſhalte put ſuche tormente thou ſhalte fayne delyuer ¶then pope sixtus ſaynt laurence came vnto treſoure ye ſhall ¶we rede yt holy man named orygines conuerted phylyp emperoure rome thenne emperoure ſent knyght fraūce wc moche people ouer come fraūce knyght called decyꝰ ſhorte tyme made fraunce ſubiectes vnto emperoure whan emperoure phylyp herde decius hadde done ſo well greate worſhyp decius thanke hym iourney themperour toke hym fewe men rode rome agaynſt decius welcome hym home thenne decius ſawe emperoure dyde hym ſo grete worſhyp thought drede loue thoughte emperoure hym ſelfe ſo nyght nexte themprour lay bed ſlepynge decyus ſlewe toke people rome wt hȳ whā romayns ſenatours herde drede loue made decius emperour whan phylyps ſone herde telle yt fader dede wyſe ferde leeſt deciꝰ wolde haue ſlayne hȳ gaue faders treſour holy chirche bare pope ſixtꝰ laurēce prayēg hȳ ſo ye deciꝰ ſlew hȳ ſholde dele treſour holy chirche poore people nede thenne decius ſlewe phylyps ſone feere leeſt wolde haue venged faders dethe whan come mannes ſtate treaſoure pope syxtus laurence treaſoure put laurence pryſon thenne man hyght lucyllus pryſon yt grete wepynge loſt ſyght thenne laurence made hym ſe agayne cryſtned hȳ wherfore many blynde men woman came laurence theyr ſyght thenne themperour ſent laurence delyuer ye treaſure thenne prayed hym thre dayes reſpyte wolde ſhewe hym treaſour theſe thre dayes laurence lete pryſon went gadred poore people gyder myght fynde blynde lame croked thyrde day brought themperoure palays ſayd lo euerlaſtynge treaſour wyl neuer fayle wyl endure euer heuen ſhewed laurence largeneſſe agaynſt couetyſe deled goddes ſake goodes rycheſſes hadde myght haue ſpente vayne pleaſures worldly operacyons yf hadde wolde alſo tourmente in paſſyon ſhewed perfyte loue feruent ſwetenes then̄e emperour grete furoure anger commaunded brynge forthe maner inſtrumentes tourmentrye ſcourges nayles ſtones ſalte pytche brymſtone brennȳ ge cole yren ſhaftes barres yren gredyrons cōmaunded ſholde ſpente worne vpon laurence wolde ſhewe treaſoure forſake god beleued adoure doo ſacryfyce mawmettes ydolles thenne ſayd laurence thou vnblyſſed man theſe mete drynkes haue euer deſyred ſought ryght ſwete delycyous mete drynkes pleaſeth ſatyſfyeth thy body ſo theſe tourmentes pleaſen ſoule maken ſtronge myghty ſuffre paſſyon lordis ſake themperour wroth commaūded bete hym ſcourges full knottes leue tyll blode ranne downe euery ſyde layde cheynes yren brennȳge ſydes yt brenned fleſſhe fro ye bone euer laurence thanked god hertely decius wode wo ſayde thoughe yu wyth thy wytchecrafte ſcorneſt tormentys yet thou ſholdeſte ſcorne cōmaunded ayene bete hȳ whyppes knottes lede tyll bone bare thenne laurence helde vp hede prayenge god thenne came voyce fro heuen ſayde thou muſte ſuffre tormentes paſſyon loue deciꝰ herde hymſelfe thou ſhall come greate ioye blyſſe thenne ſayd decius people ye maye alle fendes come cōforte hym go bete hym ayene ſcourges knyght themperours hyghte romanus ſawe angell ſhete ſylke come wype laurence ſydes forſoke emperoure became dyſcyple ſaynt laurence laurence anone cryſtened hym thenne decius made ſmyte romanus hede thenne decyus dyde make greate fyre ſet gerdyren theron roſte laurēce threſted hym downe fyre forkis thenne laurence loked vpon thēperoure ſayd yu wretche yt ſyde roſted ynough ete therof whyle ſyde roſteth drede thy tormentis caſt eyen vp god ſayde lorde iheſu take ſpyryte ſo yelde vp gooſt thenne tormentours went theyr way left body lyenge thenne come cryſten people toke body beryed wyth grete lamentacyon thus laurence ſhewed mekenes ayenſte malyce largenes ayenſt couetyſe ayenſt paſſyon loue ſwetneſſe grete loue god made hym ſet noughte tormentes body saynte gregory telleth preeſt yt hyghte ſtaculus beſy mende chirche ſaynte laurence yt deſtroyed lombardes wanted brede werke men made moche ſorowe therfore prayed god ſaynt laurence beſely helpe loked ouen foūde full newe whyte brede wende wold haue ſerued thē weke founde inough tyme werke makynge ¶narracio ¶we fynde yt emperoure curſed man lyuynge whan dede came legyon fendes fetche hym came holy heremytes cell made greate noyſe heremyte greate meruayle therof opened wyndow ſpake one came behynde aſked name god ſayde fendes ſente emperoure dede loke yf myghte haue theyr rewarde thermyte cōmaunded theym come agayne hym knowe ſped dyde ſoo ſayde ſynnes layde balaunce nye ouercome thenne come brennynge deken laurence layde greate pot balaunce drewe vp togyder pot grete chalyce themperour made worſhyppe ſaynte laurence thus ye maye lerne ſuffre ayenſte enuyous peple alſo mede largenes gyue haue nede ioye meryte ſuffre tribulacyon perſecucōn dyſeaſe pacyently lerne holy martyr saynt laurence lete v take hym myrrour praye hym wyll mediatoure god v maye come euerlaſtynge blyſſe amen ¶de aſſumptione beate marie virginis good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue aſſū pcyon lady called ſo daye ſone toke vp heuen body ſoule crowned quene heuen aungelles heuen came fetche vp aungelles ſyngyng came proceſſyon agaynſt roſes lylyes paradyſe token ſhe roſe lylye floure woman dyde homage aungelles ſayntes heuen made ioye melody worſhyp honoure ſo holy chirche maketh mynde aſſumpcyon yet goſpell daye maketh mencyon two ſyſters martha maudelayne ſayth thus intrauit iheſus quoddā caſtellum et mulier quedā c ¶iheſus entred caſtell woman called martha toke hym hous ſhe ſyſter called mary ſhe ſatte cryſtes fete herde hym ſpeke thenne martha beſy ſerue cryſte ſhe ſayd hym syr bydde ſyſter aryſe helpe anſwered cryſt maria meltorē patrē elegit q̄ nō auferet ab ea mary hathe choſen better parte yt ſhall taken awaye fro theſe ben wordes goſpell yt daye wordes oure lady ſemynge yt redeth ſaynt ancelme ſayth may ſe yt goſpel perteyneth lady lyuynge ſhe caſtell yt iheſus entred ryght caſtel hathe dyuers propryetes longeth vnto caſtell ſholde myghty ſtronge▪ ryghte ſo oure bliſſed lady woman euer woman frayle feble eaſy ouercome oure lady ſtronge caſtell agaynſtode ye cautelles fendes engynes put beſyde tymes ryght caſtell hathe fyrſt depe dytche ryght ſo lady depe mekenes ſtrengthe caſtell ſoo moche ſhe paſſed vertue mekeneſſe wherfore god choſe moder ſone al womē therto cryſt bereth wytneſſe ſaynge thus quia reſpexit humilitatem ancille ſue god behelde mekenes handmayden generacyons ſhall bleſſe dytche yf full water ſtrenger caſtel water compaſſyon man ſholde haue ſynnes people dyſeaſe water lady vpon dytche lyeth drawe brydge ſhal drawen vp agaynſt enemyes lette downe agaynſt frendes brydge vnderſtonden obedyence ryght man ſhall lete downe brydge enemye thoughe byd hym lyke wyſe man ſholde lete fende come ſoule though tempte hym none boden ony thynge helpe ſoucoure vnto ſoule ſhall lete downe brydge obedyence ſoner better dyde oure lady whan aūgell gabryell tolde concepcyon ſone ſhe lete downe brydge none rylle ſhe knewe wheder frende enemye ſayd ſhe ſholde contryue mayde kepe vowe chaſtyte ſhe made fore ſhe herde ſhe lete downe brydge obedyence ſayd ecce ancylla domini lo goddes owne honde mayde done thy worde caſtell treble thryes double walled fyrſt wall betokeneth wedlocke fyrſte ſhe wyfe vnto ioſeph elles iewes wolde haue ſtoned lechoure yf ſhe hadde contynued without wedlocke ſo ferther wall betokeneth pacyence ynner vyrginyte whiche clene maydēhode lytell worthe ſtrengthed wall pacyence lytell helpe maydenheed lytel worth nothynge ſuffre perſecucyon dyſeaſe way playnynge grudgynge claterer iangeler curſer waryer ſcolde tonge theſe defende maydenhede rather caſt downe maydenhode ſholde fewe wordes ſhe ſpeketh ſholde honoure worſhyp bothe perſone preſēce olde englyſſhe mayden ſholde ſeen herde vertue lady ſaynt bernarde ſayth rede al ye goſpel ouer yu ſhalt fȳ de yt lady ſpake lyfe ony foure tymes fyrſt gabryell ſeconde elyzabeth thyrde owne ſone temple fourthe weddynge cane galyle thus muſt wall pacyence defende wall maydenhode wall maydenhede yf well kept paſſynge bede ſayth wedlocke hye well kepte yet wydowhede hyer vyrgynyte paſſeth al hath mooſt worſhyp heuen paſſynge walle kepte lady ſhe clene frewyll vowe ſhe degre paſſynge al maydens euer euer ſhall ſhe bothe mayde moder caſtell gate betokeneth fayth ryght unpoſſyble man go wall ſtele ryght ſoo impoſſyble man pleaſe god without faythe fayth lady paſſynge ſemeth impoſſyble woman conceyue without carnal concupyſcence man neuer ſeen techynge aungell ſhe beleued ſoo came cryſte entred gate byleue ye body lady gate toure aboue whiche betokeneth charyte aboue thynge vertue lady well may ſhe called caſtell ryght maner people fle caſtell olde yonge drede enemyes ſo moche leeſt chylde crye ſpeke ferde ony thynge anone cryed lady lady ſocoure helpe ſhe ſocoure helpe yonge olde leſſe ſykeneſſe helthe holy gooſt capytayne caſtell knyghtes ben holy aungellys goth oure lady bothe nyght daye caſtell ben two maner ſyſters martha mary magdalene martha martha beſy receyue oure ſauyoure iheſu cryſt hous oure lady receyued hȳ body ix monethes ſhe fedde hym came poore naked worlde ſhe gaue hym mete drynke pappes ſoo fedde hym whan naked ſhe clothed nouryſſhed hym whan ſyke kynde youth ſhe heled hym whan bounde honde foot cradell pryſon ſhe came hym vnboūde hym toke hȳ healed ſores mylke pappes whā dede ſhe holpe burye hym tombe thus ſhe fulfylled offyce martha perfourmyng vii werkes mercy yet ſhe many tymes troubled herte whan ſhe muſt bere hym froo countre coūtre ful mawmettes ſhe knewe man whan ſhe ſawe hym taken ſtryped naked beten ſcorges body ranne wt ſtremes blode nayled c •••• e ſo done deth grete trouble thus oure lady actyue goſpel telleth ſhe gaue ſoo grete delyte ſones wordes ſhe bare herte lyfe techynge cryſt people perfourme ſame lyuinge moche may god wyll gyue theym grace ſerue lady ſhall ſhewe enſample ¶narracio ¶we fynde clerke loued lady wel redde beaute grete luſt ſe prayed beſyly myght one ſe deyed thenne ye laſt came aungell ſayd hym thou ſerueſt lady ſo wel thou ſhalt haue thy prayer one thynge tell yf yu ſe worlde thou ſhalte leſe thy ſyght grete clerenes thenne ſayd wyll well ſoo yt may ſe thenne ſayd aungel come ſuche place yu ſhal ſe thenne gladde thought wolde hyde one eye loke soo whan came yt place layde hande ouer ye one eye ſawe yt eye ſo came lady ſawe ſhe went way anone blynde eye ſawe thenne ſyght lyked hym ſo well wolde fayne ſe agayne prayed nyght day myght ſe agayne thenne ſayd aungell yf thou ſe agayne thou ſhalte leſe ſyght eye ſayd wyll well though thouſande eyen come ſuche place thou ſhalte ſe ſo whan came ſawe thenne ſayd lady good ſeruaunt whan thou ſawe fyrſt yu loſt one thyn eyen wylt thou whan yu haſt loſte eye thenne ſayd dere lady wyll well though thouſande eyen thenne ſayd lady thou haſt ſo grete lykynge yu ſhalt haue thy ſyght bothe thyn eyen agayne well euer yu haddeſt better ſo then̄e ſerued lady euer lyues ende wente euerlaſtyng blyſſe whiche almyghty god brynge v amen ¶de ſancto bartholomeo appoſtolo good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue feeſt ſaynt bartylmewe goddes owne appoſtle ye ſhall come chirche dyuyne ſeruyce worſhyp god ſaynt bartylmewe ye ſhall vnderſtonde bartylmewe aſmoche ſaye filius ſuſpendentis whiche ſaye ſone hangynge vpon vpō water ye ſhall vnderſtande god hangeth vpon water two wayes fyrſt whan hanged vpon cloudes fyrmament tyll ſeeth tyme lette downe another waye hangeth vpon water whan man woman ſory theyr ſynnes wepynge ſore treſpace bytterly god taketh teres hangeth hye hylle heuen ſayntes heuen may haue ſyght grete ioye al ſayntes aungelles ben heuen whan maye ſe man woman hathe done amyſſe many treſpaces forſake theyr ſynne therfore teres man woman ſory theyr ſynnes maner quenched fyre helle theſe teres ſpeketh iohan gryſoſtome ſayth thou teere arte mekely let oryſon prayer good deuocyon thy myght ſoo grete thou gooſt heuen takeſt worde iewes mouthe makynge hym torne ſaluacyon waye dampnacyon alſo thou makeſt thyn accuſers dombe fendes ſo thou quencheſt fyre helle fendes made redy agaynſt thy comynge thus god hangeth vpon water thenne bycauſe ſaynt bartylmewe goddes ſone ben ſerueth hym hangynge vp foure wayes deuocyon holy oryſons prayenge faith monycyon ſuffrynge paſſyon hangynge god warde deuoute oryſons whiche ſaſayd mouth thought hert ſo herte alwaye hangynge vp towarde god bothe worde dede preeſt ſayth maſſe surſum co • da holde vp hertes thus holy ſaynt barthylmew euer herte god deuocion ¶narracio ¶we fynde wryten thus kneled hōdred tymes day hondred tymes nyght grete deuocyon god ſholde bewery trauayle lorde ſent aungell euer ſhewe hym kepe hym thus hanged vp holy oryſons prayenge alſo hanged faythful monicyon wyſe god gaue hym ſo grete power ouer fendes holy monycyon ſuſpended theym wheder man woman alſo mawmettes fynde wryten ſaynt barthylmew came ynde temple whiche temple ymage therein fende mawmette called aſtaroth ymage made golde thenne ye fende therein ſpake hym dyde hȳ worſhyp ſuche wordes ſpake made people byleue god yet make byleue heled ſyke men woman bothe blynde lame many dyuerſe ſykeneſſe caſt vpon tofore hym ſelfe ſemȳge heled hym ſuche ſykeneſſe god ſente vpon theym coude helpe temple full ſyke people brought mawmette hole ſone barthylmew came ye tēple ſuſpēded ye fendes power yt myght hele mā ¶now nother god called bauruth aſkyd hȳ theyr god gaue none anſwere ſayd barthtlmew ye appoſtle god hath boū de hȳ ſo ſore yt dare one ſpeke tolde hȳ ye fetures barthylmew ſayd knoweth euery worde ſay hath aungel god wt hym telleth hym thynges euer ſayd doone hȳ ouer though ye ſeke hym ye ſhall fynde hym yf wyll hymſelfe thenne went home agayne ſought barthylmewe myght fynde hym thenne barthylmew walked amonge people madde man yt fende within hȳ anone cryed barthylmew goddes owne appoſtle thy prayer bynde ſore bren̄e alſo thenne ſayd barthilmew holde thy pea yu fende go man worde fende wente waye lefte man anone hole thenne happed ſo yt kynge ye cyte doughter madde ſore bounden chaynes harme ſhe dyde amonge people whan kynge herde man heled ſent barthylmew prayenge hym wolde hele doughter ſo dyde then̄e barthylmew preched ſo kynge torned kynge cryſtned thenne anone commaunded drawe doune mawmettes temple thenne ye people teyed rope ymages neckes wolde haue drawen downe mawmettes coude ye fendes ſo ſtronge thenne barthylmew cōmaū ded fendes come ymages pull poudre ſo dyde hadde power wt ſtande commaundement ſo brake temple ſo ful ſyke people barthylmew prayed god myght hole anone hole euerychone thenne came aungell god ſente heuen anone ſyght ye people temple ſhone ſo bryght tongue coude tell flewe temple foure partes temple made ſygne croſſe fyngers walles ſayd ryght people ben hole theyr ſykeneſſe ſo ſhall temple clenſed fylthe ſynne fendes craft hath therin wyl ſhewe ſame fende ye haue worſhypped god then̄e fende appered lyke man ynde blacke made curſed noyſe thenne people began fle fere ſo lothely thenne ſayd aungell make ſuche ſygne croſſe forehedes afrayde hȳ thenne anone ſyght people aungell vnboū de fende bad hym go neyther ſterynge man ne beeſt euer tyll daye dome neuer dyſeaſe people thenne fende went way aungell ſtyed heuen thenne ye kynge wyfe doughter meyne moche people torned faythe barthylmewe cryſtned theym thus ſaynt barthylmew hanged faythfull monycyon ſuſpended ye fendes power myght thynge alſo hanged vp ſuffrynge paſſyon whan byſſhop temple ſawe people almooſt tourned cryſten fayth lefte fendes mawmetry went vnto ye cyte kynge called aſtrages broder kynge polymyes cō playned hym ſore ſayd yt man come hym yt called barthylmew torned broder people fayth yt ſet theyr goddes drawen downe brake halowed ye temple onely cryſt cauſe prayed hȳ helpe thenne ſent kynge thouſande men barthylmew whan barthylmew come aſked hym hadde torned broder made hym beleue deed man whiche hanged vpon croſſe thenne ſayd ſaynt barthylmew haue bounde god thy broder beleued ſhewed fende yf thou may ſo god wyll byleue thou dooſt kynge commaunded hange bartylmewe croſſe longe torment hym theron toke hym downe fleyed hym quycke ſmote heed thenne came cryſten people buryed hym grete reuerence worſhyp thus hanged vp grete compaſſion ſuffrynge ¶narracio ¶we rede geſtis romanorum whan frederyk ye emperour deſtroyed grete cyte therin fayr chirche ſaynt bartylmewe dyuers ſayntes good holy man came cyte ſawe grete company men ſtandynge togyder man grete meruayll aſked theyr counſayll ſayd hym agayne ſaynt bartylmewe ſayntes chirches cyte deſtroyed toke theyr counſayl myght themperour ful purpoſe ſholde come god anſwere dedes ſo emperour deyed foule dethe dampned alſo wryten lyfe ſaynt good lake fyrſte enhabyted crowlande fennes fyrſt daye came theder ſaynt bartylmewes daye prayed holy appoſtle patrone agaynſt wycked ſpyrytes place called inhabytacyon fendes durſt man dwel fendes whan holy man come theder almooſt loſt wyttes fere grace mynde ſaynt bartylmewe prayed hertely helpe ſocoure anone came ſaȳt bartylmew cōmaunded fendes go place thenne fendes made grete horryble noyſe wente theyr waye ſaynge ala ala nowe haue loſte myghte habytacyon ſhall go hell euermore ſo ſorowynge waylynge wente theyr waye thenne holy man thanked god ſaynt bartylmewe grete helpe ſocoure hadde done hym ye maye ſe vnderſtonde holy appoſtle euer redy wyll calle hym good deuocyon wyll helpe theyr nede amen sequit̄ ſermo de natiuitate glorioſiſſime virginis marie worſhypfull frendes ſuche daye ye ſhal haue natiuite oure lady yt whan ſhe borne ye ſhall faſt euen come god holy chirche worſhyp lady ſaynt mary ioachim fader anne moder man tell ye ioye yt ioachym anne theyr hertes whan oure lady borne prayed xxx yere god nyghte daye dealed moche almeſſe good dedes yt dyde hadde reuelacyon god yt ſholde holy pleaſe god alſo ye birthe lady ye repreef yt bareynes ſholde put awaye ſo anne wente forth amō ge woman yt byrthe lady gladded yt fader moder wherfore god ſente theym fruyte theyr bodyes grace kynde ye neyghboures came conforted anne called doughter mary aſ ye aūgell bad ſhe borne ye ſhall vnderſtande ye holy chirche worſhippeth iii byrthes one lorde another lady iii ſaynt iohan baptiſt shewynge openly yt euery body yt wyll ſaued muſte thryes borne fyrſt moder worlde ye ii ſȳne water waſſhynge ye iii worlde ioye paſſynge fyrſt betokeneth lady ye ii ſaȳt iohan baptyſt ye thyrde lorde iheſu cryſte thyſe thre byrthes grete ioye myrthe ſeen herde though woman haue grete payne byrthe childe may well byleue ſaynt anne ladyes moder hadde ſo byrth childe lady ſhe halowed moders wombe holy borne holy euer whan ſhe born wened thre yere age ioachym anne frendes brought mary cyte ieruſalem tofore temple made theyr vowe tofore thenne temple ſtode hyll xv ſteyres vp dore ſo lefte mary nethermeſt ſtayere whyle made theym redy doo theyr offrynge thenne wente mary vppermooſt grece herſelf knelynge downe made prayer god ſhe grete age holy ghoſt euer gaf grace alſo god ſente angell kepe teche whan fader moder offred went home left ſhe chaūged cher • gaf herſelf ſpyrytuel occupacyon euery daye morowe vndern ſhe prayer vnderen tyll none ſhe occupyed craft weuynge clothes temple none mete drynke brought ſhe gaf poore peple deuocyon tyll angell brought mete thus ſhe lyued ſo clene ſo honeſtly felawes called quene maydens whan ony man ſpake mekely ſhe lowted heed ſayd deo gracias worde comen mouth therfore ſhe lykened ſpycers ſhop ſhe ſmelleth ſwete preſence holy ghoſt habundaunce vertues ſhe ſholde bere kyng vertues ¶and thus byrth dayly ioye good cryſten people ¶how daye fyrſt founde grete clerke iohan bellet telleth holy man prayed god often nyght nyght deuocyons herde ſonge aungell oure lady borne moder yere soo nyght herde melodye ayere wherfore holy man prayed god yt myght haue wyttynge cauſe herd ye melody nyght nomore yere came aungell hȳ ſayd yt nyght oure lady borne moder therfore melodye made heuē tyme thenne wente pope tolde hym aungell ſayd thenne pope commaunded day ſholde halowed euer thus came feeſt fyrſt holy chyrche alſo oure lady borne water waſſhynge cryſtnynge whan lorde iheſu cryſt baptyſed ye water flom iordan lady xii apoſtles ye tyme cryſtned therfor ryght lorde folowed olde newe lawe felle mā ryght ſo lady fulfylled lawes felle woman ſame cryſtenynge ſone toke ryght name ſhe bothe ye goſpel telleth whan lorde iheſus cryſtned fad heuen ſpake ſayd hic eſt filius meus c welbeloued ſone called ieſus goddes ſone fro ye tyme lady called wyf ioſeph yt ſhe called mode iheſu moche worſhyppe thyrde tyme lady born ioye paſſynge whan ſhe ſholde paſſe worlde ſone came wt grete multytude angel brought heuen moche ioye crowned quene heuen empreſſe helle lady al ye worlde ſo ſhe euerlaſtynge blyſſe ¶narracio fynde lady ther iewe born fraunce came englonde dyuers mater yt people came glouceſter bryſtowe ſo wolde go wyltſhyre take way theues ledde olde hous boū de poſt handes behynde hym ſo lete hym nyght laſt fell ſlepe ſawe fayre woman clothed whyte neuer ſeen ſuche euen therwith awoke founde hym ſelfe loſe thenne ſawe lady ſo bryght thought ſhe paſſed ſonne ſayd arte thou ſhe ſayd mary yu thy nacyon dyſpyſed ſay yt neuer bare goddes ſone come brynge thyn erroure pryſon thou art therfore come thou ſtande yonder ſtone loke downewarde ſo dyde ſawe horryble paynes hell nye mynde thenne ſayd lady hym theſe paynes ordeyned thoſe wyll beleue ſonnes paſſyon fayth holy chyrche yet come forthe ſe ſhe ſet hym hye hyll ſhewed hym place grete ioye myrth ſo moche yt rauyſſhed wt ſyght thenne ſayd lady lo theſe ben ordeyned al thoſe beleueth thyncarnacyon cryſt yt borne clene mayden ſone ſhedde blode mankynde haſt thou ſeen bothe ioye payne choſe whiche thou haſt leuer thenne went moche nyght wyſt way walked forth ye morow came bathe cryſtned named iohan holy man come agayne purpoſe lady tyme ioachym offred lady temple byſſhop kepe ſafe warde tyll ſhe xii yeres aege thenne muſt byſſhop ordeyne huſbande thenne lete crye aboute countree kynges lordes gentyles without wyues ſholde come certayne daye knowe beſte worthy wedde ye fayre mayden floure maydens ryght lylye whyte fayre amonge breers floures ryght ſo lady among maydens whan came iheruſalem ſe ye mayden beſt blood worlde byſſhoppe ordeyned olde ſtaffe aſſhe kepte ye temple many yere worme eten ſayd whiche handeleth ſtaffe burgeneth bere floures ſholde haue mayden ſhe brought forth temple people myght ſe bad byſſhop brynge forthe ſtaffe whan ony man handeled badde hym holde vp hye people mighte ſe yf burgened wente kynges prynces lordes knyghtes ſquyres gentylmen wolde fyrſte daye ſeconde daye ſo iii daye ſholde make ende thenne came olde man temple herde ſawe thought go ſe people dydde came theder ſtode ferre corner loked mayden thenne thought hymſelfe wolde handle ye ſtaffe mayde ſo paſſynge fayr ſo paſſynge olde thenne came whyte douue ſatte vpon heed golden bylle fete ſhone lyke bryght burnyſſhed golde people ſawe ſome wolde haue caught myght byſſhop ware badde ioſeph come vp hym anone ¶and ioſeph ſayd naye ſhe ſhe yonge olde gouerne eſtate ſayd ye byſſhop handle ſtaffe anone done ſo flouryſſhed bare fruyte thenne byſſhop gladde 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 ioſeph ſory haue fully purpoſed neuer haue wyfe byſſhop wedded worſhypfully badde ioſeph take home hym ſo dyde ſoone holy ghoſt lyghted gretynge aungell gabryell ſo began ware grete chylde ioſeph loked vpon thought haue gone awaye pryuely leue alone came aūgell ioſeph badde ſholde take mary kepynge ſtudye therupon leue ſuche thoughtes goddes wyll god hȳ ſelfe wyll ſo lefte al ſuche fantaſyes kepte well euery man ſholde wyfe ¶de exaltatione ſancte crucis good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue holy rode daye whiche ye ſhall come chirche worſhyp hym done vpon croſſe daye called exaltacio ſancte crucis exaltacyon croſſe ſaye lyftynge vf ye holy croſſe whan ſaynt eleyne ſet croſſe iheruſalem cryſten people dyde grete worſhyp came kyng perſe yt called coſdre toke croſſe hym made cyte bare bare waye myght wente temple toke treſour iewels precyous ſtones bare awaye thus curſyd man dyde deſtroye many kyngdomes ſo bare holy croſſe owne countree themperour eraclius herde therof full wroth ſory ſente coſdre trete wt hym eraclius cryſten man coſdre anſwered curſedly ſayd wolde treate tyll peple forſake cryſtendom ſacrefyce mawmettes emperour eraclius betoke god gadred hym ooſt peple fyght wt curſyd kyng coſdre hopynge god gete holy croſſe ayen whan curſyd kyng coſdre came fell ſuche fantaſye madneſſe toke ſone al gouernaūce reame lete make hous hymſelf maner awter lyke vnto heuen made ſhynynge golde precyous ſtones ſet hymſelf myddes chayr golde commaunded peple ſholde calle hym god ſo ſate holy croſſe ryght honde ſtede ſone left honde tame kocke ſtede holy ghoſt hymſelf myddes ſtede trynyte thus ſat lyke madde man ſone herde eraclius comynge wente ayenſt hym met hym grete water ouer whiche water brydge thaſſent theyr ooſtes two chyef captayns myddes brydge ſholde fyght theym bothe endes ye brydge ſholde drawen vp whiche yt vyctory ſholde haue kyngdomes eraclius ſo full fayth croſſe truſted prayer people yt ouercome enmye coſdres peple ſterynge holy ghoſt torned fayth free wyll themſelf whan cryſtened wente eraclius wt ooſtes ye olde kyng coſdre ſatte trone ſayd hym thus cauſe thou haſt doo worſhyp holy croſſe thou ſhalt choſe yf thou wylt cryſtened haue thy kyngdome ayen lytell trybute reſt pea elles deed forſoke cryſtened anone eraclius ſmote heed made crye yt treſour ſholde dealed amonge men precyous ſtones iewels ſholde kepte reſtore chirches deſtroyed bare croſſe ieruſalem whan came mount olyuete towardes cyte ieruſalem rydynge trapped hors wolde haue ryden ye cyte ieruſalem ſodenly yates felle togyder playne wall thenne gretely aſtonyed meruayled gretely vengeaunce made grete mone then̄e came aungell ſtode vpon gate ſayd quando rex noſter c whan kynge heuen came way theſe gate towarde paſſyon rode trapped hors clothe golde mekely ſymple aſſe gyuynge enſample mekenes people thenne aungell went way thenne kynge deuocion yt coude myght anone dyde clothes ſhyrte went bare fote bare legged thenne gate opened went gate iheruſalem ſo temple offred croſſe agayne thenne ye grete ioye people croſſe grete myracles yt god ſhewed worſhypped afore worſhyppe croſſe caſt downe lyft vp wherfore daye called exaltacyon holy croſſe ſaynt auſtyn ſaythe croſſe fyrſt grete ſpyte velony grete worſhyppe ſo emperoures kynges worſhyp grete reuerence ¶narracio ¶we hede legenda aurea iewe came chyrch defaute man chyrche went rode grete enuy cryſt cut rodes throte anone blode ſterte clothes ſo clothes al reed blode thenne hydde rode preuy place went home cryſten man mette hym ſayd hym thou haſt ſlayne ſome mā haſt thou done hym iewe ſayd nay ye cryſten man ſayd thy clothes ben blody hym thenne iewe kneled downe ſayd forſothe god theſe cryſten people beleue vpon grete vertue tolde hym done cryed mercy herte ſoo cryſtened holy man euer ſo wente vnto euerlaſtynge ioy blyſſe whiche god brynge v al amen quatuor temporum good frendes weke ye ſhall haue ymbre dayes wedneſday fryday ſaterdaye yt whiche dayes calixtus 〈◊〉 ordeyned foure tymes yere conuenable aege faſt certayn cauſes ye ſhal olde faders faſted foure tymes ye yere agaynſt foure hye ſolempne feeſtes yf wyll ſhewe v good chyldrē muſt faſte folowe ſame rule vſed therfore faſt foure tymes fyrſt marche ſeconde whytſontyde thyrde bytwene herueſt ſede tyme fourth cryſtmas marche tyme yt dryeth vp moyſture ye erthe wherfore faſt yt tyme drye erthe body humures yt nedeful body ſoule ye tyme humour lechery tempteth man mooſt ony tyme yere alſo faſt whytſontyde gete grace ye holy ghooſt yt may loue charyte god worlde caritas cooꝑit multitudinē pctō rum charyte couereth ye multytude ſynnes alſo muſt faſt haue mekenes hertes put away pryde yt renneth within v alſo faſt bytwene herueſt ſeed tyme haue grace gader fruytes good werkes ye hous conſcyence ſo enſample good lyuynge amonge people yt comyn wt bothe ryche poore alſo faſt wynter ſle ſtynkynge wedes ſynne foule erth fleſſhely luſtes yt maketh good aūgels good people wt drawe fro v ryght nettle brēneth roſes floures growe nye hym ſame wyſe vycyous man woman ſtereth ſetteth fyre yt ben company theſe cauſes faſt foure tymes yt yere euery tyme thre dayes betokeneth thre ſpecyall vertues helpeth man grace faſtynge deuout prayenge almeſſe dede doynge opynyon moche people theſe dayes ben called ymbre dayes bycauſe elder faders wolde theſe dayes ete breed cake made vnder aſſhes ſo etynge reduced theyr mynde yt aſſhes ſoo ſholde torne agayne wyſt ſoone torned away dylycious mete drynkes toke none hede eaſy ſuſtenaunce cauſed thynke dethe wyll cauſe man deſyre hym nedeth abſtayne hym ſelfe al maner bodely luſtes encreaſe vertues wherby may come euerlaſtynge blyſſe ¶de ſancto matheo appoſtolo good frendes ſuche day ye ſhal haue ſaynt mathewes daye whiche cryſtes appoſtle ye ſhall faſt euen come holy chyrche worſhyp god ſaynt mathew gretely cōmended holy chyrche certayne holy vertues obedyent cryſt ye fyrſt callynge preched goſpell wtout faynynge ſuffred paſſyon wtout ony denyenge fyrſt obedyente cryſt ye fyrſt callynge ſate certayne place beſy gete good cryſt came yt way loked hym bad hym come go hym thenne keſt ſo grete loue cryſt yt left goodes yt ſued cryſt forthe full ſymple full poore alſo fedde cryſt gladly daye prayed cryſt ete wt hym made cryſt grete feeſt dylycate mete drynkes fedynge cryſt company fedde yt wolde come cryſtes ſake moche people ſued cryſt wherſoeuer went et ſecuti ſūt eū turbe multe dyuers cauſes many folowed hȳ ſome heled theyr ſores dyuers ſykenes ſome ſe ye myracles yt cryſt dyde ſhewe ſome ete drynke wt hym ſome yt enmyes yt lerned ye lawe yf myght haue taken hym wt ony worde wherby myght haue accuſed hȳ ſome refourmed vertues doctryne techynge ye appoſtles many vn̄ verſus moribꝰ ſigna cibꝰ blaſphemia doctrina fuere cauſa cū 〈◊〉 turba ſecuta fuit whan mathew fedde cryſt thus come wt hȳ cryſt made hym one dyſcyples gaue hym knowlegynge preche beleue goddes worde ſo boldely euer yt ſpared neyther loue ne drede soo mathew appoſtle came tyme cyte preched yt called nadabar founde moche people taught fendes craft nygromancy taught ſoo many thynges ſo meruaylous yt grete wonder many mennes wytte sand al people ſholde beleue worſhyp mathewe anone delyuered theyr nygromancye ſoo people knewe openly fendes crafte wherfore theſe people whiche dyde beleue nygromancy made dragon fendes crafte ſpyt degorge flambes fyre theyr mouthes brenne ſo ſtenche ſlewe moche people dyde brynge theſe dragon haue deuoured ſaynt mathew whā ſaynt mathew herde therof made croſſe hym went ayēſt anone ye dragon fel downe deed hym thenne ſayd mathew people yf ye haue ony myght reyſe theym agayne lyfe power ſayd mathewe yf goddes ſeruaunt wolde make theym ye purpoſed techynge mayſter iheſu cryſt good ayenſt euyl wherfore bydde dragon aryſe go ſuche place ye ſhall neuer greue man beeſt anone roſe wente theyr waye thus mathewe torned moche people came ſe ſyght preched people tol ioyes paradyſe ſayd euer daye neuer nyght euer youthe neuer aege helthe neuer ſykenes roſes lylyes floures without welowynge popyngayes nyghtyngales dyuerſe byrdes euer ſyngynge loue reſt pea euerlaſtynge charyte soo byleueth cryſt dothe commaundementes ſhall come theder without endynge thus preched cyte curſed people toke hym put eyen keſt hym pryſon tyll toke aduyſement dethe ſholde deye thenne came aū gell ſaynt andrewe preched ferre countree brought hym ouer ſee ſaynt mathewe whan andrewe ſawe mathewe ſo foule anone andrewe wepte prayed god hȳ anone god reſtored mathewe ſyght agayne andrewe wente agayne owne countree preche agayne came fro whan mathewe pryſon wente preched cyte nabadaran whiche kynges ſone deyed ſente kynge mathewe prayed hym reſtore ſone lyfe agayne ſo dyde wherfore kynge wyfe doughter yt called eufegeme toke cryſtendome mooſt parte ye people god hadde choſen eufegeme holy woman godwarde mathewe bleſſid gaue vayle chaſtyte charyte ſo holy woman kepar many vyrgyns deyed fader came kynge yt called hertagus whiche loued mayden eufegeme prayed mathewe helpe hym might haue ſayd mathewe yt myght ſhe wedded kynge heuen myght breke ſpouſehede hertageus wrothe badde ſlee mathewe ſo ſtode ſayd maſſe ye auter came one behynde hym ſlewe hym cryſten people buryed body ſame chirche bad ye kynge ſette fyre eufegemes hous euery ſyde brenne therin mathewe appered badde good chere anone torned fyre frō hous kynges palays lefte nothyng ſaue kynge yonge chylde hym kynge ſmyten meſelry ſo foule grete payne wo ſlewe hymſelfe ſo vengeaunce fell hȳ ſelfe wolde haue done vnto ye may wel ſe theſe grete myracles holy man therfore lette v ſerue hym wyll praye v lorde amen ¶de ſancto michaele archangelo good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſaynt myghelles daye tharchaungell daye holy chirche maketh mynde mencyon aungelles grete ſocoure comforte helpe mankynde hadde aungelles ſpecyally ſaynt mychaell thre prerogatyues yt wonderfull appyerynge merueylous myracles werkynge vyctoryous fyghtynge wonderfull apperynge ſaȳt gregory ſayth whā almyghty god wyl werke ony wonderfull dede thenne ſendeth mychaell ſeruaūt banerer bereth ſhelde ſygne armes wherfore ſent moyſes aarō egypt werke merueyles though ſygne moyſes werkynge done mychael departed reed ſee kept water two partyes whyle people iſrahell wente thrugh ſo paſſed lad forth flom iordan kept water lyke hylle eche ſyde theym whyle paſſed ſauf ſounde londe beheſt alſo mychaell keper paradyſe taketh ſoules ſent thydre alſo ſhal ſlee antecryſte ye mount olyuete ſhal bydde ye deed aryſe come dome angelles wt hym ſhal brynge al inſtrumentes lordes paſſyon croſſe ye crowne ſpere nayles hamer ſpōge eyſell gall ſcourges thynges cryſtys paſſyon yt ſhall dampned yt ſette nought ne byleue paſſyon thus appyereth wonderfully wroughte alſo myracles merueylouſly apulia hye hylle yt hylle called garganus nye grete cyte dwelled ryche man dyuerſe catell beſtes wente hylle happed bulle lefte behynde beſtes thenne man ſeruaunt went ſeke bulle founde hym ſtandynge hole grete denne thenne one ſhot arrowe hym arowe torned ayen ſmote hym yt ſhot arrowe hurte hym ſore ¶thenne ſore ferde merueylled myght meane wente byſſhop tolde hym cauſe byſſhop prayde god haue parfyght knowleche thenne moūt garganus mychaell appyered hym ſayd goddes wyll mā ſholde hurte ye ſhall knowe well keper ye place wherfore go ye make chirche ye denne ſo byſſhop made fayre chirche alſo mychaell appyered byſſhop badde hym go hylle toppe vnto mount gardell foūde bulle tyed ſholde make chirche worſhyp god ſaynt mychaell two roches ſtone eyther ſyde yt werke myght vp thenne ſaynt mychaell appered man hyght haymo badde hym go put awaye ye roche drede thynge man wente thyder ſette ſholders badde roche go vtter name god ſaynt mychaell ſo hylles wente vtter moche neded werke ¶narracio ¶we rede alſo lyf ſaynt gregory grete multytude people rome ſawe arrowes fyre come ayer ſlewe moche people thenne ſaynt gregory prayed god ceſſe ye peſtylence ſawe angel ſtandynge vpon caſtell walle wypynge blody ſwerde ye āgell ſayd ſaynt mychael ſent thydre punyſſhe peple ſynne thus mychaell merueylle myracles werkyng alſo vyctoryous fyghtynge whan ye cytezens sepontyne oppreſſyd wt paynems ſholde gyue batayll prayed oft ſaȳt mychaell helpe ye nyght ye batayl ſholde mychaell appered ye byſſhop ſayd hȳ haue drede go ye batayll boldely wolde helpe hȳ ſoo ye morowe whā batayll ſholde hylle garganus ouercouered grette myſte ¶and arrowes come myſt fleynge fyre boltes thonder hurte moche people paynyms ſo moche ſlewe ye nyght moche people infydeles ſo many ſlayne alyue ſawe grete myracle god cryſtned saynt iohan euangelyſt ſayth appocalyps mychaell aungelles fought wt lucyfer heuen called dragon aungelles wt helpe god mychaell better droue ye dragon aungelles ayre bytwene heuen erth ſoo yet thycke mote ſonne cryſt came heuen blaſt thonder therfore yet whan thonder fall downe erthe fere goo vp agayne tyll haue doone ſome harme make debate ſtryues manſlaughter make grete wyndes bothe londe water moche harme yet wolde doo yf drede god ſaynt mychaell theyr ſorowe ſe ſoules aungelles heuen place tofore alſo ſpyrytes ſtode ſtedfaſt towardes god flaterynge whiche ſaynt mychaell droue heuen yle ſee ye ſhall ¶as ſaynt brandon ſayled ſee came yle ſawe tree ryght grete bothe heyght brede meruayle ſe whiche tree ſate many birdes thycker ye bowes whyte ſnowe thenne prayed god knowe thenne came one theym ſate ſhyppe borde batered wynges made ſounde lyke organ thenne ſayd brandon yf yt come lyke meſſager ſpeke tell ye ben then̄e ſayd aungelles ſtode ſtedfaſt beleue mychaell therfore dryuen oute whan mychaell droue lucyfer aūgelles yet haue euery day remedy worſhip god ¶than mychaell wonderfull apperynge merueylous myracles doynge wherfore lette v worſhyp holy aungelle may ſhylde fyghtynge agaynſt oure ghoſtely enemye fende ſo may haue vyctorye hym euer amen ¶de ſancto luca euangeliſta good frendes ſuche day ye ſhall haue ſaynt luke day ye euangelyſt ye ſhall vnderſtande cryſt iiii euangelyſtes marke mathewe luke iohan theſe wrote ye goſpel goſpell ſay goddes worde theſe holy euangelyſtes wrote onely yt god ſpake alſo dyde ſuffred mankynde ſholde knowen mankynde euermore thynke goddes worde theſe four lykened foure dyuers beeſtes ſo ben portrayed foure partyes croſſe euery ſyde cryſt marke lyon mathew man luke oxe iohan egle let man ſuppoſe ſuche beſtes lykened ſuche beſtes dyuers cauſes bycauſe mathew wrote mooſt cryſtes manhede therfore lykened man luke wrote mooſt cryſtes ſacryfyce dethe therfore lykened oxe oxe offred ſacryfyce olde lawe tokenynge cryſt ſholde offred ſynne people ſacryfyce auter croſſe marke wrote moche ye reſurreccyon therfore lykened lyon bokes ſaye tell whan lyon hath yonge whelpes ſhall lye deed iii dayes ben whelped cometh ye lyon ſeeth whelpes deed anone maketh ſuch rorynge cryenge yt dede whelpes wake therwith queken take lyfe whan cryſt layd thre dayes tombe thenne fader ſpake hym bad hȳ ryſe rered hym frome deth lyfe ¶alſo iohan lykened egle kynde flyeth hygheſt ayre nexte ſonne ſo iohan wrote mooſt godhede lytell manhede theſe cauſes yt lykened foure dyuerſe beſtes ¶but ye ſhall vnderſtonde luke lykened oxe iii maner wyſe yt thought worde dede offred thoughte god fyrſt beſy gete goodes worlde wt crafte bokes tel fyrſt leche couetyſe good ſlewe many mā bodely offēded god ſo greuouſly yt none offred thought ſacrefyſe bokes ſayth god hyghly pleaſed wt thought yt whā man ſory ſynnes h • herte thynketh verely ſake mende hȳ alſo offred worde ſacrafyce wonte ſpēde ſpeche many ydle wordes came appoſtle tourned ſpeche ye profyte cryſtē people wherfore wente lady ſhe taught hȳ ye goſpell yt wrote mayden lady cheryſhed hȳ ye ſo taught hȳ ful goodly ye aūgel came meſſage ſayd anſwere ſhe gaue▪ ſo thynge ſhe dyde ſone doȳg tyll oure lorde ſtyed vp heuen whan luke lerned perfyghtly loked marke mathew wryten ſo toke wrote obſcurly derkly wrote playnly openly thynge thus prechynge techynge offred worde vnto god ¶and alſo offred dede vnto god ſacrafyce payned hym ſelfe dyuerſe penaunce faſtynge alſoo harde lyuynge wepynge praynge alſo dyde wryte perſecucyon appoſtles ſuffred iewes iheruſalem whan grete purſuyte tourmentes cryſtes ſake wrote ye perſecucyon ſaynt stephen ſtoned dethe thenne went ſaynt luke ſaynt poule ſued hym many myſcheues dyſeaſes full grete drede neuer departed hym tyll poule deed thenne wente luke countree called bethany preched worde god tyll xli wynter aege deyed full fayre full holy ghooſt lyued holy vertues dethe god ſhewed hym many fayre myracles ſo ended cryſt went euerlaſtȳ ge blyſſe whiche god brynge v amen ¶de ſanctis ſimone et iuda frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ye feeſt symon iude ye ſhall faſt euen morow come chyrche worſhyp god theſe holy appoſtles ¶ye ſhall vnderſtande yt eyther hath two name yt one called symon zelotes yt iudas iacola iudas thadeus ſhewinge theſe name yt man hath worlde deyeth paſſeth mȳde whan deed wherfore euery cryſten man ſholde beſy take hym name yt ſholde wryten boke lyfe ſholde laſte euer therfore theſe two appoſtles ſuffred grete penaunce trauayle trybulacyon dyſeaſe laſt payne deth cryſtes ſake meke herte clene conſcyence symon moche ſay obedyēce yt maketh man meke herte· iudas moche ſay confeſſyon ye clenſeth mannes cōſcyence ſȳne thus dyed gaue men enſāple ſuffred dethe cryſtes ſake deyed clene conſcyēce thenne ſhall wryten booke lyfe grete worſhyp ye fraternyte heuen grutchen theyr hertes dyſeaſe perſecucyon euer pleynynge haue nede praye god healed ſykeneſſe yt haue theyr ſpyrytes ¶narracio ¶we rede lyfe apoſtle kynge called abagarus lepar herde lorde iheſu cryſte dyde many myracles heled theym yt ſeke wrote letter wyſe kynge abagarus greteth ieſus ſauyour welle ye precheth ye countrey ieruſalem haue herde thy myracles thou dooſt ſoo thou heleſte maner ſekeneſſe wythoute ony herbes ſalues blynde croked lame merueylle thou reyſeſte dede bodyes lyfe wherfore thynke herte byleue yt thou arte goddis ſone come downe frome heuen erthe lyued amonge people one wherfore wryte thou wylt come hele leperhode greueth full ſore ſoo vnderſtonde iewes haue ordeyned doo deth haue lytell cyte yt good honeſte plenteuous ſuffyſaūt v lyue ſhall haue pea then̄e cryſt wrote agayne ſayd thou art blyſſed beleueſt haſt ſeen thou woldeſt ſholde come ſay muſt doo came wyll ſende ſome dyſcyples yt ſhal hele thy leprehede thenne cryſt myght come hym grete deſyre ſe hym ſent hym paynter mayſter crafte paynte cryſtes vyſage coude whan paynter came cryſt loked vyſage ſhone ſo bryght yt myght loke theron made grete ſorowe mournynge come ſoo ferre myght ſpede purpoſe then̄e cryſt toke clothe paynter wyped face therwith thenne forme face theron thenne paynter bare ye kynge thenne kynge wonder gladde dyde grete reuerence wt herte thenne cryſtes aſcencyon thomas ynde aſſent appoſtles ſente kynge abagarus whan ſawe thomas ſaw ſuche ſhynynge face yt wende cryſt thenne ſayd thomas kynge beleue cryſt yu ſhalte hole ſayd beleue hole hym fayne wolde wroke put hym dethe anone hole thenne iudas went symon went bothe togyder percy preche dyde many myracles ſo torned ye kynge xlii thouſande cryſten fayth ſo cryſten people encreaſed ſtrongely kȳge meyny cryſtned withdrewe theyr offrynges theyr mawmettes byſſhoppes lyuȳ ge wherfore ſo wrothe gadred togyder toke theſe appoſtles ledde theym theyr temple doo ſacryfyce theyr mawmettes elles ſholde deed thenne came aungell aſked theym yf wolde haue theyr ennemyes deed ſayd deſyred haue theyr ennemyes torned cryſten faythe aungell aſked yf wolde ſuffre martyrdome cryſtes ſake ſayd wolde ſuffre dethe thenne commaunded tourned mawmettes temple commaunded fendes come pull ymages pyeces ſo dyde byſſhop wrothe theyr goddes fell ſo pyeces anone came thondrynge lyghtnynge cloue temple thre partyes downe grounde thenne theſe byſſhoppes ſodeynly ſlewe theſe appoſtles thenne kynge toke theyr bodyes buryed ryally made fayre chyrche worſhyp god theſe holy appoſtles ¶de ſolempni feſto omnium ſanctorum frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue halowen day ye ſhall faſt euen ye morowe come chyrche worſhyp god lady halowen good frendes ye ſhall vnderſtande yt feeſt ordeyned thre ſpecyall cauſes thoſe ben theſe fyrſt temple halowȳge omyſſion fulfyllynge alſo neclegent lyuinge fyrſt temple halowynge whan romayns lordes worlde made temple rome lyke doue hous named pantheon ſet myddes ye temple ymage chefe mawmet rome euery londe worlde ymage name londe ymage wryten vnder fote ymage made ſo nygromancy yf ony londe torned emperour anone ymage londe wolde torne backe ymage rome face walle whan byſſhoppes came ye temple founde ony ymage torned anone wolde goo emperour tel hym thenne wolde ordeyne hooſt people ſende ye londe ſet reſt pea ſo temple endured thus vnto ye tyme pope bonyface fourthe came thenne went emperour yt called foca prayed wolde gyue hym ye temple myght put oute multytude mawmettes halowe worſhyp god lady halowen ſo gaue temple ye pope thē came pope yt called gregory commaunded al holy chyrche halowe feeſt lyke begonne alſo feeſt ordeyned ſame pope fulfyll omyſſyons many ſayntes dayes yere leue vnſerued ſo many yt may ſerue echone hymſelfe ſaynt iherome ſayeth eche day yere xm martyr take ye fyrſt daye ianuary wherfore holy chyrche ordeyned daye ſholde fulfyll haue left behynde al yere thus euery ſayntes euen hath worſhyp v yf kepe well day worſhyp god lady halowen alſo feeſt ordeyned halowed clenſe v neclygence vnconnynge alſo worldly occupacyons doynge full recheles kepynge holy dayes therfore feeſt ordeyned ſholde make amendes moche may haue treſpaced feeſtes therfore vnderſtande ye grete peryll breke feeſt ony worldy occupacyon werkynge ſynne doynge byenge ſellȳge ony falſhode contryuynge alſo ye ſhall vnderſtande day prayer ſhall ſooner herde ony day daye ſayntes heuen come togyder pray god v therfore ye may well knowe comynge togyder ſhall ſooner herde yf came one two theymſelfe ¶the holy ſayntes whiche ben heuen ſometyme bothe fleſſhe blode body bone elder faders full gladde make moche ioye whan may gete ony prayer almeſdedes v whiche may preſente ſauyour blyſſed lady prayenge v ſhewe declare enſample ſayntes cometh aſſembleth togyder daye ye ſhall ¶narracio ¶we fynde wryten legenda aurea ſame yere feeſt ordeyned halowed keper ſaynte peter chyrche rome daye matens mydnyght whan peple gone frome matens greate deuocyon yt wente euery auter ye chirche ſayd deuocyons whan gone aboute thenne wente hye aulter felle aſlepe ſpirite rauiſſhed ſaw fader heuen ſyttynge mageſte grete multytude angellis aboute hym thenne fayre quene wt crowne hede rychely arayed greate company vyrgyns maydens ſuynge ye kyng roſe aeynſt bad fet chayre golde ſette therein thenne came one clothed camellys ſkynnes hym ſued grete cōpany gode men came nother lyke byſſhoppe hȳ many byſſhoppes came greate multytude hadde ben knyghtes moche people come kynge dyde hym worſhyp thenne byſhop began ſaye mateyns thenne ſpake man angell lad aſked hym thyſe people araye thenne ſayde ye angell ye kynge god ſelfe ye quene lady yt clothed camellys ſkynnes iohan baptyſte patriarkis prophetes hȳ byſſhoppe ſaynte peter apoſtles cōfeſſours wt hȳ ye knyght ſaynt george wt martyr comyners yt good true lyuers ſeruauntys god vpon erth came thanke god greate worſhyp ye haue erthe prayed beſely god theym erth ſhold haue mercy ¶this cauſe thys feeſt fyrſte founde therfore lete v come chirche worſhyp god al halowen yt maye praye v yt maye laſte ende ye nombre yt ſhall worſhyp god ye boke ſpeketh ſaythe thus vidi turbam magnā quā nemo dinumerare poterat ſo many yt mā nombre al pray v euermore maye come blyſſe amen ¶in die animarum good frendys ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſoules daye daye ſoules purgatory abydyng mercy god haue moche nede helpe ryght holy chyrche worſhyppethe alle ſayntes holpen prayer theym ryghte ſoo holy chirche ordeyned day ſynge rede doo almeſdedes hauynge full byleue releſe theym ben purgatorye theyr peynes wherfore god wyll yt chryſten peple theyr power daye releue thē ye leeſt prayer almeſdede day done gretly releueth thē ye ſhall vnderſtōde yt ben foure thynges yt greately helpen ſoules yt ben purgatorye ben thyſe fidelium amicorū oratio elemoſynarū largio ſalutaris hoſtia et ieiuniorū obſeruatio prayer frendes deuoutly ſayd almeſdede doynge maſſes ſyngȳ ge abſtynence faſtyng prayer helpen moche ſoule lyke lorde yt hath man pryſō ony dyſtreſſe atte yt prayer hȳ yt loueth releſeth partye ſhewed enſample ¶narracio ¶we fynde wrytē legēda aurea yt mā yt hadde houſe faſte chyrche yerde ſyde yt dore opened ye chirche vſed cuſtome ofte came wente ſay euery tyme de profūdis cryſtē ſoules happed ſo tyme purſued enmyes went homwardes whan come chyrche yarde kneled downe thought ſaye de profundis thyſe enmyes came anone ye dede bodyes roſe euerychone ſuche ſtrumētes wroughte wyth theyr lyues anone droue away hys enmyes whā ſawe cryed god mercy man euer prayed dyde almeſdedes payne thus may wel preue deuoute prayer helpen many ſoule ben purgatory alſo almeſdedes helpen many ſoule sicut aqua extinguit ignē ita elemoſina extinguit peccatū c ryght water quencheth fyre ſo almeſdede quencheth ye fyre brenneth theym yt ben purgatory yf ben good lyf parfyghte charyte done yf almeſdede done theym ben ioye haue nede therto put treſour holy chirche goddes wyll ſo dealed reueleth theym haue mooſt nede therto ſo god aſſygneth haue mooſt nede ſoules yt ben holpen therwith thanke ſoule done thus ye may well knowe ye almeſdedes helpen gretly ſoules yt done ben purgatory often holy men haue herde fēdes crye make grete ſorowe wt almeſdedes ye ſoules taken frō ¶narracio ¶we rede olde tyme good people wolde alhalowen daye bake brede deale cryſten ſoules yet ben ſome vſen fewe fynde legenda aurea knyght ſholde goo batayll hadde coſyn loued paſſynge well ſayd hym thus yf ſlayne ye batayll ſholde ſelle hors deale value poore people almeſſe praye cryſten ſoules happed ſlayne coſyn loued well hors toke hym owne vſe thē ne ſoone knyght appyered coſyn ſayd thus hym thyſe viii dayes hors thou haſt made brenne purgatory therfore god wyl take vengeaūce forſoth quod daye thy ſoule ſhall helle fende ego purgatus vado regnū dei purged ſhall goo ye kyngdome heuen anone horryble noyſe herde ayer fendes caught man bare hym awaye thyrde helpeth maſſe whan ony ſoule appyereth ony man haue ony helpe deſireth maſſes prayeth haue maſſes ſongen hym ryght mete drynke conforteth man whan feble ſo ſacramēt awter conforteth ſoules ye maſſes ben done wryten legenda aurea byſſhop ſuſpended preſt coude ſaye none maſſe requiem ſonge euery daye deuoutly connynge thenne daye byſſhop wente towardes matens ſemed hym deed bodyes roſe came aboute hym ſayd thou haſt ſayd maſſe v ouer thou haſt taken preeſt awaye v loke amended elles god wyll ſhort tyme take vengeaūce ſake thenne byſſhop gretely aferde anone badde preeſt ſynge maſſe requiem dyde tofore ſo dyde ofte myght ¶narracio ¶alſo fynde fyſſhers ſet nettes herueſt fyſſhe toke vp grete pyce yſe coldeſt yſe euer felte wolde melte ſonne ſoo brought yſe byſſhop hadde grete brennynge hete foot coldeſt euer felte ſpake voys hȳ yſe ſayd ſoule yt ſuffreth penaū ce yſe haue frendes yt wyll doo maſſes ſhall delyuered penaunce thou ſhalte hole thy ſykenes yf yu wylte ſaye maſſe ſayd wolde ſynge hym bad tell hym name euer whyle maſſe layde yſe vnder fote euer ſayd maſſe yſe melted away ſo within whyle yſe molten ſoule frome payne byſſhop hole ſykenes thenne ſoule appered hym wt moche ioy ſayd wt thy maſſes ſyngynge payne euerlaſtynge blyſſe tolde byſſhop ſholde dye ſoone come euerlaſtynge ioye whiche god brynge v amen ¶de ſancto martino epiſcopo good frendes ſuche day ye ſhall haue ſaynt martyns day whan martyn xv yere aege cut mantel two pyeces rode amonge knyghtes yet cryſtned gaue halfe mantell poore man goddes ſake yt aſked almeſſe then̄e nyght god ye ſame clothe ſayd aungell martyn yt yet cryſtned hath clothed clothe martyn herde worde heuen anone cryſtned anone left worldes occupacyon gaue hȳ holynes soo rode tyme yt waye fende came lyke man met hym aſked wheder wolde ſayd thyder god wyll ſayd fende wyll thyn enmye thenne ſayd marten god helpe therfore drede marten wexed ſo holy yt rered deed bodyes lyf ſo grete holynes choſē byſſhop turon tyme men grete peryll lyke ſpylt one knewe holynes marten ſayd marten helpe anone holpen alſo rode tyme vyſytacyon hounde ranne hare vnder hors foot thenne pyte beſt bad hounde ſtande ſtylle lete beſt go anone hounde ſtode ſtylle put erthe alſo ſawe adder ſwȳmynge water ſayd thadder nomine din̄ iubeo te redire name god cōmaūde go ayen thou comeſt fro anone ſhe torned ayen marten ſyghed wonder ſore ſayd ſory yt ſerpentes heren men wyll heren tyme came gate cyte hyght parys kyſſed horryble meſell anone hole ſame kyſſe alſo ſo pacyente many tymes owne clerkes mocked hym yet ſuffred pacyently wroth tyme rode waye vyſytacyon hymſelf maner hadde rough mantell blacke came carte waye caryage beeſtes carte ſawe blacke wauerynge wynde fledde awaye brake theyr gere carter whyppe bete marten gaf hym many ſore ſtrokes ſuffred mekely ſayd nothynge wolde haue gone theyr waye myght ſtere fro place tyll knewe martē thenne cryed hym mercy thenne anone gaue hem beeſtes paſſed fayr forth harneys ſaue ynough alſo tyme marten ſatte celle fende come hym lykeneſſe kyng ſhynynge crowne ſayd come fro heuen ſpeke byleue criſtus ego ſum cryſte marten loked hym ſayd lorde iheſu cryſt wyll come ſuche araye thou cryſte ſhewe thy woundes anone fende went waye left horryble ſtenche behynde hym yet tyme came ayen marten repreued hym toke people hym ſynned ſhryuen torned ayen ſynne done tofore ſayd though thou take theym thy grace god wyll thenne ſayd marten wretche thou wylt leue thy perſute cryſten people aſke mercy meke herte truſt god ſo mercyfull wyll gyue ye mercy whā marten ſholde paſſe worlde laye deed bedde fēde came ſatte hym dyſputynge hym yf myghte haue caught hym ony worde myſbyleue ende marten ſayd hym go hen thou cruell beſt thou ſhalt thynge fynde amyſſe god ſhall receyue thenne made laye hym aſſhes heyre thenne ſayd vii pſalmes letanye gaf vp ghooſt 〈◊〉 buryed owne chirche moche honour thenne liiii wynter came byſſhop tranſlated hym whan made thynge redy layde honde marten body haue borne forth myght thenne thought byſſhop marten wyll remeued left thenne came fayr olde man badde hym go ayene wolde helpe hym thenne bare body tombe without lettyng ſo whan ſeruyce done olde man vanyſſhed waye knewe well saynt marten thenne god ſhewed many fayr myracles hym ¶narracio ¶it happed tyme two beggers one lame myght go blynde myght ſee ſo make people haue compaſſyon theym blynde bare lame lame taught blynde ſholde goo thus gate moche good eaſy lyfe euer aferde mete ſhrene ſaynt marten leeſt wolde haue heled theyr ſykneſſe ſo ſee may moche god therfore lete v praye hym may praye god v amen de ſancta katherina good frendes ſuche daye ye ſhall haue ſaynt katherynes daye holy vyrgyn martyr ſhe kȳges doughter came grete byrthe ſhe ſet mynde god ſet nought pryde vaynglory rycheſſes worlde vanyte ſhe ſet onely iheſu whan ſhe ſcole lerned whyle anone ſhe wolde dyſpute ony clerke yt wolde come ſhe enſpyred holy gooſt yu ſhalte fynde heuenly ſayd doctryne lorde another thou wolde done vnto ſhorte tyme thou ſhalte haue ſynguler delyte execucyon ſo moche worlde thou wolde breke thy wyll ſayd loue god man may cauſe blyſſe made ¶this maner knowlege hadde forne fader adam eue ſtate theyr innocency without ony trauayle whiche ſholde haue alſo yf ſynned knowelege whiche haue herynge lernynge techynge yt whiche lawe faythe moder holy chyrche whiche haue cure ſoules bounde teche doo teche oure paryſſhens payne eternall dampnacyon ſoules moche wyll offende god neyther leſe myn owne ſoule ne purpoſe leue homely thus called ſone god ne gretter ryches thenne heyre ye blyſſe heuen ne fayrnes thā belyke ſuche fader alle bretheren ſyſters one fader moder god holy chyrche token none v ſholde ſcorne ye proude dooth forboden ſwerynge moche ſwerynge oft ſwerynge therfore ſayth moche ſwereth ſhall replete wt wyckednes ſorowe ne vengeaunce ſhall departe fro houſe ſome ſayth alſo noo man wyll beleue theym ſwere ſubtyl excuſacyon therby falſe man may ſwere well true man ſoo ſholde well beleued true man falſer ſwereth forſwereth ſo begyleth therfore yf thou wylte beleued without ony ſwerynge true thy worde lete ye ye nay nay token yu ſayſt thy mouthe thou ſholdeſt ſay thy herte ſaye one thynge thynke ¶the thyrde haue mynde halowe thy holy dayes ſay ſondayes boden almighty god vi dayes made heuen erthe ſee vii daye reſted therfore blyſſed made holy ſtede therof cryſten men grete deuocyon halow ye ſondaye whiche fyrſt daye ye worlde wherin god made lyght daye god gaue moyſes lawe ye daye roſe dethe fle ſynne fleſſhely luſtes tauernes ſuche chaffere letteth theym reſte oure lorde yet many folke yt whiche ſuche dayes beſy worldly werkis ſynnes weke euer wyll reſt techynge ne loue ne drede god thyſe moſte lyke hel neuer reſte euer laboure paine breke alſo holy day yt ſpende theyr tyme ydelnes vayne playes ydell ſpeche bacbytyng theyr euen cryſten ſayth lorde haue mynde halow thy holy day yu nonrryſſheth thy body erdly fode comforteth thy ſoule heuenly deſyres defendeth fro deuyll maketh therof blyſſe heuen thus maye noo man fader lord god ſeconde fader gate thy moder bare yt whome thou
