ſuſtenaunce thyn eſtate dewe deſyred wyſe man lorde whan ſayd neyther rycheſſe ne pouerte gyue good lorde neceſſary lyuelode ¶the viii thou ſhalte bere noo falſe wytnes forboden maner leſynges conſpyracyon forſwerȳ ge yt thy neyghboure leſeth catell frendſhyp good ſuche ben called chyldoen deuyll put trouthe brynge falſehede put cryſt brynge deuyll leſynge ſtandeth onely fals wordes alſo falſe werkes yf thou cryſten man lyue therafter elles thou lyeſt thre maner leſynges one whan thou lyeſt full purpoſe hurte thy neyghboure thenne deedly ſynne another whan thou lyeſt thy neyghboure trouthe thenne ſo moche ſynne thyrde whan yu lyeſt dyſporte wyllynge hynder ony perſone theſe two ben venyall thou haue cuſtome therfore beware maner leſynges another hate ne mede bere falſe wytnes ix thou ſhalte deſyre thy neyghbours wyfe vii commaundement god forbedeth dede lechery theyr deſyre token bothe ben deedly ſynne yet ſome wene dede ſynne cryſt therfore wyllynge ſuche clene within without bothe body ſoule ſayth whiche ſeeth woman couetyſe theyr luſt lechery theyr herte thus ſhrewde thoughtes man oftymes departed fro god yet ſaynt byrgyt vyſyons ſayeth yf euyl thoughtes ſometyme come man ſholde wene hȳ ſelfe rather aungell man ſo thynge cometh hymſelfe none god therfore man ſholde knowe infyrmyte hath cometh hym ſelfe ye ſtrength hath cometh god neceſſary ſuffre ſomtyme grete mercy god tempted wt euyll thoughtes whiche yf conſent ben purgacyon ſoule keper vertues therfore whā ſhrewde thoughtes come withſtande fyrſt ſubgeſtyon let thy ſoule alway ſo labour conſent delyte thenne haue mynde ye bytter paynes cryſt ſuffred thendles blyſſe ye ioye heuen thou muſt leſe yf thou conſent ye bytter paynes hell alſo thou ſhalte haue yf thou deye yf thou thus ſhalte thou haue mȳ de thy laſte ende neuer ſynne ¶the x commaundement laſt thou ſhalt deſyre thy neyghboures thynge houſe londe oxe horſe neyther nothynge ſuch deſyres couetyſe ſcrypture maketh mē cion balaam nachor anany gyeſy achab ieſebell many fell grete myſchefe bothe body ſoule therfore ye well ware ſuche falſe deſyre take noo mannes good agaynſt wyll leeſt fall dyde thynke alſo without ſatyſfaccyon hauynge wyll amende therof make reſtytucyon pope ne none hym may dyſpence yet thou ſtandeſt accurſed holy chyrche grete ſē tence foure tymes yere ſhall ſuche falſe deſyres thenne prouffyte whan curſe almyghty god ſhall thus abyde noo man dredeth curſe god nowe whan ſauyour iheſu cryſt ſhall ſay daye dome ſcrypture maketh mencyon go ye curſed fyre hell euerlaſtynge thenne ſhall bothe drede fele worde go ye curſed ſhall paynefull doctours ſayeth ye paynes thouſande helles though al gadred one theſe x commaundementes ben brought two ye goſpell loue god aboue al thynge thy neyghboure thy ſelfe fyrſt thou ſhalte loue god thy herte thynge nerer thyn herte god thy ſoule thou ſuffre ſynne abyde within thy ſoule loue god thy mynde yt thou ſpare myſchefe pleaſe god thy neyghbour alſo thy ſelfe good yeull moche thy ſelfe helthe ſykenes welthe wo thus loue thou ſhalte kepe goddes commaundement onely drede payne theſe commaundementes ſholde eche man tell teche chyldren thus badde lorde moyſes theſe wordes ſayd whiche take daye ſhall thy herte thou ſhal tell thy ſones thynke ſlepynge wakynge ſyttynge goynge thou ſhalte bynde ſygne thy hande wryte theym doores lanternes thy houſe ſhalte rule thy thoughtes wordes dedes preuy aperte eche place commaundemētes god forgete theſe wordes ſayd ne falle fro thy herte dayes thy lyfe thus gouerne ye meyny ſayth ſaynt auſtyn ſpeke thus chyrche ſoo ſholde ye home ye may gyue true rekenynge god theym whiche ben ſubgectes vnto tell theym ſayeth grete loue ſwetenes heuenly thynges grete bytternes horryble paynes helle ye ſhall anſwere theym mooſt ſtrayte daye dome counſeyle theym neclygent wyſe lerne theſe commaundementes drede ſentence foloweth yf thou wylte voyce thy lorde god ſaythe thou kepe doo commaundementes theſe curſes ſhall come take thou ſhalte curſed cyte fylde curſed ſhall thy relyques fruyte thy boby fruyte londe droues thyne ox flockes ſheepe yu ſhalte curſed goynge goynge oute thou ſhalte ſmyte wyth honger ſekenes peſtylence adres fyre hete corrupte ayre theſe ſayth ſhall purſue thou ſhalte peryſſhe yf thou wylte voyſe lorde yt thou lerne kepe commaundementes ſhall make hyer dwellynge erthe theſe bleſſynges ſhall come take thou ſhalte bleſſed cyte felde fruyte thy body frute londe flockes thy ſleep droues thy beſtys thy bernys thy celleres thy goynge goynge oute werkes hō dis ſoo yt euery mā ſhall ſee yt name god called vpō yt ſhall drede ſhall gyue ye rayne tyme ſayth therth ſhal brynge forthe ſede tree ſhall replete frute thou ſhalte haue pea thy coūtree thou ſhalt ſlepe noo man ſhall fere thyſe blyſſyngis ſhall take yf thou lerne kepe cōmaundementes therfo haue mynde preceptis god byddynges ye mooſt beſy yf thou kepe ſhal kepe brynge blyſſe neuer ſhall haue ende amē fourth thynge thou ſholdeſt knowe god ſeuen ſacramētis holy chirche whiche mynyſtred people perſons preſtys haue power therto whyche fyue fyrſte baptyſme confyrmacyon ſhryfte howſell anoyntynge euery man womā holde payne curſynge certeyn tyme ye lawe gyueth thother two maye noo mā take order wedlock owne wyl thyſe ſacramentis toke theyr begynnynge gracyous welle ſyde lord iheſu cryſt paſſyon ryght oute adamis ſyde whyle ſlept taken rybbe eue made ryght ſoo deth lord ranne oute ſyde bothe blood water vertue whiche paſſyon ſacramētis holy chyrche toke fyrſte theyr ſtrength theyr begynnynge fyrſte ſacrament batptȳ whiche orygynall ſynne borne ſynnes defoyled ben waſſhen awaye thrugh paſſyon criſte ther betaken v fayth byleue holy chirche wythoute whyche maye noo man ſaued therfore cōmaunded euery cryſtē woman feleth quycke chyld kepe frome heuyng ſhouynge grete trauayle fallynge myſcheues yt ſholde myſcheue chyldes lyfe ſoo loſte body ſoule eche woman byfore trauayle chylde come chirche take ſhryfte houſell peryll deth myghte falle byrthe alſo mydwyf tho yt aboute chylde yf peryll deth ſholde cryſten wyſe cryſten name fader ſone holy gooſt thenne ſprynge chyld water thou forgete thyſe wordes cryſten yf cryſtened maner atte home ſhall criſtened eftſone chirche grete peryll nayle god eftſones vpon croſſe yf lyue cryſtenyng home brynge chyrche ſhall haue hole ſeruyce lackethe tyme peryll dethe fader moder maye cryſten theyr owne chyldren without harmynge theyr ſpouſchode godfaders godmoders ben borowes tofore god theyr god chylderen therfor ben bounde teche theym loue ryghtwyſnes charyte chaſtyte kepe theym frome deedly ſynne ſpecyally teche theym commaundementes bylyue man wyfe ſholde holde atones chylde fontſtoon ne fongyth ſhall fonge atte confermynge atte nede fader ne moder ne noryſe ne none ſholde ſuffre noo yonge chylde theym bedde whyle ſlepe ne preſſe theym faſte cradell ne ſuffre theym lye ſlepynge ne wakynge withoute keper gooſtly kynrede throughe fongynge chyldern atte fontſtoon ix wyſes one betwene chylde godfader another betwene chylderen godfaders another ye chylde wyfe godfaders fleſhely knowen tofore nother betwyx godfader fader hym cryſtened nother betwix preeſt chylde baptyſed nother betwix chylde chylderen hym baptyſeth nother betwix hym baptyſeth wyfe hym baptyſed fyrſte knowe nother bytwene baptyſer moder hym baptyſed ben alſo ix afore byſſhoppe atte cō fermynge ſame forme theſe letten ſpowſehode made fordooth ſpowſehode made ſeconde ſacramente confyrmacyon byſſhop maner noyntynge forhede hondes byſſhop wherby holy gooſt gyueth ſtrength agaynſte feblenes ſynne forne fader marke impreſſed ſoule wherby thou ſhalte knowlege fayth loue cryſte euery cryſten man woman bounde brynge theyr chylderen ſoone may namely yere age ſhall haue grace lyfe blyſſe dede thoſe confermed mow receyue none ſacramente nother ſhal waſhe hede forhede thre dayes reuerence holy oyle thyrde ſacramente ſhryfte penaunce ye whiche euery man woman bounde anone reſonable wytte atte xii yere euery yere clene ſhryuen onys atte leeſt atte theyr owne curate theſe may euery daye ſee ſynnes euer dyden thynke vpon whan loke theym may haue ſhame drede theyr hertes theyr ſynne thrughe grace god mow leue theyr ſynne yet notwythſtondynge ye ben bounde ouer yere ſhewe youre ſhryfte youre owne curate yf ben ony haue affeccyon nother lette wete whome ſhall haue ryght good leue cryſtes blyſſynge myne deceyte owne ſoule hyde ſynne fro entente myghte lenger abyde therein ſome done haue done many yeres knowe theyr counſeylle wene wolde dyde suche lyke thadder yt hydeth venyme preuy place wolde engender lamprey tourneth taketh vp ayene thus ſome one yere ye come youre curate ye caſte oute venym youre ſynne atte pardon preuy place anone eeſter ye take vp ayen thefte auoutry ſuche ben worſe ye afore ye done begyle ſelfe nede grete penaunce iudas whā betrayed cryſt tolde ſynne true herdman dyd cayphas pylate whā ſayd haue ſȳned body betrayenge ryghtwyſe blode hadde ſaued toke none hede therto ſayd yt v auyſe ſayth haue cure ryght ſoo thus trowe ſome went owne herdeman whā ye go thenne ſholde brybery ſtolen goodes ſuche reſtored auoutry curſed ſynnes thus dyſtroyed ſay deſyre haue ſhryft payne ſaue charge haue ſoules leuer mynyſter al ſacramentes yt longeth myn offyce forty tymes one doo dyſtroye falſe ſubtylte yt ye vſe ſhryfte agaynſt helthe ſoules ſo god helpe alſo whan thou comeſt ſhryft thou ſhalt come grete ſorowe herte mekely knele preeſt hym goddes ſtede tell hym holy yu haſt myſgouerned thy lyfe full wyll ſo hertely thy penaunce enioyned therfore e • le ſhryfte many ſet nought theyr penaunce doynge ſo haue tolde theyr ſyn̄e preeſt ſuche begyle themſelfe veray ſacrament ſhryfte dependeth ſpecyally thre thynges wtout whiche thou mayſt truely ſhryuen yt ſorowe herte ſhryft mouthe penaūce doynge though thou ſorye thy ſynne ſhryue auayleth ſeth ne thy penaunce auayleth wyte wel thou mayſte yf thou ſholdeſt reken man ende thy rekenynge thoughe thou xx lib det ryght ſo thou ſhryueſt makeſt rekenynge wt preeſt goddes ſtede thou make ſeeth therfore paye thy det penaūce doynge nought token thou arte ſory thy ſynne yf thou ſory therfore haue ſayd tofore thy ſhryft nought ſo thou ſynneſt agaynſt holy gooſt whiche ye mooſt peryllous ſynne therfore yf thou wylte haue blyſſe heuen thy penaunce thenne thou ſhalte haue grace pardon thy ſynnes theſe thre wordes contrycion confeſſyon ſaryſfaccyon ſtandeth vertue pardon worlde lady ſaynt mary vyſyons holy woman ſaynt byrgyt telleth whan pardon prouffyteth whan ſaynge yt cometh pardon hath wyll leue ſynne reſtore hath wrongfully taken wyllynge wynne penny wronge ne falſhede lyue ony daye lenger god wolde dyde proſperyte aduerſyte ſubmytte wyll goddes wyll flee worſhyp frendſhyppe worlde ſhall haue pardon remyſſyon ſynne lyke aungell god ſyght god ſayth vyſyteth remyſſyon pardon ſynnes hath wyll leue olde vanytees ne ye inordynate affeccyon kepeth ſtyll wronge getynges falſe deceyte ſubtyltees alſo loueth world hym ſelfe wyll flee ſhrewde cuſtomes ne reſtrenyne fleſſhe ſuperfluytees ryght nought auayleth hym pardon ne indulgence accordeth ſaynt gregory ſayth thus thou makeſt neuer ſatyſfaccyon thy ſynne ſayth yf thou feere thy ſynne euery body wyll deſyre pardon fewe none wyll ſholde haue pardon thrugh truſt coloure pardon many curſed dede doo ſynne truſt therof ony good deed grete ſynne pryde yu neuer ſo full good vertues vnkyndenes thy god may dyſtroy thoſe vertues vnkyndenes thou mayſt ſhewe thenne dyſpleaſe god wylfully therfore fle ſuche vnkyndenes thynke acceptable thou arte god thy good lyuynge culpable thou ſhalte yf yu retorne agayne ſynne ſlypper hope ſayth ſaynt auſtyn whan man ſynneth vpon truſt ſaued dooth ſo neyther dredeth ne loueth god profytable holde thy ſelf feble lowe holde ſtrō ge feblenes fal loſt therfore take hede goodnes god putteth thanke hym praye contynuaunce ſynne vpon truſt pardon ne ony good dedes fourthe holy ſacramēt aulter whiche cryſtes owne body fleſſhe blode forme breed ſame borne vyrgyn mary done rode made vertue goddes wordes ye preeſt hath power whiche power neyther aungell ne archaungell onely man mynde hymſelfe ſacrament euery man woman bounde lawe one yere eeſter yf xiiii yeres aege haue dyſcrecyon receyue whā ben ſhryft penaunce made clene theyr ſynnes elles put chyrche cryſten buryelles yf ſykeneſſe ſome reaſonable cauſe whiche cauſe muſt certyfye curate vnworthely receyueth ſacrament receyueth dampnacyon alſo often ony man ſeeth body maſſe borne ſeke ſhal knele doune deuoutely ſaye pater noſter ſome good prayer worſhyppe ſouerayne lorde alſo ye ſhall vnderſtande drynke whiche ye doo receyue chalyce howſel ſacrament water brȳ ge lyghtlyer holy ſacramente thy body fourme breed hole ſauyoure iheſu cryſtes body bothe fleſſhe blode therfore thou ſhalte take hole entyere thou mayſt leeſt ony parte abyde ſtycke thy tethe leeſt parte hooſt hole mooſt precyous body lorde day thou hereſt thy maſſe god graunteth thy nedefull lawfull thynges daye ydle othes forgoten ſynnes ben gyuen day thou ſhalt leſe thyn eyen ſyght ne deye ſodayne dethe ne tyme maſſe thou ſhalte waxe aeged euery ſteppe thyderwarde homewarde aungell ſhall reken lewde men woman dyſpute ſacrament vtterly forboden ynough vnto beleue holy chyrche techeth theym ¶the fyfth ſacrament anoyntynge ſeke men whiche oyle halowed byſſhop mynyſtred preeſtes ben lawfull aege grete peryll dethe lyghtnes abatynge theyr ſykenes yf god wyll lyue forgyuynge theyr venyall ſynnes releaſynge theyr payne yf ſhal deye ſacrament may gyuen ofte nedeth euery man woman ben poynte dethe vi ſacrament holy ordres yt man may take owne wyl gyueth power taketh ſerue holy chyrche ſtate hym taketh ordre preeſthode make ſacrament cryſtes fleſſhe blode mynyſter ſacramentes people theſe muſt haue theyr crownes ſhauen theyr hedes tonſured theyr clothes honeſtly ſhapen falleth theyr eſtate namely holy chyrche muſt alſo quere rede ſynge clenneſſe conſcyence grete deuocyon ſoule ouerſcyppinge ne momblynge ne muſynge vanytes medlynge lewde ne vnthryfty tydynges ne inhoneſt comunycacyon comynge late goddes ſeruyce ne goynge oute ende without reſonable cauſe gronynge ne ſlombrynge ne ſparynge theyr voyce ſhewynge voyce holy ghooſt ſowne hole ſpeche thus ſayth ye holy man ſaynt bernarde preeſtes muſte alſo euery daye dyſpoſe theym ſay maſſe yf may therto bound ſaȳt bernard ſayth perſone lorde euery man thꝰ haue made gyue power make offre ſone incarnate tofore ye fader ſaluacyon world yf thou haue power ſynge ſyngeſte ſaythe thou benymeſte aungellys heuē theyr ioye thou benymeſt mankynde trauaylȳge erth theyr helpe grace thou benymeſte ſoules greate paynes purgatory theyre reſte theyr forgyueneſſe thyſe ben heuy wordes lytell thought many v saynt auſtyn ſayth worſhypfull dygnyte preſthode ſayd betwix whoſe hōdes sone god moders wombe incarnate bleſſyde ben preſtes ſayth yf preſtely lyue heuenly myſtetery sayth werkynge fader ſone holy gooſt ſame god heuen ſame ſelfe youre hondes ſacramente therfore ſayth oure lord ye holy holy ¶a ryghtfull lyfe neceſſary ſayth ſayncte auſtyn therfore ye muſte ſo lyue ſee lyfe accorde youre name soo yf youre order holy lete conuerſacyon ſame yf men ſaye well ſayth ſee yt weckes bere wytneſſe ſame v preeſtis ¶the ſeuenth ſacramente wedlocke whiche baynes muſte aſked thryes holy chyrche ¶this lawfull knyttynge togyder man woman fourme holy chyrche aſſent theym gyder lawe god neuer departe whyles theyr lyues laſten remyſſyon ſynnes getynge grace whan taken true entent thoughe noo trouthe plyght fleſſhely dede done yf ben full age accorde hertes gyder fore god wyfe huſbonde ¶all preuy couenaūtes trouth plygh tynge forwarde makynge without aſſent frendes knowlege forboden ſuche make ben grete peryll ſoule ¶alſo forboden noo wedded man woman one without ye others aſſent make vowe chaſtyte pylgrymage ne faſtynge yf yt wyfe auowe huſbonde fyrſt wytynge may doo yf conſent ſuffre wytingly fyrſt knowynge man ſynneth wyfe hath power owne body huſbande yf man abſtayne hym fro wyfe ſuche wyſe without wyll wyfe ſhe gyue hȳ leue cauſe ſynne wyfe ye ſame caas yf ſhe ſame huſbande ¶the ſeuen dedes mercy fyrſt thynge thou ſholdeſt knowe god ſeuen dedes mercy whiche euery man bounde byddȳge god fulfyl power yt ſay fede hungry gyue drynke thyrſty clothe naked herborow houſles vyſyte ſeke delyuer ye pryſoners bury poore whan deed theſe nedefull v pleſynge god helpynge body ſoule al thē yt therfore ſayeth cryſt gyue ſhall gyuen almeſſe ſayth ſaynt auſtyn holy thynge encreaſeth yu haſte leſſeth thy ſynne multyplyeth thy eres bleth mynde lengeth ye termes clenſeth thynge delyuereth yt frome dethe ioyneth angelles departe deuylles wall inexpugnable ſoule· therfore gyue almeſſes thynges ſhall clene ¶thre thȳges muſt conſyder ſhall gyue almeſſe fyrſt aſketh aſketh wherre fyrſt ſay god aſketh loueth ſo moche pore men ye theym name holdeth done hym ſelfe aſketh oures dauyd ſayth thynges ben thy lordes take thy hādes haue gyue yt aſketh v gyue hym lene hym wherfore wyll yelde hondred folde blyſſe heuen wherfore ſayth ſaynt gregory poore mē ſhall dyſpyſed prayed faders gyueth poore ſhall poore ſayth salomon yt ſtoppeth eeres crye poore ſhall crye herde therfore al thoſe aſke theſe aſketh vnryghtfully gyue aſketh better correccyon iherom ſayth gyue poore ſuſtayne theyr ryches may man excuſe hym almeſſe gyuynge halfpeny poore ſomtyme pleaſeth god hondred ſhelynges ryche yf yu may gyue hym gyue hym wordes cōforte thou gyueſt gyue gladly glad gyuer god loueth ¶there ben alſo ſeuen gooſtly dedes mercy fyrſt teche vnconnynge ſauour ryghfully another gyue counceyle hym aſketh werke truely thyrde chaſtyſe hym treſpaceth ſaye repreue bete doo due correccyon ¶the fourthe comforte ſorowfull gyftes wordes comforte ſuche fyfth forgyue treſpace yf thou wylt forgyue thē god wyll forgyue rancour offence thou muſt nedes forgyue accyon ye amendes ben thyn owne wyll ſyxte thou ſuffre mekely pacyently whan ony man woman ony preiudyce offence agaynſt prompte redy ſynne feruent doo penaunce good werkes operacyons moore preſte redy ſuffre dyſeaſe trybulacyon doo yf ony man chyde blame repreue doo wronge kepe ſcylence ſet ſharpe worde ye ſhylde ſuffraunce thynke mooſt benygne ſauyiour redemptoure iheſu cryſt bobbed buffeted ſpytte vpon ſcorned euermore helde peaſe therfore dyſeaſe myſfortune fal fo beleue cometh ſynne ſo thou ſhalte ſuffre lyght lyer yf thou take hede wherfore cometh ſeuenth praye ſaye thyn ennemy thoſe ſynfull yf thou mayſt helpe one theſe ſeuen aforeſayd praye vnto lorde theym cryſt ſayth loue ennemyes well hate praye dooth perſecucyon ye may chyldren heuen thus may ye fulfyll dedes mercy bodely gooſtly ¶the vi thynge thou ſholdeſt knowe god ben ſeuen pryncypall vertues euery man woman ſholde vſe fyrſt fayth whiche grounde begynnȳge ſaluacyon ſtondeth thre thynges vnyte godhede thre perſones manhode cryſt ſacramentes holy chyrche vertue nedefull cryſten people begynnynge good werkes fayth without good werkes ne good werkes true faythe ne without true fayth may man pleaſe god almyghty ¶the ſeconde hope truſt mercy god ſaued ſtandeth ye grace god good werkes owne good dedes theym bothe togyder ſhall hope ſo lytell called wanhope ſholde hope haue blyſſe yf doo well perceuer commaundementes god ne ſoo moche truſt grete mercy lorde hope ſaued without good dedes operacyons ¶the thyrde charyte ende perfeccyon alle commaundementes god ¶and vnderſtonde thou loue god aboue alle thynge thy neygbboure thyſelfe ſoo one may byloued withoute ſayth ſaynt iohan loueth god loueth broder loueth broder whiche may ſee ſholde loue god whiche may ſee ¶the fourth vertue ryghtwſnes elli payeng dewte eche thynge dewly longeth god prayſynge thankynge goodes kynde fortune grace hath gyue lente therof gyue parte many benefaytes preſeruynge frome many myſcheues vengaunce thou haddeſt fall daye ſeeſt many one fall ſholdeſte happely thyſelfe haue fall gracyous kepynge haue ¶to thy neyghboure thou muſte alſo yelde loue charyte ſaye thou doo ryghte reaſon hym thynge thou woldeſte dyde yf thou woldeſt ſholde true paye dettys begyle ſubtyltees ſleyghtes byenge ſelyng ſame yf thou woldeſt alſo proude enuyous whrathfull couetyſe glotenous ſlouthfull ne let cherous thou ſame thus thynges thou woldeſte thy neyghboure thou hym thenne thou dooſt ryghtwyſneſſe thyſelf alſo thou muſte haue beſynes lerne fulfyll wyll commaundementis god withſtonde ſynne ſhrewde lyuynge ¶the fyfth vertue wyſdome vertue departeth good frome euyll techeth v beware ſleytes deceytes wretched worlde lykewyſe freyle fleſſhe curſed ennemye deuyll helle ¶and dyſpyſe ſet noughte alle may ii good choſe better ſaynt auſtyn ſayth many one dothe thou muſt dyſpyſe ye worlde hate fleſſhe louers worlde lytell whyle ago v thynge lefte theym powder wormes take hede ben nowe men thou arte ſayth dranke laughed ladde theyr lyfe erthe myrthe iolyte poynte deſcende helle profyteteth theym theyr vayne glorye theyr ſhorte ioye pompe worlde dylycates luſte fleſſhe falſe rycheſſe grete meany euyll couetyſe theyr laughter theyr playe theyr pryde theyr booſt ¶after luſte grete payne ſorowe fylle theym maye falle ſayth thou arte man erthe erthe thou lyueſt erthe thou ſhalte tourne agayne theſe ben ye wordes holy doctoure ſaynt auſtyne remembraunce ſhall make wyſe hardy diſpyſe youre enemyes worlde fleſſhe deuyll ſaynt iſyder ſayth none thynge better thenne wyſdome ne none thynge ſweter luſtyer thenne knowlege ne none thynge worſe thenne lewdneſſe therfore knowe thou thou ſhalte flee wheder yu ſhalt go ¶loue wyſdome ſhewed ſhall come beſy aboute ſhall lerne vi vertue ſtrengthe maketh mā myghty hardy wythſtonde many grete myſcheues loue god ſtondeth ſuffrynge pacyently aduerſyte mekely make proſperyte ſuffre euenly bothe wele woo herte hye wel fare ne moche vnder none euyll fare ſtronge agaynſte oure foon bothe body ſoule noo temptacyon make v falle ne fayle oure 〈1 page duplicate〉 〈1 page duplicate〉 fayth agaynſt god almyghty ¶the ſeuenth vertue meſure whyche meane betwene moche lyke wyſe lytell ſtondeth takynge ſuffycyently nedeth ¶and refuſynge vterly moche lytell ¶the viii thynge laſt thou ſholdeſte knowe god ſeuen dedely ſynnes alle men ſholde refuſe eche euen waye helle therfore nedeful euery man konwe theym ¶therfore ſayth wyſe man fro face thadder fonde flee ſynne venyme adder ſleeth mannys body ſoo venym ſynne ſleeth mannys ſoule ¶the fyrſte ſynne lykynge hyghneſſe mannys herte hygh eſtate nobleneſſe hath fortune kynde grace canne paſſynge nother hath nother cometh many ſhrewd ſpyces booſtyng bacbytyng diſpite thy neyghboure vnbuxumnes ypocryſy proudberynge diſpleaſyng ſcornynge inobedyence hye herte gaye araye pryde grete kynne vayn glory boldneſſe ſynne booſtynge good dedes auauntynge euyll dedes indignacion ſhame leſſed preſumpciō ſtourdynes worſte ſoo ſayth ſaynte auſtyn ¶that none worſe dampnable ſynne ſynne pryde ben gyltye lyſte repreued theyr ſynnes ne theyr defautes anone wyth greate ſtourdynes galled horſe touched ſore wyncheth wryeth ¶and ſeken may mayntene ſuche lewdenes ſynne ¶thus dyde kynge dauyd whan nathan prophete god came hym tolde hym ſynne vengaunce ſholde haue therfore ſhewed ſtourdynes prophete ne rebuked hym ne chydde hym mekely ſayd oure lord haue ſynned ſayth ſory ſynne wyll amende therfore god toke awaye moche vengaunce ſhold haue ſynne ryghte thus ſhold ye repreued youre ſynne mekely come curate miniſter god occupyeth ſtede tyme ſaye ſyr knowlege defaute wote well dyde amys wyll amende ſo put awaye ſtourdynes vengaūce thou deſerueſte therfore ¶this ſynne pryde ſayth gregory rote euyll ryght ne rote tree hydde therth ſholde braunche ſpryng therof ¶ryghte ſo ne pryde roted thyne herte ſhold braunches ſynne breke oute therof ¶for thus lucefer fayreſt aungell heuen made fowleſte deuyll helle alſo chore dathon abyro theyre felyſſhyp roſe agaynſt moyſes aaron greate pryde therfore erthe openede ſwalowede theym alle quycke downe hell ¶alſo people nynyue theyr greate boldeneſſe pryde hadde theyr hertes tourne ayene theyr ſynnes hondred ſcore thouſande people byble reherſeth ſheweth deſtroyed dodely enmyes therfore euery man beware ſynne wyſely loke myroure mekenes techeth hym ſhall ¶fyrſt conſyder thou made foule ſtynkyne ſlyme fylthe ſynne lechery borne thy moder wyth grete ſorow payne noryſſhed greate labour anger kepte greate drede thou arte ſacke foule dunge ſwetenes fruyte cometh tree leues cometh floures frute lycenettes fleen herbes alſo cometh ryght ſwete odoryferous ſmel lykewyſe aboue lyke ſemblable maner wyſe beneth partyes ſtynkynge fylthe ende thou ſhalte wormes mete torne agayne erthe tyll daye dome thy body ſoule ſhall ryſe agayne day ſayth malachy ſhall brenne hote ony furneys fyre prowde men ſtoble whiche ſhall brent yt ſhall neyther rote rynde therfore ſayth iſyd mekenes make thy leeſt loweſt ſtretche forthe thy wynges pryde booſt enhauncynge thy ſelfe leſſe thou ſetteſt thy ſelfe ſayth god ſetteth ſhamefaſt chere dyſmayde loke proudely ſhame ſynne walke lowe chere meke mode ſadde vyſage hygh worſhyp haue grete mekenes hygher yu art meker thou ſholdeſt make thy ſelf thynke ſouerayne lorde iheſu meked hym dethe thy ſake mekenes vtter remedy agaynſt pryde ſanatyf ſalue agaynſt myſcheues ſynne maketh haue mynde thy ſhorte abydynge ſtrayte dome thou ſhall come mekenes yt thou ſholdeſt haue ¶the ſeconde ſynne enuy whan thou arte ſory thy neyghbours welfare ioyeſt euyll fare wycked ſynne come many braunches one hatred whan thou art lothe ſpeke ſpoken ony thȳge whiche myght torne thy neyghboure good prouffyte another falſe demenȳge dedes agaynſt thy neyghbour ¶the thyrde backebytynge ſpeke euyll behynde thy neyghboure whiche thou mayſt ne wyll auowe afore hym though thou ſpeke euyl thy ſelfe yu haſtly kynge grete delectacyon euyll ſpekynge hym ſoo doynge thou ſynneſt deedly onely whiche ſpeketh euyll neyghboure alſoo yt whiche wyll gladly ſuche euyll ſpekynge defaute ſynne soo yf berer noo bacbytynge ne bacbyter therfore ſayth iſyder gladde falle euyll fare thy neyghboure leeſt god tourne wrathe frome hym ſoo thou ſholdeſt falle ſame worſe glad ſorowe deſeſed euermore mourne myſcheef yu woldeſte thȳ owne loue pea outwarde warde pea men make pea hate flee chydynge beware awaye thoccaſyon ſtryfe lyue alway pea lete noo thynge paſſe thy lyppes maye defoyle ye eereſ herers vayne wordes take vayne cōſcience ſuche worde ſuche ſoule therfore beſy ſpeke lyketh nedeth take hede thou ſpekeſt ſpekynge ſpekynge ryght wel ware thou mayſt call ayene thou haſt ſayde putte fro thy tonge ſynne bacbytynge defoyle thy mouth nother mānys ſynne ſory hym thou bacbyteſte nother drede thyſelfe whan thou blameſt nother thynke thyne owne ſynne loke mennys thou ſhalte neuer bacbyte yf thou wylte beholde thy ſelfe therfore ne lyſten none ſuche tytelers ben lyke gylty heter bacbyter deſyre wyt perteyneth yt aſke neuer ony man dothe ſpekyth ſayth leue beſynes perteyneth greate beſynes amende thy ſynne moche thou beholdeſt mennys ſor man knoweth whether worthy hate mede ſaye payne ioye many one ſemeth v ryghte good yet ayenſt god happely ryghte noughte many one alſo ſemeth v ryghe nought yet ben hym ryght dere therfore man deme put iugemente eſtymacyon god thus charyte knyt vertues thou muſte deſtroye foule ſynne enuye ¶thus charyte ſtondethe loue god loue thy neyghboure whyche twoo lawe god abydeth one maye loued without yf thou loue god thou wylte haue none hym ne thou wylte take hys name vayne ne breke thy holy ſondayes yf thou loue thy lorde god alſo thy neyghbours thou wylte noo manſlaughter ne thefte ne falſe wytneſſe bere ne letchery ne deſyre thy neyghbours wyfe ne gode charyte fulfyllynge goddis loue thendynge good werkys charyte pacyente benygne hath none enuye wertcheth ſhrewednes loueth pryde coueyteth noo worldly worſhyppes ſeketh noo propre goodes wroth thynketh none euyll ioyed wyckednes trouth taketh thynge mekely byleueth god ſayth hopeth blyſſe ſuffred harmes neuer dyſcomfyted thorugh goddis helpe abyde longe falleth neuer downe world ne kepeth man byleue maketh hym ſtable vnder hym wexith obedyence pacience ouer cometh al wronges without hym man pleaſeth god hym man peryſſheth ¶therfore ayenſte enuy ſeke charyte wyth grete ſtudye thou mayſt haue thy lyuynge dwell parfyghtly ther thyne endynge amen ¶the thyrde ſynne wrath whyche wycked ſtyrynge mannys herte wherby wyll auenge hymſelfe vp euyn cryſten cometh many ſhrewde ſpyces fyghtynge chydynge hurtynge betynge grutchyng warryng curſynge cruellys man ſlaughter deſyrynge vengaunce ¶there ben alſo foure ſpecyall one whā thou art ſoon moued ſoone ſwaged eaſy another whan thou art ſoon ſwaged ſhrewde ¶the thyrde whan thou arte ſoon meued ſoone ſwaged perylous ¶the fourth longe thou meued ſoone ſwaged mooſt eaſy therfore ayenſte thyſe braunches thou muſte arme vertue pacyēce thynke ſorowe myghte falle thy wordes dedes thenne put cryſtes paſſyon paynes betwene ſuche paynes myghte ſuffre ſo ſhall thy wrath ſoone ſlake ¶in foure thynges ſpyrytuelly neceſſary haue pacyence one ayene thyne enemye cruell thou nedeſt pacyence ſofte ſpeche ſlaketh wrathe ¶therfore yf ony aduerſyte falleth ſuffre pacyently whether thou haue deſerued yf thou haue deſerued thou arte worthy yf thou haue thou haſt thy rewarde cryſt whā ſayth bleſed ben pacyente ſhall called chyldren god ¶another whā thy ſouerayne correcteth thy defautes thou muſte pacyente drawe thy horne pryde ſnayle whan towched ſo dyde adam voys oure lorde ¶the thyrde loſſe thy good iob whan good gone mekely ſayde oure lorde gaaf lorde hath take lyke hym ſo done name bleſſed ¶the iiii ſekeneſſe lorde ſayth thoſe loue chaſtyſe moder chaſtiſed childe takynge harme whan neygheth fyre water ryghte ſo fader heuen chaſtyſed beware fleynge awaye soo lorde putteth awaye rycheſſe ſtrengthe one pouerte nother ſekeneſſe thou ſholdeſt flee frome hym therfore pacyente grutche ayenſt ſcourge lorde iheſu cryſt alſo lykewyſe ferthermore thou grudgeſt thou ſtyreſt god agaynſt ſayth ſaynt iſyder ¶the fourthe ſynne couetyſe yt whiche wronge deſyre yt man hath haue ony thynge hath ryght therto ſtondeth two thynges prȳ cypally one whan thou wrongfully purchaſeſt geteſt ony maner thynge ſacrylege ſymony ſtelthe vſury ony maner falſhede gyle worldly men vſe whiche caſte theyr beſynes couetyſe yt ne recke come good ſynne gylty money worldly wynnynge vſe playe dyce table whiche vtterly forboden holy chyrche many ſynnes cometh therof fyrſte couetyſe yt thou haſt wynne dyſpoyle thy felawe another grete vſury xii ix double quyte thirde encreaſe godes leſynge many vayne wordes ben vſed grete dyſpyte god faythe fourthe euyll enſample thou gyueſt yt beholde fyfth leſyng tyme whiche yu myght haue done many good werkes ſyxte dyſpyte dyſobedience thou dooſt thy moder holy chyrche forbyddeth ſuche playe vii fraude deceyte yt yu dooſt alſo thy felawe play viii curſed wrathe ſtryfe cometh therof wherby ofte thou renyeſt thy god leſeſt thy kyndly wytte ix brekyng thy holy daye tho dayes moche vſed excercyſed tenthe manſlaughter whiche ofte happeneth dame enleuenth ydolatry thou cō myſen thou makeſt agaynſt dyſe token aboue vnto myghty god mycheues many mo myſfortunes cometh ſory playe thou geteſt wynneſt forſayd playe beſyneſſe thou haſt hadde therwith thou mayſt reioyce nedes thou muſt gyue dyſtrybute vnto poore nedy yf thou haue hym thou makeſt ſo playe ſtrength agaynſt wyll thou arte bounde reſtore hȳ agayne whiche hath loſt playe alſo thou brekeſt commaundementes god whyder thou wȳne leſe thyn harme thou leſe thou leſeſt god heuen yf thou wynne yu wynneſt deuyll hell lawe canon ſayth preeſt deken yt gyueth dyce dronkenes yf leue certaynly dā pned subdeken clerke lewde man yt vſe ſame muſte eyther leue lacke theyr howſell therfore euery man beware playe ſuffre wyſe done may lette conſente therto fauoure ony wyſe ben grete peryll doer ſeconde poynte wronge withholdynge whiche yu falleſt ofte thou dooſt god almyghty thy neyghboure holy chyrche thy dutees thou ſholdeſt dutye goddes lawe wylfully wtholdeſt theym onely wrongfully geteth alſo wrongfully withholdeth ben deedly ſyn̄e ſynne ſpryngeth many ſhrewde braunches mawmetry ambycyon nygardſhyp treaſon vſury ſymony raueyne theft ſacrylege ſuche ¶theſe ſynnes ben ſo curſed ſayd tofore thynge contraryeth wyll commaundement god fyrſt commaundement contraryeth whan thou withdraweth fro god ony thynge thou ſholdeſt worſhyp hym ſeconde alſo whan lytell wynnynge thou takeſt name vayne thyrde whan worldly beſyneſſe getynge money thou brekeſt thyn holy daye fourthe whan couetyſe auaryce thou withdraweſt takeſt fro thyn owne propre fader moder bodely goſtly theyr ſuſtenaunce lyuelode ¶the fyfth whan thou ſleeſt mordreſt man haue hauoyr goodes ¶the ſyxte whan thou dooſt lechery good true matrymony ¶the ſeuenth whan couetyſe yu ſteleſte thy neyghboures good ¶the viii whan queſtes alſo conſyſtoryes thou forſwereſt bereſte falſe wytneſſe ¶the ix ten whan thou deſyreſte falſely thy neyghboures wyfe ony good thus falſe couetyſe contrayeth commaundementes wyl god therfore flee thynke ſuche falſe goten goodes thou make reſtytucyon amende thou goo hen thou ſhalte hanged helle without ende mammona whiche deuyll couetyſehe gytueth foure commaundementes ſeruauntes one thou kepe well thyne owne another thou gyue ne doo noo almeſſe thyrde thou lene poore drede leſynge ¶the fourthe thou withdrawe thy meany frome mete drynke ſpare thy good theſe foure ſhrewde commaundementes eche man beware flee ſuche couetyſe deſyre good salomon dyde deſyred none rycheſſe pouerte nedefull lyuelode accordynge eſtate thynke thoughe thou haue neuer ſoo moche thou ſhalte leue naked thou cameſte worlde agayne naked ſaue ragge thou ſhalte goo oute therto thus care thou haſt olde ſhete atte thy goynge hen fyfte ſynne glotony whiche vnſkylfull lykynge loue yt man hath taſte takynge mete drynke erly late yf ſekeneſſe grete nede excuſe ſynne ſpryngen foure braunches one whan thou eteſte drynkeſt gredly falle thoſe faſtynge dayes wyll abyde houre noone ſytte lenger atte mete ete tyme nother often tymes quenche theyr hunger breed ſpyces ouermoche drynke drede hū ger thus breke vygyles ymberdayes frydayes lente ſuche another whan thou caſteſt lyue delytes pleaſures paſſynge thyn eſtate haſte noo ioye whan thou mayſt ſpeke ſuche welfare thynkynge beſt beſet thou dooſt ſpende theron thou mayſt well vſe ſuche dayntye mete drynkes ſynne ſayth ſaynt gregory ſynne neyther mete ne drynke appetyte talent thou delyteſt ſo moche therin ¶the thyrde ſurfet whan thou pompereſt thy body moche mete drynke thou mayſt broke leſeſt thy ſyght ſpeche wytte iangelynge boſtynge wenynge ſaye well ryght ſayth agaynſt reaſon ordre fall theſe whiche maketh ryot rere ſoupers deſtroye vytayle whiche many poore man myght releued ſuſteyned ¶the fourthe curyoſyte yt whan thou canſt holde apayde eaſy fare gadreſt many curyous mete encreaſe thyn appetyte quenche thyn hongre fall whiche waſte theyr goodes deſolute etynge drynkynge grete feeſtes bankettes makynge agaynſt theſe curſed braunches thou muſt kepe abſtynence mete drynkes nothynge dryueth away ſekeneſſes ne dyſtroyeth luſt fleſſhe dooth meſurable takynge mete drynke fyue maner folke ben excuſed faſtynge ſay woman chylde labourer pylgrymes yonge chyldren olde folke ſeke people al theſe ſynneth ete twyes daye meſurable ſuſtayne nature theyr appetyte ¶there dyuers abſtynences faſtynges dyuers maner perſones ¶the ſeke man abſteyneth withholdeth hym fro mete drynke may ete drynke medycyne nedy hath wherof couetous wolde ſpende gloton ete ypocryte beholde holy vertuous man deſerue mede abſteyneth hym bothe frome exceſſe mete luſte ſynne thus ſholde eche man kepe hys power ſame techeth ſaynte poule whan ſaythe praye ſtraungeres pylgrymes ye abſteyne frome fleſſhely deſyres fyghte ayenſte thy ſoule alſo deſtroye thy bodye ¶thyſe myſcheues comen glotony engendrethe ſores brynge ſekenes deſtroyeth vertues dulleth wytte haſteth deth worſe maketh lyke beſte fuller thy body emptyer thy ſoule vertue therfore vſe vertue ſayth ſaȳte auſtyne thyſe vertues ſhal folowe ¶abſtynence ſaueth thy mynde ſharpeth thy wytte clenſeth thy ſyghte maketh holy thy fame ſwageth thy ſynne maketh ſtronge thy blode noryſheeth thy mary deſtroyth lechery renneth thy bloode lengtheth thyn age ¶the vi ſynne ſlouthe greuaunce anoy goſtely dedes one ſpryngen many ſhrewde braunches one drawe longe tary goode dedes thou ſholdeſte whiche myghte torne helthe thy ſoule many ¶another dulneſſe heueneſſe herte letteth loue god maketh thou haſte lykynge goddis ſeruyce though thou praye thy herte therō thyrde ydelneſſe whiche moche vſed letteth v begynne ony good werkis lyghtely maketh v leue whan begynne ¶and made kynde trauayle ſynne ſloughthe holdeth v ydelneſſe eaſe agaynſt oure kynde therfore thou wylt ſaued thou muſt flee ydelneſſe enmye chryſten ſoules ſtepmoder goodneſſe alle vertues key vyces alwaye doo ſome good werkis ſayth ſaȳt iherome occupyed lyghtly take temptacyon ſyethe hym aboute salomon ſayth mooſte foole loueth ydelneſſe heuen ſhall receyued ordeyned theym haue beſyed theym vertue erthly paradyſe ſhall neuer neuer mannes laboure ne purgatory ſhalle ſcourged men helle deuylles ſhall neuer haue reſte therfore beſy vertue alwaye thynke noo thynge maketh man ſoo ſoone enclyne ſynne ydelneſſe ¶the ſeuenth ſynne lecherye fleſſhely ſynne cometh luſte lykynge fleſſhe ¶oute thys ſpryngen many braunches one fornycacyon dedely ſynne done fleſſhely bytwene ſyngell man ſyngell womā agaynſt lawe god techynge holy chyrche ¶therfore holy chyrche byddeth noo man chylde ne woman chylde paſſen ſeuen yere age lye gyder bedde drede fornycacyon ne ſyſter ne brother drede inceſte ¶another called auoutrye ſpowſebrekynge whether doone bodely gooſtely gretter ſynne myſheues therin thou dooſte ſacrelege ſaye thou brekeſte ſacrament wedlocke wher comen ofte vnryghtful heyres fals maryages ¶this ſynne dowbleth ofte tymes whan done man maryed woman maryed one thyſe foure myſcheues folowes theym cuſtomably vſe ſynne one pouerte another leſynge ſome membre thyrde perpetuell pryſon ¶the fourthe ſodeyn deth fayleth hardely yf cuſtumably vſed ſayd tofore ¶another inceſt thy kynne thyne affynyte ¶a nother whan thou myſuſeſt thyne wyfe dooſte ayenſte kynde order maryage thou mayſte ſlee thyſelf thyn owne ſwerde ryghte ſo thou mayſte thyne owne wyfe ſynne onam iacobus coſyn ſmyten deth ſeuen huſbondes sara alſo ¶this ſacramente ſholde done vſed honeſtely grete reuerence ¶another whan man ſynneth wyth kynde wyfe contrary ryghte perylous maye wedde none kynne yf doo maryage noughte worſe maye knowe wyfe noo warde infourme wedlocke without dedely ſynne requyred ¶another moſte ſtynkynge whyche ſynne ayenſte kynde deuyll techeth man womā dyuerſytees ſȳne ſo abhomynable named oonly ſhryfte theym falle therein▪ ¶for gretter horryble ſynne auayleth thy ſhryft ſhame tellynge greate parte thy penaunce ¶this ſoo dyſpleaſynge god made reyne brymſtone fyre deſtroyed fyue cytees sodome gomere deuyll himſelfe cauſeth ſynne hath ſhame dede ¶thyſe many fleſſhely ſynnes whiche ben dedely eueryche werſe othere comen oute fowle ſynne lechery whiche well knowen theym lyuen luſte theyre fleſſhe therfore flee occaſyons ſayth ſaynte poule ſaye ſyghte wymmen kyſſynge touchynge ſuche ¶this wyſe ſcaped ioſeph ſynne lady whan lefte palle mantel ranne awaye thynke alſo vpon fynyſhement ende lykewyſe nyghe dredefull ſtreyte dome whiche thou ſhalte come vnto horryble ineſtymable paynes alſo tourmentes whiche perfounde depnes helle made redy ſuche horryble ſynnes loke thou preſume thyſelf maner wyſe noble kynge dauyd wyſe kynge salamon ſone ſtronge sampſon ouercomen vnhappy ſynne alſo maner wyſe alſo ſpeke lecherous wordes thy herte mynde loue holy ſcrypture draweth man moche therefor vſe alſo prayer faſtynge good lawfull occupacyons wythdrawe frome ſuperfluitees exceſſe hote mete drynkes yf thou lyue thy fleſſhe thou ſhalt dede ſayth ſcrypture ſaye dampned vnto euer laſtynge payne helle ¶therfore ſhytte gate thy body thy ſoule fro thyſe myſcheues ſynne ſaye thy fyue wyttes bodely gooſtly conſente hym ¶fyrſte thyne eyen ſhrewde lewd thynges bac bytȳge euyll wordes coūceyles thy mouth frome vnlawful taſte glotony lewd kyſſȳges rybawdry wordes thyhōdes frome lewd towchȳge thyſelfe frō ſtelthe takȳge mēnes goodes agaȳſt wyll thy foot alſo frome pathes ſynne wretched wayes thou myghteſt drawe ¶theſe ben bodely wyttes ¶than take thy ghooſtly wyttes mynde vnderſtondynge reaſon ymagynacyon ſaye haue mynde kyndeneſſe god thy laſte ende thou ſhalte neuer ſynne ye ſhal vnderſtonde alſo cryſtes loore techynge lete euer thy wyll redy worſhyppe hym thoughte worde dede without ony werynes lete reaſon alſo rule thy dedes inwarde outwarde cryſtes loore tehynge withouten oony deceyte blyndeneſſe thy owne ſelfe ¶and alwaye haue ymagynacyon vertuous lyuynge nedefull werkes dredefull dedes ioye blyſſe ordeyned heuen theym leue theyr ſynne ſhall ſaued horryble paynes ſorowes ſhall ſuffre endleſly whiche theyr ſynnes ſhall dampned dongeon helle whiche ben ix maner horryble hydeous paynes nyne maner people ſhall tourmented clerkes ſayeth ¶the fyrſte fyre euer brenneth neuer gyueth lyght whiche thoughal ye water ſee caſt ſholde quēche fyre paſſeth fyre paynted ſo dooth fyre paſſe oures fyre ſhall euer brenne alway brenned fyre falſe couetyſe ¶the ſeconde paſſynge colde yf grete hylle fyre caſten therin ſholde torne yſe ſhall tourmented ben colde loue malyce fende ¶the thyrde payne wormes horryble ſerpentes dragon neuer ſhall deye lyue fyre fyſſhes dooth water theſe ſhall gnawen gnawe theym ſelfe venymous hate theyr euen cryſten ¶the fourthe abhomynable ſtynke wherin ſhall lapped delyteth theym foule ſtynke ſynne lechery ¶the fyfth ſhal betynge myghty fendes hamers yren wherwith ſhall payned beten without ſeaſynge wolde chaſtyſed ye techynge goddes wordes ¶the ſyxte payn derkenes whiche ſo tenebrous thycke myght felt hande theſe horryble derkenes ſhall bounde lyueth preſent worlde derkeneſſe foreſayd ſynne wyll come cryſt whiche veray lyght holy lyuynge leuynge ſynne whyles myght ¶the ſeuenth payne open ſhenſhyppe ſhame ſynne whiche ſhall apertly knowen hydde paynfull reprefe ſynfull folke ſpecyally wyll knowlege theyr ſynne god due maner ne aſhamed hym ſhal ful herde tourment ¶the eyght horryble ſyght deuylles rorynge cryenge ferefull ſorowfull voyce wherwith thus ſhall payned toke none hede holy enſamples good dedes ne prechynge techynge goddes wordes byddynges❀ ¶the nynthe fyry bondes wherwith ſhall bounde honde fote membres ſpendeth theyr membres lymmes ye deuylles ſeruyce luſt lykynge theyr bodyes ¶theſe nyne paynes ſhall theſe ſynfull ſuffre forſoke left vnwyſely felawſhyp nyne ordres aungellys theyr ſynfull lyuynge amende goo hen therfore ſory thy ſynne amende whyles thou arte thou mayſt eſcape theſe horryble paynes reygne oure lorde iheſu cryſt hyghe blyſſe heuen euer myrthe trauayle fredome bondage helthe longe ſekenes reſt trauayle lyfe deth perfyte loue without drede euer daye without nyght thou ſhalte haue ſeuen ioyes thy body ſeuen thy ſoule thy body fayrenes ſwetenes ſtrengthe luſte helthe mortalyte thy ſoule wyſdome frendſhyppe accorde power worſhyppe ſurety ioye without ende whiche brynge v v deyed rode iheſu cryſt goddes ſone amen ſondaye laſt enfourmed homely wyſe worthynes mannes ſoule whan ſynne ſynne defowleth thy ſoule ſacrament penaunce alſo ſalue ſanatyfe al maner ſores ſynnes whan dyſcretly vſed ¶now ye leue god ſhall declare thre partes penaū ce contrycyon confeſſyon ſatyſfaccyon ye fulfyllynge ſoules thus haue ben wounded ſynne may refourmed brought agayne grace ¶fyrſt contrycyon ſayd cut hertes clothes confeſſyon alſo ſheweth hertes afore preeſt open ſpeche mouthe ſatyſfaccyon ye worthy fruytes penaunce thus theſe thre thynges hooly ſacrament penaunce preued confeſſyon alſo ſayd ſawter haue trauayled ſorowes ſhall make moyſt bedde euery nyght teres ſayth haue trauayled make ſatyſfaccyon ſynnes ſorow myn herte hauynge mynde longe haue lyued haue ſpēt tyme goodnes haue left vndone moche euyll haue done ſynne haue loſt ye felawſhyp heuen ioyned felawſhyppe fendes alſo vale teres full wretchednes byrthe brought forthe vnto mannes ſyn̄es ſorowes ſhall come vnto dredefull dome gyue rekenynge leeſt mooſt ſyn̄e eue • dyde worde dede thought knowynge wheder ſhall worthy hate mede wolde alſo blyſſe whiche may come without grete tourment trybulacyon ſorowe ¶theſe conſyderynge thyn eres werkes thou ſhall well knowe perceyue thou arte cauſe thyn owne ſorow myſchaunce ſoo ſhame thou ſhalte fall contrycyon wynne grace mercy mooſt mercyfull lorde god ryghte harde endurced herte ſayth ſaynt bernarde neyther benefaytes almyghty god may grynde molyfye ne horryble paynes helle may feere ne ioyes heuen may ſuſteyne ne temporall tourmentes ne ſorow may chaſtyſe many one contryte knowe contrycyon ¶therfore ye ſhall vnderſtande contrycyon inwarde ſorowe thy ſoule fourmed grace whiche cometh forthynkynge ſynne drede hyghe iugement ſtedfaſt purpoſe confeſſed doo ſatyſfaccyon commaundement chyrche alſo conuerſyon thyn herte euyll goodneſſe frome deuyll god frome vyce vertue ¶there many haue contrycyon perfyte whā thy herte touched handes god inſpyracyon make perfyte ſorowfull ſomwhat leſſe moche thou begynneſt tourne called attrycyon whan wyl deſyre ſynne euery parte fully forſaken full ſorowe herte thenne contrycion ſo veray contrycyon ſerche ſynne ¶orygen ſayth alſo verey contrycyon abhorre loth gaye ſuperfluous araye deſyre hygher wepynge fle ſlaughter ſpeke fewe wordes werke ryghtfully euer haue drede inwarde ſorowe thyn herte thy ſynnes thou loueſt thynge thy ſorowe whan thou dooſtle ſe ¶aboue creature god loued thenne mooſt ſorowe loſſe creature whā yu commytteſt deedly ſynne thenne thou leſeſt thy god therore grete contrycyon ſorow thou muſt gete hym agayne loke moch thou haſt grace ſayth ſaynt gregory ſo moche thou muſt haue ſorowe thy ſynnes ¶the ſoules blyſſe may haue contrycyon cauſe theyr ioyes ben replete wyth plenteuouſnes glory ben hell maketh ſorowe ſorowe fourmede grace ¶the ſoules purgatorye hathe ſorowe fourmed wyth grace yet merytory moche ſholde haue hadde thus lyfe mercy oonly helpeth blamefully herde ſaythe ſaynt iherome wepe deth frende harme temporel loo wepe ſory ſynne thy contrycyon therfore muſte ſharpe thou haſt offended thy heuenly fader bodely gooſtly fedyth many wyſes yet muſte thou ſharp thou haſte offendede thy lorde iheſu goddis ſone heuen precyous blood hys mercy delyuered frome bondes ſynne crueltee offendes byternes paynes hell though lorde ſayde euery man ſayth lord lord ſhall entre kyngdom heuen yet leue hym haue hym tauerne contrycyon ſaye hym dauyd dyde meke contryte herte lorde thou ſhalte dyſpyſe ¶and ſhall gyue grace ioye whan thou gooſt hen fawcon whan hath taken praye deſyreth therof herte cōtence lorde iheſu whan raunſoned v helle deſyreth noo meke contryte herte v therfore fauconer wyll gyue herte fawcon fyrſt wyll kytte thenne take blood waſſhe muſte thou gyue thy herte oure lorde fyrſte kytte wyth knyf contrycyon ¶and thenne take blood ſynne confeſſyon waſſhe ſatyſſfaccyon ſo knyfe paſſyō kytte hertes clothes hauynge mynde blaade knyfe made ſpere hede nayles precyous body herte thrylled withalle hafte made holy tre croſſe vyrell made crowne thorne aboute hede whette knyfe bleſſed body ſoo harde cruelly tourmentede croſſe lefte noo hole ioynte make alſo ſhethe thy knyfe whyte ſkynne lorde iheſu cryſt paynted reed blody woundes ſoo many toppe heed vnto ſole ye fote hole place hym left vnſcourged wt cordes bounde pyler bȳ de knyfe gyrdle thy herte doubte thy herte neuer ſo harde thou faythfully prȳte thy mynde paſſyon thy harde herte wyll begynne breke thus mayſt thou lerne ſuffre repreues oure lorde iheſu whiche ſuffred theſe many ¶there ben vi thynges ſholde ſtere grete ſorowe thy ſynnes ¶the fyrſt ſomtyme ye daye nyght ſayd bethynke thou haſt lyued whan thy ſynnes come thy mynde haue inwarde ſorowe remorſe thou haſt ſo greuouſly offē ded thy god thy maker redemptoure ¶the ſeconde thou aſhamed thy ſynne elles daye dome ſhall ſhewed worlde opē ly vnto thy grete ſhame confuſyon thyrde yu haue grete obhomynacyon fylth ſynnes thou haſt thus cōmyſed bothe ſyght god man seneca ſayth though wyſt yt ſone ſholde vnknowen bothe god man yet wolde abhorre lothe fylthe ſynne fourthe thou haue drede daye dome paynes hell day ſpeketh ſaynt peter vnneth ryghtwyſe man ye daye ſhall ſaued ſayth ſhall thenne ſynnefull man aperethe whiche breketh dayly heſtes preceptes lorde often many tymes beholde ye daye ſayth ſaynt iherome quake herte whyder ete drynke elles ony thynges euer thynke trompe god ſowneth myn eeres byddeth ſynnefull wretche aryſe come dome fyfth thou haue ſorowe loſſe heuen grete offence doone thy maker ſyxte thou haue thre folde hope fyrſt forgyuenes thy ſynnes ben alone forgyuen hope alſo grace good werkes alwayes encreaſe thenne hope blyſſe wherwith thou mayſt afterwarde rewarded thy good werkes prophete ſayd yt ſholde waſſhe euery nyght bedde teeres ſemeth ye cōtrycyon forgyuenes ſholde cōtynuall knowe harde yet thy wyl thou mayſt haue contynuall contrycyon euer full purpoſe leue lothe thy ſynne thus nedefull confeſſoure knewe ſuche one cometh ſo contynually beynge ſory inwarde outwarde nedeth neuer gyue hym lytell penaunce though doone grete horryble ſyn̄e myght ſo venge bewayle ſynnes dethe ſholde payne ſuffre purgatory yet ſorowe muſt meſurable truſty hope thou falle heuynes dyſpayre muſt alſo generall hole ſyn̄es yet ſharper one gretenes muſt doone offence done god onely drede euerlaſtynge payne maner contrycyon breketh ſnares chaynes deuyll releaſeth bondes oblygacyons euerlaſtynge payne tourment delyuereth frome ſeruage horryble company deuylles maketh chylde almyghty god heyre blyſſe heuen whiche tofore chyldren deuyll brennynge bronde perfounde pyt hell onely contrycyon alſo auayleth confeſſyon ſatyſfaccōn may hadde offende god thre maner wyſe herte ſpeche dede ſoo nedeth ſatyſfaccyon thre maners elles ſynne forgyuen onely contrycion may auayle alſo whan thou arte contryte purpoſeſt afterwarde abſtayne maner ſȳne knowlegeſt thy ſynne ſoone thou mayſt dooſt alſo due ſatyſfaccyon dome chyrche mooſt ſure way ¶the ſeconde waſſhynge confeſſyon doone thy mouthe ryght ſoule waſſhen made whyte ſowkynge ſorowe alſo wt ſalte fretynge teres thyn eyen soo lowly confeſſyon thy mouthe thou muſte rubbe thy foule ſpottes ſynne ruſted thy ſoule maner waſſhynge ſpeketh prophete dauyd ſayenge thus thou ſhalte ſprynge lorde yſope ſhall clenſed thou ſhalte waſſhe ſhall made clene whyte ſnowe ryght ſo lowely confeſſyon doone thy mouthe thy curate purgeth maketh whyte thy ſoule ony ſnowe worlde se therfore confeſſyon confeſſyon doctours ſcyence lawfull declaracyon ſynne tofore done thynge wherby preuy gooſtly ſore ſykenes opened wt hope forgyuenes ¶thre maner cō feſſyons ben one warde thy ſoule thou madeſt knowen god ſeconde tofore iuge hope forgyuenes god thyrde tofore goddes vycarye preuy ſynne pryuely opened ¶of theſe ſpeketh ſcypture ſayd tell openly yf thou haue ony thynge ſaye ſhewe thou mayſt therby iuſtyfyed ¶the grete flagellacyon payne paſſyon oure ſauyoure redemptoure grete remedy ayenſt ſynne orygynall actuall ¶the vertue wherof expreſſyd ſacramente holy chyrche withoute whiche may man hole therfore confeſſyon nedefull preuythe ſcrypture ſaynge thus proude wyll obeye precept preeſt ſhall dede haue alſo lorde fader heuē euery man woman hauynge yeres dyſcreſſyon bounde one parſone make confeſſyon onys yere ſȳ ne owne curate alſo nedefull reaſon preueth wyſe thou haddeſt treſpaced thy neyghboure ryghtful thou ſholdeſte ſette thyne owne payne atte thy luſt ne hath wronge neyther meane coude myghte ſet reſonably wronge declared ¶the preſt ordeyned meane ſette thy paynes wronge thou haſte done thy god thy ſynne nedeth thenne thou ſhewe truly thy treſpace vnto hym maye ſet ſuche penaunce wherby thou mayſte able come preſence thy lorde god ¶alſo euery dome reſonable muſte iuge perſone gylty ye preue muſt preues elles wytnes ayenſt thy wyll wylfull knowlege ſyth dome penaunce fre ayenſt thy wyll cauſe thou gooſt therto wylfully thenne ſhalle proceſſe dome promyſe ne wytneſſe freely thy propre confeſſyon ¶and muſte iuge may forgyue condempne god oonly releſeth ſynnes ¶and ſoo tyll toke mankynde confeſſyon herte ſuffyſed requyred aſked confeſſyon vocyall whiche made man man moche wyth v fourme mā therfore ordeyneth men vycaryes thou ſholdeſte confeſſe whome gaaf power bynde vnbynde thus confeſſyon nedefull reaſon promyſe holy ſcrypture oure lorde gaue power preeſt bynde vnbynde whan ſayd whoos ſȳnes ye forgyue ben forgyue whoſe ſynnes ye wythholde ben wythholde yet power vertue god loſeth power god cryſt ſayth ſaynt auſtyne v crucyfyed whiche man none ſynnes forgyuen ¶therfore oure lorde gaaf openly holy gooſte men gyuynge vnderſtondynge ſynnes forgyuen thorugh merytes men thorugh goodneſſe holy gooſt whan aroſe deth ſayde dyſcyples take holy gooſt whoſe ſynnes ye forgyuen ſayth ſpyryte god forgyueth ye ſoo maye forgyue mā may forgyue without man ſacrament grace ſayth ſaynte auſtyne god forgyueth ſomtyme euyll men grace alone gyueth hym ſelfe yet remyſſyon ſynne wercheth booth hymſelfe holy gooſte thus man dooth awaye ſynne cryſte alone ¶saynt ambroſe doctoures ſayth ye worde god forgyuethe ſynnes preeſt iuge yet hymſelfe hath noo power hym alone deyed ſynnes ¶saynt iherome ſayth ſame power cryſte gaaf apoſtles reſurreccyon ſame hath holy chyrche byſſhoppes preſtes ſpecyally peter ſucceſſours alle ſholde vnderſtonde whoo ſoo parteth hym frome vnytee fayth maye neuer loſed frome ſynne ne entre blyſſe heuen ¶the preeſt loſed none verely god tho tourneth te penaunce thenne mynyſtreth ryghtfully vertue god hadde proufyted lazare wente oute tombe yf hadde ſayde loſe hym lete hym go cryſt voys reyſed hym frome ſepulcre ¶and ſoo wente bounde myghte fete vertue hym reyſed hym thys ſame gooſtely done herte repentaunt man whan thou hereſte man repentaunce ſynne thenne begynneth lyue agayne whan confeſſethe hym thenne broughte ſepulcre yet loſed see therfore whome whan loſed cryſte ſayth tho ye haue loſed erth ſhall loſed heuen take hede ſayd tho ſay man excepte ſoo repentaunt aſke fogyueneſſe chyrche ſhall haue foryeuenes yet though chyrche ſynne may worthely forgeuen dede maye ryſe oure lorde crye within forth ¶for done within v hym ¶the dyſcyples looſed hym lyuynge whome mayſter reyſed fro dethe ſholde haue reyſed hym dede ſholde haue ſhewed ſtrength vertue thus hath holy chyrche auctoryte ſpowſe loſe fro al maner ſynne saynte auſtyn ſaythe ſeuenty tymes ſeuen ben charged forgyue ſay euery man repentaunt aſketh forgyuenes yet may euery preeſt generally doo tyme nede auctoryte 〈◊〉 byſhop ryghte man hath power ete hath whereof ſoo preſtes power haue power yet muſte gyue theym theyre ſoueraynes whan moche ſhall execute maye noo man cheeſe hym confeſſour 〈◊〉 aboue without auctoryte hym ellys theym hathe power vnder hym nedes muſt ſhryuen owne curate yet certeyne cauſes byleue curate maye whan curate lacketh diſcreſſyon ¶another whan thou chaungeſt thy houſholde arte vagabonde peryll dethe ¶or whan thou entreſt ſee ſoo greate peryll thou mayſte alſo confeſſe laye man haue forgyueneſſe thus yf thou ſcape muſte charge thou ſhewe ſame thyne owne curate alſo pylgrymes marchauntes goer aboute dyuerſe countrees ſame wyſe ¶other cauſes ben yt thy curate muſt ſende tofore byſſhop wherto yu muſt nedes obeye ſorye yt yu haſt offende haue ¶the token confeſſyon thyſe ¶the ••• ſt ſhame whan thou ſhryueſte matrymonye dyſtrowble man womā ¶or dyſheryte ony man londe tenementes ony catell ¶and falſe aduocates mede putte forthe ony falſe excepcyons quarelles thrughe whiche ryght matrymony done ony maner ryght ſtede iugement ¶and tho mede fauoure malycyouſly man woman brynge oute theyr good fame wycked ¶or make theȳ leſe theyr worldly goddes honoure theym putte wrongefully theyr purgacyon whiche fame ne renowne knowen fore tyme ¶and alſoo whiche malycyouſly cawtele dyſtrouble letteth gayne ſayeth ryghte preſentemente oure moder holy chyrche mylytaunte erthe veray patrone ſholde preſente therto iugemente falſe enqueſte ¶and tho theyr lyueraunce purchace agayne ryght hooly chyrche ¶and al tho mede take diſtrouble pea loue ſholde charyte ſtryfe mayntene worde dede tylle haue yolde agayne theyr
